什麼是詞根	詞根是構詞的基本詞素，它與詞綴相對，並帶有主要的詞彙信息。	
詞根分為	能獨立構詞的是自由詞根，必須與其他詞素結合構詞的是粘附詞根。	
英語經歷了三個發展階段	古英語（Old English，盎格魯—撒克遜人統治）、中古英語（Middle English，使用法語與拉丁語的諾爾曼人統治）和現代英語（Modern English，歐洲文藝復興運動的影響）。	
詞綴分成兩種：	能與自由詞根結合的是派生詞綴，只能與粘附詞根結合的是原生詞綴。	
英語的主要構詞方式	有3 種：轉化、合成與派生	
零級派生=	粘附詞根+零原生詞綴 或 自由詞根+零派生詞綴	
一級派生=	粘附詞根+原生詞綴→原始派生詞或原生詞	
二級派生=	自由詞根+派生詞綴→二次派生詞	
大部分派生詞是	由粘附詞根與原生詞綴構成的原始派生詞	
英語詞根只有	單音節與雙音節兩種。從比例來看，單音節詞根占80％以上，雙音節詞根不到20％。本族語詞根中單音節的占90％左右，拉丁詞根中單音節的占90％以上，而希臘詞根中單音節的比例較低，約占30％左右。	
單音節詞根的基本模式是：	「輔音字母+元音字母+輔音字母」，如：man，vis，log 等	
構詞過程中發生的形態變化	主要有4 種：1.字母的增加，2.字母的脫落，3.字母的變更，4.連字符的使用	
派生詞中一般讀法	詞根重讀、詞綴輕讀	
自由詞根的讀音是	固定的，它等於充當自由詞根的基本單詞在詞典中的讀音	
粘附詞根讀音	在多數同根詞中都表現出相對固定的	
如果詞根在派生詞中重讀，其讀音	保持不變。這時，派生詞的讀音即等於各種詞素讀音總和。	
詞根是非重讀或次重讀音節，詞根的音值就	可能發生變化	
「詞根重讀、詞綴輕讀」例外有哪幾種4 種與前綴有關：	1.表示否定意義的派生前綴un-和non-與詞根同樣重讀；2.雙音節的前綴原生詞由動詞轉化成名詞或形容詞時，重音從詞根所在音節（第二音節）轉移到詞綴所在音節（第一音節）；3.借用的派生前綴（尤其是拉丁語源的派生前綴），為了表示其有別於同源同形的原生詞綴往往與詞根（單詞）一起重讀。；4.少數前綴在單詞中往往重讀。比較典型的有post-，self-，semi-等	
「詞根重讀、詞綴輕讀」例外有哪幾種3 種與後綴有關：	5.個別後綴總是重讀，典型的有-ee， -ese，-esque，-ette；6.有些後綴本身並不重讀，卻會使派生詞的重音發生有規則的轉移。最有代表性的是-ian，-ic，-ion 和-ity，它們總是使單詞重音落在自己的前一個音節上。7.有些派生詞重讀的例外現象並無規律可尋，只能把它歸因於歷史或習慣使然。對這些真正的「搗亂分子」，要特別予以注意。例如：`dif·fer，`com·mon，`com·fort 等。	
隱性詞按照隱性的程度，分三種情況	1.有些距離；2.本義在使用過程發生了變化。有的詞義擴大，有的縮小，有的揚升，有的貶降，有的則被用於比喻或引申；3.不但包含了詞根和詞綴的含義，還包括一定的背景知識。需要瞭解這些背景，才能理解在特定條件下才能成立的派生詞詞義。	
詞素間的制約關係	後綴＞詞根，後綴的屬性決定了派生詞的詞性；動詞詞素＞名詞詞素＞形容詞詞素＞副詞詞素。	
同源異形根現象主要出現於	拉丁動詞詞根，因為拉丁動詞有各種變化形式	
同源異形根現象輔音字母收尾的詞根，變成	以t 收尾的異形詞根,volv→volut,mov→mot	
同源異形根現象以t、d 收尾的詞根變成	以s 收尾的詞根,flect→flex,sent→sens	
術語詞綴有一個非常特殊的功能，即	一個術語前綴可以與一個術語後綴構成一個帶術語性質的單詞,aero-（空氣）+-logy（……學）→aerology n.氣象學	
術語前綴後面往往有	連接字母-o-或-i-，如：bio-，thermo-，denti-（齒）等。	
分析不同語源的粘附詞根，可以發現，（）詞根常構成一般用詞，（）詞根常構成科技術語	拉丁；希臘	
有些詞根是多義的。這主要是（）詞根，而且為數不多	拉丁動詞	
動詞詞根pend，pens 原意是()，由於把東西掛在天平上才能稱量，所以又有()的含義，又因為用天平稱量金銀來付款，又多了個(()的含義。	to hang（懸掛）;to weigh（稱量）;to pay（支付）	
詞根ag，act 既有()的意思，也有「驅使他人去做」的()之意	to do（做）;to drive（驅使）	
3. anim [L]=	life 生命<br>anim 是常用詞animal 的詞根，源於拉丁名詞anima，含有mind（思想），spirit（精神），<br>soul（靈魂），life（生存）等與生命現象有關的概念，可以看成英語基本詞life（生命）的對<br>等詞。<br>animal [anim=life 生命；-al n.=thing characterized by 有……特徵的東西→「thing characterized<br>by having life 有生命的東西」→] n. １ any creature 動物：Is it an animal, vegetable, or mineral?<br>它是動物，植物，還是礦物？２ any creature other than man 除人以外的任何動物：the animals<br>in the zoo 動物園裡的動物<br>▽animalism [animal;-ism n.] n.動物性；獸慾<br>animalize [animal;-ize v.] v.使動物化<br>animate [anim=life 生命；-ate a.=having 有……的→「having life or spirits 有生命的，有精神<br>的」→]Ⅰa. １ living 有生命的：animate objects 生物２ full of life or spirits 生氣勃勃的：<br>animate youth 朝氣蓬勃的年青人→Ⅱ v. give life to, or make alive 使活躍：His jokes an-imated<br>the conversation.他的笑話使交談活躍起來。<br>▽animation [animat(e) v;-ion n.] n.活躍；生氣<br>reanimate [re-;animate v.] v.使復活；激勵<br>animosity [anim=life, spirit 生命，精神；-osity（-ous+-ity）n.=special state or quality 表特殊狀<br>態或性質→ 「 special spirit 特殊的精神」 → 「 strong feeling 強烈的感情」 → ] n. strong<br>dislike;hatred 敵意；仇恨：animosities between classes 階級仇恨<br>magnanimity [magn=great 大；anim=spirit 精神；-ity n.=the quality 表性質→「the greatness of<br>spirit or mind 精神上的大度」→] n. the spirit of being unusually generous, or generosity 寬宏大<br>量：He showed his magnanimity in forgiving you.他原諒了你，可見其寬宏大量。<br>▽magnanimous [magn;anim;-ous a.] a.寬宏大量的<br>equanimity [equ=even 平衡的；anim=spirit 精神；-ity n.=the quality 表性質→「the spirit with an<br>even quality 平穩的精神品質」→] n. calmness or steadiness of mind 沉著；鎮定：He faced the<br>disaster with equanimity.面對災難，他泰然若定。<br>▽equanimous [equ;anim;-ous a.] a.沉著的；鎮定的<br>longanimity [long（來自形容詞longus）=long 長久的；anim=spirit 精神；-ity n.=the quality 表<br>性質→ 「 the spirit with the quality of enduring long 能長久忍耐的精神素質」 → ] n.<br>endurance;forbearance 忍耐性；堅韌性：He is remarkable for his longanimity in struggle.他在<br>鬥爭中以堅韌著稱。<br>▽longanimous [long;anim;-ous a.] a.堅韌的；忍耐的<br>unanimous [un=one 一；anim=spirit, mind 精神，思想；-ous a.=having 有……的→] a. having one<br>mind or sharing the same view 思想一致的；觀點統一的：The conference was unanimous in<br>support of the decision.會議一致擁護這項決議。<br>▽unanimity [un;anim;-ity n.] n.全體一致；無異議	
2. am, amat [L]=	to love 愛<br>常用詞amiable 和amateur 分別來自同源異形根am 和amat。am 是拉丁動詞amare 的不定式詞干；amat 是這個動詞的動名詞詞干，意思都相當於to love（愛）。<br><br><br>amiable [am=to love 愛；-i-；-able a.=capable of 可……的→「capable of being loved 可愛的」→] a. lovable, or kindly 可愛的；和藹的：an amiable old lady 可親的老太太<br><br><br>amateur [amat=to love; -eur (-er) n.=person 人→「persaon who does something for loving it(rather than for money)因愛好（不是為金錢）從事某項活動者」→] n. person who practices an&nbsp;art, sport or science for his own pleasure（藝術、體育、科學等）業餘愛好者：radio amateur<br>業餘無線電愛好者<br><br>▽amateurism [amateur;-ism n.] n.業餘活動<br><br><br>amateurish [amateur n.業餘愛者；-ish a.=like 像…的→「like an amateur（rather than a&nbsp;professional hand）像業餘的，不內行的」→] a. unskillful 不老練的，外行的：He is still amateurish&nbsp;in playing golf.他打高爾夫球還不老練。<br><br>▽amateurishness [amateurish;-ness n.] n.外行<br><br><br>amicable [amic（來自am 的同根名詞amicus）=person one loves, or friend 親愛者，朋友；<br>-able a.=able to be 能當……的→「able to be one's friend 能做朋友的」→] a. in a friendly spirit,<br>or peaceable 友好的；和睦的：amicable settlement 和解<br><br>▽amicability [amicab(le);-ility n.] n.友好；和睦<br><br><br>amour [am=to love 愛；-our n.=the state or result 表狀態或結果→「loving or the result of loving<br>戀愛或戀愛的結果）」→] n.１ love 戀愛２ love affair 桃色事件，偷情<br><br>▽amorous [amo(u)r;-ous a.] a.戀愛的；多情的<div><br><br>enamour [en-v.=to cause to be 使；amour n.=love 戀愛→「to cause to be in love 使戀愛」→] v.inflame with love 使迷戀：Her beauty enam-oured the prince.王子被她的美貌迷住了。<br><br><br>amatory [amat=to love 愛；-ory a.=related to 與……有關的→] a. related to loving;expressing<br>love 戀愛的；愛慕的：amatory poems 情詩</div>	
1. ag, act [L]=	to do, to drive 做，驅使<br>詞根ag 來自拉丁動詞agere 的詞幹部分，意思相當於英語的to do（做）或to drive（驅使）。<br>act 是個英語核心單詞，其實它的前身act 是ag 的同源異形詞根，來自agere 的動名詞形式<br>actum 的詞幹部分，基本含義也是to do 或to drive。下面先分析幾個由ag 構成的常見派生<br>詞。<br><br><br>agent [ag=to do 做；-ent n.=person 人→「person who does 辦事者」→] n. person who works for<br>another person or organization 代理人：a sales agent 代售商<br><br>▽agential [agent;-ial a.] a.代理人的；起媒介作用的<br><br><br>agency [ag=to do 做；-ency n.=the quality or state of 表性質或狀態→「the abiliy or place of<br>doing business 辦事的能力或場所」→] n.１power or force which causes a result 力量；作用：<br>human agency 人力２ the office of an agent;service organization 代理處；機構：travel agency<br>旅行社<br><br><br>agenda [ag=to do 做；-enda（-a 表複數）n.=things 事情→「things to be done 要辦的事項」<br>→] n. list of things to be discussed or decided upon 議事日程：the most important item on the<br>agenda 議事日程的首項<br><br><br>agile [ag=to do 做；-ile a.=able 能……的→「able to do 能幹的」→] a. able to do or move quickly<br>or easily 敏捷的；靈活的：as agile as a monkey 像猴子般靈活<br><br>▽agility [agil(e);-ity] n.敏捷；靈活<br><br><br>agitate [ag=to drive or keep moving 驅使，使運動；-itate（-ate）v.=make or cause 使……→「cause<br>to keep moving steadily 引起不斷的動盪」→] v. disturb 鼓動：The audience were agitated by his<br>speech 聽眾被他的演說所鼓動。<br><br>▽agitation [agitat(e);-ion n.] n.鼓動；激動不安<br>agitator [agitat(e);-or n.] n.鼓動者<br><br><br>以下介紹的是幾個常用act 的同根詞。<br><br><br>act [act=to do 做→「to do what is required 做要求的事」→] v. １ do something 行動：to act<br>at once 立刻行動２ function 起作用：The brakes wouldn't act.剎車失靈。３ take part in a play<br>or film 扮演：Who is acting Hamlet? 誰演哈姆雷特？<br><br>▽actor [act;-or n.] n.男演員；行動者<br>actress [act (o)r;-ess n.] n.女演員<br>re-act [re-;act v.] v.重做，再做；重演，再演<br>overact [over-;act v.] v.演得過於誇張<br><br><br>action [act=to do 做；-ion n.=the process or result 表過程或結果→] n.１ process of doing, or<br>deed 行動，活動：Actions speak louder than words.行動比語言更有說服力。２ result of doing,<br>or effect 作用：the action of an acid on metal 酸對金屬的作用３ charge 訴訟：to bring an<br>action against someone 起訴某人<br><br>▽actionable [action;-able a.] a.可控訴的<br>active [act=to do 做；-ive a.=able 會……的→] a. able to do 活躍的，積極的：Although he is over<br>70, he is still active.他雖然年過70，但依然很活躍。<br><br>▽activate [activ(e);-ate v.] v.使活動<br>activism [activ(e);-ism n.] n. [哲] 能動主義；積極，活躍<br>activist [activ(e);-ist n.] n.活動分子，積極分子<br>activity [activ(e);-ity n.] n.能動性；活躍；[復] 活動<br><br><br>actual [act=to do 做；-u-;-al a.=the act or fact 表行為或事實→] a. existing in fact;real 實際的；<br>現實的：the actual amount of money 實際金額<br><br>▽actualist [actual;-ist n.] n.現實主義者<br>actuality [actual;-ity n.] n.事實，現存情況；現實性<br>actualize [actual;-ize v.] v.實行，使現實化<br><br><br>actuate [act=to do 做；-u-;-ate v.=to make or cause 使……→] v. cause to do 驅動，激勵：What<br>motives actuated her? 什麼動機驅使她這樣做的？<br><br>▽actuation [actuat(e);-ion n.] n.驅動，激勵；開動<br><br><br>exact [ex-=out 出；act=to drive 驅使→「to drive out;driven out 逼出來（的）」→] I v. demand or<br>obtain by force 強求，索取：He exacted obedience from his students.他強要學生服從他。→<br>Ⅱ a. correct and without mistake 準確的，精確的：to be exact in conduct 行為一絲不苟<br><br>▽exacting [exact v.;-ing a.] a.苛求的，嚴厲的；強索的<br>exaction [exact v.;-ion n. ] a.強索；勒索；搾取<br>exactitude [exact a.;-itude n.] n.精確（性）；嚴格，嚴謹<br><br><br>react [re-=back 回返；act=to do 做→] v.１ do or act in reply 反應：She was slow to react.她反<br>應遲鈍。２ do against 反動，反作用：to react against oppression 反抗壓迫<br><br>▽reaction [react;-ion n.] n.反應；反作用；反動<br>reactor [react;-or n.] n.引起反應的人或物；[原] 反應堆<br>reactive [react;-ive a.] a.反應的；反動的<br><br><br>interact [inter-=between 在……之間；act=to do 做→「to do between two things 在兩者之間互<br>動」→] v. have an effect on each other 互相作用，互相影響：All things are inter-related and<br>interacted on each other.一切事物都是互相聯繫又互相影響的。<br><br>▽interaction [interact;-ion n.] n.相互作用；相互<br>interactant [interact;-ant n.] n. [化] 反應物<br>interactive [interact;-ive a.] a.互相作用的；[計] 交互的<br><br><br>transact [trans-=across or through 穿過；act=to drive 驅使→「to drive through 使通過」→] v.<br>carry on;manage 執行，辦理：He transacted some businesss at bank.他在銀行處理了一些事務。<br><br>▽transaction [transact;-ion n.] n.辦理，處理；交易，業務<br>transactor [transact;-or n.] n.辦事人，處理者	
各種語源的單詞在英語詞彙總量中占的百分比是	日耳曼語源（即本族語源） 33％；拉丁與希臘語源（即古典語源） 56％；凱爾特語源2％；混合語源3％；東方、非洲、美洲等語源6％	
有些後綴本身並不重讀，卻會使派生詞的重音發生有規則的轉移。最有代表性的是（），它們總是使單詞重音落在自己的前一個音節上	-ian，-ic，-ion 和-ity	
4. ann, enn [L]=	year 年<br>ann 來自拉丁名詞annus，意思為year（年）；enn 是ann 在添加前綴時產生的音變異體。ann<br>在構詞中常帶有連接字母-u-或-i-，也可以把annu 和anni 作為詞根異體看待。<br><br><br>annual [annu=year 年；-al a.=of……的→] I a. of one year;yearly 一年的；每年的：annual report<br>年度報告→Ⅱn. book or pamphlet issued once a year 年鑒；年刊：the annuals of the Historical<br>Society 歷史協會的年鑒<br><br><br>anniversary [anni=year 年；vers=to turn 轉；-ary n.=thing 物→「the date connected with the<br>turning of a year 與時間周轉一年相關的日子」→] n. the date of a year on which something<br>happened 週年紀念日：the 400th anniversary of Shakespeare's birth 莎士比亞誕生四百週年紀<br>念日<br><br><br>annals [ann=year 年；-al n.=thing 物；-s 表複數→「many things of a year 一年中的事情」→] n.<br>yearly records;historical records 編年史；歷史記載：the war annals of the Red Army 紅軍戰史<br><br>▽annalist [annal(s);-ist n.] n.編年史作者<br><br><br>perennial [per-=through 通；enni=year 年；-al a.→「through a year 通年的」→] a.１lasting through<br>the year 常年不斷的：perennial snow and ice 終年不化的冰雪２ overlasting 長久的：perennial<br>efforts 持久努力<br><br>▽perenniality [perennial;-ity n.] n.常年性；長久性<br><br><br>annuity [annu=year 年；-ity n.=thing connected with 表相關事物→「money connected with one<br>year 按一年計算的錢」→] n. yearly allowance or income 年金；年收入：life annuity 終身年金<br><br>▽annuitant [annuit(y);-ant n.] n.領受年金者<br><br><br>superannuate [super-=over 超；annu=year 年→age 年齡；-ate v.=to cause to be 使成為→「to<br>cause to be over-aged 使成為超齡者」→] v. make to retire when one is over a certain age 因超<br>過年齡而令退休：He was superannuated as soon as he reached the age of sixty.他剛滿六十歲，<br>就被指令退休了。<br><br><br>annu 和enni 還能與表示數目的前綴構成表示以「年」為單位的時間的單詞。以下是常見的<br>幾個。<br><br><br>semiannual [semi-=half 半；annu=year 年；-al a.=of……的→] a. of a half year 半年一度的：<br>semiannual meeting 半年一度的會議<br>biannual [bi-=two, twice 二，兩次；annu=year 年；-al a.=of……的→a. of twice a year 每年兩<br>度的：biannual examination 每年兩次的考試<br>biennial [bi-=two 二；enni=year 年；-al a.=of……的→「of two years 二年的」→] a. lasting two<br>years 持續兩年的：a biennial research course 兩年的研究課程<br>biennium [bi-=two 二；enni=year 年；-um n.=thing 物→「the time of two years 兩年的時間」<br>→] n. period of two years 兩年	
5. anthrop [GK]=	man 人類<br>anthrop 是本書介紹的第一個來自希臘語的詞根，它的詞源是希臘名詞anthropos，意思為<br>man 或human kind（人類）。在構詞中，anthrop 後面常跟著連接字母-o-，也可以把anthropo<br>看作異形詞根。<br><br><br>anthropology [anthropo=man 人類；-logy n.=branch of science 一門科學→「the science about<br>man 研究人類的科學」 → ] n. the science dealing with the physical, social, and cultural<br>development of man 人類學<br><br>▽anthropologist [anthropolog(y);-ist n.] n.人類學者<br><br><br>philanthropist [phil=to love 愛；anthrop=man 人類；-ist n.=person 人→「person who loves man<br>愛人類者」→] n. person who loves his fellow men, especially, who is engaged in helping the poor<br>men 博愛主義者；慈善家<br><br>▽philanthropy [phil;anthrop;-y n.] n.慈善；仁愛<br>philanthropic [phil;anthrop;-ic a.] a.博愛的<br><br><br>misanthropist [mis=to hate 恨；anthrop=man 人類；-ist n.=person 人→「person who hates his<br>fellow men 厭惡人類者」→] n. person who hates everybody and avoids being in the company of<br>others 離群索居者；憤世嫉俗者：A misanthropist can never become a philanthropist.憤世嫉俗<br>者是成不了慈善家的。<br><br>▽misanthropy [mis;anthrop;-y n.] n.厭世<br>misanthropic [mis;anthrop;-ic a.] a.厭世的；厭世者的<br><br><br>anthropoid [anthrop=man 人類；-oid a.=like 像……→] a. like a man;in the form of a man 類人<br>的；有人形的：anthropoid ape 類人猿<br><br><br>anthropography [anthropo=man 人類；-graphy n.=the study……學→「the study about man 有<br>關人類情況的學說」→] n. the study of the geographical distribution of human races 人種地理分<br>布學<br><br><br>anthropogenesis [anthropo=man 人類；genesis=the origin 起源→] n. the study of man's origin<br>and development 人類起源和發展學<br><br><br>anthropotomy [anthropo=man 人類；tomy=anatomy 解剖學→] n. human anatomy 人體解剖學	
6. arch [GK]=	rule 統治<br>在政治術語anarchy, monarch, monarchy 和oligarch 中，有個常用詞根arch。它來自希臘名詞<br>arkhos，意為rule（統治）。在派生詞中arch 常作ruler（統治者）或government（政體）解。<br><br>anarchy [an-(a-)=no, without 無；arch=rule 治理；-y n.=the state 表狀態→「the state without rule<br>or government 缺乏治理，沒有政府」→] n. absence of government or control 無秩序；無政府<br>狀態：Any form of government is better than anarchy. 任何形式的政體都比無政府狀態好。<br><br>▽anarchic [anarch(y);-ic a.] a.無政府主義的<br>anarchism [anarch(y);-ism a.] n.無政府主義<br>anarchist [anarch(y);-ist n.] n.無政府主義者<br><br><br>monarch [mon=one, alone 單一；arch=ruler 統治者→「only one ruler, or one who rules a country<br>alone 單獨治理國家者」→] n. king of sovereign 國王，君主：The monarch was ousted.國王被<br>趕下台了。<br><br>▽monarchal [monarch;-al a.] a.國王的，君主的<br><br><br>monarchy [mon-=one, alone 單一；arch=ruler 統治者；-y n.=the state 表狀態→「the state or<br>government of only one ruler 單人統治的政體」→] n. government ruled by a monarch 君主政<br>體；君主國：China was once a monarchy.中國曾經是個君主國。<br><br>▽monarchic [monarch(y);-ic a.] a.君主制的；君主國的<br>monarchism [monarch(y);-ism n.] n.君主制度；君主主義<br><br><br>oligarch [olig-=few 少，寡；arch=ruler 統治者→「one of a few rulers 少數統治者之一」→] n.<br>member of an oligarchy 寡頭統治成員：finan-cial oligarch 金融寡頭<br><br><br>oligarchy [olig-=few 少，寡；arch=ruler 統治者；-y n.=the state 表狀態→「the state or government<br>by a few rulers 由少數人統治的政府」→] n. rule or government by a few, often for their own<br>interests 寡頭政治；寡頭統治的政府：Ancient Sparta was really an oligarchy.古斯巴達實際上<br>是個寡頭統治的國家。<br><br>▽oligarchic [oligarch(y);-ic a.] a.寡頭政治的<br><br><br>polyarchy [poly-=many 多；arch=ruler 統治者；-y n.=the state 表狀態→「the state or government<br>by many rulers 多人的統治」→] n. rule or government by many heads 多頭政治<br><br><br>matriarch [matri=mother 母；arch=ruler 統治者→「a ruler who is a mother 母權統治者」→] n.<br>woman who rules a large family or tribe 女家長；女族長：This tribe is still led by matriarchs.該<br>部落依然以女族長為首。<br><br>▽matriarchal [matriarch;-al a.] a.女家長的；女族長的<br><br><br>matriarchy [matri=mother 母；arch=rule 統治；-y n.=the state 表狀態→「the state of rule by<br>mothers 母權統治」→] n. social group or system ruled only by women 母權制；母系氏族制：<br>Many ancient societies were matriarchies.許多遠古社會是母權制社會。<br><br><br>archives [arch=ruler 統治者；-ive n.=thing 物；-s 表複數→「documents belonging to rulers 屬<br>於統治者的文件」→] n.１ public records 檔案２ place in which public records are stored 檔案<br>室（館）：the central archives of the state 國家檔案館<br><br>▽archivist [archiv(es);-ist n.] n.檔案保管員<br>archival [archiv(es);-al a.] a.關於檔案的；在檔案中的<br><br><br>arch 還可以當前綴使用。arch-意思是chief（主要的）。<br><br><br>archenemy [arch-=chief 主要的；enemy n.敵人→] n. chief enemy 首敵；大敵<br><br><br>architect [arch-=thief 首要的；-i-;tect=builder 建築者→「chief builder 建築者的首領」→] n.<br>designer of buildings 建築設計師<br><br>▽architecture [architect;-ure n.] n.建築學<br>architectonic [architect;-onic(-ic) a.] a.關於建築的	
7. aud, audit [L]=	to hear 聽<br>在常用詞audience 和auditorium 中，有一對同源異形詞根aud 和audit，其詞源拉丁動詞audire<br>的意思是to hear（聽）。aud 是不定式詞干，audit 是動名詞詞干。<br><br><br>audience [aud=to hear 聽；-i-;-ence n.=the act or state 表行為或狀態→「the act or state of<br>hearing 聽的行為或狀態」→] n.１ interview or con-ference 會見；接見：The foreign guests had<br>an audience with the may-or.外賓拜會了市長。２ the people assembled to hear 聽眾：There will<br>be a large audience today.今天會有很多聽眾來。<br><br><br>auditorium [audit=to hear 聽；-orium n.=place 場所→「place for hearing 聽的場所」→] n.１<br>building or room for public meetings 禮堂；演講廳２ the space allocated to the hearers 聽眾席：<br>The author was found sitting in the auditorium.有人發現作者正坐在聽眾席中。<br><br><br>audible [aud=to hear 聽；-ible a.=capable of being 能被……的→] a. capable of being heard 聽得<br>見的：Their whispers are hardly audible.他們竊竊私語，別人聽不見。<br><br>▽inaudible [in-;audible a.] a.聽不見的<br><br><br>audit [audit=to hear 聽→「to hear a lecture or a report 聽課；聽取匯報」→] v. １ attend class<br>in a university without intending to receive a grade（在大學）旁聽：to audit a history course at<br>college 旁聽大學歷史課程２examine（financial accounts）審查（賬目）：The yearly accounts will<br>be audited by a special committee.年度賬目將由特別委員會審查。<br><br>▽auditor [audit;-or n.] n.（大學）旁聽生；查賬員<br><br><br>audition [audit=to hear 聽；-ion n.=the act 表行為→] n. １ hearing 聽２ trial hearing（to an<br>actor or singer）（對演員等）試聽：to give an audition to a singer 聽歌手試唱決定是否錄用<br><br><br>audile [aud=to hear 聽；-ile a.=pertaining to……的→] a. pertaining（關於，有關）to hearing or<br>the sense of hearing 聽的；聽覺的：audile power 聽的功能<br><br><br>auditory [audit=to hear 聽； -ory a.=relating to 與… … 有關的→ ] a. relating to the sense of<br>hearing 聽覺的：auditory nerves 聽覺神經<br><br><br>audiology [audi=to hear 聽；-o-;-logy n.=branch of science 一門科學→] n. the science dealing<br>with the sense of hearing 聽覺學<br><br>▽audiologist [audiolog(y);-ist n.] n.聽覺學學者<br><br><br>audio [形容詞性的合詞成分：aud=to hear 聽；-io→「of hearing 與聽有關的」→] I a. pertaining<br>to sound or sound waves 聲音的；聲波的：audio frequency 音頻→Ⅱ n. broadcast or recorded<br>sound 播音；錄音：My television set has a good picture by weak audio.我的電視機圖像清晰，<br>但是收音不好。	
8. aug, auct, auth [L]=	to increase 增加<br>讀者可能想不到August（八月），auction（拍賣）和author（作者）居然是同根詞吧！它們<br>分別來自拉丁動詞aguere、它的過去分詞auctus 及其變體auth，其基本意思都是to increase<br>（增加）或to cause to grow（使產生，使增大）。<br><br><br>august [aug=to increase 使增大；-ust a.=the most 最→「to increase to the most 增到最大」→<br>「the greatest 最偉大的」→]Ⅰa. majestic 威嚴的：august palaces 威嚴的王宮→Ⅱ（大寫<br>August）n.１ 奧古斯特（即古羅馬Augustus 凱撒大帝，他自認為是最偉大的帝王）２ 八月<br>（奧古斯特大帝以自己的名字命名八月份）<br><br><br>augment [aug=to increase 增加；-ment v.→] v.１ make greater or enlarge 增加，擴大：to<br>augment the power 擴大權力２ become greater 增加，增大：The sound of traffic augments<br>during the rush hour.高峰時間交通噪音會增大。<br><br>▽augmentative [augment;-ative a.] a.有擴大（增加）作用的<br><br><br>auction [auct=to cause to grow 使增加；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「the act of causing the price to<br>grow 使價格上升的行為」→]Ⅰn. sale in which goods are sold to the person offering the most<br>money 拍賣：to sell the old furniture by auction 拍賣舊傢俱→Ⅱv. sell by auction 拍賣：When<br>the artist died, his family auctioned his paintings.藝術家去世後，家人把他的畫拍賣了。<br><br>▽auctioneer [auction v.-eer n.] n.拍賣商<br><br><br>author [auth（auct）=to cause to grow 使成長；-or n.=person 人→「person who causes anything<br>to grow 使事物產生者」→] n.１ person who begins or creates 發起人，創始者：the author of<br>the new plan 新計劃的倡議者２ writer 著作者，作家：His favorite author is Dickens.他最喜歡<br>的作家是狄更斯。<br><br>▽authorless [author;-less a.] a.作者不明的；隱名的<br><br><br>auctorial [auctor=author 作者；-i-;-al a.=of……的→] a. of or having to do with an author 作者的：<br>auctorial comments 作者說明<br><br><br>authority [author n. 創始者；-ity n.=the quality 表特性→「the quality of an author 創始者的特<br>性」→] n.１ the power or right to control or make decisions 權力，權威：Rulers have no<br>authority from God to do mischief.上帝並沒有給統治者製造禍害的權力。２ person(s) having<br>authority 當權者：higher authority 上級領導<br><br><br>authorize [author n.創始者（→power 權力）；-ize v.=to cause to have 使有→「to cause to have<br>power 使有權力」→] v. give power to 授權：The president authorized his ambassador to sign the<br>treaty.總統授權大使簽訂該條約。<br><br>▽authorization [authoriz(e);-ation n.] n.授權，委託	
9. bi, bio [GK]=	life 生命，生物<br>biology（生物學）中的bi 是個希臘詞根，它來自希臘名詞bios，意思為life（生命，生物）。<br>在構詞中，bi 常通過連接字母-o-與其他詞素結合，所以，也可以把bio 看作bi 的異體。<br><br><br>biology [bio=life 生命，生物；-logy n.=branch of science 一門科學→] n. the science of life in all<br>生物學：Zoology and botany are main divisions of biology.動物學和植物學是生物學的兩門主要<br>分科。<br><br>▽biologist [biolog(y);-ist n.] n.生物學者<br>biological [biolog(y);-ical a.] a.生物學的<br><br><br>biography [bio=life 生命；-graphy n.=writing 著作→「writing about one's life 關於一個人生平<br>的著作」→] n. written account about a person's life 傳記：a biography of Darwin 達爾文傳記<br><br>▽biographer [biograph (y);-er n.] n.傳記作者<br>biographical [biograph(y);-ical a.] a.傳記的；傳記體的<br>biographize [biograph (y);-ize v.] v.為……作傳記<br><br><br>biocide [bio=life 生物→living beings 蟲；-cide n.=that which kills 殺……物→] n. substance which<br>kills harmful living beings 殺蟲劑<br><br><br>antibiotic [anti-=against 抗；bi=life 生命，生物；-otic a.=having the quality 有……性能的→<br>「against the growing of a certain life 能抵制某種生物生長的」→] a. opposing the living of<br>disease carrying bacteri-a 抗病菌的；抗生的：antibiotic substance 抗生素<br><br><br>microbial [micro-=tiny 微小的；bi=life 生物；-al a.=of ……的→「of a tiny life 微小生物的」→]<br>a. of microscopic organisms 微生物的：the microbial enemy of man 人類的微生物敵人<br>bio 也可以作為術語前綴，與其他充當術語的單詞結合，構成新的術語。bio-的意思為「生<br>物」或「生物的」。<br><br><br>biochemistry [bio-=life 生物；chemistry 化學n.→] n. the branch of chem-istry relating to life or<br>living organisms 生物化學<br><br>▽biochemist [bio-;chem.;-ist n.] n.生物化學家<br><br><br>biophysics [bio-=life 生物；physics n.物理學→] n. the branch of physics relating to life or living<br>organisms 生物物理學<br><br>▽biophysicist [biophysic(s);-ist n.] n.生物物理學家	
10. cad, cas, cid [L]=	to fall, to befall 降，降臨<br>cad，cas，cid 是同源異形詞根，都源於拉丁動詞cadere，意思相當於to fall（降落）或to befall<br>（降臨）。其中，cad 是不定式詞干，cas 是動名詞詞干，而cid 是cadere 的異體cidere 的不<br>定式詞干。這族同根詞的數量較大。<br><br><br>decadent [de-=down 下；cad=to fall 降；-ent a.=-ing 表性質→「falling down 下降的」] a. falling<br>down morally;falling into ruin 墮落的；頹敗的：The Ching Empire had become decadent by that<br>time.當時清帝國已經腐敗了。<br><br>▽decadence [de-;cad;-ence n.] n.衰落；頹廢<br><br><br>case [cas=to befall 降臨；-e→「that which befalls 降臨之事」→] n. event;condition 事件；情<br>況：a typical case 典型事件<br><br><br>casual [cas=to befall 降臨；-u-;-al a.=having the quality 有……性質的→「having the quality of<br>befalling, or happening by chance 帶有偶發性質的」→] a.１ not planned 偶然的：a casual<br>meeting 巧遇２ infor-mal 非正式的：casual clothing 便服<br><br>▽casualty [casual;-ty n.] n.事故的傷亡者<br><br><br>occasion [oc-（ob-）=in the way of 在……面前；cas=to befall 降臨；-ion n.=the state or result<br>表狀態或結果→「that which befalls in one's way 降臨在面前的事」→] n.１ instance or case<br>情況２ favorable time, or opportunity 時機；機會：as occasion serves 一旦有適當的機會<br><br>▽occasional [occasion;-al a.] a.偶爾的<br><br><br>accident [ac-(ad-)=towards 朝向；cid=to befall 降臨；-ent n.=thing 事→「thing that befalls towards<br>a person 朝著某人降臨的事」→] n. １unexpected event 意外的事；偶然的事：I met her quite<br>by accident.我碰到她是很偶然的事。２ unfortunate happening 事故：traffic acci-dents 交通事<br>故<br><br>▽accidental [accident;-al a.] a.意外的；偶然的<br><br><br>incident [in-=on, upon 在……上；cid=to befall 發生；-ent n.=thing 事→「thing that befalls on a<br>particular person or happens at a particular time 發生在某人身上或某個時刻的事」→] n. event,<br>or occurence 事件；事變：the July 7th Incident 七七事變<br><br>▽incidental [incident;-al a.] a.偶然的；伴隨的<br>incidence [in-;cid;-ence n.] n.發生；發生率<br><br><br>coincide [co-（com-）=together 共同；in-=upon 在……之上；cid=to befall 降臨→「to befall upon<br>together 共同降臨在……之上」] v. １happen at the same time or same place（時間、空間）<br>恰好相合：My birthday coincides with yours. 我恰好和你同一天生日。２ agree;correspond<br>一致；符合：to coincide in opinion 意見相符<br><br>▽coincident [coincid(e);-ent a.] a.同時發生的；一致的<br><br><br>deciduous [de-=off 脫離；cid=to fall 降；-u-;-ous a.=having the quality 有……性質的→] a. having<br>the quality of falling off at a certain time 定期脫落的：deciduous trees 落葉林<br><br><br>occident [oc-（ob-）=down 下；cid=to fall 降落；-ent n.=thing connected with 表相關事物→<br>「the direction towards which the heavenly bodies were supposed to fall down 前人認為的天體<br>降落的方向」→] n.１ the west 西方２ the western hemisphere 西半球：the Occident 亞洲以<br>西的全部國家；歐洲；歐美<br><br>▽occidental [occident;-al a.] a.西方的<br><br><br>decay [de-=down 下；cay（cad 的變形）=to fall 降→] v. fall down from a state of health and<br>excellence;rot 衰退；腐朽：The old man's teeth are all decayed.這老人的牙齒全壞了。	
11. cap, capt, cept, ceive [L]=	to take 取<br>這是一組形態變化比較複雜，孳生能力又很強的詞根。cap 來自拉丁動詞capere，意為to take<br>（取），capt，cept 來自它的過去分詞。由於該族同根詞多由法語引入英語，因此又多了一<br>個帶法語痕跡的變體ceive。先介紹幾個由cap，capt 構成的派生詞。<br><br><br>capable [cap=to take 取；-able a.=able 能……的→「able to take 能取到的」→] a. able;talented<br>有能力的；有才能的：capable teachers 能幹的教師<br><br>▽capability [capab(le);-ility n.] n.能力，才能，技能<br><br><br>capacious [cap=to take or hold 取，抓；-acious (-ac +-ious) a.=having the nature 有……性能的<br>→「having the nature of holding 能容納的」→] a. able to hold much 容量大的：capacious stage<br>寬敞的戲台<br><br>▽capacity [cap;-ac;-ity n.] n.容量，容積；可容性，可能性<br><br><br>capture [capt=to take 取；-ure n.=the result 表結果→「the result of being taken or catched 被奪<br>取的結果」→]Ⅰn. person or thing seized 俘虜，捕獲物：The lion became their capture.那隻獅<br>子成為他們的獵物。→Ⅱv. take as a prize by force 捕獲：to capture butterflies with a net 用網<br>捕捉蝴蝶<br><br>▽capturer [captur(e);-er n.] n.捕獲者<br>capturable [captur(e);-able a.] a.可捕獲的<br><br><br>captive [capt=to take 取；-ive a.=being...被……的→「being taken 被抓的」→]Ⅰa. taken or made<br>a prisoner 被俘虜的：captive birds 籠中之鳥→Ⅱ n. a person or animal captured 俘虜；獵獲物：<br>The captives were sold as slaves.俘虜被販賣為奴。<br><br>▽captivity [captiv(e) a.;-ity n.] n.囚虜；監禁（期）；羈絆<br>captivate [captiv(e) a.;-ate v.] v. [古]捕獲；迷惑，蠱惑<br><br><br>ceive 用來構成動詞，其對應的名詞和形容詞多由cept 構成。<br><br>receive [re-=back 回；ceive=to take 取→「to take back 取回」→] v.１ get or accept 收到，收<br>受：It is more blessed to give than to receive.施惠比收受更好。２ allow to enter 容納，接待：<br>to receive the guests warmly 熱情接待客人<br><br>▽receiver [receiv(e);-er n.] n.收受者；聽筒；接收機<br>reception [re-;cept;-ion n.] n.接待；歡迎；接受，容納<br>receptive [re-;cept;-ive a.] a.能容納的；可接受的<br><br><br>deceive [de-=away 離；ceive=to take 取→「to take somebody away from what is true 帶某人離<br>開真相」→] v. cause to believe what is false 欺騙，蒙蔽：Deceive boys with toys, but men with<br>oaths.用玩具騙小孩，用誓言騙大人。<br><br>▽deceiver [deceiv(e);-er n.] n.欺騙者，騙子<br>deception [de-;cept;-ion n.] n.欺騙，蒙蔽；騙人的東西<br>deceptive [de-;cept;-ive a.] a.騙人的；容易使人上當的<br><br><br>conceive [con-=in 入；ceive=to take 取→「to take in 取進，吸收」→] v.１ become pregnant<br>懷（胎）：to conceive a child 懷孕２ form in the mind 構想，設想：I can't conceive why you said<br>so.我想不出你為什麼這樣說。<br><br>▽conceivable [conceiv(e);-able a.] a.可想到的，可想像的<br>conception [con-;cept;-ion n.] n.概念；構想，設想；懷孕<br>conceptive [con-;cept;-ive a.] a.有構想力的；構想的<br>conceptual [con-;cept;-ual a.] a.概念的；概念藝術的<br><br><br>perceive [per-=thoroughly 12. ced, ceed, cess [L]=	to go 走<br>ced，ceed，cess 是同源異形根，來自拉丁動詞cedere，意為to go（走）。其中，ced 是不定<br>式詞干；ceed 是ced 在英語中的音變形式，它在英語中只有proceed，succeed 和exceed 三<br>個原生派生詞；cess 是動名詞詞干，用來組成與某些動詞相應的名詞或形容詞。<br><br><br>antecedent [ante-=before 在……前；ced=to go 走；-ent a.=-ing……的→] a. going before 先行<br>的，居先的：The Ming Dynasty was antecedent to the Ching the times 時代的先行者<br>proceed [pro-=forward 向前；ceed=to go 行走→] v.１ go forward 前進，進行：The talk proceeded<br>in a friendly atmosphere.會談在友好的氣氛中進行。２ go forward after a stop, or continue 繼<br>續：Let's proceed to the next item on the agenda.讓我們進入下一項議程。<br><br>▽proceeding [proceed;-ing n.] n.程序；[複數] 會議記錄<br><br><br>procedure [pro-=forward 向前；ced=to go 行走；-ure n.=the manner 表方式→「the manner of<br>going forward forward<br>movement 過程，進程：the process of history 歷史的進程<br><br>▽procession [pro-;cess;-ion n.] n.隊伍行進；行列<br><br><br>succeed [suc-(sub-)=from under 自下而上；ceed=to go 行走→「to go from under（to a higher<br>position）上升到較高位置」→] v.１ take the place previously occupied 繼承，接替：A new<br>cabinet succeeded the old one.新內閣接任了。２reach one's aim 成功，成就：He succeeded in<br>everything.他事事如意。<br><br>▽succession [succeed１的對應名詞] n.繼承；連續<br>successive [succeed１的對應形容詞] a.相繼的；連續的<br>success [succeed２的對應名詞] n.成就；成功<br><br><br>accede [ac-(ad-)=to 到；ced=to go 走；-e→「to go to an office 走馬上任」→] v. enter upon an<br>office 就職：The prince acceded to the throne and became the monarch.王子即位成了國君。<br><br>▽accession [ac-(ad-);cess;-ion n.] n.就職<br><br><br>access [ac-(ad-)=to 到；cess=to go 走→「going to some place 走到某處」→] n. approach 接近；<br>進入：a place difficult of access 難以進入的地方<br><br>▽accessible [ac-(ad-);cess;-ible a.] a.可進去的；易接近的<br><br><br>exceed [ex-=out, beyond 外；ceed=to go 行走→「to go beyond 走出界」→] v. 13. centr [GK→L]=	the middle point 中心<br>常用詞centre，central，centric 和concentrate 的共同成分是centr。它是隨著法語進入英語<br>的拉丁化的希臘詞。遠祖是希臘名詞kentron，意為sharp point（尖端）。kentron 的拉丁化<br>形式是cenrtum，因為「尖端點」的概念與「中心點」緊密相連，所以又添上the middle point<br>（中心）的含義。不妨說centr 相當於the middle point，或者等於它在英語中的替身——center<br>（中心）。<br><br><br>centre [centr=the middle point 中心點；-e→] n. the middle point of any-thing 中心點，中心/the<br>center of a circle 圓心<br><br><br>central [centr=the middle point 中心點；-al a.=of……的→] a.１ of the middle point;belonging<br>to the center 中心的；中央的/the central com-mittee 中央委員會２ principal;dominate 主要的；<br>支配的/the central idea of an article 文章的主題思想<br><br>▽centralism [central;-ism n.] n.集中制；中央集權制<br>centrality [central;-ity n.] n.中心性；中心地位<br>centralize [central;-ize v.] v.形成中心；使集中<br><br><br>decentralize [de-=to undo 表示相反行為；centralize v.使集中→「to undo that of centralizing 取<br>消集中」→] v. １ do away with centralization of 廢棄中央集權２ distribute（powers）among<br>local governments 分權於地方政府/decentralized management 分散經營<br><br>▽decentralization [decentraliz(e);-ation n.] n.分散；地方分權<br><br><br>centric [centr=the middle point 中心點；-ic a.=having 有……的→] a. having a center; belonging<br>to the center 有中心的；中心的/ centric position 中心位置<br><br>▽centricity [centric;-ity n.] n.中心性<br><br><br>concentrate [con- (com)=together 共；centr=center 中心；-ate v.=to cause to be 使→to cause to<br>be together in the center 使共處於中心→ ] v. bring together to one point 集中/You should<br>concentrate yourself on your studies.你要專心學習。<br><br>▽concentration [concentrat(e);-ion n.] n.集中；專心<br>concentrator [concentrat(e);-or n.] n.集中者；專業研究者<br><br><br>concentric [con-=together 共同；centr=cenrte 中心；-ic a.=having 有……的→] a. having a<br>common center 同心的/concentric circles 同心圓<br><br>▽concentricity [concentric;-ity n.] n.同心；同心度<br><br><br>eccentric [ec-=from 離；centr=center 中心；-ic a.=being……的→「being away from the center<br>離開中心的」→] I a. not concentric;not having the axis placed centrally 離心的；偏心的/eccentric<br>circles 偏心圓→II n. odd person 行為古怪的人<br><br>▽eccentricity [eccentric a.;-ity n.] n.偏心率；離心率<br><br><br>centrifugal [centr=center 中心；-i-;fug=to flee 逃；-al a.=of……的→「of fleeing the center 逃離<br>中心的」→] a. moving from the center 離心的/centrifugal machine 離心機<br><br>▽centrifugalize [centrifugal;-ize v.] v.使受離心機的作用<br><br><br>centripetal [centr=center 中心；-i-;pet=to seek after 趨向；-al a.=of……的→「of seeking after the<br>center 趨向中心的」→] a. moving towards the center 向心的/centripetal force 向心力	
14. cern, cret [L]=	to separate 分離<br>cern 和cret 是一對同源異形根，來自拉丁動詞cernere，意思相當於to separate（分離，區<br>分）。cern 是不定式詞干，常用來構成動詞，cret 是動名詞詞干，多出現於名詞或形容詞。<br><br><br>concern [con-(com-)=thoroughly 徹底地；cern=to for his owner 秘書：private secretary<br>私人秘書<br><br>▽secretariat [secretar(y);-iat n.] n.秘書處；書記處<br>secretarial [secretar(y);-ial a.] a.秘書的；有關秘書事務的<br><br><br>discreet [dis-=apart 離開；creet（cret [discreet;-ness n.] n.謹慎<br>discretion1 [dis-;cret;-ion n.] n.謹慎；判斷<br><br><br>discrete [dis-=apart 開；cret=separated 分離的；-e→] a. separated apart;totally different 分離的；<br>相異的：Modesty and coyness are 16. claim, clam [L]=	to call out 喊<br>claim 和clam 都源於拉丁動詞clamare，意為to call out 或to shout（喊叫）。claim 是不定式<br>詞干在英語中的重讀形式，用來構成動詞；clam 是動名詞詞干，只出現於相應的名詞和形<br>容詞中。<br><br><br>claim [claim=to call out 呼喊→「to speak loudly for one's own interest 為自己的利益而呼喊」<br>→] v. demand as one's due or property 要求；索取：We have claimed compensation for the losses<br>from the foreign company.我們已向外國公司提出索賠要求。<br><br>▽claimer [claim;-er n.] n.根據權利提出要求者<br>claimable [claim;-able a.] a.可要求的；可認領的<br><br><br>disclaim [dis-=to undo 做相反之事；claim v. 要求，索取→「to undo that of claiming 做與要求<br>或索取相反的事」→] v. deny;disavow 否認；抵賴：He disclaimed his responsibility for the<br>accident.他否認自己對事故負有責任。<br><br>▽disclaimer [disclaim;-er n.] n.否認者<br><br><br>declaim [de-=completely 完全地；claim=to call out 叫喊→「to call out or speak loudly 喊話；大<br>聲說話」→] v. give a formal speech 演講：The candidates declaimed against the government. 競<br>選人發表演說責難政府。<br><br>▽declaimer [declaim;-er n.] n.演講者；朗誦者<br><br><br>declamation [declaim 的對應名詞：declam=to declaim 演講；-ation n.=the act 表行為→] n.１<br>the act or art of declaiming 演講； 雄辯術２ formal speech 正式演說： to deliver a long<br>declamation 發表長篇演說<br><br><br>declamatory [declaim 的對應形容詞：declam=to declaim 演說；-atory a.=characterized by 有……<br>特點的→ ] a. １ characterized by declaiming 演說的２ bombastic 誇誇其談的： long and<br>declamatory speech 誇誇其談的長篇大論<br><br><br>exclaim [ex-=out 出；claim=to call or shout 喊→「to call or shout out 喊出來」→] v. cry out<br>suddenly from pain, anger, surprise, etc.驚叫；驚歎：「Help! 17. clud, clus [L]=	to shut or close 關閉<br>clud 和clus 是一對同源異形根，詞源是拉丁動詞claudere，意思相當於to shut（關閉）。clud<br>來自不定式詞干claud，常見於英語動詞；clus 來自動名詞詞干claus，多見於相應的名詞和<br>形容詞。<br><br><br>conclude 18. cord [L]=	heart 心<br>常用詞accord，concord，discord 和record 等，都以詞根cord 為基礎。cord 源於拉丁名詞<br>cor 的屬格（即所有格）形式cordis 的詞幹部分，意義等於英語基本詞heart（心）。<br><br><br>accord [ac-(ad-)=towards 向；cord=heart 心→「a heart towards another heart 心心相向」→] I<br>n. agreement, or harmony 一致；和諧：Our opinions are in accord.我們的意見一致。→Ⅱv. be<br>of one heart, or agree 與……一致：His opinions accord with mine.他與我觀點一致。<br><br>▽accordance [accord;-ance n.] n.一致<br>accordant [accord;-ant a.] a.一致的<br>according (to) [accord;-ing a.] a.與……一致的；根據……<br><br><br>concord [con-(com-)=together 共同；cord=heart 心→「a heart together with another 心心與共」<br>→] n. the state of having the same heart, or agreement, or harmony 同心；一致；和諧：The old<br>couple live in concord.這對老夫妻相親相愛。<br><br>▽concordance [corcord;-ance n.] n.和諧；一致<br>concordant [concord;-ant a.] a.和諧的；一致的<br><br><br>discord [dis-=apart 離； cord=heart 心→ 「 a heart apart from another 心心相離」 → ] I n.<br>disagreement, or opposition of views 不一致；不和：The couple split up after years of discord.<br>吵了幾年，這對夫妻分手了。→Ⅱv. disagree, or quarrel 不和；爭吵：They often discord with<br>each other.他們經常鬧矛盾。<br><br>▽discordance [discord;-ance n.] n.不和；爭吵<br>discordant [discord;-ant a.] a.不和的；爭吵的<br><br><br>record [re-=back 回；cord=heart 心→「back in the heart 回到心裡」→「to put in the heart again,<br>as by writing it down 記下來以便回憶」→] I v. write down in permanent form 記錄，記載：A<br>great event like this should be recorded.這樣的大事應該記錄下來。→Ⅱn. recorded permanent<br>account 記錄，記載：original records 原始記錄材料<br><br>▽recordable [record;-able a.] a.可記錄的<br>recorder [record;-er n.] n.錄音機；記錄員<br>recordist [record;-ist n.] n.錄音員<br><br><br>cordial [cord=heart 心；-i-; 19. cresc, cret, cre [L]=	to grow 生長<br>常用詞crescent，increase，create 和concrete，表面看來似乎關係不大，其實是同根生的。<br>它們的詞幹部分cresc，cret 和cre 是一組同源異形根，都來自拉丁動詞crescere，意為to grow<br>（生長）。其中，cresc 是不定式詞干；cret 是動名詞詞干；cre 是cret 在添加後綴時的變形。<br><br><br>crescent [cresc=to grow 生長，變化；-ent n.=the state 表行為狀態→「the growing state（of the<br>moon）（月亮）變化的狀態」→] n.１ the visible part of the quarter moon which is growing larger<br>or smaller 月牙２ any object like a crescent 月牙形的東西/The national emblem of Turkey is a<br>crescent.土耳其的國徽是個月牙。<br><br><br>increase [in-=into 成；creas（cresc 的重讀式）=to grow 生長；-e→] I v. grow into a larger<br>amount;become greater or larger 增長；增加；增大：The production increases with years. 生<br>產逐年增長。→Ⅱn. growth 增長：the rate of increase 增長率<br><br><br>create [cre=to grow 生長；-ate v.=to make 使……→「to make to grow into shape 使生長成形」<br>→] v. make something exist 創造：to create more jobs 創造更多的就業機會<br><br>▽creation [creat(e);-ion n.] n.創造；創作；（大寫）創世<br>creator [creat(e);-or n.] n. 創造者；創始者；（大寫）造物主creature [creat(e);-ure n.] n.創造<br>物；生物；動物<br>creative [creat(e);-ive a.] a.有創造力的；創造性的；創作的<br><br><br>concrete [con-=together 一起；cret=to grow 生長；-e→「to grow or stick together 長在一起或<br>結成一塊」→] I v. solidify or harden 凝固；固結：The sands concreted into a mass. 沙土結成<br>塊。→Ⅱa. relating to a solidified thing; particular; real 固定有形的；具體的；實際的：a concrete<br>problem 具體問題III n. any mass of solidified particles, especially used in building 混凝土：<br>reinforced concrete 鋼筋混凝土<br><br>▽concretion [concret(e) v.;-ion n.] n.凝固；凝固物<br>concretive [concret(e) v.;-ive a.] a.凝結性的<br><br><br>decrease [de-=downward 向下；creas=to grow 生成，變化；-e→「to grow downward 向下變<br>化」→] I v. become less, or make less 減少；使變少：Water comsumption decreased.耗水量降<br>低了。→Ⅱn. reduction 減少；減少量：A big decrease in sales caused the supermarket to close.<br>銷售量銳減使得超市關了門。<br><br><br>increment [in-=into 成；cre=to grow 生長；-ment n.=the result 表行為結果→「the result of<br>growing into a larger amount 數量增長的結果」→] n. the amount of increase 增加量：monthly<br>increments 月增加額<br><br>▽incremental [increment;-al a.] a.增加的；增值的<br><br><br>increscent [in-=into 成；cresc=to grow 生長；-ent a.=-ing 有……特徵的→「growing into（the full<br>moon）長成（滿月）的」→] a. waxing of the moon（月亮）漸盈的：an increscent moon 盈<br>月<br><br><br>accretion [ac（- ad-）=to 向；cret=to grow 生長；-ion n.=the act or state 表動作或狀態→「growing<br>to 向……生長」→] n.１ continued growth 生長；增大：the accretion of cancer 腫瘤增大２<br>growing of parts into each other 合生，連生：accretion of two kinds of plants 兩種植物的合生<br>現象<br><br><br>excrescence [ex-=out 出；cresc=to grow 生長；-ence n.=the result 表行為結果→「growing or<br>growth which is out of the normal state 超出正常狀態的生長物」→] n. １ abnormal outgrowth<br>贅生物，瘤：an excresence on the neck 脖子上的瘤２ superfluous part 累贅，多餘物：This tree<br>is an excrescence in the painting.這棵樹在畫中是多餘的。<br><br>▽excrescent [ex-;cresc;-ent a.] a.贅生的；多餘的	
20. cub, cumb [L]=	to lie down 躺<br>常用詞incumbent，succumb，concubine 和incubate 是一組同根詞。詞根cub 來自拉丁動詞<br>cubare，詞根cumb 來自拉丁動詞cumbere；而cumbere 和cubare 實際上是同一個詞的異體，<br>意思都相當於英語的to lie down（躺，臥）。<br><br><br>incumbent [in-=upon 在……之上；cumb=to lie down 躺；-ent a.=-ing……的→「lying upon<br>somebody 躺在或賦予某人身上的」→] I a. lying or resting on（somebody）as an obligation 作<br>為責任的：It is incumbent on you to warn them.你有責任告誡他們。→Ⅱn. person on whom an<br>obligation lies;one who holds public office 負有責任者；任公職者：the struggle between the<br>incumbents and the candidates 現任者與候選人之間的鬥爭<br><br>▽incumbency [in-;cumb;-ency n.] n.責任；任職；職權<br><br><br>succumb [suc（- sub-）=under 在……之下；cumb=to lie down 躺倒→「to lie down under pressure,<br>illness etc.在壓力、疾病等之下躺倒」→] v.１ give way;yield 讓步，屈服：We will not succumb<br>to difficulties.我們決不向困難低頭。２ die 死：He succumbed to cancer.他死於癌症。<br><br><br>concubine [con-=together 共同；cub=to lie down 臥；-ine n.=female 女人→「woman who lies<br>down together with a man 與某男人同臥共宿的女人」→] n. woman who inhabits with a man<br>without being married 姘婦，情婦<br><br>▽concubinage [concubin(e);-age n.] n.情婦身份；非法同居<br><br><br>incubate [in-=on 在……上；cub=to lie 臥；-ate v.=to cause 使……→「to cause (a hen, etc.) to lie<br>on eggs 使（母雞等）臥在卵上」→] v.１sit on eggs in order to hatch them 孵卵，孵化：Even<br>a good hen can't incubate a wooden egg.母雞再好也孵不了木頭蛋。２ give form to;develop<br>把……醞釀成熟；使發展：to incubate a plan 醞釀一個計劃<br><br>▽incubation [incubat(e);-ion n.] n.孵化；醞釀<br>incubator [incubat(e);-or n.] n.孵化器<br>incubative [incubat(e);-ive a.] a.孵卵的；潛伏期的<br><br><br>incubus [in-=upon 在……之上；cub=to lie down 臥；-us n.=thing 物→「thing inclined to lie down<br>upon a person 喜歡臥在人的身上的東西」→] n. evil spirit supposed to lie down upon sleeping<br>persons;nightmare 壓在睡眠者身上的惡魔；夢魔：The debt is like an incubus on me.這筆債務<br>使我夢寐不安。<br><br><br>cubicle [cub=to lie 躺；-icle n.=small thing 小東西→「small room for lying down 供躺下歇息的<br>小房間」→] n.１ small bedroom 小臥室２ any small room 小室<br><br>▽cubicular [cub;-icular a.] a.寢室的<br><br><br>recumbent [re-=backward 向後；cumb=to lie 躺；-ent a.=-ing……的→] a. lying backward;reclining<br>躺著的；斜臥的：recumbent statue 雕塑的臥像<br><br>▽recumbency [recumben(t);-cy n.] n.斜臥；依靠<br><br><br>procumbent [pro-=forward 向前；cumb=to lie 躺；-ent a.=-ing……的→「lying forward 向前臥<br>著的」→] a. leaning forward;prostrate;prone 前俯的；平臥的；爬在地下的：The man fell<br>procumbent on the ground.那個人摔了個嘴啃泥。	
21. cult [L]=	to till 耕作<br>在culture，cultivate，agriculture 等常用詞中，包含著一個很重要的詞根cult，它是拉丁動詞<br>colere 的動名詞詞干（這個動詞的不定式詞干col 在英語中的派生詞很少，例詞見練習第4<br>題）。colere 的意思包含了古代社會的三種基本的社會活動：居住、耕作、敬神。所以，可<br>以用三個英語動詞來表示它的意思：inhabit，till 和worship。相應地，詞根cult 也包含了這<br>三種意思，但是主要意思是to till（耕作，栽培）。<br><br><br>cult [cult=to worship 崇拜→] n. system of formal worship or religious belief 禮拜；迷信：the cult<br>of personality 個人崇拜<br><br>▽cultism [cult;-ism n.] n.崇拜；迷信<br>cultist [cult;-ist n.] n.熱衷於搞迷信崇拜的人<br><br><br>cultivate [cult=to till 耕作；-iv(e)；-ate v.=to make capable of 使能……→「to make capable of<br>being tilled 使能用來耕種」→] v. １ make arable land;produce by tillage 耕作；栽培：to<br>cultivate the soil 耕地２ improve;develop 改進；培養：to cultivate the habit of analysis 養成分<br>析的習慣<br><br>▽cultivation [cultivat(e);-ion n.] n.耕作；培養；教養<br>cultivatable [cultivat(e);-able a.] a.可耕作的；可培養的<br><br><br>culture [cult=to till 耕作，栽培；-ure n.=the act or result 表示行為或結果→「tilling or the result<br>of tilling 耕作或栽培的結果」→] n.１ tillage 耕作２ cultivation 培養：moral culture 德育３<br>improvement by physical or mental training 教養：a man of considerable culture 文化修養高的<br>人４ special form or stage of civilization 文化；文明：the ancient culture 古代文化<br><br>▽cultural [cultur(e);-al a.] a.文化的；教養的<br><br><br>-culture 常作為合詞成分與其他詞根構詞，表示cultivation（栽培；培養）的意思。<br><br><br>agriculture [agri=field 田地；-culture=cultivation 栽培→「cultivation about fields 田地上的栽<br>培術」→] n. the science or practice of cultivating the soil and rearing animals 農學；農藝；農業<br><br>▽agricultural [agricultur(e);-al a.] a.農業的；農藝的；農學的<br>agriculturist [agricultur(e);-ist n.] n.農學家<br><br><br>apiculture [api(apis)=bee 蜂；-culture=cultivation 培養→] n. cultivation of bee;bee-keeping 養蜂<br>業；養蜂<br><br>▽apicultural [apicultur(e);-al a.] a.養蜂的<br>apiculturist [apicultur(e);-ist n.] n.養蜂專家<br><br><br>aquaculture [aqua=water 水；-culture=cultivation 培養→] n. cultivation of plans or breeding of<br>animals in water 水產養殖<br><br>▽aquacultural [aquacultur(e);-al a.] a.水產養殖的<br>aquaculturist [aquacultur(e);-ist n.] n.水產養殖專家<br><br><br>floriculture [flori (floris)=flower 花；-culture=cultivation 栽培→] n. cultivation of flowers 養花；<br>花卉栽培術<br><br>▽floricultural [floricultur(e);-al a.] a.養花的；花卉栽培的<br>floriculturist [floricultur(e);-ist n.] n.花匠；花卉栽培專家<br><br><br>pisciculture [pisci (piscis)=fish 魚； -culture=cultivation 培養→ ] n. cultiva-tion of fish;artificial<br>rearing of fish 魚類養殖<br><br>▽piscicultural [piscicultur(e);-al a.] a.養魚的；養魚術的<br>pisciculturist [piscicultur(e);-ist n.] n.養魚專家	
22. cur(r), curs, cours [L]=	to run 跑<br>cur(r)，curs，cours 都來源於拉丁動詞currere，意思相當於英語的to run（跑）。其中，cur(r)<br>來自不定式詞干curr；curs 是動名詞詞干；cours 是curs 的重讀形式。在構詞中，cur(r) 用<br>來構成動詞；curs 和cours 一般只出現於名詞和形容詞中。先介紹幾個常見的cur(r) 的派生<br>詞。<br><br><br>occur [oc-(ob-)=towards 向；cur=to run 跑→「to run towards 向……跑來」→] v.１ come about<br>出現：These animals occur in Africa only.這些動物只出現在非洲。２ happen 發生：Don't let<br>such accidents occur again.別讓這類事情再發生了。<br><br>▽occurrence [occur(r);-ence n.] n.出現；發生<br>occurrent [occur(r);-ent a.] a.目前正發生的；偶然發生的<br><br><br>current [curr=to run 跑；-ent a.=-ing……的→「running 跑動的，流動的」→] I a. running along<br>with the times 流行的：the current mode 流行式樣；→Ⅱn. the running of water, electricity, etc.<br>水流；電流等：the main current 主流<br><br><br>recur [re-=back, again 回，復；cur=to run 跑→「to run back again 又跑回來」→] v. come upon<br>or happen again 重來；復發：His illness recurred.他的病復發了。<br><br>▽recurrence [recur(r);-ence n.] n.重現；復發<br>recurrent [recur(r);-ent a.] a.再發生的；經常發生的<br><br><br>concur [con-=together 一起；cur=to run 跑→「to run together 一起跑來」→] v.１happen at the<br>same time 同時發生：Several mistakes concurred to bring about this accident.幾樁失誤同時發<br>生，造成了這場事故。２ agree or approve 同意；贊成：The whole class concurred with him.<br>全班都贊同他的意見。<br><br>▽concurrence [concur(r);-ence n.] n.同時發生；同意；贊同<br><br><br>以下介紹的是幾個含curs 的常用派生詞。<br><br><br>cursory [curs=to run 跑；-ory a.=like 像……的→「like running or going hastily 像奔跑或疾走的」<br>→] a. hasty;hurried 倉猝的；草率的：He is a cursory reader.他看書一目十行，不求甚解。<br><br>▽cursoriness [cursor(y);-ness n.] n.倉猝；草率<br><br><br>excursion [ex-=out of 外；curs=to run 跑；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「running out of home 離家<br>跑到外頭去」→] n. pleasure outing or trip 遠足，短途旅行：excursion train 旅遊列車<br><br>▽excursionist [excursion;-ist n.] n.遠足者，短途旅行者<br><br><br>precursor [pre-=before 前；curs=to run 跑；-or n.=person 人→「person running before others<br>跑在他人前面的人」→] n. forrunner;predecessor 先行者；前輩：Kepler was the precursor of<br>Newton.開普勒是牛頓的前輩人物。<br><br>▽precursory [precursor;-y a.] a.先行的；前輩的<br>最後，再介紹幾個cours 的常見派生詞。<br><br><br>course [cours=to run 跑；-e→「running forward 向前的跑動」→] I n.１onward movement 行進；<br>進程：the course of events 事態的發展過程２ path in which anything runs or moves 道路，路<br>線：the course of a river 河道→Ⅱv. run; run after 跑；追：Blood courses through the veins.<br>血液在血管中循環流動。<br><br><br>discourse [dis-=away, out 離，出；cours=to run 跑；-e→「running out or outpouring（of words）<br>（話語的）滔滔而出」→] n. speech; talk or conversation 演說；會談：a discourse on ancient<br>Rome civilization 有關古羅馬文化的演講<br><br>        <br>recourse [re-=back 回；cours=to run 跑；-e→「running back or return 往回跑，回歸」→] n. the<br>freedom to a return, or the right to a payment 要求歸返權；追索權：I maintain my recourse to<br>you.我保留對你的追索權。	
23. cur [L]=	care 關心<br>在常用詞cure，curious，accurate，secure 中含有詞根cur，它來自拉丁名詞cura，意思相當<br>於care（關心，注意）。這個詞根與剛剛介紹的意為to run（跑）的詞根cur(r)形態相同。但<br>是，在實際構詞中，兩者除了含義不同，發音與形狀也不一樣。舉例來說，詞根cur(r)在recur，<br>current，curriculum 等派生詞中，或者出現在重讀尾音節，發[k?:]的音，或以curr 的形式添<br>加後綴，發[kɑ:]或[k?]的音。現在要介紹的這個cur，一定要添加後綴構詞，發音總是[kj??]。<br><br><br>cure [cur=care 關心；-e→「care for the sick 對病人的關心」→] I n. means of healing;remedy<br>治療；治法：Scientists are working on a cure for cancer. 科學家正在研究治療癌症的方法。→<br>Ⅱv. relieve the sickness;make well 治療；治癒：The doctor cured him of bad cold.醫生治好了他<br>的重感冒。<br><br>▽cureless [cure n.;-less a.] a.無法治療的<br>curable [cur(e) v.-able a.] a.可治療的<br>curative [cur(e) v.;-ative a.] a.治療的<br><br><br>curious [cur=care 關心，注意；-i-; -ous a.=causing 引起……的→「causing one's care 惹人注<br>意的」 →] a.１ strange;surprising 奇怪的；新奇的：a curious idea 怪念頭２ eager to<br>learn;inquisitive 好奇的；愛打聽的：Don't be too curious about what you are not supposed to<br>know.不要你知道的事，就不要多打聽。<br><br>▽curiosity [curio(u)s;-ity n.] n.新奇；好奇<br>incurious [in-;curious a.] a.無好奇心的；沒興趣的<br><br><br>accurate [ac- (ad-)=to 對；cur=care 關心，注意；-ate a.=having 有……的→「having much care<br>to 對……極為注意的」→] a. exact;without error 精確的；準確的：The answer is accurate in<br>every detail.這個答案精確無誤。<br><br>▽accuracy [ac-;cur;-acy n.] n.精確；準確<br><br><br>secure [se-=apart 離開；cur=care 關心；-e→「apart from the state of care 離開掛念狀態的」<br>→] I a. untroubled by danger or apprehension 無憂無慮的；安心的：She felt secure to her own<br>future.她對未來感到放心。２ safe against attack 安全的：secure place 安全的地方→Ⅱv. cause<br>or make safe 使安全：We must secure our supply line.我們必須保障運輸線的安全。<br><br>▽security [secur(e) a.;-ity n.] n.安全；保護<br>securement [secure v.;-ment n.] n.把握；穩當性<br><br><br>procure [pro-=for 為；cur=care 關心；-e→「to give one's care for 為……而關心」→] v. obtain<br>by care or effort;acquire 獲取；取得：He can procure a ticket for you.他會替你弄到一張票。<br><br>▽procurable [procur(e);-able a.] a.可獲得的<br>procural [procur(e);-al n.] n.獲得；取得<br><br><br>curate [cur=care 關心；-ate n.=person 人→「person in charge of the care of others 負責關心他<br>人者」→] n. person who assists a parish priest with the care of souls 副牧師（協助牧師關心人<br>們靈魂的人）<br><br><br>curator [cur=care 關心，照料；-ator (-ate +-or) n.=person who acts 做……者→] n.１ manager<br>or keeper 管理者２ keeper or custodian of museum, library, etc.（博物館、圖書館等）館長<br><br>▽curatorship [curator;-ship n.] n.管理者或館長的職位或身份	
24. cycl [GK]=	circle 圓環<br>常用詞cycle，bicycle 和encyclopaedia 中，含有詞根cycl，它源於希臘名詞kuklos，意為circle<br>（圓環）。cycl 多見於科技術語，一般只與希臘語源的詞根或詞綴相結合。<br><br><br>cycle [cycl=circle 圓環； -e → 「 a circle of time running 時間轉了一圈」 → ] n. recurrent<br>period;period of a thing completion 循環；週期：the cycle of the seasons 季節的循環<br><br>▽cyclic [cycl(e);-ic a.] a.週期的；循環的<br><br><br>bicycle [bi-=two 二；cycl=circle 圓環；-e→「two circles 兩個圓輪」→] I n. two-wheeled vehicle<br>兩輪腳踏車，自行車→Ⅱv. ride on a bicycle 騎自行車：to bicycle to school 騎自行車上學<br><br>▽bicyclist [bicycl (e);-ist n.] n.騎自行車的人<br><br><br>unicycle [un=one 一；-i-; cycl=circle 圓環；-e→「one-circled vehicle 一個輪的車」→] n.<br>one-wheeled vehicle used by acrobats（雜技演員用的）獨輪車<br><br><br>autocycle [auto-=automatic 自動；cycle=bicycle 腳踏車→] n. automatic bicycle, or bicycle with<br>auxiliary engine 機器腳踏車<br><br><br>encyclopaedia [en-=in 在……之內；cycl=circle 圓圈→all directions or fields 各方面；-o-;paedia<br>（與pacideia「教育」混淆）=education 教育→「book giving education or knowledge in all fields<br>提供各方面知識的書」→] n. work containing information on all branches of knowledge 百科全<br>書：Encyclopaedia Britannica《大不列顛百科全書》<br><br>▽encyclopaedic [encyclopaed(ia);-ic a.] a.百科全書（式）的<br>encyclopaedism [encyclopaed(ia);-ism n.] n.知識淵博<br>encyclopaedist [encyclopaed(i);-ist n.] n.百科全書編纂者<br><br><br>cyclone [cycl=cicle 圓；-one n.=thing, wind 物，風→「wind in a circle 圓環狀的風」→] n. wind<br>whirling around a low barometric center 旋風，氣旋（圍繞低氣壓中心旋轉的風）<br><br>▽cyclonic [cyclon(e);-ic a.] a.氣旋的<br><br><br>hemicycle [hemi=half 半；cycl=circle 圓；-e→「half circle 半個圓」→] n. semicircular figure 半<br>圓形<br><br><br>tetracycline [tetra=four 四；cycl=circle, ring 環；-ine n.=medicine 藥→] n. medicine of four-ring<br>compounds in which carbon atoms are linked with other atoms 四環素	
25. dem [GK]=	the people 人民<br>dem 源於希臘名詞demos，意思相當於the people（人民）。在添加後綴時，它常帶有連接<br>字母-o-，可以把demo 當作dem 的異體。<br><br><br>democracy [demo=the people 人民；-cracy n.=power 權力→rule or ruling body 統治，政體→<br>「 rule or ruling body by the people 人民的統治或政權」 → ] n. government by all the<br>people;society characterized by recog-nizing the equal rights of all the people 民主政權；民主社<br>會<br><br><br>democrat [demo=the people 人民；-crat n.=supportor of a government 某種政體的支持者→<br>「supportor of a government by all the people 人民政權的支持者」→] n. supportor or advocate<br>of democracy 民主主義者<br><br>▽democratism [democrat;-ism n.] n.民主主義<br>democratic [democrat;-ic a.] a.民主主義的；民主政體的<br>democratize [democrat;-ize v.] v.使民主化<br><br><br>demos [demos=the people 人民→] n. the people;the populace 人民，民眾；大眾<br><br>▽demotic [dem(os);-otic a.] a.民眾的；通俗的<br><br><br>demography [demo=the people 人民→the population 人口；-graphy n.=writing 著作→recording<br>and study 記錄與研究→「the recording and study of the population 對人口的記錄與研究」→]<br>n. the study of statistics of births, deaths, disease, etc.人口統計學<br><br>▽demographic [demograph(y);-ic a.] a.人口統計的<br>demographer [demograph(y);-er n.] n.人口統計學者<br><br><br>demagogue [dem=the people 人民；agogue=leader 引導者→「leader of the people 民眾領袖」<br>→] n. political agitator appealing to desires of the mob 蠱惑民眾的政治鼓動家<br><br>▽demagogic [demagog (ue);-ic a.] a.蠱惑的；煽動的<br>demagogism [demagog(ue);-ism n.] n.煽動；煽動主義<br>demagogy [demagog(ue);-y n.] n.煽動；煽動性宣傳<br><br><br>epidemic [epi-=upon 在……之上；dem=the people 民眾；-ic a.=being……的→「being upon the<br>people 發生在民眾身上的」→] I a. prevalent among the people in a certain place at a certain<br>time 流行性的：Polio was once an epidemic disease.小兒麻痺症曾是一種流行性傳染病。→Ⅱ<br>n. epidemic disease 流行病：to prevent epidemics 預防流行病<br><br><br>endemic [en-=in 在……之中；dem=the people 人民；-ic a.=being……的→「being in the people<br>of a certain area 存在於某個地區民眾中的」→] I a. prevalent in a particular area or nation 某地<br>（或某種人）特有的，地方性的：Cholera was an endemic disease in India.霍亂曾是印度特有<br>的地方病。→Ⅱn. disease of an endemic nature 地方性流行病；風土病：Some endemics have<br>become epidemic diseases in the world.有些地方性疾病已變成世界性的流行病。<br><br>▽endemicity [endemic a.;-ity n.] n.地方性；風土性<br><br><br>pandemic [pan-=whole 全，遍；dem=the people 人民；-ic a.=pertaining to……的→「pertaining<br>to the whole people 涉及全民的」→] a. prevalent over the whole of a country or the whole<br>world 流行全國（或全世界）的：a pandemic influenza 世界性流感	
26. dic, dict [L]=	to say 說<br>詞根dic 是拉丁動詞dicere 的不定式詞干；dict 是動名詞詞干，意思都相當於to say（說）。<br>在英語中，dic 的派生詞較少，dict 的派生能力卻很強。<br><br><br>indicate [in-=towards 對；dic=to say 說；-ate v.→「to say towards some-thing 針對某事說話」<br>→] v.１ point out;make known 指出；表明：The arrow indicates the direction of advance. 箭頭<br>指出前進方向。２ show;suggest 表示；暗示：High fever indicates severe illnesss.高燒表示病<br>重。<br><br>▽indication [indicat(e);-ion n.] n.指示；象徵<br>indicator [indicat(e);-or n.] n.指示者；指示器<br>indicative [indicat(e);-ive a.] a.指示的；象徵的；陳述的<br><br><br>dictate [dict=to say 說→saying 話；-ate v.=to do 做→「to do a saying 做一次講話」→] v.１say or<br>read for another to write 口述，使聽寫：He dictated a letter to the typist.他向打字員口授一封<br>信。２say commands 命令，支配：He will not be dictated to you.他不會聽命於你的。<br><br>▽dictation [dictat(e);-ion n.] n.口述；聽寫<br><br><br>dictator [dictate(e) v.命令；-or n.=person 人→「person who dictates laws, commands, etc.發佈<br>法令者」→] n. absolute ruler 獨裁者，專政者：fascist dictators 法西斯獨裁者<br><br>▽dictatorship [dictator;-ship n.] n.獨裁；專政<br>dictatorial [dictator;-ial a.] a.獨裁的；專政的<br><br><br>diction [dict=to say 說話；-ion n.=the manner 表行為方式→「the manner or art of saying 說話<br>的方式或藝術」→] n. choice of words and phrases in speaking 措詞，辭令：Bad diction marred<br>the effectiveness of his speech.措詞不當削弱了他講話的效果。<br><br><br>dictionary [diction n. 措詞；-ary n.=thing 物→「book for diction 措詞用書」→] n. book explaining<br>the use of words in a language 詞典，字典：an English-Chinese dictionary 英漢詞典<br><br><br>contradict [contra-=against 對抗；dict=to say 說→「to say against 以言相抗」→] v.１ speak<br>against 反駁：Students may contradict their teachers.學生可以反駁教師。２ deny 否認：Don't<br>contradict what you just testified.別否認你剛剛證實的東西。３ hold the opposite of 同……矛<br>盾：to contradict oneself 自相矛盾<br><br>▽contradiction [contradict;-ion n.] n.矛盾<br>contradictory [contradict;-ory a.] a.矛盾的；對立的<br><br><br>dictum [dict=to say 說；-um n.=thing done 所做的事→「something said 有人說過的話」→] n.<br>saying;authoritative saying 名言；格言：There is an old dictum that blood is thicker than water.<br>古話說，血濃於水。<br><br><br>edict [e-（ex-）=out from 自……而出；dict=to say 說→saying 話→「saying out from（the<br>authorities）（當權者）發出的話」→] n. order issued by authority 法令：the king's edict 國王<br>的命令<br><br>▽edictal [edict;-al a.] a.法令的<br><br><br>predict [pre-=beforehand 事先；dict=to say 說→「to say beforehand 事先說出」→] v. say what<br>will happen in the future;foretell 預言；預告：The weather forecasting center predicted rain for<br>tomorrow.氣象站預告明天有雨。<br><br>▽prediction [predict;-ion n.] n.預言；預告<br>predictive [predict;-ive a.] a.預兆的<br><br><br>benediction [bene=good 好；dict=to speak 說；-ion n.=-ing 表行為→「good speaking 說好話」<br>→] n. blessing 祝福：sincere benediction 誠心的祝福<br><br>▽benedictive [bene;dict;-ive a.] a.祝福的<br><br><br>malediction [male=ill, evil 壞，惡；dict=to speak 說；-ion n.=-ing 表行為→] n. evil-speaking;curse<br>誹謗；咒罵：irresponsible malediction 不負責任的誹謗<br><br>▽maledictive [male;dict;-ive a.] a.誹謗的；咒罵的	
27. doc, doct [L]=	to teach 教<br>在常用詞doctor，document 和doctrine 中，doc 和doct 是來自拉丁動詞docere 的一對同源<br>異形根，意思相當於to teach（教）。<br><br><br>doctor [doct=to teach 教；-or n.=person 人→「person who teaches, or a learned person 為師者，<br>有學問的人」→] n. １ one who holds the highest degree in a certain field 博士（獲得某學科<br>最高學位的人）：Doctor of Science 理科博士２one who is trained and licensed to practice<br>medicine 醫生：to go to see the doctor's 去就醫<br><br>▽doctorate [doctor;-ate n.] n.博士頭銜；博士學位<br>doctoral [doctor;-al a.] a.博士的<br><br><br>document [doc=to teach 教； -u-;-ment n.=thing 物→ 「 thing written for teaching or giving<br>information 用以示教的書面材料」→] n. paper or other material giving information, proof, or<br>evidence 文件；文獻：clas-sified documents 保密文件<br><br>▽documentary [document;-ary a./n.] a.公文的n.紀錄片documental<br><br><br>[document;-al a.] a.文件的；文獻的<br>doctrine [doctr（doct）=to teach 教；-ine n.=something done 表行為對像→「something taught<br>教導的內容」→] n. body of teachings orinstructions 教義；教條：Christian doctrine 基督教教<br>義<br><br>▽doctrinaire [doctrin(e) n.;-aire n.] n.教條主義者<br>doctrinal [doctrin(e);-al a.] a.教條的<br><br><br>docile [doc=to teach 教；-ile a.=capable of 可……的→「capable of being taught」→] a. easy to<br>teach, train or manage 易管教的；易馴服的；馴良的：a docile horse 一匹馴良的馬<br><br>▽docility [docil(e);-ity n.] n.馴服；溫順<br><br><br>indoctrinate [in-=into 進入；doctrin(e）n.=principle 教義；-ate v.=to cause 使……→「to cause<br>some principle or belief into one's mind 使某種教義或信仰進入頭腦」→] v. imbue;instruct in 灌<br>輸；教授：They often indoctrinate their children with patriotic thoughts.他們經常向孩子們灌輸<br>愛國思想。	
28. duc, duct [L]=	to lead 引導<br>常用詞conduct, educate, introduce, produce 等是同根詞。它們的詞根duc 或duct 都來自拉丁<br>動詞ducere，意思相當於to lead（引導）。這對詞根的孳生能力很強，其同根詞不下百個。<br><br><br>conduct [con-表加強詞義；duct=to lead 引導→] I n.１ leading;guidance 引導；指導：His conduct<br>of the business is successful.他對企業的指導是有成效的。２ leading oneself to a certain result,<br>or behaviour 行為；品行：His conduct in school is good.他在學校品行良好。→Ⅱv.１ lead or<br>guide 引導；帶領：The mayor conducted us through the town.市長帶我們參觀了城市。２direct<br>（oneself）為人，表現：The children conducted themselves well tonight.孩子們今晚表現得很<br>好。<br><br>▽conductor [conduct v.;-or n.] n.指導者；（樂隊）指揮；導體<br>conductible [conduct v.;-ible a.] a.能傳導的<br>conductive [conduct v.;-ive a.] a.傳導性的<br><br><br>educate [e-（ex-）=out of 從……出來；duc=to lead 引導；-ate v.→「to lead out of（the ignorant<br>state）從（無知狀態）引導出來」→] v. give training or schooling to 教養；教育：He has been<br>well educated.他受過良好的教育。<br><br>▽education [educat(e);-ion n.] n.教育；教育的過程<br>educator [educat(e);-or n.] n.教育工作者<br>educative [educat(e);-ive a.] a.有教育意義的<br><br><br>introduce [intro-=into 進；duc=to lead 引導；-e→「to lead into 引進」→] v.１ lead or bring into<br>use 引用；採用：to introduce new techniques 採用新技術２ lead into acquaintance with 介紹：<br>to introduce a new teacher to the class 把新老師介紹給班上學生<br><br>▽introducer [introduc(e);-er n.] n.引進者；介紹人<br>introduction [intro-;duct;-ion n.] n.引進；介紹；導言<br>introductory [intro-;duct;-ory a.] a.介紹的；導言的<br><br><br>produce [pro-=forward 向前；duc=to lead 引導；-e→「to lead or bring forward to some result<br>向前引導，引出結果來」→] v. bring forth;make or create 生產；製造；創造：This factory produces<br>lathes.這家工廠生產車床。<br><br>▽producer [produc(e);-er n.] n.生產者；製造者<br>product [pro-;duct] n.產品；成果<br>production [pro-;duct;-ion n.] n.生產；總產品；總成果<br>productive [pro-;duct;-ive a.] a.生產的；多產的<br><br><br>deduce [de-=down from 從……出來；duc=to lead 引導；-e→「to lead a conclusion down from<br>從……引出結論」→] v. draw as conclusion;infer 演繹；推理：I deduced that she was married by<br>the ring on her finger.根據她手上的戒指我推斷她已經結婚。<br><br>▽deduction [de-;duct;-ion n.] n.演繹；推論；扣除<br>deductive [de-;duct;-ive a.] a.演繹的；推論的<br><br><br>reduce [re-=backward 向後；duc=to lead 引導；-e→「to lead backward 引回頭，使後退」→] v.<br>１ bring from a higher position to a lower position 使降級：The officer was reduced to the ranks.<br>那個軍官被降為士兵。２make less in size, amount, value, etc.縮小；減少；貶值等：to reduce<br>the costs 降低成本<br><br>▽reducer [reduc(e);-er n.] n.縮減者；減速器<br>reducible [reduc(e);-ible a.] a.可縮減的<br>reduction [re-;duct;-ion n.] n.減少；縮小<br>reductive [re-;duct;-ive a.] a.減少的；縮減的<br><br><br>seduce [se-=aside 離，偏；duc=to lead 引導；-e→「to lead aside 引離正道」→] v. lead astray,<br>or draw aside from what is right 勾引；引誘：She seduced him to crime.她引誘他犯罪。<br><br>▽seducible [seduc(e);-ible a.] a.易受誘惑的<br>seduction lead into some group 引導加入某種團體」→] v.<br>１introduce formally 使正式加入：He was inducted into the trade union.他入了工會。２ put in<br>possession 使就職：This ceremony inducts the cabinet into 29. equ [L]=	even, equal 相等的<br>在常用詞equal，equate，adequate 和equivalent 中，可以看到詞根equ，它來自拉丁形容詞<br>aequus，意思相當於even（相等的）。這個詞根與其他詞根構詞時，常帶有連接字母-i-，也<br>可以把equi 看作equ 的異體。<br><br>equal [equ=even 相等的；-al a.=being 有……性質的→「being even 相等的」→] a. of the even<br>equlity, value, number, degree, etc.相等的；等值的；等量的：equal pay for equal work 同工同<br>酬<br><br>▽equality [equal;-ity n.] n.同等；平等；均等<br>equalize [equal;-ize v.] v.使相等；使平均<br><br><br>equate [equ=even 相等；-ate v.=to make 使……→] v. make equal;even out 使相等；使平衡：<br>to equate the debits and credits on the balance sheet 使結算表中借貸雙方平衡<br><br>▽equation [equat(e);-ion n.] n.平均；相等；等式；方程式<br><br><br>adequate [ad-=to 對；equ=equal 相等；-ate a.=being 有……性質的→「being equal to the needs<br>與需求相等的」→] a.１ equal to a job, or competent 勝任的：She is adequate, though not so<br>perfect.她雖不完美，但能勝任。２ equal to what is required;sufficient 足夠的；充分的：The<br>supply is not adequate to the demand.供不應求。<br><br>▽adequacy [ad-;equ;-acy n.] n.適合；足夠<br><br><br>equivalent [equi=equal 相等的；val=value 價值；-ent a.=being 是……的→]Ⅰa. being equal in<br>value, power, meaning 等值的；等效的；同義的：One dollar is equivalent to one hundred cents.<br>一元等於一百分。→Ⅱ n. equivalent thing 對等物：What is the Chinese equivalent for the word<br>「sun」? 英語「sun」在漢語中的對等詞是什麼？<br><br>▽equivalency [equi;val;-ency n.] n.均等；等重；同義<br><br><br>equable [equ=even 平穩的；-able a.=able to be 能……的→「able to be even in temper, climate,<br>etc.在心境、環境等方面能平穩的」→] a.１even-tempered; good-natured 平穩的；平靜的：<br>He has an equable disposition.他性情平穩。２unchanging 穩定的：The temperature is equable<br>this week.這星期氣溫沒什麼變化。<br><br>▽equability [equab(le);-ility n.] n.平穩；平靜<br><br><br>equator [equat(e) v.使相等；-or n.=thing 表示物→「line that equates 等分線」→] n. the great<br>circle of the earth which equates the distance between the poles 赤道（地球上等分經線的緯<br>線）<br><br>▽equatorial [equator;-ial a.] a.赤道的<br><br><br>equilibrium [equi=even 相等的；libr=balance 天平；-ium=the state 表狀態→] n. state of even<br>balance 平衡狀態：the equilibrium of supply and demand 供求平衡<br><br>▽equilibrant [equi;libr;-ant n.] n.平衡力<br>equilibrist [equi;libr;-ist n.] n.使自己保持平衡的人<br>equilibrate [equi;libr;-ate v.] v.平衡<br><br><br>equivocal [equi=equal 相等的；voc=voice 聲音；-al a.=having 有……的→「having another equal<br>voice 有另一相等聲音的」→] a. having a double meaning; purposely vague 多義的；模稜兩可<br>的：equivocal answer 模稜兩可的回答<br><br>▽equivocality [equivocal;-ity n.] n.（語言）多義性；含糊<br>equivocate [equi;voc;-ate v.] v.含糊其詞；支吾<br><br><br><br><br><br>30. fac, fact, fect [L]=        to do, to make 做	
31. fer [L]=	to carry, to bring, to bear 拿，帶，產生<br>在常用詞conference，different，offer 和prefer 中，可以看到一個很常用的詞根fer，它來自<br>拉丁動詞ferre 的不定式詞干。這個詞根的含義在不同的派生詞中略有差異，可以用三個近<br>義詞來概括它的含義：to carry（拿）；to bring（帶來）；to bear（負擔，產生）。<br><br><br>confer [con-(com-)=together 一起；fer=to bring 帶→「to bring everyone's opinion together 把<br>各人的意見帶到一起來」→] v. talk or consult together 交換意見；協商：Two lawyers conferred<br>on how to handle the case.兩位律師協商處理該案。<br><br>▽conference [confer;-ence n.] n.會談；會議<br>conferee [confer;-ee n.] n.參加商談者；參加會議者<br><br><br>differ [dif-(dis-)=apart 離；fer=to carry 拿→「to carry apart from each other 拿開，互相分離」<br>→] v. be unlike;disagree 不同；相異：I differ from you on this point.在這問題上，我和你意見<br>不同。<br><br>▽difference [differ;-ence n.] n.分歧；差異<br>different [differ;-ent a.] a.不同的；各種各樣的<br><br><br>offer [of-(ob-)=towards 向；fer=to carry 拿→「to carry towards somebody 向某人送去」→] v. １<br>present for acceptance;lay before 提供；奉獻：She offered the guests some gifts.她給客人獻上<br>禮物。２ propose 提議：He offered his help.他主動提出幫助。<br><br>▽offering [offer;-ing n.] n.提供；禮物<br><br><br>prefer [pre-=before 在……之前；fer=to bring 帶→「to bring something before all the others 把<br>某物放在他物之前」→] v. choose rather;like better 寧要；偏愛：The hero preferred death to<br>surrender. 英雄寧死不屈。<br><br>▽preference [prefer;-ence n.] n.優先；偏愛<br>preferable [prefer;-able a.] a.更可取的；更好的<br><br><br>refer [re-=back 回；fer=to bring 帶→「to bring back to the starting point 帶回出發點」→] v.１<br>trace to ...as cause or source 把……歸諸於：She refers the success to efforts. 她把成功歸諸於<br>努力。２ bring some information back for consideration 參考：Please refer to the dictionary.請<br>查閱詞典。<br><br>▽reference [refer;-ence n.] n.參考<br>referable [refer;-able a.] a.與……有關的<br><br><br>suffer [suf-(sub-)=under 在……之下；fer=to bear 承擔→「to bear under 在下面承擔著」→] v.<br>１ undergo;experience 遭受；經受：to suffer losses 遭受損失２ endure 忍受：These plants<br>cannot suffer a severe cold.這些作物耐不住嚴寒。<br><br>▽sufferance [suffer;-ance n.] n.忍耐；忍耐力<br>sufferable [suffer;-able a.] a.可忍受的<br><br><br>transfer [trans-=across 從……到……；fer=to carry 送→「to carry across an area 送過一個地區，<br>從甲地送到乙地」→] v. remove from one place to another 轉移：to transfer property 轉移財<br>產<br><br>▽transference [transfer;-ence n.] n.轉移；轉讓<br>transferor [transfer;-or n.] n.轉讓人<br>transferee [transfer;-ee n.] n.受讓人<br>transferable [transfer;-able a.] a.可轉移的；可轉讓的<br><br><br>順便指出：詞根fer 能與後綴-ous 結合成術語後綴-ferous，意為bearing，即「含……的，<br>產……的，有……的，發出……的」。<br><br><br>auriferous [auri (aurum)=gold 金；-ferous a.=bearing 含……的→] a. bearing or yielding gold 含<br>金的：auriferous ore 金礦<br><br><br>fructiferous [fructi (fructus)=fruit 果實；-ferous a.=bearing 產……的→] a. bearing fruit 結果實<br>的：fructiferous trees 結果實的樹<br><br><br>luminiferous [lumini (lumen)=light 光；-ferous a.=bearing 產……的→] a. giving light 32. fid [L]=	to trust 信任<br>在高保真音響器材上，常寫著Hi-Fi，即High-Fidelity。單詞fidelity 和confide，confidence 是<br>同族詞。詞根fid 來自拉丁動詞fidere，意思相當於to trust（信任）。<br><br><br>fidelity [fid=to trust 信任；-elity (-al+-ity) trust or belief in oneself;self-reliance 信心；自信：to<br>have full confidence 信心十足<br><br>▽confident [confid(e);-ent a.] a.確信的；有信心的；自信的<br><br><br>diffident [dif-(dis-)=not 不；fid=to trust 信任；-ent a.=-ing……的→「not trusting (oneself)不信<br>任（自己）的」→] a. distrusting;lacking in self-reliance 沒有信心的；缺乏自信的：He is diffident<br>of his own opinion.他對自己的觀點缺乏信心。<br><br>▽diffidence [dif-;fid;-ence n.] 34. flu, flux [L]=	to flow 流動<br>常用詞fluid，fluent，influence，influenza 等，都是詞根flu 的派生詞。flu 來自拉丁動詞fluere，<br>意思是to flow（流動）。flu 有個異形根flux，它來自動名詞fluxum 的詞幹部分。<br><br><br>fluid [flu=to flow 流；-id a.=having 35. form [L]=	shape;to form 形狀；形成<br>form 是英語常用詞，既可當名詞，又可當動詞。其實，form 還是個重要的拉丁詞根，作為<br>名詞性詞根，它來自forma，意為shape（形狀）；作為動詞性詞根，它來自formare，意為<br>to give a shape to 即to form（形成）。<br><br><br>form [form=to give 37. frag, fract [L]=	to break 破<br>在同根詞fragile，fragment，fraction 和fracture 中，詞根frag 和fract 來自拉丁動詞<br>frangere，意思相當於英語的to break（破）。其中，frag 是不定式詞干frang 的變體；fract<br>是動名詞詞干。frang 和它的另一變體fring，在英語中出現率比較低（見本節練習2 和4）。<br><br><br>fragile [frag=to break 破；-ile a.=easy to be 易被……的→「easy to be broken 易打破的」→] a.<br>easily broken or damaged, or breakable 易破的；易碎的：Glass is fragile.玻璃容易破。<br><br>▽fragility [fragil;-ity n.] n.脆性；脆弱<br><br><br>fragment [frag=to break 破；-ment n.=the result 表行為結果→「the result of being broken 破<br>碎的結果」→] n.１ part of something broken off 破片，碎片：fragments of a vase 一個花瓶的<br>碎片２ part of some-thing left unfinished 未完成的部分：This poem is only a fragment.這首詩<br>僅是未完稿。<br><br>▽fragmentary [fragment;-ary a.] a.碎片的；片斷的<br>fragmentate [fragment;-ate v.] v.使裂成碎片<br><br><br>fraction [fract=to break 破；-ion n.=the result 表行為結果→「the result of breaking something<br>破壞或分裂某物的結果」→] n.１ something broken off from the whole 碎片：The cup crumbled<br>into fractions.杯子破成碎片。２ any part of a unit or number 部分；分數：One-third is a fraction.<br>三分之一是分數。<br><br>▽fractional [fraction;-al a.] a.部分的；分數的<br>fractionize [fraction;-ize v.] v.使分成幾部分；把……化為分數<br><br><br>fracture [fract=to break 破；-ure n.=the act or state 表行為或狀態→] n. breaking or breakage,<br>especially of bone 破裂；骨折：She suffered a fracture of her wrist.她的手腕骨折了。<br><br><br>infraction [in-=in 入；fract=to break 破；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「breaking in law or rule 破<br>壞法律，侵犯規則」→] n. violation of law;breach 違犯；違背：infraction of martial law 違反戒<br>嚴法<br><br><br>refract [re-=back 回，返；fract=to break, to bend or turn 破，轉，折→「to turn back 折回」→]<br>v. turn aside（rays of light, sound, etc. passing into a medium from another medium）使（光線、<br>聲波等從一種介質進入另一種介質時）發生偏轉；使折射：Water refracts light.水使光折射。<br><br>▽refractable [refract;-able a.] a.可折射的<br>refractive [refract;-ive a.] a.折射的<br><br><br>refractory [re-=against 反抗；fract=to 一條蜿蜒的小溪	
30. fac, fact, fect [L]=	to do, to make 做<br>fac，fact 和fect 是一組同源異形根，它們都來自拉丁動詞facere，意思相當於to do 或to make<br>（做）。其中，fac 是不定式詞干；fact 是動名詞詞干；fect 是動詞facere 的異體ficere 動名<br>詞詞干。<br><br><br>facile [fac=to do 做；-ile a.=able or easy to be 能……的，易……的→「able or easy to be done<br>能做的，易辦的」→] a.１ working with ease;skilled 駕輕就熟的；熟練的：a man with a facile<br>tongue 能說會道的人２ easily done 易做的：The work is facile, but take it serious.工作容易，<br>但還要認真對待。<br><br>▽facility [facil(e);-ity n.] n.容易；熟練<br>facilitate [facil(e);-itate(-ate) v.] v.使容易；促進<br><br><br>faculty [fac=to do 做；-ulty（-ile+-ty）n.=ability 表能力→「ability of doing things 做事情的能力」<br>→] n. ability to do;any particular power 能力；才能：faculty for painting 繪畫的才能<br><br>▽facultative [facult (y);-ative a.] a.能力上的；才能上的<br><br><br>fact [來自動名詞factum=thing done 做過的事情→「anything done or occurred 做過的或發生<br>過的事」→] n.１ thing known to have occurred or to be ture 事實：Facts speak louder than<br>eloquence.事實勝於雄辯。２ what is true or existent;truth;reality 實際；真相；實情：in fact<br>實際上<br><br>▽factual [fact;-u-;-al a.] a.事實的；真實的<br><br><br>factor [fact=to do 做；-or n.=thing 物→「thing that does or acts 起作用的事物」→] n. element<br>that brings about a result 因素；要素：positive factors 積極因素<br><br>▽factorial [factor;-ial a.] a. 做；-or n.=person 人→] n. person who does good deeds or<br>gives friendly aid 做好事者；恩人：benefactors of an orphanage 孤兒院的施主<br><br>▽benefaction [bene;fact;-ion n.] n.行善；施恩<br><br><br>affect [af-(ad-)=upon 在……之上；fect=to do or act 起作用→「to act upon 作用於……之上」<br>→] v.１ influence 影響：Climate affects the agricultural production.氣候影響農業生產。２ act<br>upon the feeling of 感動：The audience were deeply affected.觀眾深為感動。<br><br>▽affection [affect;-ion n.] n.影響；感情<br>affective [affect;-ive a.] a.感情方面的；表達感情的<br><br><br>effect [ef-(ex-)=out 出；fect=to make 造→「to make out 造出」→]Ⅰv.１ produce;bring
