什麼是詞根	詞根是構詞的基本詞素，它與詞綴相對，並帶有主要的詞彙信息。	
詞根分為	能獨立構詞的是自由詞根，必須與其他詞素結合構詞的是粘附詞根。	
英語經歷了三個發展階段	古英語（Old English，盎格魯—撒克遜人統治）、中古英語（Middle English，使用法語與拉丁語的諾爾曼人統治）和現代英語（Modern English，歐洲文藝復興運動的影響）。	
各種語源的單詞在英語詞彙總量中占的百分比是	日耳曼語源（即本族語源） 33％；拉丁與希臘語源（即古典語源） 56％；凱爾特語源2％；混合語源3％；東方、非洲、美洲等語源6％	
詞綴分成兩種：	能與自由詞根結合的是派生詞綴，只能與粘附詞根結合的是原生詞綴。	
英語的主要構詞方式	有3 種：轉化、合成與派生	
零級派生=	粘附詞根+零原生詞綴 或 自由詞根+零派生詞綴	
一級派生=	粘附詞根+原生詞綴→原始派生詞或原生詞	
二級派生=	自由詞根+派生詞綴→二次派生詞	
大部分派生詞是	由粘附詞根與原生詞綴構成的原始派生詞	
英語詞根只有	單音節與雙音節兩種。從比例來看，單音節詞根占80％以上，雙音節詞根不到20％。本族語詞根中單音節的占90％左右，拉丁詞根中單音節的占90％以上，而希臘詞根中單音節的比例較低，約占30％左右。	
單音節詞根的基本模式是：	「輔音字母+元音字母+輔音字母」，如：man，vis，log 等	
構詞過程中發生的形態變化	主要有4 種：1.字母的增加，2.字母的脫落，3.字母的變更，4.連字符的使用	
派生詞中一般讀法	詞根重讀、詞綴輕讀	
自由詞根的讀音是	固定的，它等於充當自由詞根的基本單詞在詞典中的讀音	
粘附詞根讀音	在多數同根詞中都表現出相對固定的	
如果詞根在派生詞中重讀，其讀音	保持不變。這時，派生詞的讀音即等於各種詞素讀音總和。	
詞根是非重讀或次重讀音節，詞根的音值就	可能發生變化	
「詞根重讀、詞綴輕讀」例外有哪幾種4 種與前綴有關：	1.表示否定意義的派生前綴un-和non-與詞根同樣重讀；2.雙音節的前綴原生詞由動詞轉化成名詞或形容詞時，重音從詞根所在音節（第二音節）轉移到詞綴所在音節（第一音節）；3.借用的派生前綴（尤其是拉丁語源的派生前綴），為了表示其有別於同源同形的原生詞綴往往與詞根（單詞）一起重讀。；4.少數前綴在單詞中往往重讀。比較典型的有post-，self-，semi-等	
「詞根重讀、詞綴輕讀」例外有哪幾種3 種與後綴有關：	5.個別後綴總是重讀，典型的有-ee， -ese，-esque，-ette；6.有些後綴本身並不重讀，卻會使派生詞的重音發生有規則的轉移。最有代表性的是-ian，-ic，-ion 和-ity，它們總是使單詞重音落在自己的前一個音節上。7.有些派生詞重讀的例外現象並無規律可尋，只能把它歸因於歷史或習慣使然。對這些真正的「搗亂分子」，要特別予以注意。例如：`dif·fer，`com·mon，`com·fort 等。	
隱性詞按照隱性的程度，分三種情況	1.有些距離；2.本義在使用過程發生了變化。有的詞義擴大，有的縮小，有的揚升，有的貶降，有的則被用於比喻或引申；3.不但包含了詞根和詞綴的含義，還包括一定的背景知識。需要瞭解這些背景，才能理解在特定條件下才能成立的派生詞詞義。	
詞素間的制約關係	後綴＞詞根，後綴的屬性決定了派生詞的詞性；動詞詞素＞名詞詞素＞形容詞詞素＞副詞詞素。	
同源異形根現象主要出現於	拉丁動詞詞根，因為拉丁動詞有各種變化形式	
同源異形根現象輔音字母收尾的詞根，變成	以t 收尾的異形詞根,volv→volut,mov→mot	
同源異形根現象以t、d 收尾的詞根變成	以s 收尾的詞根,flect→flex,sent→sens	
術語詞綴有一個非常特殊的功能，即	一個術語前綴可以與一個術語後綴構成一個帶術語性質的單詞,aero-（空氣）+-logy（……學）→aerology n.氣象學	
術語前綴後面往往有	連接字母-o-或-i-，如：bio-，thermo-，denti-（齒）等。	
分析不同語源的粘附詞根，可以發現，（）詞根常構成一般用詞，（）詞根常構成科技術語	拉丁；希臘	
有些詞根是多義的。這主要是（）詞根，而且為數不多	拉丁動詞	
動詞詞根pend，pens 原意是()，由於把東西掛在天平上才能稱量，所以又有()的含義，又因為用天平稱量金銀來付款，又多了個(()的含義。	to hang（懸掛）;to weigh（稱量）;to pay（支付）	
詞根ag，act 既有()的意思，也有「驅使他人去做」的()之意	to do（做）;to drive（驅使）	
有些後綴本身並不重讀，卻會使派生詞的重音發生有規則的轉移。最有代表性的是（），它們總是使單詞重音落在自己的前一個音節上	-ian，-ic，-ion 和-ity	
1. ag, act [L]=	to do, to drive 做，驅使 詞根ag 來自拉丁動詞agere 的詞幹部分，意思相當於英語的to do（做）或to drive（驅使）。 act 是個英語核心單詞，其實它的前身act 是ag 的同源異形詞根，來自agere 的動名詞形式 actum 的詞幹部分，基本含義也是to do 或to drive。下面先分析幾個由ag 構成的常見派生 詞。   agent [ag=to do 做；-ent n.=person 人→「person who does 辦事者」→] n. person who works for another person or organization 代理人：a sales agent 代售商  ▽agential [agent;-ial a.] a.代理人的；起媒介作用的   agency [ag=to do 做；-ency n.=the quality or state of 表性質或狀態→「the abiliy or place of doing business 辦事的能力或場所」→] n.１power or force which causes a result 力量；作用： human agency 人力２ the office of an agent;service organization 代理處；機構：travel agency 旅行社   agenda [ag=to do 做；-enda（-a 表複數）n.=things 事情→「things to be done 要辦的事項」 →] n. list of things to be discussed or decided upon 議事日程：the most important item on the agenda 議事日程的首項   agile [ag=to do 做；-ile a.=able 能……的→「able to do 能幹的」→] a. able to do or move quickly or easily 敏捷的；靈活的：as agile as a monkey 像猴子般靈活  ▽agility [agil(e);-ity] n.敏捷；靈活   agitate [ag=to drive or keep moving 驅使，使運動；-itate（-ate）v.=make or cause 使……→「cause to keep moving steadily 引起不斷的動盪」→] v. disturb 鼓動：The audience were agitated by his speech 聽眾被他的演說所鼓動。  ▽agitation [agitat(e);-ion n.] n.鼓動；激動不安 agitator [agitat(e);-or n.] n.鼓動者   以下介紹的是幾個常用act 的同根詞。   act [act=to do 做→「to do what is required 做要求的事」→] v. １ do something 行動：to act at once 立刻行動２ function 起作用：The brakes wouldn't act.剎車失靈。３ take part in a play or film 扮演：Who is acting Hamlet? 誰演哈姆雷特？  ▽actor [act;-or n.] n.男演員；行動者 actress [act (o)r;-ess n.] n.女演員 re-act [re-;act v.] v.重做，再做；重演，再演 overact [over-;act v.] v.演得過於誇張   action [act=to do 做；-ion n.=the process or result 表過程或結果→] n.１ process of doing, or deed 行動，活動：Actions speak louder than words.行動比語言更有說服力。２ result of doing, or effect 作用：the action of an acid on metal 酸對金屬的作用３ charge 訴訟：to bring an action against someone 起訴某人  ▽actionable [action;-able a.] a.可控訴的 active [act=to do 做；-ive a.=able 會……的→] a. able to do 活躍的，積極的：Although he is over 70, he is still active.他雖然年過70，但依然很活躍。  ▽activate [activ(e);-ate v.] v.使活動 activism [activ(e);-ism n.] n. [哲] 能動主義；積極，活躍 activist [activ(e);-ist n.] n.活動分子，積極分子 activity [activ(e);-ity n.] n.能動性；活躍；[復] 活動   actual [act=to do 做；-u-;-al a.=the act or fact 表行為或事實→] a. existing in fact;real 實際的； 現實的：the actual amount of money 實際金額  ▽actualist [actual;-ist n.] n.現實主義者 actuality [actual;-ity n.] n.事實，現存情況；現實性 actualize [actual;-ize v.] v.實行，使現實化   actuate [act=to do 做；-u-;-ate v.=to make or cause 使……→] v. cause to do 驅動，激勵：What motives actuated her? 什麼動機驅使她這樣做的？  ▽actuation [actuat(e);-ion n.] n.驅動，激勵；開動   exact [ex-=out 出；act=to drive 驅使→「to drive out;driven out 逼出來（的）」→] I v. demand or obtain by force 強求，索取：He exacted obedience from his students.他強要學生服從他。→ Ⅱ a. correct and without mistake 準確的，精確的：to be exact in conduct 行為一絲不苟  ▽exacting [exact v.;-ing a.] a.苛求的，嚴厲的；強索的 exaction [exact v.;-ion n. ] a.強索；勒索；搾取 exactitude [exact a.;-itude n.] n.精確（性）；嚴格，嚴謹   react [re-=back 回返；act=to do 做→] v.１ do or act in reply 反應：She was slow to react.她反 應遲鈍。２ do against 反動，反作用：to react against oppression 反抗壓迫  ▽reaction [react;-ion n.] n.反應；反作用；反動 reactor [react;-or n.] n.引起反應的人或物；[原] 反應堆 reactive [react;-ive a.] a.反應的；反動的   interact [inter-=between 在……之間；act=to do 做→「to do between two things 在兩者之間互 動」→] v. have an effect on each other 互相作用，互相影響：All things are inter-related and interacted on each other.一切事物都是互相聯繫又互相影響的。  ▽interaction [interact;-ion n.] n.相互作用；相互 interactant [interact;-ant n.] n. [化] 反應物 interactive [interact;-ive a.] a.互相作用的；[計] 交互的   transact [trans-=across or through 穿過；act=to drive 驅使→「to drive through 使通過」→] v. carry on;manage 執行，辦理：He transacted some businesss at bank.他在銀行處理了一些事務。  ▽transaction [transact;-ion n.] n.辦理，處理；交易，業務 transactor [transact;-or n.] n.辦事人，處理者	
2. am, amat [L]=	to love 愛 常用詞amiable 和amateur 分別來自同源異形根am 和amat。am 是拉丁動詞amare 的不定 式詞干；amat 是這個動詞的動名詞詞干，意思都相當於to love（愛）。   amiable [am=to love 愛；-i-；-able a.=capable of 可……的→「capable of being loved 可愛的」 →] a. lovable, or kindly 可愛的；和藹的：an amiable old lady 可親的老太太   amateur [amat=to love; -eur (-er) n.=person 人→「persaon who does something for loving it (rather than for money)因愛好（不是為金錢）從事某項活動者」→] n. person who practices an art, sport or science for his own pleasure（藝術、體育、科學等）業餘愛好者：radio amateur 業餘無線電愛好者  ▽amateurism [amateur;-ism n.] n.業餘活動   amateurish [amateur n.業餘愛好者；-ish a.=like 像…的→「like an amateur（rather than a professional hand）像業餘的，不內行的」→] a. unskillful 不老練的，外行的：He is still amateurish in playing golf.他打高爾夫球還不老練。  ▽amateurishness [amateurish;-ness n.] n.外行   amicable [amic（來自am 的同根名詞amicus）=person one loves, or friend 親愛者，朋友； -able a.=able to be 能當……的→「able to be one's friend 能做朋友的」→] a. in a friendly spirit, or peaceable 友好的；和睦的：amicable settlement 和解  ▽amicability [amicab(le);-ility n.] n.友好；和睦   amour [am=to love 愛；-our n.=the state or result 表狀態或結果→「loving or the result of loving 戀愛或戀愛的結果）」→] n.１ love 戀愛２ love affair 桃色事件，偷情  ▽amorous [amo(u)r;-ous a.] a.戀愛的；多情的   enamour [en-v.=to cause to be 使；amour n.=love 戀愛→「to cause to be in love 使戀愛」→] v. inflame with love 使迷戀：Her beauty enam-oured the prince.王子被她的美貌迷住了。   amatory [amat=to love 愛；-ory a.=related to 與……有關的→] a. related to loving;expressing love 戀愛的；愛慕的：amatory poems 情詩	
3. anim [L]=	life 生命 anim 是常用詞animal 的詞根，源於拉丁名詞anima，含有mind（思想），spirit（精神）， soul（靈魂），life（生存）等與生命現象有關的概念，可以看成英語基本詞life（生命）的對 等詞。   animal [anim=life 生命；-al n.=thing characterized by 有……特徵的東西→「thing characterized by having life 有生命的東西」→] n. １ any creature 動物：Is it an animal, vegetable, or mineral? 它是動物，植物，還是礦物？２ any creature other than man 除人以外的任何動物：the animals in the zoo 動物園裡的動物  ▽animalism [animal;-ism n.] n.動物性；獸慾 animalize [animal;-ize v.] v.使動物化   animate [anim=life 生命；-ate a.=having 有……的→「having life or spirits 有生命的，有精神 的」→]Ⅰa. １ living 有生命的：animate objects 生物２ full of life or spirits 生氣勃勃的： animate youth 朝氣蓬勃的年青人→Ⅱ v. give life to, or make alive 使活躍：His jokes an-imated the conversation.他的笑話使交談活躍起來。  ▽animation [animat(e) v;-ion n.] n.活躍；生氣 reanimate [re-;animate v.] v.使復活；激勵   animosity [anim=life, spirit 生命，精神；-osity（-ous+-ity）n.=special state or quality 表特殊狀 態或性質→ 「 special spirit 特殊的精神」 → 「 strong feeling 強烈的感情」 → ] n. strong dislike;hatred 敵意；仇恨：animosities between classes 階級仇恨   magnanimity [magn=great 大；anim=spirit 精神；-ity n.=the quality 表性質→「the greatness of spirit or mind 精神上的大度」→] n. the spirit of being unusually generous, or generosity 寬宏大 量：He showed his magnanimity in forgiving you.他原諒了你，可見其寬宏大量。  ▽magnanimous [magn;anim;-ous a.] a.寬宏大量的   equanimity [equ=even 平衡的；anim=spirit 精神；-ity n.=the quality 表性質→「the spirit with an even quality 平穩的精神品質」→] n. calmness or steadiness of mind 沉著；鎮定：He faced the disaster with equanimity.面對災難，他泰然若定。  ▽equanimous [equ;anim;-ous a.] a.沉著的；鎮定的   longanimity [long（來自形容詞longus）=long 長久的；anim=spirit 精神；-ity n.=the quality 表 性質→ 「 the spirit with the quality of enduring long 能長久忍耐的精神素質」 → ] n. endurance;forbearance 忍耐性；堅韌性：He is remarkable for his longanimity in struggle.他在 鬥爭中以堅韌著稱。  ▽longanimous [long;anim;-ous a.] a.堅韌的；忍耐的   unanimous [un=one 一；anim=spirit, mind 精神，思想；-ous a.=having 有……的→] a. having one mind or sharing the same view 思想一致的；觀點統一的：The conference was unanimous in support of the decision.會議一致擁護這項決議。  ▽unanimity [un;anim;-ity n.] n.全體一致；無異議	
4. ann, enn [L]=	year 年 ann 來自拉丁名詞annus，意思為year（年）；enn 是ann 在添加前綴時產生的音變異體。ann 在構詞中常帶有連接字母-u-或-i-，也可以把annu 和anni 作為詞根異體看待。   annual [annu=year 年；-al a.=of……的→] I a. of one year;yearly 一年的；每年的：annual report 年度報告→Ⅱn. book or pamphlet issued once a year 年鑒；年刊：the annuals of the Historical Society 歷史協會的年鑒   anniversary [anni=year 年；vers=to turn 轉；-ary n.=thing 物→「the date connected with the turning of a year 與時間周轉一年相關的日子」→] n. the date of a year on which something happened 週年紀念日：the 400th anniversary of Shakespeare's birth 莎士比亞誕生四百週年紀 念日   annals [ann=year 年；-al n.=thing 物；-s 表複數→「many things of a year 一年中的事情」→] n. yearly records;historical records 編年史；歷史記載：the war annals of the Red Army 紅軍戰史  ▽annalist [annal(s);-ist n.] n.編年史作者   perennial [per-=through 通；enni=year 年；-al a.→「through a year 通年的」→] a.１lasting through the year 常年不斷的：perennial snow and ice 終年不化的冰雪２ overlasting 長久的：perennial efforts 持久努力  ▽perenniality [perennial;-ity n.] n.常年性；長久性   annuity [annu=year 年；-ity n.=thing connected with 表相關事物→「money connected with one year 按一年計算的錢」→] n. yearly allowance or income 年金；年收入：life annuity 終身年金  ▽annuitant [annuit(y);-ant n.] n.領受年金者   superannuate [super-=over 超；annu=year 年→age 年齡；-ate v.=to cause to be 使成為→「to cause to be over-aged 使成為超齡者」→] v. make to retire when one is over a certain age 因超 過年齡而令退休：He was superannuated as soon as he reached the age of sixty.他剛滿六十歲， 就被指令退休了。   annu 和enni 還能與表示數目的前綴構成表示以「年」為單位的時間的單詞。以下是常見的 幾個。   semiannual [semi-=half 半；annu=year 年；-al a.=of……的→] a. of a half year 半年一度的： semiannual meeting 半年一度的會議 biannual [bi-=two, twice 二，兩次；annu=year 年；-al a.=of……的→a. of twice a year 每年兩 度的：biannual examination 每年兩次的考試 biennial [bi-=two 二；enni=year 年；-al a.=of……的→「of two years 二年的」→] a. lasting two years 持續兩年的：a biennial research course 兩年的研究課程 biennium [bi-=two 二；enni=year 年；-um n.=thing 物→「the time of two years 兩年的時間」 →] n. period of two years 兩年	
5. anthrop [GK]=	man 人類 anthrop 是本書介紹的第一個來自希臘語的詞根，它的詞源是希臘名詞anthropos，意思為 man 或human kind（人類）。在構詞中，anthrop 後面常跟著連接字母-o-，也可以把anthropo 看作異形詞根。   anthropology [anthropo=man 人類；-logy n.=branch of science 一門科學→「the science about man 研究人類的科學」 → ] n. the science dealing with the physical, social, and cultural development of man 人類學  ▽anthropologist [anthropolog(y);-ist n.] n.人類學者   philanthropist [phil=to love 愛；anthrop=man 人類；-ist n.=person 人→「person who loves man 愛人類者」→] n. person who loves his fellow men, especially, who is engaged in helping the poor men 博愛主義者；慈善家  ▽philanthropy [phil;anthrop;-y n.] n.慈善；仁愛 philanthropic [phil;anthrop;-ic a.] a.博愛的   misanthropist [mis=to hate 恨；anthrop=man 人類；-ist n.=person 人→「person who hates his fellow men 厭惡人類者」→] n. person who hates everybody and avoids being in the company of others 離群索居者；憤世嫉俗者：A misanthropist can never become a philanthropist.憤世嫉俗 者是成不了慈善家的。  ▽misanthropy [mis;anthrop;-y n.] n.厭世 misanthropic [mis;anthrop;-ic a.] a.厭世的；厭世者的   anthropoid [anthrop=man 人類；-oid a.=like 像……→] a. like a man;in the form of a man 類人 的；有人形的：anthropoid ape 類人猿   anthropography [anthropo=man 人類；-graphy n.=the study……學→「the study about man 有 關人類情況的學說」→] n. the study of the geographical distribution of human races 人種地理分 布學   anthropogenesis [anthropo=man 人類；genesis=the origin 起源→] n. the study of man's origin and development 人類起源和發展學   anthropotomy [anthropo=man 人類；tomy=anatomy 解剖學→] n. human anatomy 人體解剖學	
6. arch [GK]=	rule 統治 在政治術語anarchy, monarch, monarchy 和oligarch 中，有個常用詞根arch。它來自希臘名詞 arkhos，意為rule（統治）。在派生詞中arch 常作ruler（統治者）或government（政體）解。  anarchy [an-(a-)=no, without 無；arch=rule 治理；-y n.=the state 表狀態→「the state without rule or government 缺乏治理，沒有政府」→] n. absence of government or control 無秩序；無政府 狀態：Any form of government is better than anarchy. 任何形式的政體都比無政府狀態好。  ▽anarchic [anarch(y);-ic a.] a.無政府主義的 anarchism [anarch(y);-ism a.] n.無政府主義 anarchist [anarch(y);-ist n.] n.無政府主義者   monarch [mon=one, alone 單一；arch=ruler 統治者→「only one ruler, or one who rules a country alone 單獨治理國家者」→] n. king of sovereign 國王，君主：The monarch was ousted.國王被 趕下台了。  ▽monarchal [monarch;-al a.] a.國王的，君主的   monarchy [mon-=one, alone 單一；arch=ruler 統治者；-y n.=the state 表狀態→「the state or government of only one ruler 單人統治的政體」→] n. government ruled by a monarch 君主政 體；君主國：China was once a monarchy.中國曾經是個君主國。  ▽monarchic [monarch(y);-ic a.] a.君主制的；君主國的 monarchism [monarch(y);-ism n.] n.君主制度；君主主義   oligarch [olig-=few 少，寡；arch=ruler 統治者→「one of a few rulers 少數統治者之一」→] n. member of an oligarchy 寡頭統治成員：finan-cial oligarch 金融寡頭   oligarchy [olig-=few 少，寡；arch=ruler 統治者；-y n.=the state 表狀態→「the state or government by a few rulers 由少數人統治的政府」→] n. rule or government by a few, often for their own interests 寡頭政治；寡頭統治的政府：Ancient Sparta was really an oligarchy.古斯巴達實際上 是個寡頭統治的國家。  ▽oligarchic [oligarch(y);-ic a.] a.寡頭政治的   polyarchy [poly-=many 多；arch=ruler 統治者；-y n.=the state 表狀態→「the state or government by many rulers 多人的統治」→] n. rule or government by many heads 多頭政治   matriarch [matri=mother 母；arch=ruler 統治者→「a ruler who is a mother 母權統治者」→] n. woman who rules a large family or tribe 女家長；女族長：This tribe is still led by matriarchs.該 部落依然以女族長為首。  ▽matriarchal [matriarch;-al a.] a.女家長的；女族長的   matriarchy [matri=mother 母；arch=rule 統治；-y n.=the state 表狀態→「the state of rule by mothers 母權統治」→] n. social group or system ruled only by women 母權制；母系氏族制： Many ancient societies were matriarchies.許多遠古社會是母權制社會。   archives [arch=ruler 統治者；-ive n.=thing 物；-s 表複數→「documents belonging to rulers 屬 於統治者的文件」→] n.１ public records 檔案２ place in which public records are stored 檔案 室（館）：the central archives of the state 國家檔案館  ▽archivist [archiv(es);-ist n.] n.檔案保管員 archival [archiv(es);-al a.] a.關於檔案的；在檔案中的   arch 還可以當前綴使用。arch-意思是chief（主要的）。   archenemy [arch-=chief 主要的；enemy n.敵人→] n. chief enemy 首敵；大敵   architect [arch-=thief 首要的；-i-;tect=builder 建築者→「chief builder 建築者的首領」→] n. designer of buildings 建築設計師  ▽architecture [architect;-ure n.] n.建築學 architectonic [architect;-onic(-ic) a.] a.關於建築的	
7. aud, audit [L]=	to hear 聽 在常用詞audience 和auditorium 中，有一對同源異形詞根aud 和audit，其詞源拉丁動詞audire 的意思是to hear（聽）。aud 是不定式詞干，audit 是動名詞詞干。   audience [aud=to hear 聽；-i-;-ence n.=the act or state 表行為或狀態→「the act or state of hearing 聽的行為或狀態」→] n.１ interview or con-ference 會見；接見：The foreign guests had an audience with the may-or.外賓拜會了市長。２ the people assembled to hear 聽眾：There will be a large audience today.今天會有很多聽眾來。   auditorium [audit=to hear 聽；-orium n.=place 場所→「place for hearing 聽的場所」→] n.１ building or room for public meetings 禮堂；演講廳２ the space allocated to the hearers 聽眾席： The author was found sitting in the auditorium.有人發現作者正坐在聽眾席中。   audible [aud=to hear 聽；-ible a.=capable of being 能被……的→] a. capable of being heard 聽得 見的：Their whispers are hardly audible.他們竊竊私語，別人聽不見。  ▽inaudible [in-;audible a.] a.聽不見的   audit [audit=to hear 聽→「to hear a lecture or a report 聽課；聽取匯報」→] v. １ attend class in a university without intending to receive a grade（在大學）旁聽：to audit a history course at college 旁聽大學歷史課程２examine（financial accounts）審查（賬目）：The yearly accounts will be audited by a special committee.年度賬目將由特別委員會審查。  ▽auditor [audit;-or n.] n.（大學）旁聽生；查賬員   audition [audit=to hear 聽；-ion n.=the act 表行為→] n. １ hearing 聽２ trial hearing（to an actor or singer）（對演員等）試聽：to give an audition to a singer 聽歌手試唱決定是否錄用   audile [aud=to hear 聽；-ile a.=pertaining to……的→] a. pertaining（關於，有關）to hearing or the sense of hearing 聽的；聽覺的：audile power 聽的功能   auditory [audit=to hear 聽； -ory a.=relating to 與… … 有關的→ ] a. relating to the sense of hearing 聽覺的：auditory nerves 聽覺神經   audiology [audi=to hear 聽；-o-;-logy n.=branch of science 一門科學→] n. the science dealing with the sense of hearing 聽覺學  ▽audiologist [audiolog(y);-ist n.] n.聽覺學學者   audio [形容詞性的合詞成分：aud=to hear 聽；-io→「of hearing 與聽有關的」→] I a. pertaining to sound or sound waves 聲音的；聲波的：audio frequency 音頻→Ⅱ n. broadcast or recorded sound 播音；錄音：My television set has a good picture by weak audio.我的電視機圖像清晰， 但是收音不好。	
8. aug, auct, auth [L]=	to increase 增加 讀者可能想不到August（八月），auction（拍賣）和author（作者）居然是同根詞吧！它們 分別來自拉丁動詞aguere、它的過去分詞auctus 及其變體auth，其基本意思都是to increase （增加）或to cause to grow（使產生，使增大）。   august [aug=to increase 使增大；-ust a.=the most 最→「to increase to the most 增到最大」→ 「the greatest 最偉大的」→]Ⅰa. majestic 威嚴的：august palaces 威嚴的王宮→Ⅱ（大寫 August）n.１ 奧古斯特（即古羅馬Augustus 凱撒大帝，他自認為是最偉大的帝王）２ 八月 （奧古斯特大帝以自己的名字命名八月份）   augment [aug=to increase 增加；-ment v.→] v.１ make greater or enlarge 增加，擴大：to augment the power 擴大權力２ become greater 增加，增大：The sound of traffic augments during the rush hour.高峰時間交通噪音會增大。  ▽augmentative [augment;-ative a.] a.有擴大（增加）作用的   auction [auct=to cause to grow 使增加；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「the act of causing the price to grow 使價格上升的行為」→]Ⅰn. sale in which goods are sold to the person offering the most money 拍賣：to sell the old furniture by auction 拍賣舊傢俱→Ⅱv. sell by auction 拍賣：When the artist died, his family auctioned his paintings.藝術家去世後，家人把他的畫拍賣了。  ▽auctioneer [auction v.-eer n.] n.拍賣商   author [auth（auct）=to cause to grow 使成長；-or n.=person 人→「person who causes anything to grow 使事物產生者」→] n.１ person who begins or creates 發起人，創始者：the author of the new plan 新計劃的倡議者２ writer 著作者，作家：His favorite author is Dickens.他最喜歡 的作家是狄更斯。  ▽authorless [author;-less a.] a.作者不明的；隱名的   auctorial [auctor=author 作者；-i-;-al a.=of……的→] a. of or having to do with an author 作者的： auctorial comments 作者說明   authority [author n. 創始者；-ity n.=the quality 表特性→「the quality of an author 創始者的特 性」→] n.１ the power or right to control or make decisions 權力，權威：Rulers have no authority from God to do mischief.上帝並沒有給統治者製造禍害的權力。２ person(s) having authority 當權者：higher authority 上級領導   authorize [author n.創始者（→power 權力）；-ize v.=to cause to have 使有→「to cause to have power 使有權力」→] v. give power to 授權：The president authorized his ambassador to sign the treaty.總統授權大使簽訂該條約。  ▽authorization [authoriz(e);-ation n.] n.授權，委託	
9. bi, bio [GK]=	life 生命，生物 biology（生物學）中的bi 是個希臘詞根，它來自希臘名詞bios，意思為life（生命，生物）。 在構詞中，bi 常通過連接字母-o-與其他詞素結合，所以，也可以把bio 看作bi 的異體。   biology [bio=life 生命，生物；-logy n.=branch of science 一門科學→] n. the science of life in all 生物學：Zoology and botany are main divisions of biology.動物學和植物學是生物學的兩門主要 分科。  ▽biologist [biolog(y);-ist n.] n.生物學者 biological [biolog(y);-ical a.] a.生物學的   biography [bio=life 生命；-graphy n.=writing 著作→「writing about one's life 關於一個人生平 的著作」→] n. written account about a person's life 傳記：a biography of Darwin 達爾文傳記  ▽biographer [biograph (y);-er n.] n.傳記作者 biographical [biograph(y);-ical a.] a.傳記的；傳記體的 biographize [biograph (y);-ize v.] v.為……作傳記   biocide [bio=life 生物→living beings 蟲；-cide n.=that which kills 殺……物→] n. substance which kills harmful living beings 殺蟲劑   antibiotic [anti-=against 抗；bi=life 生命，生物；-otic a.=having the quality 有……性能的→ 「against the growing of a certain life 能抵制某種生物生長的」→] a. opposing the living of disease carrying bacteri-a 抗病菌的；抗生的：antibiotic substance 抗生素   microbial [micro-=tiny 微小的；bi=life 生物；-al a.=of ……的→「of a tiny life 微小生物的」→] a. of microscopic organisms 微生物的：the microbial enemy of man 人類的微生物敵人 bio 也可以作為術語前綴，與其他充當術語的單詞結合，構成新的術語。bio-的意思為「生 物」或「生物的」。   biochemistry [bio-=life 生物；chemistry 化學n.→] n. the branch of chem-istry relating to life or living organisms 生物化學  ▽biochemist [bio-;chem.;-ist n.] n.生物化學家   biophysics [bio-=life 生物；physics n.物理學→] n. the branch of physics relating to life or living organisms 生物物理學  ▽biophysicist [biophysic(s);-ist n.] n.生物物理學家	
10. cad, cas, cid [L]=	to fall, to befall 降，降臨 cad，cas，cid 是同源異形詞根，都源於拉丁動詞cadere，意思相當於to fall（降落）或to befall （降臨）。其中，cad 是不定式詞干，cas 是動名詞詞干，而cid 是cadere 的異體cidere 的不 定式詞干。這族同根詞的數量較大。   decadent [de-=down 下；cad=to fall 降；-ent a.=-ing 表性質→「falling down 下降的」] a. falling down morally;falling into ruin 墮落的；頹敗的：The Ching Empire had become decadent by that time.當時清帝國已經腐敗了。  ▽decadence [de-;cad;-ence n.] n.衰落；頹廢   case [cas=to befall 降臨；-e→「that which befalls 降臨之事」→] n. event;condition 事件；情 況：a typical case 典型事件   casual [cas=to befall 降臨；-u-;-al a.=having the quality 有……性質的→「having the quality of befalling, or happening by chance 帶有偶發性質的」→] a.１ not planned 偶然的：a casual meeting 巧遇２ infor-mal 非正式的：casual clothing 便服  ▽casualty [casual;-ty n.] n.事故的傷亡者   occasion [oc-（ob-）=in the way of 在……面前；cas=to befall 降臨；-ion n.=the state or result 表狀態或結果→「that which befalls in one's way 降臨在面前的事」→] n.１ instance or case 情況２ favorable time, or opportunity 時機；機會：as occasion serves 一旦有適當的機會  ▽occasional [occasion;-al a.] a.偶爾的   accident [ac-(ad-)=towards 朝向；cid=to befall 降臨；-ent n.=thing 事→「thing that befalls towards a person 朝著某人降臨的事」→] n. １unexpected event 意外的事；偶然的事：I met her quite by accident.我碰到她是很偶然的事。２ unfortunate happening 事故：traffic acci-dents 交通事 故  ▽accidental [accident;-al a.] a.意外的；偶然的   incident [in-=on, upon 在……上；cid=to befall 發生；-ent n.=thing 事→「thing that befalls on a particular person or happens at a particular time 發生在某人身上或某個時刻的事」→] n. event, or occurence 事件；事變：the July 7th Incident 七七事變  ▽incidental [incident;-al a.] a.偶然的；伴隨的 incidence [in-;cid;-ence n.] n.發生；發生率   coincide [co-（com-）=together 共同；in-=upon 在……之上；cid=to befall 降臨→「to befall upon together 共同降臨在……之上」] v. １happen at the same time or same place（時間、空間） 恰好相合：My birthday coincides with yours. 我恰好和你同一天生日。２ agree;correspond 一致；符合：to coincide in opinion 意見相符  ▽coincident [coincid(e);-ent a.] a.同時發生的；一致的   deciduous [de-=off 脫離；cid=to fall 降；-u-;-ous a.=having the quality 有……性質的→] a. having the quality of falling off at a certain time 定期脫落的：deciduous trees 落葉林   occident [oc-（ob-）=down 下；cid=to fall 降落；-ent n.=thing connected with 表相關事物→ 「the direction towards which the heavenly bodies were supposed to fall down 前人認為的天體 降落的方向」→] n.１ the west 西方２ the western hemisphere 西半球：the Occident 亞洲以 西的全部國家；歐洲；歐美  ▽occidental [occident;-al a.] a.西方的   decay [de-=down 下；cay（cad 的變形）=to fall 降→] v. fall down from a state of health and excellence;rot 衰退；腐朽：The old man's teeth are all decayed.這老人的牙齒全壞了。	
11. cap, capt, cept, ceive [L]=	to take 取 這是一組形態變化比較複雜，孳生能力又很強的詞根。cap 來自拉丁動詞capere，意為to take （取），capt，cept 來自它的過去分詞。由於該族同根詞多由法語引入英語，因此又多了一 個帶法語痕跡的變體ceive。先介紹幾個由cap，capt 構成的派生詞。   capable [cap=to take 取；-able a.=able 能……的→「able to take 能取到的」→] a. able;talented 有能力的；有才能的：capable teachers 能幹的教師  ▽capability [capab(le);-ility n.] n.能力，才能，技能   capacious [cap=to take or hold 取，抓；-acious (-ac +-ious) a.=having the nature 有……性能的 →「having the nature of holding 能容納的」→] a. able to hold much 容量大的：capacious stage 寬敞的戲台  ▽capacity [cap;-ac;-ity n.] n.容量，容積；可容性，可能性   capture [capt=to take 取；-ure n.=the result 表結果→「the result of being taken or catched 被奪 取的結果」→]Ⅰn. person or thing seized 俘虜，捕獲物：The lion became their capture.那隻獅 子成為他們的獵物。→Ⅱv. take as a prize by force 捕獲：to capture butterflies with a net 用網 捕捉蝴蝶  ▽capturer [captur(e);-er n.] n.捕獲者 capturable [captur(e);-able a.] a.可捕獲的   captive [capt=to take 取；-ive a.=being...被……的→「being taken 被抓的」→]Ⅰa. taken or made a prisoner 被俘虜的：captive birds 籠中之鳥→Ⅱ n. a person or animal captured 俘虜；獵獲物： The captives were sold as slaves.俘虜被販賣為奴。  ▽captivity [captiv(e) a.;-ity n.] n.囚虜；監禁（期）；羈絆 captivate [captiv(e) a.;-ate v.] v. [古]捕獲；迷惑，蠱惑   ceive 用來構成動詞，其對應的名詞和形容詞多由cept 構成。  receive [re-=back 回；ceive=to take 取→「to take back 取回」→] v.１ get or accept 收到，收 受：It is more blessed to give than to receive.施惠比收受更好。２ allow to enter 容納，接待： to receive the guests warmly 熱情接待客人  ▽receiver [receiv(e);-er n.] n.收受者；聽筒；接收機 reception [re-;cept;-ion n.] n.接待；歡迎；接受，容納 receptive [re-;cept;-ive a.] a.能容納的；可接受的   deceive [de-=away 離；ceive=to take 取→「to take somebody away from what is true 帶某人離 開真相」→] v. cause to believe what is false 欺騙，蒙蔽：Deceive boys with toys, but men with oaths.用玩具騙小孩，用誓言騙大人。  ▽deceiver [deceiv(e);-er n.] n.欺騙者，騙子 deception [de-;cept;-ion n.] n.欺騙，蒙蔽；騙人的東西 deceptive [de-;cept;-ive a.] a.騙人的；容易使人上當的   conceive [con-=in 入；ceive=to take 取→「to take in 取進，吸收」→] v.１ become pregnant 懷（胎）：to conceive a child 懷孕２ form in the mind 構想，設想：I can't conceive why you said so.我想不出你為什麼這樣說。  ▽conceivable [conceiv(e);-able a.] a.可想到的，可想像的 conception [con-;cept;-ion n.] n.概念；構想，設想；懷孕 conceptive [con-;cept;-ive a.] a.有構想力的；構想的 conceptual [con-;cept;-ual a.] a.概念的；概念藝術的   perceive [per-=thoroughly 完全；ceive=to take or grasp 握→「to grasp thoroughly 完全掌握」 →] v. grasp through the senses 感覺，察覺：She perceived a faint aroma.她聞出一種淡淡的香 味。  ▽perceivable [perceiv(e);-able a.] a.可感知的；有洞察力的 perception [per-;cept;-ion n.] n.感知，感覺；察覺 perceptive [per-;cept;-ive a.] a.感知的；有洞察力的 perceptual [per-;cept;-ual a.] a.感知的；[心]知覺的 perceptible [per-;cept;-ibe a.] a.可感知的；可察覺的   以下幾組同根詞均由cept 構成，請注意其構詞規律。   except [ex-=out 出；cept=to take 取→「to take out 取出，排除」→]Ⅰv. leave out or exclude 把……除外：She was excepted from the short list.她被排除在首選名單之外。Ⅱprep. but not 除……外：He works every day except Sunday.除了星期天，他天天幹活。  ▽exception [except v.;-ion n.] n.除外，例外；異議，反對 exceptive [except v.;-ive a.] a.例外的，除外的，特殊的 exceptious [except v.;-ious a.] a.好提異議的，喜歡反對的   incept [in-=in 在……中；cept=to take 取→「to take in hand 取在手中」→] v.１ begin 開始： The party incepted 80 years ago.該黨成立於80 年前。２ complete the taking of a degree 取得 學位：to incept one's MA 取得碩士學位  ▽inception [incept;-ion n.] n.開始，初期；學位授予典禮 inceptive [incept;-ive a.] a.開始的，最初的   intercept [inter-=between 在……之間；cept=to take 取→「to take between 在中途取得」→] v. seize or stop on the way 攔截，截住：The drug shipment was intercepted at the airport.那批毒 品在機場被截獲了。  ▽interception [intercept;-ion n.] n.攔截；截擊；竊聽   precept [pre-=before 在……之前；cept=to take 取→「words taken before an action 行動前應 記取的話」→] n. a rule of action or behaviour;maxim 規矩，戒律；箴言：Example is better than precept.身教重於言傳。  ▽perceptive [per-;cept;-ive a.] a.規誡的，訓誡的；規定的   susceptible [sus-(sub-)=(up from) under 自下而上；cept=to take 取；-ible=able to be 可被…… 的→「able to be taken up 可被佔取的」→] a.１easily affected by 易受影響的：He is susceptible to suggestion.他沒有主見。２easily influenced by feelings 易受感動的，多情的：susceptible girls 多情少女  ▽susceptibility [susceptib(le);-ility n.] n.敏感性；多情 hypersusceptible [hyper-;susceptible a.] a.過敏的   cap 還有一個異體cip，以下是cip 的幾個主要的派生詞。  anticipate [anti-(ante-)=before 前；cip=to take 取；-ate v.→「to take before or realize before 先 取，先實現」→] v.１ do before others do 先於……做成：The Chinese anticipated the European in discovery of gunpowder.中國人在歐洲人之前發現了火藥。２ consider in advance預先考慮， 預見：Our hotel anticipates your every need.本賓館預先考慮到您的各種需要。３ expect 期望， 期待：We anticipate a good time at the party.我們期待著晚會上的愉快時光。  ▽anticipation [anticipat(e);-ion n.] n.期望；預期；先發制人 anticipative [anticipat(e);-ive a.] a.預期的；先發制人的   principal [prin=first 首位；cip=to take 取；-al a.=of……的→「of taking first 佔取首位的」→] Ⅰa. most important;chief 首要的；主要的：principal city 首府→Ⅱ n. the chief person or head 首長：the principal of school 校長   participate [part=part 份兒，角色；-i-;cip=to take 取；-ate v.→] v. take part or partake 參加，參 與：The teacher participated in the chil-dren's games.教師參加了孩子們的遊戲。  ▽participation [participat(e);-ion n.] n.參與，參加；分享 participator [participat(e);-or n.] n.參與者；分享者   emancipate [e-(ex-)=out 出；man=hand 手；cip=take 取；-ate v.→「to take out of one's hand 從某人手中取出」→] v. set free or release 解放，使不受束縛：Lincoln emancipated the slaves on Jan. 1st, 1863.林肯於1863 年1 月1 日解放了奴隸。  ▽emancipation [emancipat(e);-ion n.] n.解放；無拘束 emancipator [emancipat(e);-or n.] n.解放者	
12. ced, ceed, cess [L]=	to go 走 ced，ceed，cess 是同源異形根，來自拉丁動詞cedere，意為to go（走）。其中，ced 是不定 式詞干；ceed 是ced 在英語中的音變形式，它在英語中只有proceed，succeed 和exceed 三 個原生派生詞；cess 是動名詞詞干，用來組成與某些動詞相應的名詞或形容詞。   antecedent [ante-=before 在……前；ced=to go 走；-ent a.=-ing……的→] a. going before 先行 的，居先的：The Ming Dynasty was antecedent to the Ching Dynasty.明朝在清朝之前。  ▽antecedence [ante-;ced;-ence n.] n.先行；居先   antecessor [ante-=before 前；cess=to go 走；-or n.=person 人→] n. person who goes before the others 先行者；先驅者：antecessors of the times 時代的先行者 proceed [pro-=forward 向前；ceed=to go 行走→] v.１ go forward 前進，進行：The talk proceeded in a friendly atmosphere.會談在友好的氣氛中進行。２ go forward after a stop, or continue 繼 續：Let's proceed to the next item on the agenda.讓我們進入下一項議程。  ▽proceeding [proceed;-ing n.] n.程序；[複數] 會議記錄   procedure [pro-=forward 向前；ced=to go 行走；-ure n.=the manner 表方式→「the manner of going forward 前行的方式」→] n. course of action 過程，程序：legal procedure 法律程序  ▽procedural [procedur(e);-al a.] a.過程的，程序的   process [pro-=forward 向前；cess=to go→going 行走→「going forward 前進運動」→] n. forward movement 過程，進程：the process of history 歷史的進程  ▽procession [pro-;cess;-ion n.] n.隊伍行進；行列   succeed [suc-(sub-)=from under 自下而上；ceed=to go 行走→「to go from under（to a higher position）上升到較高位置」→] v.１ take the place previously occupied 繼承，接替：A new cabinet succeeded the old one.新內閣接任了。２reach one's aim 成功，成就：He succeeded in everything.他事事如意。  ▽succession [succeed１的對應名詞] n.繼承；連續 successive [succeed１的對應形容詞] a.相繼的；連續的 success [succeed２的對應名詞] n.成就；成功   accede [ac-(ad-)=to 到；ced=to go 走；-e→「to go to an office 走馬上任」→] v. enter 13. centr [GK→L]=	the middle point 中心 常用詞centre，central，centric 和concentrate 的共同成分是centr。它是隨著法語進入英語 的拉丁化的希臘詞。遠祖是希臘名詞kentron，意為sharp point（尖端）。kentron 的拉丁化 形式是cenrtum，因為「尖端點」的概念與「中心點」緊密相連，所以又添上the middle point （中心）的含義。不妨說centr 相當於the middle point，或者等於它在英語中的替身——center （中心）。   centre [centr=the middle point 中心點；-e→] n. the middle point of any-thing 中心點，中心/the center of a circle 圓心   central [centr=the middle point 中心點；-al a.=of……的→] a.１ of the middle point;belonging to the center 中心的；中央的/the central com-mittee 中央委員會２ principal;dominate 主要的； 支配的/the central idea of an article 文章的主題思想  ▽centralism [central;-ism n.] n.集中制；中央集權制 centrality [central;-ity n.] n.中心性；中心地位 centralize [central;-ize v.] v.形成中心；使集中   decentralize [de-=to undo 表示相反行為；centralize v.使集中→「to undo that of centralizing 取 消集中」→] v. １ do away with centralization of 廢棄中央集權２ distribute（powers）among local governments 分權於地方政府/decentralized management 分散經營  ▽decentralization [decentraliz(e);-ation n.] n.分散；地方分權   centric [centr=the middle point 中心點；-ic a.=having 有……的→] a. having a center; belonging to the center 有中心的；中心的/ centric position 中心位置  ▽centricity [centric;-ity n.] n.中心性   concentrate [con- (com)=together 共；centr=center 中心；-ate v.=to cause to be 使→to cause to be together in the center 使共處於中心→ ] v. bring together to one point 集中/You should concentrate yourself on your studies.你要專心學習。  ▽concentration [concentrat(e);-ion n.] n.集中；專心 concentrator [concentrat(e);-or n.] n.集中者；專業研究者   concentric [con-=together 共同；centr=cenrte 中心；-ic a.=having 有……的→] a. having a common center 同心的/concentric circles 同心圓  ▽concentricity [concentric;-ity n.] n.同心；同心度   eccentric [ec-=from 離；centr=center 中心；-ic a.=being……的→「being away from the center 離開中心的」→] I a. not concentric;not having the axis placed centrally 離心的；偏心的/eccentric circles 偏心圓→II n. odd person 行為古怪的人  ▽eccentricity [eccentric a.;-ity n.] n.偏心率；離心率   centrifugal [centr=center 中心；-i-;fug=to flee 逃；-al a.=of……的→「of fleeing the center 逃離 中心的」→] a. moving from the center 離心的/centrifugal machine 離心機  ▽centrifugalize [centrifugal;-ize v.] v.使受離心機的作用   centripetal [centr=center 中心；-i-;pet=to seek after 趨向；-al a.=of……的→「of seeking after the center 趨向中心的」→] a. moving towards the center 向心的/centripetal force 向心力	
14. cern, cret [L]=	to separate 分離 cern 和cret 是一對同源異形根，來自拉丁動詞cernere，意思相當於to separate（分離，區 分）。cern 是不定式詞干，常用來構成動詞，cret 是動名詞詞干，多出現於名詞或形容詞。   concern [con-(com-)=thoroughly 徹底地；cern=to separate 區分→「to separate thoroughly in the mind 心裡區分得一清二楚」→「to interest oneself very much 非常感興趣」→] I v. １ involve or worry（oneself）關心；牽掛：to concern oneself with the state affairs 關心國家大事２relate to;affect 與……有關；影響：The policy concerns the life of the people.該政策關係到人民的生 活。→Ⅱn. the act or state of concerning 關心；關係：He showed much concern for me.他很關 心我。  ▽concernment [ concern v.１;-ment n.] n.關心的事；掛念 concerned [concern v.２;-ed a.] a.有關的   discern [dis-=apart 離開；cern=to separate 區分→「to separate apart 區分開來」→] v.１ recognize;make out 認出；辨別：to discern the truth from the false 辨別真假２ perceive 覺察： to discern a strange odour 聞到一種怪味  ▽discernment [discern;-ment n.] n.識別；明辨；見識 discernible [discern;-ible a.] a.看得清的；辨得出的   secret [se-=apart 離開；cret=to separate 分隔→「being separated apart from the knowledge of others 被分隔開不為他人所知的」→] I a. concealed 秘密的：a secret treaty 秘密條約→Ⅱn. something secret 秘密的事物：open secrets 公開的秘密  ▽secrecy [secre(t);-cy n.] n.秘密；秘密狀態   secretary [secret n. 秘密的事物；-ary n.=person 人→「person related to secrets 與機密相關的 人」→] n. person who handles secret records, papers, etc. for his owner 秘書：private secretary 私人秘書  ▽secretariat [secretar(y);-iat n.] n.秘書處；書記處 secretarial [secretar(y);-ial a.] 相異的：Modesty and coyness are two discrete qualities.謙虛有節與忸怩作態是兩碼事。  ▽discretion2 [discret(e);-ion n.] n.離散；分立；不連續   secrete1 [se-=apart 離；cret=to separate 分離；-e→「to separate oneself apart from others 使 自己與他人相隔離」→] v. conceal, or hide 藏匿：He secreted himself in a cave.他藏在洞裡。  ▽secretion1 [secret(e);-ion n.] n.隱藏；藏匿 secretive [secret(e);-ive a.] a.愛遮遮掩掩的   secrete2 [se-=apart 離；cret=to separate 15. cid, cis [L]=	to cut 切 cid 和cis 是一對同源異形根，來自拉丁動詞caedere，意為to cut（切）。cid 是不定式詞干， cis 是動名詞詞干。   decide [de-=away 離；cid=to cut 切；-e→「to cut away 切掉」→「to cut short and bring an end to something 16. claim, clam [L]=	to call out 喊 claim 和clam 都源於拉丁動詞clamare，意為to call out 或to shout（喊叫）。claim 是不定式 詞干在英語中的重讀形式，用來構成動詞；clam 是動名詞詞干，只出現於相應的名詞和形 容詞中。   claim [claim=to call out 呼喊→「to speak loudly for one's own interest 為自己的利益而呼喊」 →] v. demand as one's due or property 要求；索取：We have claimed compensation for the losses from the foreign company.我們已向外國公司提出索賠要求。  ▽claimer [claim;-er n.] n.根據權利提出要求者 claimable [claim;-able a.] a.可要求的；可認領的   disclaim [dis-=to undo 做相反之事；claim v. 要求，索取→「to undo that of claiming 做與要求 或索取相反的事」→] v. deny;disavow 否認；抵賴：He disclaimed his responsibility for the accident.他否認自己對事故負有責任。  ▽disclaimer [disclaim;-er n.] n.否認者   declaim [de-=completely 完全地；claim=to call out 叫喊→「to call out or speak loudly 喊話；大 聲說話」→] v. give a formal speech 演講：The candidates declaimed against the government. 競 選人發表演說責難政府。  ▽declaimer [declaim;-er n.] n.演講者；朗誦者   declamation [declaim 的對應名詞：declam=to declaim 演講；-ation n.=the act 表行為→] n.１ the act or art of declaiming 演講； 雄辯術２ formal speech 正式演說： to deliver a long declamation 發表長篇演說   declamatory [declaim 的對應形容詞：declam=to declaim 演說；-atory a.=characterized by 有…… 特點的→ ] a. １ characterized by declaiming 演說的２ bombastic 誇誇其談的： long and declamatory speech 誇誇其談的長篇大論   exclaim [ex-=out 出；claim=to call or shout 喊→「to call or shout out 喊出來」→] v. cry out suddenly from pain, anger, surprise, etc.驚叫；驚歎：「Help! Help!」she exclaimed.她大聲驚叫： 「快來人呀！救命呀！」  ▽exclamation [ex-;clam;-ation n.] n.呼喊；驚歎   proclaim [pro-=forward 向前；claim=to cry out 呼喊→「to call or speak forward（before the public）向前面的公眾講話」→] v. make known before the public;declare or announce officially 宣佈；公告：to proclaim a new law 公佈一項新法令  ▽proclamation [pro-;clam;-ation n.] n.宣佈；公告   reclaim [re-=back 回；claim=to call 呼喚→ 「to call back (from vice, error, savagery or waste condition) (從罪惡、錯誤或荒廢狀態)召喚回來」→] v. １ reform;civilize 改造；感化：We reclaimed him from vice.我們使他改惡從善。２ bring under cultivation 墾荒：to reclaim fields from wasteland 開荒造田  ▽reclaimable [reclaim;-able a.] a.可改造的；可開墾的 reclaimant [reclaim;-ant n.] n.開墾者；糾正者 reclamation [re-;clam;-ation n.] n.開墾；感化   acclaim [ac-(ad-)=to 對；claim=to call out 呼喊→「to call out cheerfully to somebody 高興地向 某人呼喊」→] v. hail or praise publicly 歡呼；稱讚：His play was acclaimed as a masterpiece. 他的劇本被讚許為傑作。  ▽acclamation [ac-;clam;-ation n.] n.歡呼；稱讚   clamour [clam=to shout 叫喊；-our n.=the state 表狀態→「the state of shouting 叫喊的狀態」 →] n.１ shout or outcry for demand, appeal, etc.叫喊；呼聲：A clamour of protest went up from the masses.群眾發出了抗議的呼聲。２noise made by shouting 吵鬧聲，喧嚷：The clamour of the traffic gave me a headache.車馬喧鬧，叫人頭痛。	
17. clud, clus [L]=	to shut or close 關閉 clud 和clus 是一對同源異形根，詞源是拉丁動詞claudere，意思相當於to shut（關閉）。clud 來自不定式詞干claud，常見於英語動詞；clus 來自動名詞詞干claus，多見於相應的名詞和 形容詞。   conclude [con-(com-)=thoroughly 完全地；clud=to shut 關閉；-e→「to shut off thoroughly so as to bring to an end 完全關閉，使之結束」→] v.１ finish 結束：She concluded her speech.她結 束了發言。２ settle or decide 決定；斷定：The judge concluded that he was guilty.法官判定他 有罪。   conclusion [conclude 的對應名詞：conclus=to conclude 結束，決定；-ion n.=the act or result 表行為或結果→「the act or result of concluding 結束，決定的行為或結果」→] n.１ end 結束； 結局：to come to a conclusion 告終２final outcome or decision 結論：to draw a conclusion from facts 從事實得出結論   conclusive [conclude 的對應形容詞：conclus=to conclude 結束，決定；-ive a.=characterized by 有……特點的→「characterized by concluding 帶有結束或結論特點的」→] a.１ final 最後的： conclusive decision 最後的決定２ convincing 確定性的：conclusive evidence 確鑿的證據３ decisive 結論性的：a conclusive ruling by the judge 法官的裁決   include [in-=in 內；clud=to shut 關閉；-e→「to shut in 關閉在內」→] v.１ contain, or enclose 包含；包住：The nutshell includes the kernel.果殼包住果仁。２ comprise as a part 包括：The freight is included.運費包括在內。  ▽includable [includ(e);-able a.] a.可包括在內的 inclusive [in-;clus;-ive a.] a.包圍住的；包括的   exclude [ex-=out 外；clud=to shut 關閉；-e→「to shut out 關在外面」] v.１ keep from entering;bar 排除在外；排斥：The club excluded him from membership.俱樂部拒絕吸收他。２ expel 逐出： An officer was excluded from his position.一個官員被撤職了。  ▽excludable [exclud(e);-able a.] a.可除外的 exclusive [ex-;clus;-ive a.] a.排他的；唯一的   preclude [pre-=beforehand 事先；clud=to shut 關閉；-e→「to shut beforehand in order to keep out 事先關閉不讓進入」→] v.１ prevent 免除，預防：She explained it in detail so as to preclude all doubts.她對此詳加說明，以免產生各種疑慮。２ make impracticable 阻礙：A prior engagement will preclude me from coming.另有約會在先，我無法前來。  ▽preclusive [pre-;clus;-ive a.] a.預防性的；妨礙的   seclude [se-=apart 分離；clud=to shut 關閉；-e→「to shut oneself apart from others 自我關閉， 與他人隔離」→] v. shut off from association or influence outside 隱居：He almost secludes himself from the society.他幾乎與世隔絕。  ▽seclusive [se-;clus;-ive a.] a.隱居性的；愛隱居的   occlude [oc-(ob-)=against 對抗；clud=to shut 關閉；-e→「to shut against going through 關住不 讓通過」→] v. stop up, or obstruct 堵塞；閉塞：His imagination was occluded by something.某 件事情阻斷了他的思路。  ▽occlusive [oc-;clus;-ive a.] a.閉塞的   recluse [re-=back 退；clus=to shut 關閉；-e→「being shut back or away（from active social life） 被關在世外的，退居世外的」→] I. a. retired;secluded 退居林下的；隱居的：a recluse monk 隱居的和尚→Ⅱn. one who lives in a recluse way 隱居者  ▽reclusion [re-;clus;-ion n.] n.隱居；遁世 reclusive [re-;clus;-ive a.] a.隱居的；遁世的	
18. cord [L]=	heart 心 常用詞accord，concord，discord 和record 等，都以詞根cord 為基礎。cord 源於拉丁名詞 cor 的屬格（即所有格）形式cordis 的詞幹部分，意義等於英語基本詞heart（心）。   accord [ac-(ad-)=towards 向；cord=heart 心→「a heart towards another heart 心心相向」→] I n. agreement, or harmony 一致；和諧：Our opinions are in accord.我們的意見一致。→Ⅱv. be of one heart, or agree 與……一致：His opinions accord with mine.他與我觀點一致。  ▽accordance [accord;-ance n.] n.一致 accordant [accord;-ant a.] a.一致的 according (to) [accord;-ing a.] a.與……一致的；根據……   concord [con-(com-)=together 共同；cord=heart 心→「a heart together with another 心心與共」 →] n. the state of having the same heart, or agreement, or harmony 同心；一致；和諧：The old couple live in concord.這對老夫妻相親相愛。  ▽concordance [corcord;-ance n.] n.和諧；一致 concordant [concord;-ant a.] a.和諧的；一致的   discord [dis-=apart 離； cord=heart 心→ 「 a heart apart from another 心心相離」 → ] I n. disagreement, or opposition of views 不一致；不和：The couple split up after years of discord. 吵了幾年，這對夫妻分手了。→Ⅱv. disagree, or quarrel 不和；爭吵：They often discord with each other.他們經常鬧矛盾。  ▽discordance [discord;-ance n.] n.不和；爭吵 discordant [discord;-ant a.] a.不和的；爭吵的   record [re-=back 回；cord=heart 心→「back in the heart 回到心裡」→「to put in the heart again, as by writing it down 記下來以便回憶」→] I v. write down in permanent form 記錄，記載：A great event like this should be recorded.這樣的大事應該記錄下來。→Ⅱn. recorded permanent account 記錄，記載：original records 原始記錄材料  ▽recordable [record;-able a.] a.可記錄的 recorder [record;-er n.] n.錄音機；記錄員 recordist [record;-ist n.] n.錄音員   cordial [cord=heart 心；-i-; -al a.=pertaining to……的→「pertaining to one's heart 內心的」→] a. hearty or sincere 衷心的；誠心的：cordial congratulations 衷心的祝賀  ▽cordiality [cordial;-ity n.] n.熱誠，誠心   cordiform [cord=heart 心；-i-;form n.=having the shape 有……形狀的→] a. having the shape like a heart 心形的：a cordiform leaf 心形葉片   obcordate [ob-=reversed 倒轉的；cord=heart 心；-ate a.=having 有……性質的→] a. having the shape like a reversed heart 倒心形的：an obcordate leaf 倒心形的葉片	
19. cresc, cret, cre [L]=	to grow 生長 常用詞crescent，increase，create 和concrete，表面看來似乎關係不大，其實是同根生的。 它們的詞幹部分cresc，cret 和cre 是一組同源異形根，都來自拉丁動詞crescere，意為to grow （生長）。其中，cresc 是不定式詞干；cret 是動名詞詞干；cre 是cret 在添加後綴時的變形。   crescent [cresc=to grow 生長，變化；-ent n.=the state 表行為狀態→「the growing state（of the moon）（月亮）變化的狀態」→] n.１ the visible part of the quarter moon which is growing larger or smaller 月牙２ any object like a crescent 月牙形的東西/The national emblem of Turkey is a crescent.土耳其的國徽是個月牙。   increase [in-=into 成；creas（cresc 的重讀式）=to grow 生長；-e→] I v. grow into a larger amount;become greater or larger 增長；增加；增大：The production increases with years. 生 產逐年增長。→Ⅱn. growth 增長：the rate of increase 增長率   create [cre=to grow 生長；-ate v.=to make 使……→「to make to grow into shape 使生長成形」 →] v. make something exist 創造：to create more jobs 創造更多的就業機會  ▽creation [creat(e);-ion n.] n.創造；創作；（大寫）創世 creator [creat(e);-or n.] n. 創造者；創始者；（大寫）造物主creature [creat(e);-ure n.] n.創造 物；生物；動物 creative [creat(e);-ive a.] a.有創造力的；創造性的；創作的   concrete [con-=together 一起；cret=to grow 生長；-e→「to grow or stick together 長在一起或 結成一塊」→] I v. solidify or harden 凝固；固結：The sands concreted into a mass. 沙土結成 塊。→Ⅱa. relating to a solidified thing; particular; real 固定有形的；具體的；實際的：a concrete problem 具體問題III n. any mass of solidified particles, especially used in building 混凝土： reinforced concrete 鋼筋混凝土  ▽concretion [concret(e) v.;-ion n.] n.凝固；凝固物 concretive [concret(e) v.;-ive a.] a.凝結性的   decrease [de-=downward 向下；creas=to grow 生成，變化；-e→「to grow downward 向下變 化」→] I v. become less, or make less 減少；使變少：Water comsumption decreased.耗水量降 低了。→Ⅱn. reduction 減少；減少量：A big decrease in sales caused the supermarket to close. 銷售量銳減使得超市關了門。   increment [in-=into 成；cre=to grow 生長；-ment n.=the result 表行為結果→「the result of growing into a larger amount 數量增長的結果」→] n. the amount of increase 增加量：monthly increments 月增加額  ▽incremental [increment;-al a.] a.增加的；增值的   increscent [in-=into 成；cresc=to grow 生長；-ent a.=-ing 有……特徵的→「growing into（the full moon）長成（滿月）的」→] a. waxing of the moon（月亮）漸盈的：an increscent moon 盈 月   accretion [ac（- ad-）=to 向；cret=to grow 生長；-ion n.=the act or state 表動作或狀態→「growing to 向……生長」→] n.１ continued growth 生長；增大：the accretion of cancer 腫瘤增大２ growing of parts into each other 合生，連生：accretion of two kinds of plants 兩種植物的合生 現象   excrescence [ex-=out 出；cresc=to grow 生長；-ence n.=the result 表行為結果→「growing or growth which is out of the normal state 超出正常狀態的生長物」→] n. １ abnormal outgrowth 贅生物，瘤：an excresence on the neck 脖子上的瘤２ superfluous part 累贅，多餘物：This tree is an excrescence in the painting.這棵樹在畫中是多餘的。  ▽excrescent [ex-;cresc;-ent a.] a.贅生的；多餘的	
20. cub, cumb [L]=	to lie down 躺 常用詞incumbent，succumb，concubine 和incubate 是一組同根詞。詞根cub 來自拉丁動詞 cubare，詞根cumb 來自拉丁動詞cumbere；而cumbere 和cubare 實際上是同一個詞的異體， 意思都相當於英語的to lie down（躺，臥）。   incumbent [in-=upon 在……之上；cumb=to lie down 躺；-ent a.=-ing……的→「lying upon somebody 躺在或賦予某人身上的」→] I a. lying or resting on（somebody）as an obligation 作 為責任的：It is incumbent on you to warn them.你有責任告誡他們。→Ⅱn. person on whom an obligation lies;one who holds public office 負有責任者；任公職者：the struggle between the incumbents and the candidates 現任者與候選人之間的鬥爭  ▽incumbency [in-;cumb;-ency n.] n.責任；任職；職權   succumb [suc（- sub-）=under 在……之下；cumb=to lie down 躺倒→「to lie down under pressure, illness etc.在壓力、疾病等之下躺倒」→] v.１ give way;yield 讓步，屈服：We will not succumb to difficulties.我們決不向困難低頭。２ die 死：He succumbed to cancer.他死於癌症。   concubine [con-=together 共同；cub=to lie down 臥；-ine n.=female 女人→「woman who lies down together with a man 與某男人同臥共宿的女人」→] n. woman who inhabits with a man without being married 姘婦，情婦  ▽concubinage [concubin(e);-age n.] n.情婦身份；非法同居   incubate [in-=on 在……上；cub=to lie 臥；-ate v.=to cause 使……→「to cause (a hen, etc.) to lie on eggs 使（母雞等）臥在卵上」→] v.１sit on eggs in order to hatch them 孵卵，孵化：Even a good hen can't incubate a wooden egg.母雞再好也孵不了木頭蛋。２ give form to;develop 把……醞釀成熟；使發展：to incubate a plan 醞釀一個計劃  ▽incubation [incubat(e);-ion n.] n.孵化；醞釀 incubator [incubat(e);-or n.] n.孵化器 incubative [incubat(e);-ive a.] a.孵卵的；潛伏期的   incubus [in-=upon 在……之上；cub=to lie down 臥；-us n.=thing 物→「thing inclined to lie down upon a person 喜歡臥在人的身上的東西」→] n. evil spirit supposed to lie down upon sleeping persons;nightmare 壓在睡眠者身上的惡魔；夢魔：The debt is like an incubus on me.這筆債務 使我夢寐不安。   cubicle [cub=to lie 躺；-icle n.=small thing 小東西→「small room for lying down 供躺下歇息的 小房間」→] n.１ small bedroom 小臥室２ any small room 小室  ▽cubicular [cub;-icular a.] a.寢室的   recumbent [re-=backward 向後；cumb=to lie 躺；-ent a.=-ing……的→] a. lying backward;reclining 躺著的；斜臥的：recumbent statue 雕塑的臥像  ▽recumbency [recumben(t);-cy n.] n.斜臥；依靠   procumbent [pro-=forward 向前；cumb=to lie 躺；-ent a.=-ing……的→「lying forward 向前臥 著的」→] a. leaning forward;prostrate;prone 前俯的；平臥的；爬在地下的：The man fell procumbent on the ground.那個人摔了個嘴啃泥。	
21. cult [L]=	to till 耕作 在culture，cultivate，agriculture 等常用詞中，包含著一個很重要的詞根cult，它是拉丁動詞 colere 的動名詞詞干（這個動詞的不定式詞干col 在英語中的派生詞很少，例詞見練習第4 題）。colere 的意思包含了古代社會的三種基本的社會活動：居住、耕作、敬神。所以，可 以用三個英語動詞來表示它的意思：inhabit，till 和worship。相應地，詞根cult 也包含了這 三種意思，但是主要意思是to till（耕作，栽培）。   cult [cult=to worship 崇拜→] n. system of formal worship or religious belief 禮拜；迷信：the cult of personality 個人崇拜  ▽cultism [cult;-ism n.] n.崇拜；迷信 cultist [cult;-ist n.] n.熱衷於搞迷信崇拜的人   cultivate [cult=to till 耕作；-iv(e)；-ate v.=to make capable of 使能……→「to make capable of being tilled 使能用來耕種」→] v. １ make arable land;produce by tillage 耕作；栽培：to cultivate the soil 耕地２ improve;develop 改進；培養：to cultivate the habit of analysis 養成分 析的習慣  ▽cultivation [cultivat(e);-ion n.] n.耕作；培養；教養 cultivatable [cultivat(e);-able a.] a.可耕作的；可培養的   culture [cult=to till 耕作，栽培；-ure n.=the act or result 表示行為或結果→「tilling or the result of tilling 耕作或栽培的結果」→] n.１ tillage 耕作２ cultivation 培養：moral culture 德育３ improvement by physical or mental training 教養：a man of considerable culture 文化修養高的 人４ special form or stage of civilization 文化；文明：the ancient culture 古代文化  ▽cultural [cultur(e);-al a.] a.文化的；教養的   -culture 常作為合詞成分與其他詞根構詞，表示cultivation（栽培；培養）的意思。   agriculture [agri=field 田地；-culture=cultivation 栽培→「cultivation about fields 田地上的栽 培術」→] n. the science or practice of cultivating the soil and rearing animals 農學；農藝；農業  ▽agricultural [agricultur(e);-al a.] a.農業的；農藝的；農學的 agriculturist [agricultur(e);-ist n.] n.農學家   apiculture [api(apis)=bee 蜂；-culture=cultivation 培養→] n. cultivation of bee;bee-keeping 養蜂 業；養蜂  ▽apicultural [apicultur(e);-al a.] a.養蜂的 apiculturist [apicultur(e);-ist n.] n.養蜂專家   aquaculture [aqua=water 水；-culture=cultivation 培養→] n. cultivation of plans or breeding of animals in water 水產養殖  ▽aquacultural [aquacultur(e);-al a.] a.水產養殖的 aquaculturist [aquacultur(e);-ist n.] n.水產養殖專家   floriculture [flori (floris)=flower 花；-culture=cultivation 栽培→] n. cultivation of flowers 養花； 花卉栽培術  ▽floricultural [floricultur(e);-al a.] a.養花的；花卉栽培的 floriculturist [floricultur(e);-ist n.] n.花匠；花卉栽培專家   pisciculture [pisci (piscis)=fish 魚； -culture=cultivation 培養→ ] n. cultiva-tion of fish;artificial rearing of fish 魚類養殖  ▽piscicultural [piscicultur(e);-al a.] a.養魚的；養魚術的 pisciculturist [piscicultur(e);-ist n.] n.養魚專家	
22. cur(r), curs, cours [L]=	to run 跑 cur(r)，curs，cours 都來源於拉丁動詞currere，意思相當於英語的to run（跑）。其中，cur(r) 來自不定式詞干curr；curs 是動名詞詞干；cours 是curs 的重讀形式。在構詞中，cur(r) 用 來構成動詞；curs 和cours 一般只出現於名詞和形容詞中。先介紹幾個常見的cur(r) 的派生 詞。   occur [oc-(ob-)=towards 向；cur=to run 跑→「to run towards 向……跑來」→] v.１ come about 出現：These animals occur in Africa only.這些動物只出現在非洲。２ happen 發生：Don't let such accidents occur again.別讓這類事情再發生了。  ▽occurrence [occur(r);-ence n.] n.出現；發生 occurrent [occur(r);-ent a.] a.目前正發生的；偶然發生的   current [curr=to run 跑；-ent a.=-ing……的→「running 跑動的，流動的」→] I a. running along with the times 流行的：the current mode 流行式樣；→Ⅱn. the running of water, electricity, etc. 水流；電流等：the main current 主流   recur [re-=back, again 回，復；cur=to run 跑→「to run back again 又跑回來」→] v. come upon or happen again 重來；復發：His illness recurred.他的病復發了。  ▽recurrence [recur(r);-ence n.] n.重現；復發 recurrent [recur(r);-ent a.] a.再發生的；經常發生的   concur [con-=together 一起；cur=to run 跑→「to run together 一起跑來」→] v.１happen at the same time 同時發生：Several mistakes concurred to bring about this accident.幾樁失誤同時發 生，造成了這場事故。２ agree or approve 同意；贊成：The whole class concurred with him. 全班都贊同他的意見。  ▽concurrence [concur(r);-ence n.] n.同時發生；同意；贊同   以下介紹的是幾個含curs 的常用派生詞。   cursory [curs=to run 跑；-ory a.=like 像……的→「like running or going hastily 像奔跑或疾走的」 →] a. hasty;hurried 倉猝的；草率的：He is a cursory reader.他看書一目十行，不求甚解。  ▽cursoriness [cursor(y);-ness n.] n.倉猝；草率   excursion [ex-=out of 外；curs=to run 跑；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「running out of home 離家 跑到外頭去」→] n. pleasure outing or trip 遠足，短途旅行：excursion train 旅遊列車  ▽excursionist [excursion;-ist n.] n.遠足者，短途旅行者   precursor [pre-=before 前；curs=to run 跑；-or n.=person 人→「person running before others 跑在他人前面的人」→] n. forrunner;predecessor 先行者；前輩：Kepler was the precursor of Newton.開普勒是牛頓的前輩人物。  ▽precursory [precursor;-y a.] a.先行的；前輩的 最後，再介紹幾個cours 的常見派生詞。   course [cours=to run 跑；-e→「running forward 向前的跑動」→] I n.１onward movement 行進； 進程：the course of events 事態的發展過程２ path in which anything runs or moves 道路，路 線：the course of a river 河道→Ⅱv. run; run after 跑；追：Blood courses through the veins. 血液在血管中循環流動。   discourse [dis-=away, out 離，出；cours=to run 跑；-e→「running out or outpouring（of words） （話語的）滔滔而出」→] n. speech; talk or conversation 演說；會談：a discourse on ancient Rome civilization 有關古羅馬文化的演講           recourse [re-=back 回；cours=to run 跑；-e→「running back or return 往回跑，回歸」→] n. the freedom to a return, or the right to a payment 要求歸返權；追索權：I maintain my recourse to you.我保留對你的追索權。	
23. cur [L]=	care 關心 在常用詞cure，curious，accurate，secure 中含有詞根cur，它來自拉丁名詞cura，意思相當 於care（關心，注意）。這個詞根與剛剛介紹的意為to run（跑）的詞根cur(r)形態相同。但 是，在實際構詞中，兩者除了含義不同，發音與形狀也不一樣。舉例來說，詞根cur(r)在recur， current，curriculum 等派生詞中，或者出現在重讀尾音節，發[k?:]的音，或以curr 的形式添 加後綴，發[kɑ:]或[k?]的音。現在要介紹的這個cur，一定要添加後綴構詞，發音總是[kj??]。   cure [cur=care 關心；-e→「care for the sick 對病人的關心」→] I n. means of healing;remedy 治療；治法：Scientists are working on a cure for cancer. 科學家正在研究治療癌症的方法。→ Ⅱv. relieve the sickness;make well 治療；治癒：The doctor cured him of bad cold.醫生治好了他 的重感冒。  ▽cureless [cure n.;-less a.] a.無法治療的 curable [cur(e) v.-able a.] a.可治療的 curative [cur(e) v.;-ative a.] a.治療的   curious [cur=care 關心，注意；-i-; -ous a.=causing 引起……的→「causing one's care 惹人注 意的」 →] a.１ strange;surprising 奇怪的；新奇的：a curious idea 怪念頭２ eager to learn;inquisitive 好奇的；愛打聽的：Don't be too curious about what you are not supposed to know.不要你知道的事，就不要多打聽。  ▽curiosity [curio(u)s;-ity n.] n.新奇；好奇 incurious [in-;curious a.] a.無好奇心的；沒興趣的   accurate [ac- (ad-)=to 對；cur=care 關心，注意；-ate a.=having 有……的→「having much care to 對……極為注意的」→] a. exact;without error 精確的；準確的：The answer is accurate in every detail.這個答案精確無誤。  ▽accuracy [ac-;cur;-acy n.] n.精確；準確   secure [se-=apart 離開；cur=care 關心；-e→「apart from the state of care 離開掛念狀態的」 →] I a. untroubled by danger or apprehension 無憂無慮的；安心的：She felt secure to her own future.她對未來感到放心。２ safe against attack 安全的：secure place 安全的地方→Ⅱv. cause or make safe 使安全：We must secure our supply line.我們必須保障運輸線的安全。  ▽security [secur(e) a.;-ity n.] n.安全；保護 securement [secure v.;-ment n.] n.把握；穩當性   procure [pro-=for 為；cur=care 關心；-e→「to give one's care for 為……而關心」→] v. obtain by care or effort;acquire 獲取；取得：He can procure a ticket for you.他會替你弄到一張票。  ▽procurable [procur(e);-able a.] a.可獲得的 procural [procur(e);-al n.] n.獲得；取得   curate [cur=care 關心；-ate n.=person 人→「person in charge of the care of others 負責關心他 人者」→] n. person who assists a parish priest with the care of souls 副牧師（協助牧師關心人 們靈魂的人）   curator [cur=care 關心，照料；-ator (-ate +-or) n.=person who acts 做……者→] n.１ manager or keeper 管理者２ keeper or custodian of museum, library, etc.（博物館、圖書館等）館長  ▽curatorship [curator;-ship n.] n.管理者或館長的職位或身份	
24. cycl [GK]=	circle 圓環 常用詞cycle，bicycle 和encyclopaedia 中，含有詞根cycl，它源於希臘名詞kuklos，意為circle （圓環）。cycl 多見於科技術語，一般只與希臘語源的詞根或詞綴相結合。   cycle [cycl=circle 圓環； -e → 「 a circle of time running 時間轉了一圈」 → ] n. recurrent period;period of a thing completion 循環；週期：the cycle of the seasons 季節的循環  ▽cyclic [cycl(e);-ic a.] a.週期的；循環的   bicycle [bi-=two 二；cycl=circle 圓環；-e→「two circles 兩個圓輪」→] I n. two-wheeled vehicle 兩輪腳踏車，自行車→Ⅱv. ride on a bicycle 騎自行車：to bicycle to school 騎自行車上學  ▽bicyclist [bicycl (e);-ist n.] n.騎自行車的人   unicycle [un=one 一；-i-; cycl=circle 圓環；-e→「one-circled vehicle 一個輪的車」→] n. one-wheeled vehicle used by acrobats（雜技演員用的）獨輪車   autocycle [auto-=automatic 自動；cycle=bicycle 腳踏車→] n. automatic bicycle, or bicycle with auxiliary engine 機器腳踏車   encyclopaedia [en-=in 在……之內；cycl=circle 圓圈→all directions or fields 各方面；-o-;paedia （與pacideia「教育」混淆）=education 教育→「book giving education or knowledge in all fields 提供各方面知識的書」→] n. work containing information on all branches of knowledge 百科全 書：Encyclopaedia Britannica《大不列顛百科全書》  ▽encyclopaedic [encyclopaed(ia);-ic a.] a.百科全書（式）的 encyclopaedism [encyclopaed(ia);-ism n.] n.知識淵博 encyclopaedist [encyclopaed(i);-ist n.] n.百科全書編纂者   cyclone [cycl=cicle 圓；-one n.=thing, wind 物，風→「wind in a circle 圓環狀的風」→] n. wind whirling around a low barometric center 旋風，氣旋（圍繞低氣壓中心旋轉的風）  ▽cyclonic [cyclon(e);-ic a.] a.氣旋的   hemicycle [hemi=half 半；cycl=circle 圓；-e→「half circle 半個圓」→] n. semicircular figure 半 圓形   tetracycline [tetra=four 四；cycl=circle, ring 環；-ine n.=medicine 藥→] n. medicine of four-ring compounds in which carbon atoms are linked with other atoms 四環素	
25. dem [GK]=	the people 人民 dem 源於希臘名詞demos，意思相當於the people（人民）。在添加後綴時，它常帶有連接 字母-o-，可以把demo 當作dem 的異體。   democracy [demo=the people 人民；-cracy n.=power 權力→rule or ruling body 統治，政體→ 「 rule or ruling body by the people 人民的統治或政權」 → ] n. government by all the people;society characterized by recog-nizing the equal rights of all the people 民主政權；民主社 會   democrat [demo=the people 人民；-crat n.=supportor of a government 某種政體的支持者→ 「supportor of a government by all the people 人民政權的支持者」→] n. supportor or advocate of democracy 民主主義者  ▽democratism [democrat;-ism n.] n.民主主義 democratic [democrat;-ic a.] a.民主主義的；民主政體的 democratize [democrat;-ize v.] v.使民主化   demos [demos=the people 人民→] n. the people;the populace 人民，民眾；大眾  ▽demotic [dem(os);-otic a.] a.民眾的；通俗的   demography [demo=the people 人民→the population 人口；-graphy n.=writing 著作→recording and study 記錄與研究→「the recording and study of the population 對人口的記錄與研究」→] n. the study of statistics of births, deaths, disease, etc.人口統計學  ▽demographic [demograph(y);-ic a.] a.人口統計的 demographer [demograph(y);-er n.] n.人口統計學者   demagogue [dem=the people 人民；agogue=leader 引導者→「leader of the people 民眾領袖」 →] n. political agitator appealing to desires of the mob 蠱惑民眾的政治鼓動家  ▽demagogic [demagog (ue);-ic a.] a.蠱惑的；煽動的 demagogism [demagog(ue);-ism n.] n.煽動；煽動主義 demagogy [demagog(ue);-y n.] n.煽動；煽動性宣傳   epidemic [epi-=upon 在……之上；dem=the people 民眾；-ic a.=being……的→「being upon the people 發生在民眾身上的」→] I a. prevalent among the people in a certain place at a certain time 流行性的：Polio was once an epidemic disease.小兒麻痺症曾是一種流行性傳染病。→Ⅱ n. epidemic disease 流行病：to prevent epidemics 預防流行病   endemic [en-=in 在……之中；dem=the people 人民；-ic a.=being……的→「being in the people of a certain area 存在於某個地區民眾中的」→] I a. prevalent in a particular area or nation 某地 （或某種人）特有的，地方性的：Cholera was an endemic disease in India.霍亂曾是印度特有 的地方病。→Ⅱn. disease of an endemic nature 地方性流行病；風土病：Some endemics have become epidemic diseases in the world.有些地方性疾病已變成世界性的流行病。  ▽endemicity [endemic a.;-ity n.] n.地方性；風土性   pandemic [pan-=whole 全，遍；dem=the people 人民；-ic a.=pertaining to……的→「pertaining to the whole people 涉及全民的」→] a. prevalent over the whole of a country or the whole world 流行全國（或全世界）的：a pandemic influenza 世界性流感	
26. dic, dict [L]=	to say 說 詞根dic 是拉丁動詞dicere 的不定式詞干；dict 是動名詞詞干，意思都相當於to say（說）。 在英語中，dic 的派生詞較少，dict 的派生能力卻很強。   indicate [in-=towards 對；dic=to say 說；-ate v.→「to say towards some-thing 針對某事說話」 →] v.１ point out;make known 指出；表明：The arrow indicates the direction of advance. 箭頭 指出前進方向。２ show;suggest 表示；暗示：High fever indicates severe illnesss.高燒表示病 重。  ▽indication [indicat(e);-ion n.] n.指示；象徵 indicator [indicat(e);-or n.] n.指示者；指示器 indicative [indicat(e);-ive a.] a.指示的；象徵的；陳述的   dictate [dict=to say 說→saying 話；-ate v.=to do 做→「to do a saying 做一次講話」→] v.１say or read for another to write 口述，使聽寫：He dictated a letter to the typist.他向打字員口授一封 信。２say commands 命令，支配：He will not be dictated to you.他不會聽命於你的。  ▽dictation [dictat(e);-ion n.] n.口述；聽寫   dictator [dictate(e) v.命令；-or n.=person 人→「person who dictates laws, commands, etc.發佈 法令者」→] n. absolute ruler 獨裁者，專政者：fascist dictators 法西斯獨裁者  ▽dictatorship [dictator;-ship n.] n.獨裁；專政 dictatorial [dictator;-ial a.] a.獨裁的；專政的   diction [dict=to say 說話；-ion n.=the manner 表行為方式→「the manner or art of saying 說話 的方式或藝術」→] n. choice of words and phrases in speaking 措詞，辭令：Bad diction marred the effectiveness of his speech.措詞不當削弱了他講話的效果。   dictionary [diction n. 措詞；-ary n.=thing 物→「book for diction 措詞用書」→] n. book explaining the use of words in a language 詞典，字典：an English-Chinese dictionary 英漢詞典   contradict [contra-=against 對抗；dict=to say 說→「to say against 以言相抗」→] v.１ speak against 反駁：Students may contradict their teachers.學生可以反駁教師。２ deny 否認：Don't contradict what you just testified.別否認你剛剛證實的東西。３ hold the opposite of 同……矛 盾：to contradict oneself 自相矛盾  ▽contradiction [contradict;-ion n.] n.矛盾 contradictory [contradict;-ory a.] a.矛盾的；對立的   dictum [dict=to say 說；-um n.=thing done 所做的事→「something said 有人說過的話」→] n. saying;authoritative saying 名言；格言：There is an old dictum that blood is thicker than water. 古話說，血濃於水。   edict [e-（ex-）=out from 自……而出；dict=to say 說→saying 話→「saying out from（the authorities）（當權者）發出的話」→] n. order issued by authority 法令：the king's edict 國王 的命令  ▽edictal [edict;-al a.] a.法令的   predict [pre-=beforehand 事先；dict=to say 說→「to say beforehand 事先說出」→] v. say what will happen in the future;foretell 預言；預告：The weather forecasting center predicted rain for tomorrow.氣象站預告明天有雨。  ▽prediction [predict;-ion n.] n.預言；預告 predictive [predict;-ive a.] a.預兆的   benediction [bene=good 好；dict=to speak 說；-ion n.=-ing 表行為→「good speaking 說好話」 →] n. blessing 祝福：sincere benediction 誠心的祝福  ▽benedictive [bene;dict;-ive a.] a.祝福的   malediction [male=ill, evil 壞，惡；dict=to speak 說；-ion n.=-ing 表行為→] n. evil-speaking;curse 誹謗；咒罵：irresponsible malediction 不負責任的誹謗  ▽maledictive [male;dict;-ive a.] a.誹謗的；咒罵的	
27. doc, doct [L]=	to teach 教 在常用詞doctor，document 和doctrine 中，doc 和doct 是來自拉丁動詞docere 的一對同源 異形根，意思相當於to teach（教）。   doctor [doct=to teach 教；-or n.=person 人→「person who teaches, or a learned person 為師者， 有學問的人」→] n. １ one who holds the highest degree in a certain field 博士（獲得某學科 最高學位的人）：Doctor of Science 理科博士２one who is trained and licensed to practice medicine 醫生：to go to see the doctor's 去就醫  ▽doctorate [doctor;-ate n.] n.博士頭銜；博士學位 doctoral [doctor;-al a.] a.博士的   document [doc=to teach 教； -u-;-ment n.=thing 物→ 「 thing written for teaching or giving information 用以示教的書面材料」→] n. paper or other material giving information, proof, or evidence 文件；文獻：clas-sified documents 保密文件  ▽documentary [document;-ary a./n.] a.公文的n.紀錄片documental   [document;-al a.] a.文件的；文獻的 doctrine [doctr（doct）=to teach 教；-ine n.=something done 表行為對像→「something taught 教導的內容」→] n. body of teachings orinstructions 教義；教條：Christian doctrine 基督教教 義  ▽doctrinaire [doctrin(e) n.;-aire n.] n.教條主義者 doctrinal [doctrin(e);-al a.] a.教條的   docile [doc=to teach 教；-ile a.=capable of 可……的→「capable of being taught」→] a. easy to teach, train or manage 易管教的；易馴服的；馴良的：a docile horse 一匹馴良的馬  ▽docility [docil(e);-ity n.] n.馴服；溫順   indoctrinate [in-=into 進入；doctrin(e）n.=principle 教義；-ate v.=to cause 使……→「to cause some principle or belief into one's mind 使某種教義或信仰進入頭腦」→] v. imbue;instruct in 灌 輸；教授：They often indoctrinate their children with patriotic thoughts.他們經常向孩子們灌輸 愛國思想。	
28. duc, duct [L]=	to lead 引導 常用詞conduct, educate, introduce, produce 等是同根詞。它們的詞根duc 或duct 都來自拉丁 動詞ducere，意思相當於to lead（引導）。這對詞根的孳生能力很強，其同根詞不下百個。   conduct [con-表加強詞義；duct=to lead 引導→] I n.１ leading;guidance 引導；指導：His conduct of the business is successful.他對企業的指導是有成效的。２ leading oneself to a certain result, or behaviour 行為；品行：His conduct in school is good.他在學校品行良好。→Ⅱv.１ lead or guide 引導；帶領：The mayor conducted us through the town.市長帶我們參觀了城市。２direct （oneself）為人，表現：The children conducted themselves well tonight.孩子們今晚表現得很 好。  ▽conductor [conduct v.;-or n.] n.指導者；（樂隊）指揮；導體 conductible [conduct v.;-ible a.] a.能傳導的 conductive [conduct v.;-ive a.] a.傳導性的   educate [e-（ex-）=out of 從……出來；duc=to lead 引導；-ate v.→「to lead out of（the ignorant state）從（無知狀態）引導出來」→] v. give training or schooling to 教養；教育：He has been well educated.他受過良好的教育。  ▽education [educat(e);-ion n.] n.教育；教育的過程 educator [educat(e);-or n.] n.教育工作者 educative [educat(e);-ive a.] a.有教育意義的   introduce [intro-=into 進；duc=to lead 引導；-e→「to lead into 引進」→] v.１ lead or bring into use 引用；採用：to introduce new techniques 採用新技術２ lead into acquaintance with 介紹： to introduce a new teacher to the class 把新老師介紹給班上學生  ▽introducer [introduc(e);-er n.] n.引進者；介紹人 introduction [intro-;duct;-ion n.] n.引進；介紹；導言 introductory [intro-;duct;-ory a.] a.介紹的；導言的   produce [pro-=forward 向前；duc=to lead 引導；-e→「to lead or bring forward to some result 向前引導，引出結果來」→] v. bring forth;make or create 生產；製造；創造：This factory produces lathes.這家工廠生產車床。  ▽producer [produc(e);-er n.] n.生產者；製造者 product [pro-;duct] n.產品；成果 production [pro-;duct;-ion n.] n.生產；總產品；總成果 productive [pro-;duct;-ive a.] a.生產的；多產的   deduce [de-=down from 從……出來；duc=to lead 引導；-e→「to lead a conclusion down from 從……引出結論」→] v. draw as conclusion;infer 演繹；推理：I deduced that she was married by the ring on her finger.根據她手上的戒指我推斷她已經結婚。  ▽deduction [de-;duct;-ion n.] n.演繹；推論；扣除 deductive [de-;duct;-ive a.] a.演繹的；推論的   reduce [re-=backward 向後；duc=to lead 引導；-e→「to lead backward 引回頭，使後退」→] v. １ bring from a higher position to a lower position 使降級：The officer was reduced to the ranks. 那個軍官被降為士兵。２make less in size, amount, value, etc.縮小；減少；貶值等：to reduce the costs 降低成本  ▽reducer [reduc(e);-er n.] n.縮減者；減速器 reducible [reduc(e);-ible a.] a.可縮減的 reduction [re-;duct;-ion n.] n.減少；縮小 reductive [re-;duct;-ive a.] a.減少的；縮減的   seduce [se-=aside 離，偏；duc=to lead 引導；-e→「to lead aside 引離正道」→] v. lead astray, or draw aside from what is right 勾引；引誘：She seduced him to crime.她引誘他犯罪。  ▽seducible [seduc(e);-ible a.] a.易受誘惑的 seduction [se-;duct;-ion n.] n.誘惑；勾引 seductive [re-;duct;-ive a.] a.誘人墮落的  abduct [ab-=away from 離開；duct=to lead 引導→「to lead away from home 引離家庭」→] v. take away by fraud or violence;kidnap 誘拐；劫持：His forefather was abducted to America a long time ago.他的祖先是很久前被綁架到美洲的。  ▽abductor [abduct;-or n.] n.誘拐者 abduction [abduct;-ion n.] n.誘拐；劫持   induct [in-=into 入；duct=to lead 引導→「to lead into some group 引導加入某種團體」→] v. １introduce formally 使正式加入：He was inducted into the trade union.他入了工會。２ put in possession 使就職：This ceremony inducts the cabinet into office.儀式之後，新內閣正式就職。  ▽inductee [induct;-ee n.] n.入會者；就任者 inductor [induct;-or n.] n.引導者；授職人 induction [induct;-ion n.] n.入會；就職 inductive [induct;-ive a.] a.引入的；誘入的	
29. equ [L]=	even, equal 相等的 在常用詞equal，equate，adequate 和equivalent 中，可以看到詞根equ，它來自拉丁形容詞 aequus，意思相當於even（相等的）。這個詞根與其他詞根構詞時，常帶有連接字母-i-，也 可以把equi 看作equ 的異體。  equal [equ=even 相等的；-al a.=being 有……性質的→「being even 相等的」→] a. of the even equlity, value, number, degree, etc.相等的；等值的；等量的：equal pay for equal work 同工同 酬  ▽equality [equal;-ity n.] n.同等；平等；均等 equalize [equal;-ize v.] v.使相等；使平均   equate [equ=even 相等；-ate v.=to make 使……→] v. make equal;even out 使相等；使平衡： to equate the debits and credits on the balance sheet 使結算表中借貸雙方平衡  ▽equation [equat(e);-ion n.] n.平均；相等；等式；方程式   adequate [ad-=to 對；equ=equal 相等；-ate a.=being 有……性質的→「being equal to the needs 與需求相等的」→] a.１ equal to a job, or competent 勝任的：She is adequate, though not so perfect.她雖不完美，但能勝任。２ equal to what is required;sufficient 足夠的；充分的：The supply is not adequate to the demand.供不應求。  ▽adequacy [ad-;equ;-acy n.] n.適合；足夠   equivalent [equi=equal 相等的；val=value 價值；-ent a.=being 是……的→]Ⅰa. being equal in value, power, meaning 等值的；等效的；同義的：One dollar is equivalent to one hundred cents. 一元等於一百分。→Ⅱ n. equivalent thing 對等物：What is the Chinese equivalent for the word 「sun」? 英語「sun」在漢語中的對等詞是什麼？  ▽equivalency [equi;val;-ency n.] n.均等；等重；同義   equable [equ=even 平穩的；-able a.=able to be 能……的→「able to be even in temper, climate, etc.在心境、環境等方面能平穩的」→] a.１even-tempered; good-natured 平穩的；平靜的： He has an equable disposition.他性情平穩。２unchanging 穩定的：The temperature is equable this week.這星期氣溫沒什麼變化。  ▽equability [equab(le);-ility n.] n.平穩；平靜   equator [equat(e) v.使相等；-or n.=thing 表示物→「line that equates 等分線」→] n. the great circle of the earth which equates the distance between the poles 赤道（地球上等分經線的緯 線）  ▽equatorial [equator;-ial a.] a.赤道的   equilibrium [equi=even 相等的；libr=balance 天平；-ium=the state 表狀態→] n. state of even balance 平衡狀態：the equilibrium of supply and demand 供求平衡  ▽equilibrant [equi;libr;-ant n.] n.平衡力 equilibrist [equi;libr;-ist n.] n.使自己保持平衡的人 equilibrate [equi;libr;-ate v.] v.平衡   equivocal [equi=equal 相等的；voc=voice 聲音；-al a.=having 有……的→「having another equal voice 有另一相等聲音的」→] a. having a double meaning; purposely vague 多義的；模稜兩可 的：equivocal answer 模稜兩可的回答  ▽equivocality [equivocal;-ity n.] n.（語言）多義性；含糊 equivocate [equi;voc;-ate v.] v.含糊其詞；支吾	
30. fac, fact, fect [L]=	to do, to make 做 fac，fact 和fect 是一組同源異形根，它們都來自拉丁動詞facere，意思相當於to do 或to make （做）。其中，fac 是不定式詞干；fact 是動名詞詞干；fect 是動詞facere 的異體ficere 動名 詞詞干。   facile [fac=to do 做；-ile a.=able or easy to be 能……的，易……的→「able or easy to be done 能做的，易辦的」→] a.１ working with ease;skilled 駕輕就熟的；熟練的：a man with a facile tongue 能說會道的人２ easily done 易做的：The work is facile, but take it serious.工作容易， 但還要認真對待。  ▽facility [facil(e);-ity n.] n.容易；熟練 facilitate [facil(e);-itate(-ate) v.] v.使容易；促進   faculty [fac=to do 做；-ulty（-ile+-ty）n.=ability 表能力→「ability of doing things 做事情的能力」 →] n. ability to do;any particular power 能力；才能：faculty for painting 繪畫的才能  ▽facultative [facult (y);-ative a.] a.能力上的；才能上的   fact [來自動名詞factum=thing done 做過的事情→「anything done or occurred 做過的或發生 過的事」→] n.１ thing known to have occurred or to be ture 事實：Facts speak louder than eloquence.事實勝於雄辯。２ what is true or existent;truth;reality 實際；真相；實情：in fact 實際上  ▽factual [fact;-u-;-al a.] a.事實的；真實的   factor [fact=to do 做；-or n.=thing 物→「thing that does or acts 起作用的事物」→] n. element that brings about a result 因素；要素：positive factors 積極因素  ▽factorial [factor;-ial a.] a. [數]因子的 factorize [factor;-ize v.] v. [數]將……分解因子   factory [fact=to make 製作； -ory n.=place 場所→ 「 place for making 製作場所」 → ] n. working-building;workshop 工廠：chemical factory 化工廠   benefactor [bene=good 好；fact=to do 做；-or n.=person 人→] n. person who does good deeds or gives friendly aid 做好事者；恩人：benefactors of an orphanage 孤兒院的施主  ▽benefaction [bene;fact;-ion n.] n.行善；施恩   affect [af-(ad-)=upon 在……之上；fect=to do or act 起作用→「to act upon 作用於……之上」 →] v.１ influence 影響：Climate affects the agricultural production.氣候影響農業生產。２ act upon the feeling of 感動：The audience were deeply affected.觀眾深為感動。  ▽affection [affect;-ion n.] n.影響；感情 affective [affect;-ive a.] a.感情方面的；表達感情的   effect [ef-(ex-)=out 出；fect=to make 造→「to make out 造出」→]Ⅰv.１ produce;bring about 產生；招致：to effect a change in climate 引起氣候變化２ accomplish 實現：to effect the greatest economy 力求節約→Ⅱ n. result made out, or influence 結果；影響：cause and effect 因與果  ▽effective [effect v.;-ive a.] a.有效的；生效的 effectual [effect n.;-u-;-al a.] a.奏效的；有效的 effectuate [effect n.;-u-;-ate a.] v.使奏效；實現   defect [de-=away, down 離，下降；fect=to do 做→「to do away with one's duty, etc.離開所做 之事」→]Ⅰv. desert 開小差；背叛：He defected to the enemy.他叛變投敵了。→Ⅱn. things down from the normal quality 毛病；缺點：He has the defects of his qualities.他有美中不足之 處。  ▽defector [defect v.;-or n.] n.逃兵；叛徒 defection [defect v.;-ion n.] n.背信；變節 defective [defect n.;-ive a.] a.有缺點；不完全的   infect [in-=into 進入；fect=to make 使……→「to make...into the body 使……進入身體」→] v. spread a disease to;affect with a disease 傳染；侵染：The wound is infected.傷口受感染。  ▽infection [infect;-ion n.] n.傳染；傳染病 infectious [infect;-i-;-ous a.] a.易傳染的   perfect [per-=throughout 徹底；fect=to do 做→「to do throughout, or done thoroughly 做得徹 底」→]Ⅰa. complete and faultless 完美的：perfect method 完美的辦法→Ⅱv. finish;make fully skilled 使完成；使精通：Try to perfect yourself in English.努力精通英語。  ▽perfection [perfect v.;-ion n.] n.盡善盡美   perfective [perfect v.;-ive a.] a.導致完美的；改善的 perfectible [perfect v.;-ible a.] a.可完成的；可改善的	
31. fer [L]=	to carry, to bring, to bear 拿，帶，產生 在常用詞conference，different，offer 和prefer 中，可以看到一個很常用的詞根fer，它來自 拉丁動詞ferre 的不定式詞干。這個詞根的含義在不同的派生詞中略有差異，可以用三個近 義詞來概括它的含義：to carry（拿）；to bring（帶來）；to bear（負擔，產生）。   confer [con-(com-)=together 一起；fer=to bring 帶→「to bring everyone's opinion together 把 各人的意見帶到一起來」→] v. talk or consult together 交換意見；協商：Two lawyers conferred on how to handle the case.兩位律師協商處理該案。  ▽conference [confer;-ence n.] n.會談；會議 conferee [confer;-ee n.] n.參加商談者；參加會議者   differ [dif-(dis-)=apart 離；fer=to carry 拿→「to carry apart from each other 拿開，互相分離」 →] v. be unlike;disagree 不同；相異：I differ from you on this point.在這問題上，我和你意見 不同。  ▽difference [differ;-ence n.] n.分歧；差異 different [differ;-ent a.] a.不同的；各種各樣的   offer [of-(ob-)=towards 向；fer=to carry 拿→「to carry towards somebody 向某人送去」→] v. １ present for acceptance;lay before 提供；奉獻：She offered the guests some gifts.她給客人獻上 禮物。２ propose 提議：He offered his help.他主動提出幫助。  ▽offering [offer;-ing n.] n.提供；禮物   prefer [pre-=before 在……之前；fer=to bring 帶→「to bring something before all the others 把 某物放在他物之前」→] v. choose rather;like better 寧要；偏愛：The hero preferred death to surrender. 英雄寧死不屈。  ▽preference [prefer;-ence n.] n.優先；偏愛 preferable [prefer;-able a.] a.更可取的；更好的   refer [re-=back 回；fer=to bring 帶→「to bring back to the starting point 帶回出發點」→] v.１ trace to ...as cause or source 把……歸諸於：She refers the success to efforts. 她把成功歸諸於 努力。２ bring some information back for consideration 參考：Please refer to the dictionary.請 查閱詞典。  ▽reference [refer;-ence n.] n.參考 referable [refer;-able a.] a.與……有關的   suffer [suf-(sub-)=under 在……之下；fer=to bear 承擔→「to bear under 在下面承擔著」→] v. １ undergo;experience 遭受；經受：to suffer losses 遭受損失２ endure 忍受：These plants cannot suffer a severe cold.這些作物耐不住嚴寒。  ▽sufferance [suffer;-ance n.] n.忍耐；忍耐力 sufferable [suffer;-able a.] a.可忍受的   transfer [trans-=across 從……到……；fer=to carry 送→「to carry across an area 送過一個地區， 從甲地送到乙地」→] v. remove from one place to another 轉移：to transfer property 轉移財 產  ▽transference [transfer;-ence n.] n.轉移；轉讓 transferor [transfer;-or n.] n.轉讓人 transferee [transfer;-ee n.] n.受讓人 transferable [transfer;-able a.] a.可轉移的；可轉讓的   順便指出：詞根fer 能與後綴-ous 結合成術語後綴-ferous，意為bearing，即「含……的， 產……的，有……的，發出……的」。   auriferous [auri (aurum)=gold 金；-ferous a.=bearing 含……的→] a. bearing or yielding gold 含 金的：auriferous ore 金礦   fructiferous [fructi (fructus)=fruit 果實；-ferous a.=bearing 產……的→] a. bearing fruit 結果實 的：fructiferous trees 結果實的樹   luminiferous [lumini (lumen)=light 光；-ferous a.=bearing 產……的→] a. giving light 發光的： luminiferous insects 發光的昆蟲   somniferous [somni (somnus)=sleep 睡眠；-ferous a.=bearing or bringing to 產生……的，導 致……的→] a.bringingtosleep 催眠的：somniferous medicine 催眠藥	
32. fid [L]=	to trust 信任 在高保真音響器材上，常寫著Hi-Fi，即High-Fidelity。單詞fidelity 和confide，confidence 是 同族詞。詞根fid 來自拉丁動詞fidere，意思相當於to trust（信任）。   fidelity [fid=to trust 信任；-elity (-al+-ity) n.=the quality 表性質→「the quality of being trusted 可被信任之品質」→] n.１ faithfulness;loyalty 忠誠；忠實：fidelity to one's cause 對事業的忠 誠２ (radio, video) precision of reproduction（收音、錄像的）逼真度，保真度：a high fidelity recorder 高保真錄音機   confide [con-(com-)=completely 完全地；fid=to trust 信任；-e→「to trustcompletely 完全信任」 →] v.１ have trust or faith in 信任：I confide in every one of you.我信任你們每一個人。２ impart ( secrets) with trust 吐露（秘密等）：He often confides his private affairs to me.他常把心 腹之事告訴我。  ▽confidant [confid(e);-ant n.] n.密友；知己 confidante [confid(e);-ante n.] n.知己的女友   confidence [confide 的對應名詞：confid(e)信任；-ence n.=the act or state 表行為或狀態→ 「confiding somebody or oneself 對他人或對自己的信任」→] n.１ firm trust 信任：to enjoy one's confidence 得到某人的信任２ firm trust or belief in oneself;self-reliance 信心；自信：to have full confidence 信心十足  ▽confident [confid(e);-ent a.] a.確信的；有信心的；自信的   diffident [dif-(dis-)=not 不；fid=to trust 信任；-ent a.=-ing……的→「not trusting (oneself)不信 任（自己）的」→] a. distrusting;lacking in self-reliance 沒有信心的；缺乏自信的：He is diffident of his own opinion.他對自己的觀點缺乏信心。  ▽diffidence [dif-;fid;-ence n.] n.缺乏自信   fideism [fide（來自fidere 的同根名詞fides）=faith 信仰；-ism n.=belief or doctrine 主義→] n. doctrine that knowledge depends on faith 信仰主義（認為知識依賴於信仰）  ▽fideist [fide;-ist n.] n.信仰主義者   infidel [in-=not 不；fid=to trust 信任；-el (-al) a.=having the quality 有……性質的→「not trusting or believing in religion 不相信宗教的」→]Ⅰa. unfaithful in religion 不信宗教的/infidel writers 不信教的作家→Ⅱ n. one who does not believe in religion 不信仰宗教的人：He remained an infidel to his dying day.他至死還是一個不信教的人。  ▽infidelity [infidel;-ity n.] n.無宗教信仰；背信   perfidious [per-=through, to destruction 穿透，毀壞；fid=trust 信仰；-i-;-ous a.=causing 使…… 的→「cauing one's trust to destruction 使信仰徹底破壞的」→] a. faithless;unfaithful;violating faith 不忠的；背信的；叛賣的：perfidious activities 背信棄義的行為  ▽perfidy [per-;fid;-y n.] n.背信棄義；叛變；出賣	
33. fin [L]=	end, limit 末尾，界限 在final，finish，fine 等常用詞中，有一個拉丁詞根fin，它來自拉丁名詞finis，意思相當於 end（末尾）或limit（界限）。   final [fin=end 末尾；-al a.=of……的→「of an end 末尾的」→] a.１ last 最後的：the final day of a year 一年的最後一天２ bring to an end;complete 結束；完成： to finish homework 完成功課  ▽finisher [finish;-er n.] n.完工者；決定性的事件 refinish [re-;finish] v.整修（傢俱等）表面   fine1 [fin=end 結尾→completeness 完成；-e→「being complete or perfect 圓滿的，完善的」 →] a.１ fair 好的：a fine son 好兒子２ excellent 優秀的：fine tradition 優良傳統  ▽finery [fin(e);-ery n.] n.華麗的服飾  fine2 [fin=end 了結→final settlement 了結辦法；-e→「a sum of money paid as a final settlement of an [fin（=fine2）=to punish by money penalty 處以罰款→to deal with money affairs 處理金 錢事務；-ance n.=the act or manner 表行為或方式→] n. management of money affairs 理財， 財政：skill in finance 理財手腕  ▽financier 34. flu, flux [L]=	to flow 流動 常用詞fluid，fluent，influence，influenza 等，都是詞根flu 的派生詞。flu 來自拉丁動詞fluere， 意思是to flow（流動）。flu 有個異形根flux，它來自動名詞fluxum 的詞幹部分。   fluid [flu=to flow 流；-id a.=having the quality 有……性質的→「having the quality of flowing 有 流動性質的」→]Ⅰa. able to flow 流動的：fluid mechanics 流體力學→Ⅱn. substance that flows;gas or liquid 流體；氣體；液體：Water is a kind of fluid.水是一種流體。  ▽fluidity [fluid;-ity n.] n.流動性；流質；液態 fluidify [fluid;-ify v.] v.使成流體   fluent [flu=to flow 流；-ent a.=-ing 有……性質的→] a. flowing easily 流暢的：She can speak fluent English.她能說一口流利的英語。  ▽fluency [flu;-ency n.] n.流暢；流利   influence [in-=into 進入；flu=to flow 流；-ence n.=the act or result 表行為結果→「a planet's flowing into some area, which was supposed to work on other planets 某行星流入某方位，古時 候認為這對其他行星有所影響」→]Ⅰn. the power to produce effects on others 影響力：I have no influence to his decision. 我無法影響他的決定。→Ⅱv. produce effects on 影響：Bad weather influenced the grain production.壞天氣影響了糧食生產。  ▽influential [in-;flu;-ent;-ial a.] a.有影響的   influenza [influenz=to influence 影響；-a n.=disease 疾病→「disease that influences many people at a time 同時影響許多人的疾病」→] n. epidemic virus disease attacking the upper respiratory tract 流行性感冒（侵染上呼吸道的病毒性流行病）   affluent [af-(ad-)=to 向；flu=to flow 流；-ent a.=-ing……的→「flowing freely to 向……湧流而 來的」→] a. abundant;wealthy 豐富的；富裕的：affluent society 富裕的社會  ▽affluence [af-;flu;-ence n.] n.豐富；富裕   confluence [con-(com-)=together 共；flu=to flow 流；-ence n.=the state 表狀態→] n. flowing of water together with another 匯流，匯合/a city at the confluence of two rivers 兩河交匯處的城 市  ▽confluent [con-;flu;-ent a.] a.合流的；匯合的   influent [in-=into 入；flu=to flow 流；-ent a.=-ing ……的→] Ⅰa. flowing into 流入的：influent water from a lake 從湖泊流進的水→Ⅱn. tributary stream 支流   effluent [ef-(ex-)=out 出；flu=to flow 流；-ent a.=-ing……的→]Ⅰa. flowing out 流出的：an effluent stream from a lake 湖泊流出的支流→Ⅱn. stream flowing from a large stream, lake, etc. 從河、湖等出來的水流：the effluent from a chemical factory 從化工廠流出來的廢水  ▽effluence [ef-;flu;-ence n.] n.流出；（光、電等）射出   refluent [re-=back 回；flu=to flow 流；-ent a.=-ing……的→] a. flowing back;ebbing 逆流的；退 潮的：the refluent tide 退潮  ▽refluence/refluency [re-;flu;-ence/-ency n.] n.逆流；退潮 superfluous [super-=beyond 超出；flu=to flow 流；-ous a.=having the quality 有……性質的→ 「 having the quality of flowing beyond or over 流過界的」 → ] a. overflowing;above what is enough 過剩的；多餘的：superfluous remarks 多餘的話  ▽superfluity [super-;flu;-ity n.] n.多餘；奢侈	
35. form [L]=	shape;to form 形狀；形成 form 是英語常用詞，既可當名詞，又可當動詞。其實，form 還是個重要的拉丁詞根，作為 名詞性詞根，它來自forma，意為shape（形狀）；作為動詞性詞根，它來自formare，意為 to give a shape to 即to form（形成）。   form [form=to give a shape to 形成→] v.１ make in a centain shape 使成形，製作：to form vessels out of clay 用粘土製成器皿２ organize 組成：to form a club 組成一個俱樂部３ take shape 成形，生成：to form an idea 想出一個主意  ▽formation [form;-ation n.] n.形成；組成；形成物；組成物   formal [form=shape 形狀；-al a.=of……的→] a.１ of shape or appear-ance 形式上的，表面的： the formal structure of a poem 詩的形式結構２ regular or routine 正式的，例行的：formal invitation 正式請柬  ▽formality [formal;-ity n.] n.拘泥形式；正式手續；禮節 formlism [forml;-ism n.] n.形式主義 formalist [formal;-ist n./a.] n.形式主義者a.形式主義的 formalize [formal;-ize v.] v.使形式化；使正式；使定形 informal [in-;formal] a.非正式的；不拘禮節的   inform [in-=in 入；form=to give form to 給……形狀→「to give form into something 給某物以 形狀」→「to describe it 描述某物」→] v. give knowledge to 告知，通知：Please inform him of the changes in the schedule.請將計劃變動的事通知他。  ▽informant [inform;-ant n.] n.提供消息（或情報）的人 information [inform;-ation n.] n.通知；消息；信息；資料   reform [re-=again 再；form=to give form to 使成形→「to give a new form to 使再成形」→] Ⅰ v. １ make or become better 改造：to reform prisoners 改造犯人２ improve by removing faults or abuses 改革，改良：to reform city administration 改革市政管理→Ⅱn. improvement 改革，改良：a reform in fundamental point of view 基本觀點的改革  ▽reformism [reform;-ism n.] n.改良主義 reformist [reform;-ist n./a.] n.改良主義者a.改良主義的 reformation [reform;-ation n.] n.改革，改良，革新   formula [form=shape 形成；-ula n.=little thing 小東西→「a little shape 小形式」→] n.１ set form of words used regularly 俗套話：polite formula 禮貌用語２ prescription 處方，配方：a formula for making perfume 制香水的配方３expression showing algebraic rule 數學公式，方程式： algebraic formula 數學公式  ▽formular [formul(a);-ar a.] a.公式的 formulary [formul(a);-ary n.] n.公式彙編；俗套話；藥典   conform [con-(com-)=together 共同；form=to shape 形成→「to shape together with 與…… 共同成形」→] v.１ become the same in form 相似，一致：The goods conformed to the sample. 貨物和貨樣一致。２ be in agreement with 遵照，適應：to conform to the rules 遵守規則  ▽conformable [conform;-able a.] a.相似的；相適應的 conformity [conform;-ity n.] n.遵照；相似；一致 conformism [conform;-ism n.] n.因循守舊，墨守成規 conformist [conform;-ist n./a.] n.遵奉習俗者a.墨守成規的   deform [de-=away 離；form=to shape 使成形→「to be away from shape 使離形」→] v. １ put out of shape 使變形：Heat deforms plastic.熱使塑料變形。２ spoil the shape of 使畸形：Tight shoes may deform feet.鞋子太緊會使腳畸形。  ▽deformation [deform;-ation n.] n.損形；變醜；畸形；變形 deformity [deform;-ity n.] n.畸形狀態；畸形的人（或物） deformable [deform;-able a.] a.能變形的，可使之變形的   transform [trans-=across 到另一方；form=to give shape to 使成形→「to give shape across or give one shape from the other 使轉化、使改觀」→] v. １ change in form or appearance 使變形， 使改觀：A tadpole is transformed into a frog.蝌蚪變成青蛙。２ change in nature or quality 使
