改造，轉變：Responsibility transformed him form a careless boy into a capable teacher.責任把 他從一個粗心的男孩改變成一位能幹的教師。  ▽transformation [transform;-ation n.] n.變化；轉變；改革	
36. fort , forc [ L ]=	stong 強 在常用詞effort，comfort，force 和enforce 中，可以找到同源異形根fort 和forc。它們來自 拉丁形容詞fortis 和它的舊體forctis，意思相當於strong（強）。   effort [ef-(ex-)=out 出；fort=strong, or of strength 強，力量→「putting out of strength 使出力 氣」→] n. vigorous attempt;trying hard 艱難的嘗試；努力：to spare no efforts 不遺餘力  ▽effortless [effort;-less a.] a.不費力的；容易的   comfort [com-=completely 完全地；fort=strong 強→「to make strong in mind 使精神上堅強起 來」→]Ⅰv. relieve from distress;ease 安慰；使舒適：The doctor comforted the patients.醫生安 慰病人。→Ⅱn. relief 安慰：He often takes comfort in his friends.他時常從朋友身上得到安慰。  ▽comforter [comfort v.;-er n.] n.安慰者 comfortless [comfort n.-less a.] a.無安慰的；不舒適的   force [forc=strong 強；-e→「strength 力量」→]Ⅰn. strength;power 力量；勢力：the force of nature 大自然的力量；→Ⅱv. compel 強迫：to force the enemy to surrender 強迫敵人投降  ▽forceful [force n.;-ful a.] a.強有力的 forceless [force n.;-less a.] a.無力的；軟弱的   enforce [en-(in-)=to put into 投進……中；force n.強力→] v. put in force, or carry out 實施；執 行：to enforce the law 執行法律  ▽enforcement [enforce;-ment n.] n.實施；厲行   fort [fort=strong 強→「strong building 堅固的建築物」→] n. stronghold 堡壘，要塞：The fort was the enemy's headquarters.那個要塞是敵軍指揮部。   fortify [fort=strong 強；-ify v.=to make 使……→「to make strong 使強固」→] v.１ strengthen with forts, etc.設防：to fortify the city 鞏固城防２ strengthen or confirm 加強；使堅強：to fortify one's confidence 增強信心  ▽fortifier [fortif(y);-ier n.] n.設防者；使堅固的東西 fortification [fortif(y);-ication n.] n.設防；築城學；防禦區   fortitude [fort=strong 強；-i-;-tude n.=the quality 表性質→「the quality of being strong 堅強的 品質」→] n. courage in endurance 堅忍，剛毅：to bear a calamity with fortitude 毅然忍受災難  ▽fortitudinous [fortitud(e);-in-;-ous a.] a.堅忍的；剛毅的   reinforce [re-=again 再；in-=to put into 投入；force n.力→「to put into force again 再投入兵力」 →] v. strengthen by new force or support 增強，增援：to reinforce an army at the front 增援前 線部隊  ▽reinforcement [reinforce;-ment n.] n.增援；加強	
37. frag, fract [L]=	to break 破 在同根詞fragile，fragment，fraction 和fracture 中，詞根frag 和fract 來自拉丁動詞 frangere，意思相當於英語的to break（破）。其中，frag 是不定式詞干frang 的變體；fract 是動名詞詞干。frang 和它的另一變體fring，在英語中出現率比較低（見本節練習2 和4）。   fragile [frag=to break 破；-ile a.=easy to be 易被……的→「easy to be broken 易打破的」→] a. easily broken or damaged, or breakable 易破的；易碎的：Glass is fragile.玻璃容易破。  ▽fragility [fragil;-ity n.] n.脆性；脆弱   fragment [frag=to break 破；-ment n.=the result 表行為結果→「the result of being broken 破 碎的結果」→] n.１ part of something broken off 破片，碎片：fragments of a vase 一個花瓶的 碎片２ part of some-thing left unfinished 未完成的部分：This poem is only a fragment.這首詩 僅是未完稿。  ▽fragmentary [fragment;-ary a.] a.碎片的；片斷的 fragmentate [fragment;-ate v.] v.使裂成碎片   fraction [fract=to break 破；-ion n.=the result 表行為結果→「the result of breaking something 破壞或分裂某物的結果」→] n.１ something broken off from the whole 碎片：The cup crumbled into fractions.杯子破成碎片。２ any part of a unit or number 部分；分數：One-third is a fraction. 三分之一是分數。  ▽fractional [fraction;-al a.] a.部分的；分數的 fractionize [fraction;-ize v.] v.使分成幾部分；把……化為分數   fracture [fract=to break 破；-ure n.=the act or state 表行為或狀態→] n. breaking or breakage, especially of bone 破裂；骨折：She suffered a fracture of her wrist.她的手腕骨折了。   infraction [in-=in 入；fract=to break 破；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「breaking in law or rule 破 壞法律，侵犯規則」→] n. violation of law;breach 違犯；違背：infraction of martial law 違反戒 嚴法   refract [re-=back 回，返；fract=to break, to bend or turn 破，轉，折→「to turn back 折回」→] v. turn aside（rays of light, sound, etc. passing into a medium from another medium）使（光線、 聲波等從一種介質進入另一種介質時）發生偏轉；使折射：Water refracts light.水使光折射。  ▽refractable [refract;-able a.] a.可折射的 refractive [refract;-ive a.] a.折射的   refractory [re-=against 反抗；fract=to break 破；-ory a.=having the quality 有……性能的→ 「having the quality against breaking 抗破碎的」→] a. １ resistant to treatment 耐處理的： refractory bricks 耐火磚２ stubborn 頑固的：refractory diseases 痼疾   anfractuous [an-(ambi-)=about 周圍；fract=to break, to turn 破，轉；-u-;-ous a.=having the quality 有……性能的→「turning about 來回轉折的」→] a. winding;circuitous 彎曲的；迂迴：an anfractuous streamlet 一條蜿蜒的小溪	
38. fund, found, fus [L]=	to melt, to pour 熔化，澆注 從表面上看，常用詞confuse，refund 和foundry 似乎互不相干，其實卻是同根生的。它們 的詞根fus，fund 和found 是來自拉丁動詞fundere 的同源異形根，意思相當於to melt 或 to pour，即與金屬冶煉有關的「熔化」或「澆注」。三個異形根中，fund 是不定式詞干；found 是fund 是重讀形式；fus 是動名詞詞干。fus 的構詞能力最強。   confuse [con-(com-)=together 一起；fus=to melt 熔化；-e→「to melt together and mix up 熔 化在一起無法分清」→] v.１ jumble 搞亂，混淆：to confuse black and white 混淆黑白２ fail to distinguish 分不清，弄糊塗：He was confused about the foreign names in the novel.他被小說 中的外國名字弄糊塗了。  ▽confusion [confus(e);-ion n.] n.混亂；慌亂 confusable [confus(e);-able a.] a.可能被混淆的   refuse [re-=back 回；fus=to pour 澆灌；-e→「to pour back 往回倒灌」→「to be unable to take in 不能容納」→] v. be unwilling to accept 拒絕：He refused my advice.他不聽我的忠告。  ▽refusal [refus(e);-al n.] n.拒絕   profuse [pro-=forward 向前；fus=to pour 灌注，傾瀉；-e→「to pour forward 向前傾瀉」→「liberal to pour out 能隨意澆灑的」→] a.１ overflowing or overabounding;liberal to excess 極其豐富 的；過多的：profuse thanks 多謝２ lavish;extravagant 十分慷慨的；浪費的：He was profuse of his money.他揮金如土。  ▽profusion [profus(e);-ion n.] n.豐富；慷慨；浪費   effuse [ef-(ex-)=out 出；fus=to pour 澆注；-e→「to pour out 傾注出來」→] v.１ pour forth 傾 吐，抒發：to effuse one's bosom words 傾吐肺腑之言２ flow out; shed 流出；淌出：The blood effused from the wound.血從傷口淌出來。  ▽effusion [effus(e);-ion n.] n.抒發；流出 effusive [effus(e);-ive a.] a.溢於言表的；流出的   fuse [fus=to melt 熔化；-e→]Ⅰv. melt or join by melting 熔化；熔合：The copper and the zinc are fused by heat.銅和鋅受熱熔合在一起。→Ⅱ n. device used to break an electric circuit by melting itself 保險絲（自熔以切斷電路的裝置）  ▽fusion [fus(e);-ion n.] n.熔化；熔合 fusible [fus(e);-ible n.] a.易熔的   refund [re-=back 回；fund=to pour 灌注→「to pour back or flow back 倒灌或倒流回去」→] v. give or pay back 歸還；償還：If you are not satisfied with the goods, your money may be refunded. 你若不滿意，貨款可以退還。  ▽refundable [refund;-able a.] a.可歸還的；可償還的   foundry [found=to melt and pour 溶注；-ry (-ery) n.=place 場所→] n. place where metal is melted and poured 鑄工車間；鑄造廠   confound [con-=together 一起；found=to melt 熔化→「to melt together 熔在一起」→] v. mix up mentally;puzzle or confuse 使（思想）混亂；混淆：I was always confounded by the twin brothers. 我總是分不清這一對孿生兄弟。	
39. gen, gener [GK, L]=	birth, race 出生，種族 常用genius，genuine，generate 和general 等，都是詞根gen 或gener 的派生詞。含有gen 這個詞根的單詞數量很大，有的來自拉丁語，有的來自希臘語，不過詞根的形態與含義都是 一致的。因為gen 的拉丁語源genus 和希臘語源genos 是同源同義的，它們都來自印歐語詞 根gen，意思相當於英語的birth（出生），以及與之相關的race（種族，種類）。詞根gener 是拉丁名詞genus 的屬格generis 的詞幹部分，可當作gen 的異形根看待。   genius [gen=birth 出生；-ius n.=the quality 表性質；→「the quality connected with one's birth 與生俱有的品性」→] n.１ natural ability or tendency 天性：a genius for making friends 交友的 天性２ outstanding natural aptitude 天資；天賦：a genius for music 音樂天賦３ person who has outstanding natural aptitude 天才人物：Beethoven was a musical genius.貝多芬是個音樂天 才。   genuine [gen=birth 出生；-u-;-ine a.=connected with 與……相關的→「connected with birth or origin 與出生或來源相關的」→] a.１ native 生來的：genuine Australians 澳大利亞土著２ original 天然的：genuine breed 純種   generate [gener=birth 出生；-ate v.=to make or cause 使……→「to cause the birth of 使……出 生」→] v.１ give birth to 生育：to generate one's young 生育後代２ produce 生產：to generate electricity 發電  ▽generation [generat(e);-ion n.] n.生育；產生；代；一代人 generative [generat(e);-ive a.] a.生殖的；產生的   general [gener=race 種族，種類；-al a.=relating to……的→「relating to the whole race or class 與整個種類有關的」→] a.１ public;common 公共的；一般的：the general opinion 一般輿論 ２ universal 全面的，總的：general offensive 全面進攻  ▽generality [general;-ity n.] n.一般性；普遍性 generalize [general;-ize v.] v.使一般化   genesis [gen=birth 生出；-esis n.=the act or state 表行為狀況→「the act or state of the birth 出 生或初生的狀況」→] n. creation;origin 創造；起源：the genesis of civilization 文明的起源 genetic [gen=birth or origin 出生，起源；-etic a.=of……的→「of birth or origin about plants and animals 關於動植物的發生或起源的」→] a. of heredity or variation of animals and plants 遺傳 的（關於動植物的遺傳和變異的）：genetic diseases 遺傳性疾病  ▽genetics [genetic;-s n.] n.遺傳學   eugenic [eu-=fine 優；gen=birth, or production of offspring 出生，生育；-ic a.=of……的→] a. of the production of fine offspring 優生的：eugenic inherited qualities 優生遺傳因素  ▽eugenics [eugenic;-s n.] n.優生學   congenial [con-(com-)=together with 共同；gen=race of kind 種類；-i-;-al a.=of……的→「of the same race or kind with 與……同種類的」→] a.１of the same genius or taste 志趣相投的：a congenial companion 意氣相投的伴侶２agreeable 相宜的：Do you find the climate congenial? 你覺得這氣候適宜嗎？  ▽congeniality [congenial;-ity n.] n.同性質；投合；適宜	
40. ger, gest [L]=	to carry 運送 ger 和gest 是一對同源異形根。ger 是拉丁動詞gerere 的不定式詞干；gest 是這個動詞的動 名詞詞干，其意思相當於to carry（運送，攜帶，傳送）。在英語中，ger 只出現於belligerent （交戰中的），congeries（堆積）和gerund（動名詞）等單詞中；gest 卻有較強的孽生能力。   belligerent [bell (bellum)=war 戰爭；-i-;ger=to carry or wage 運送，從事；-ent a.=-ing……的→ 「carrying or waging war 從事戰爭的」→]Ⅰa.１ at war 交戰中的：belligerent countries 交戰 國２ eager to be at war 好戰的：a belligerent nation 好戰的民族→Ⅱn. nation, party or person waging war 交戰方：They did not recognize the puppet state as a belligerent.他們不承認傀儡政 權為交戰國。  ▽belligerency [bell;-i-;ger;-ency n.] n.交戰狀態；好戰性   digest1 [di-(dis-)=away 離；gest=to carry 運送→「to carry away 運走或取去」→「to take in 吸收進來」→] v.１ dissolve food in the stomach 消化：This food is hard to digest.這種食物不 容易消化。２take in the meaning of 領會，理解：to digest an article 領會一篇文章  ▽digestion [digest;-ion n.] n.消化；領悟 digestible [digest;-ible a.] a.易消化的   digest2 [di-(dis-)=away 離；gest=to carry 帶→「to carry away from books, papers, etc. 從書籍、 文件中取走」→] Ⅰv. take in and condense;summarize 摘錄；摘要：to digest a report 摘要一 篇報告→Ⅱn. condensation or summary 摘要；概要：Reader's Digest《讀者文摘》 suggest [sug-(sub-)=under 在……下面；gest=to carry 送→「to carry (some idea) from under 從下面呈上（某種想法）」→「to bring up for consideration 提出以供參考」→] v.１ introduce indirectly;imply 暗示；啟發：His silence suggested agreement. 他的沉默表示同意。２ put forward; propose 建議：I suggest that you leave early for the airport.我建議你早點動身去機場。  ▽suggestion [suggest;-ion n.] n.暗示；建議 suggestive [suggest;-ive a.] a.暗示的   gesture [gest=to carry 傳達，表達；-ure n.=the act 表動作→「an act carrying or behaving oneself 表達意思的動作」→]Ⅰn. movement of body or limbs as expression of feeling 表感情的姿勢或 手勢：The lecturer made a gesture of quiet.演講人做手勢請聽眾安靜。→Ⅱv. make vigorous gestures, or gesticulate 用姿勢示意；打手勢：He gestured the car to stop.他招手讓汽車停下。   gestation [gest=to carry 攜帶；-ation n.=the condition 表行為狀況→「the condition of carrying young inside the body 懷胎的狀況」→] n. the period during which the unborn young must be carried 懷孕期，妊娠期：gestation in human beings 人類妊娠期   ingest [in-=into 入；gest=to carry 運送→「to carry food into the body 把食物送進體內」→] v. swallow;absorb 嚥下；吸收：The patient ingested food well.這病人飲食情況良好。  ▽ingestion [ingest;-ion n.] n.嚥下；吸收 ingestive [ingest;-ive n.] a.供吸收的   congest [con-(com-)=together 一起；gest=to carry 送→「to carry together 送到一起來」→] v. heap up;cause to be crowded 堆積；使擁擠：The streets are often congested on Sundays.星期 天街上往往很擠。  ▽congestion [congest;-ion n.] n.擁塞	
41. gnos, gnit, gniz [L, GK]=	to know 知 詞根gnos 來自拉丁動詞gnoscere，意為to know（知），它與noscere 是同一個拉丁詞， 只是添加前綴時前面加上g，（這個g 在詞根中不讀音，在前綴之後才讀音。）gnit 是gnoscere 的分詞詞干，gniz 是gnit 在英語中的變體。   diagnose [dia-=through 通過；gnos=to know 知道；-e→「to know through inquiry 通過查詢知 道」→] v. identify a disease after examining the patient 診斷：The doctor diagnosed the illnesss as influenza.醫生診斷該病為流行性感冒。  ▽diagnosis [diagnos(e);-is n.] n.診斷（法）；診斷結論   cognition [co-=completely 完全；gnit=to know 知；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「the act of knowing completely 全知的行為」→] n. knowing;perception 認識（能力）：cognition theory 認識理論  ▽cognitive [co-;gnit;-ive a.] a.認識的；認識能力的   recognition [re-=again 再；cognition=knowing 知道→] n.１ knowing again 認出，識別：She gave no sign of recognition of me.她根本沒有表示認識我。２ admission 承認：We insisted on recognition of our rights.我們堅持要求承認我們的權利。  ▽recognitive [re-;co-;gnit;-ive a.] a.認識的；承認的   recognize [re-=again 再；co-=completely 完全；gniz=to know 知道；-e→] v.１ know again 認出： The boy recognized the word. 男孩認出了那個字。２ admit 承認： His qualifications are recognized in China.他的資格在中國得到承認。  ▽recognizable [recogniz(e);-able a.] a.可以認出的；可承認的 recognizee [recogniz(e);-ee n.] n. [律]被保人 recognizor [recogniz(e);-or n.] n. [律]擔保人，具保證書人   agnostic [a-=not 不；gnos=to know 知；-tic a.=of……的→「of not knowing 不知道的」→] a. of the beliefs that nothing can be known 不可知論的：He is agnostic about any phenomenon.他對 任何現象都持不可知的態度。  ▽agnostically [（agnostic;-al a.）-ly ad.] ad.持不可知態度地   incognito [in-=not 不；co-=completely 完全；gnit=to know 知；-o a.=-ing ……的→「not being known 不為人知的」→] Ⅰ a. with one's name hidden 隱姓埋名的：to travel incognito 匿名 旅行Ⅱ n. person who is incognito 隱姓埋名者：to preserve one's incognito 保持隱姓埋名的 身份   precognition [pre-=beforehand 事先；cognition n. 認識→] n. previous cognition or knowledge 預知，早知：He claims the laboratory proof of his precognition.他聲稱他的預言已獲實驗證明。  ▽precognitive [pre-;cognitive a.] a.預知的，早知的   prognosis [pro-=forward 向前；gnosis=knowing 知→「knowing of forward conditions 知道前景」 →] n. estimate of what will probably happen 預測：The prognosis on finance is poor.財政預測的 前景不佳。  ▽prognostic [pro-;gnos;-tic a./n.] a.預兆的n.預兆；預測	
42. grad, gress [L]=	to step 步 在常用grade，gradual，graduate 以及aggress，progress 中有兩個同源異形根：grad 和gress。 grad 來自拉丁名詞gradus，意為step（步），或者來自拉丁動詞gradi，意為to step（跨步）； gress 來自gradi 的動名詞詞干，意思也是to step（跨步）。   grade [grad=step 步；-e→]Ⅰn. step;degree;stage 步；級；階段→Ⅱv.１ arrange according to grade 按等級分類：to grade the tea 給茶葉分級２ assign a grade to 評級，評分：to grade papers 評試卷  ▽gradation [grad (e) v.;-ation n.] n.等級；分等級   gradual [grad=step 步；-u-;-al a.=of……的→「of steps 一步步的」→] a. step by step 逐步的： gradual recovery 逐漸康復  ▽gradualism [gradual;-ism n.] n.漸進主義   graduate1 [grad=step 步，級；-u-;-ate v.=to make or take 做，取得→「to take a step in receiving education 取得接受教育的一步」→]Ⅰv. receive a diploma or degree at a college 畢業；得學位： He graduated in mathematics. 他是數學專業畢業的。→Ⅱn. one who graduates, especially from a college（大學）畢業生  ▽graduation [graduat(e) v.;-ion n.] n.畢業；授學位   graduate2 [grad=step or degree 步，度；-u-;-ate v.=to make 做→「to make steps or degrees for measurement 做測量用的度數」→] v. mark with degrees in measured units 刻度，分度：a graduated glass 刻度杯  ▽graduator [graduat(e);-or n.] n.刻度器；刻度員   aggress [ag-(ad-)=toward 向；gress=to step 跨步→「to step toward 向……逼進一步」→] v. make a first attack;intrude 挑釁；侵略：Who aggressed in the fight?誰先動手的？  ▽aggression [aggress;-ion n.] n.侵略 aggressive [aggress;-ive a.] a.侵略的；愛尋釁的 aggressor [aggress;-or n.] n.侵略者   progress [pro-=forward 向前； gress=to step 邁步→ 「 to step forward 向前邁步」 → ] Ⅰ n. advancement;improvement 進步；發展：Make progress every day.天天向上。→Ⅱv. go forward 前進，進步：to progress to the goal 朝著目標前進  ▽progression [progress v.;-ion n.] n.行進   congress [con-=together 一起；gress=to step or go 邁步，走→「going together to meet 走到一 起聚會」→] n. meeting of delegates for discussion or settlement of problems 代表大會：the Congress（美國）國會  ▽congressman [congress;-man n.] n.國會議員 congressional [(congress;-ion);-al a.] a.代表大會的；國會的   degrade [de-=downward 向下；grad=to step 邁步；-e→「to step or go downward 向下邁步， 走下坡」→] v. lower in grade, value, etc;deprive of office or dignity 降級；貶值；貶黜；墮落： The officer was degraded to the ranks. 該軍官被降為士兵。  ▽degradation [degrad(e);-ation n.] n.降級；墮落   digress [di-(dis-)=aside 偏離；gress=to step 邁步→「to step aside 步伐偏離」→] v. depart from the main subject 離開主題：Don't digress from the point at issue.別離開爭論的要點。  ▽digression [digress;-ion n.] n.離題；枝節話 digressive [digress;-ive a.] a.離題的；枝節的   regress [re-=backward 向後；gress=to step 邁步→「 to step backward 向後邁步」→]Ⅰn. return;backward movement 返回；倒退：the regress of floods 洪水的退潮→Ⅱv. go back;move backward 返回；倒退：No one can make history regress.誰也不能叫歷史倒退。  ▽regression [regress;-ion n.] n.回歸；倒退 regressive [regress;-ive a.] a.回歸的；倒退的	
43. gram [GK]=	written character 書寫符號 在grammar，gramophone，program，telegram 中，詞根gram 來自希臘名詞gramme，意為 written or recorded character（書寫或記錄符號），尤指letter of alphabet（字母）。   grammar [gramm=letter 字母，文字；-ar n.=thing 物→「art of letters 文字的技巧」→] n. art or science dealing with the right use of a language 文法，語法：English grammar 英語語法  ▽grammarian [grammar;-ian n.] n.語法學家 grammatical [gramma(r);-tical a.] a.語法的   gramophone [gram=thing for recording 記錄用的東西；-o-;phon=sound 聲音；-e→「tool for recording sound 記錄聲音的工具」→] n. instrument for reproduction of recorded sound in a disc 留聲機：a gramophone record 唱片   program [pro-=forward, beforehand 向前，事先；gram=letter 字母，文字→「letters written beforehand 事先寫好的文字」→] n. paper giving a scheme of events beforehand, especially in an entertainment, conference, course of study 節目單；方案；大綱：program of concert 音樂會節 目單  ▽programmer [program(m);-er n.] n.計劃者；程序編製員 programmatic [program(m);-atic a.] a.綱領性的   telegram [tele-=distant 遠的；gram=letter 字母，文字→「letters sent to a distant place 送往遠 方的文字」→] n. message sent by telegraph 電報：urgent telegram 急電   diagram [dia-=through, across 穿過；gram=thing written, or figure 書寫的東西,圖形→「figure made of lines going across it 由穿行其間的線條構成的圖形」→] n. figure by lines drawn to explain an idea 圖表，圖解：a diagram showing daily production 表示日產量的圖表  ▽diagrammatic [diagram(m);-atic a.] a.圖表的   phonogram [phon=sound 聲音； -o-;gram=written character 書寫符號→ ] n. character representing a sound 表音符號；音標   cryptogram [crypt=hidden 隱密的；-o-;gram=letter 字母，文字→「hidden letters 隱密的文字」 →] n. anything written in cipher 密碼文，暗記：numerical cryptograms 數字密碼文  ▽cryptogrammic [cryptogram(m);-ic a.] a.密碼的，暗記的   dactylogram [dactyl=finger 手指；-o-;gram=thing recorded，or print 記錄下的東西，印記→] n. fingerprint 指紋：the dactylograms of a criminal 罪犯的指紋	
44. grat [L]=	pleasing, thankful 使人高興的，感激的 在常用詞congratulate，grateful，gratitude 和gratify 中，grat 是個形容詞性的詞根，它來自 拉丁形容詞gratus，意思相當於英語的pleasing（使人高興的）或thankful（感激的，感謝的）。   congratulate [con-(com-)=together 一起；grat=pleasing 使人高興的；-ul-;-ate v.=to make 使…… →「to make oneself pleased together with others 使自己與他人一起高興」→] v. express one's pleasure at the success, joy, etc. of other(s)祝賀：I congratulated him when he won the prize.我 祝賀他得了獎。  ▽congratulatant [congratulat(e);-ant a./n.] a.祝賀的n.祝賀者   grateful [grat=pleasing, thankful 令人高興的，感謝的；-e-;-ful a.=having the quality 有……性質 的→] a.１ pleasing, or causing pleasure 令人愉快的；可喜的：a grateful rain 一場喜雨２ thankful, or appreciative 感謝的；感激的：grateful letter 感謝信   gratitude [grat=thankful 感謝的；-itude n.=the state or quality 表性質或狀態→] n. thankfulness; appreciation 感謝；感激：We express our gratitude for your help.對你們的幫助，我們表示感 謝。   gratify [grat=pleasing 令人高興的；-ify v.=to make 使……→] v.１ make pleased 使高興：She was gratified to get the news.得知消息，她很高興。２make pleased by giving satisfaction to 使滿意： Don't gratify every wish of a child.對小孩子不能有求必應。  ▽gratification [gratif(y);-ication n.] n.喜悅；滿足   ingratiate [in-=into 成；grat=pleasing 惹人喜歡的；-i-;-ate v.=to make 使……→「to make into a pleasing person 使成為討人喜歡的人」→] v. bring oneself into favour with 討好，巴結：He tried his best to ingratiate himself with the boss.他盡力巴結老闆。  ▽ingratiating [ingratiat(e);-ing a.] a.討好的；奉承的   gratuity [grat=pleasing 使人高興的；-u-;-ity n.=things with the quality 有……性質的東西→ 「things causing pleasure 使人高興的東西」→] a. gift of money given for some service;tip 賞金； 小費：We don't accept gratuities.我們不收小費。   gratis [來自拉丁詞gratis=pleasing 令人高興的→「for pleasing other than for payment 為使人 高興而不是為報酬的」→]Ⅰa. free of charge 免費的：Entrance is gratis.免費入場。→Ⅱ ad. done or given for nothing;without charge 無償地；免費地：We render assistance gratis.我們無 償提供援助。   ingrate [in-=not 不；grat=thankful 感激的；-e→「not thankful 不感激的」→]Ⅰa. ungrateful 忘恩負義的→Ⅱ n. one who is ungrateful 忘恩負義者：You base ingrate.你這忘恩負義的小人。	
45. it [L]=	to go 走 在常用詞ambition，exit 和transit 中有個詞根it，它是拉丁動詞ire 的過去分詞詞干，與英 語代詞it 毫不相干。   ambition [amb-=round 周圍；it=to go 走；-ion n.=-ing 表行為→「going round（for votes）（為 選票）四方奔走」→] n.１ desire to be successful 強烈慾望：He is filled with ambition to become famous.他一心想成名。２ object of such desire 追求的目標，抱負：She realized her ambitions. 她實現了自己的抱負。  ▽ambitionless [ambition;-less a.] a.無抱負的   exit [ex-=out 出；it=to go 走→]Ⅰv. go out 出去，離去：He exited in a hurry.他匆匆離去。→Ⅱ n.１ departure 出去，離去：The actor made a graceful exit.演員優雅地退場。２ way out 出 口：Exit doors must open outwards.太平門必須朝外開。   transit [trans-=across 穿過；it=to go 走→「to go across 走過」→]Ⅰv. pass across or through 通 過，越過：Only small ships can transit the canal.只有小船能通過運河。Ⅱn.１ the act of going across or through 通過，越過：Transit across the bridge is dangerous.過那座橋有危險。２ the act of carrying across 運輸：The goods were damaged in transit.貨物在運輸途中受損。  ▽transition [transit;-ion n.] n.過渡，過渡時期；轉變，變遷 transitive [transit;-ive a.] a.過渡的；轉變的；[語]及物的 transitory [transit;-ory a.] a.短暫的，曇花一現的；無常的   circuit [circu=ring 圓環； it=to go → 「 going along a ring 沿圓環走」 → ] n. １ round about movement 環行：We made a circuit of the lake.我們繞湖走了一圈。２ line enclosing an area 周線，範圍：a 40-kilometer circuit of mountains 四十公里方圓的山區３ path of electric current 電路：short circuit 短路  ▽circuitous [circuit;-ous a.] a.迂迴的，繞行的；曲折的 circuity [circuit;-y n.] n.曲折性；迂迴，拐彎抹角的行動 circuitry [circuit;-ry n.] n.電路系統；電路元件總稱   initial [in-=in 入；it=to go 走；-i-;-al a.=of……的→「of going in 剛走進的」→]Ⅰa. of or at the beginning 開始的，最初的：He failed in his initial attempts.他初試即敗。→Ⅱn. the first letter of one's name 首字母：He signed with his initials.他用首字母簽名。  ▽initialism [initial n.;-ism n.] n.首字母縮略詞 initialize [initial a.-ize v.] v.（計算機）預置   initiate [in-=in 入；it=to go 走；-i-;-ate v.=to make 使→「to make to go in 使走進去」→] v.１ set going;begin 發起；開始：to initiate a new programme of reform 開始實施新的改革方案。２ introduce into membership 介紹（入會）：The old members initiate the new ones.老會員引進新 會員。３ intrduce into knowledge 傳授，使初步瞭解：The book initiated him into foreign trade. 該書教他外貿的基本知識。  ▽initation [initat(e);-ion n.] n.開始，發起；入會；傳授 initiator [initiat(e);-or n.] n.創始人，發起者；傳授者 initiative [initiat(e);-ive a.] a.開始的n.倡議；首創精神   sedition [sed-(se-)=apart 離；it=to go 走；-ion n.=-ing 表行為→「going apart 走開，脫離」→] n. speech or action causing rebellion 煽動叛亂的言行：He was charged with sedition.他被控犯 有煽動叛亂罪。  ▽seditionary [sedition;-ary n.] n.煽動分子 seditionist [sedition;-ist n.] n.煽動叛亂者 seditious [sed-;it;-ious a.] a.煽動叛亂的；煽動性的   obit [ob-=away 離開；it=to go 走→「going away or passing away 離去，去世」→] n. ceremony in memory of the anniversary of one's death 週年祭禮：They hold a simple obit to remember him. 他們召開了一個簡樸的週年祭禮來追思他。  ▽obituary [obit;-u-;-ary n. ] n.訃告 obituarist [obituar(y);-ist n.] n.訃告作者	
46. jac, ject [L]=	to throw 投擲 詞根jac 和ject 是同源的，它們都來自拉丁動詞jacere，意思相當於to throw（投擲）。其中， jac 是不定式詞干，在英語中派生詞較少；ject 是動名詞詞干，有較強的派生能力。   adjacent [ad-=to, next to 向，靠近；jac=to throw 投；-ent a.=-ing……的→「being thrown to something，or lying next to it 被投向某物的，靠近某物放置的」→] a. situated or located near one another;adjoining 鄰近的；毗連的：adjacent troops 友鄰部隊  ▽adjacency [ad-;jac;-ency n.] n.毗鄰；接近；鄰接物   inject [in-=into 入；jest=to throw 投→「to throw or shoot into 投入或射入」→] v. shoot or force some fluid or drug into the body with a syringe 注射：The nurse injected penicillin for him.護士給 他打了青黴素。  ▽injection [inject;-ion n.] n.注射；針劑   project [pro-=forward 向前；ject=to throw 投射→]Ⅰv. throw forward 投擲，發射：to project a guided missile 發射導彈→Ⅱn. something put forth or proposed;plan 提出或規劃的事；計劃： a project for developing local industry 發展地方工業的規劃  ▽projector [project v.;-or n.] n.放映機；計劃人 projectile [project v.;-ile a./n.] a.拋射的n.拋射體   eject [e-(ex-)=out 出；ject=to throw 投→「to throw out 扔出去，拋棄」→] v. cast out;expel 逐 出；驅逐：He was ejected from the country.他被驅逐出國。  ▽ejector [eject;-or n.] n.驅逐者；噴射器 ejective [eject;-ive a.] a.噴出的；逐出的   reject [re-=back 回；ject=to throw 投→「to throw back something given or unneeded 拋回所給 的或不需要的東西」→] v.１ refuse to accept 拒受，抵制：to reject an offer of help 拒絕別人 的幫助２ throw away;put aside 拋棄；剔除：to reject weak seeds 剔除不好的種子  ▽rejectee [reject;-ee n.] n.被拒絕者；遭剔除者 rejector [reject;-or n.] n.拒絕者；拋棄者   adjective [ad-=to 向；ject=to throw 投；-ive a.=being……的→「being thrown to a main body 被投向主體的」→]Ⅰa.１ added;dependent 添加的；從屬的：adjective dyes 間接染料２ added to noun as to qualify it 修飾名詞的；形容詞的：an adjective phrase 形容詞短語→Ⅱn. word added to a noun to qualify it 形容詞：attributive adjective 定語性形容詞  ▽adjectival [adjectiv (e) n.;-al a.] a.形容詞的   object [ob-=in the way of 在……的面前；ject=to throw 投→「something thrown in one's way 被投放在眼前的物體」→] n.１ things observed or material things 客觀物；物體：shining objects 發光體２ things aimed at, or purpose 目的物；對像：an object of study 研究對像３ word or group of words aimed at by a verb or preposition（動詞或介詞的）賓語：the object of a transitive verb 及物動詞的賓語  ▽objective [object;-ive a.] a.客觀的；賓語的 objectify [object;-ify v.] v.使客觀化；使具體化   subject [sub-=under 在……之下；ject=to throw 投→「to throw under one's control 投在某人 控制之下」→]Ⅰv. throw or bring under control 使受制，使隸屬：Accient Rome subjected most of Europe to her rule.古羅馬帝國使歐洲大部分臣屬於它。→Ⅱa. subordinate 從屬的：a subject state 屬國→Ⅲ n.１ one who is subject to a sovereign 臣民：the subjects of a king 國王的臣民 ２ that which subjects the purpose of speaking or writing 主題； 題目： the subject of conversation 談話的主題３ the part in a sentence which subjects 主語：「I」is the subject in「I see the cat」.「I」是「I see the cat」的主語。  ▽subjective [object;-ive a.] a.主語的；主觀的   deject [de-=down 下；ject=to throw or cast 投，拋→「to cast down in spirit 情緒拋落下去」→] v. discourage;make sad or gloomy 使沮喪；使氣餒：She looked dejected.她顯得垂頭喪氣的。	
47. junct, join [L]=	to connect 連接 在常用詞conjunction，juncture，disjunctive 中，詞根junct 來自拉丁動詞jungere 的動名詞 形式junctum，其意思相當於to connect 或to join，即「連接」。常用詞join 其實是拉丁詞根 junct 在法語中的變形。作為英語詞根，join 主要構成動詞。  conjunction [con-(com-)=together 一起；junct=to connect 連接；-ion n.=the act or state 表行為 或狀態→「connecting together 連接在一起」→] n.１ connection;association 連接；結合： We'll have a party in conjunction with Class One.我們要和一班聯合開晚會。２word connecting two grammatical elements together 連詞：「But」is a conjunction.「But」是個連詞。  ▽conjunctive [con-;junct;-ive a.] a.連接的；聯繫的   junctrure [junct=to join 連接；-ure n.=the state 表行為狀態→「joining of places or times 地點 或時間相連的狀態」→] n.１ place where several pieces of land joined 交界處：the juncture of three provinces 三省交界處２ point of time which joins affairs 關頭：an important juncture in history 歷史的重要關頭   disjunctive [dis-=not 不；junct=to connect 連接；-ive a.=having the quality 有……性質的→「not connecting 不連接的」→] a.１ tending to separate 分離的：disjunctive element 分離因素２ disjoining the sense, or making an adverse sense when uniting sentences 轉折的：disjunctive conjunction 轉折連詞   injunction [in-=in 入；junct=to join 連；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「the act of joining in or butting in legally 合法的牽連進去或介入」→] n. act of ordering authoritaively 命令，指令：an injunction against strikes 禁止罷工的命令  ▽injunctive [in-;junct;-ive a.] a.命令的；指令的   adjunct [ad-=to 於；junct=to join 連接→「being joined to a main body 被連接在主體上」→] Ⅰa. subordinate;secondary 附屬的；次要的：an adjunct phrase 附加語→Ⅱn. things joined or added, but subordinate 附屬物，附屬品：The chain is an adjunct to the watch.表鏈是掛表的附 屬品。   junction [junct=to connect 連接；-ion n.=the state 表狀態→「the state of connecting 連接的狀 態」→] n. place where lines or routes connect or cross 線路的接合點；交叉點：the junction of two highways 兩條公路的交會點   subjunctive [sub-=under 在……之下；junct=to join 連接；-ive a.=having the quality 有……性質 的→「joining under a certrain condition 連接在某種條件之下的」→] a. joining to a sentence, expressing condition, hypothesis, possibility 虛擬的（添在句子上用以表示條件、假設、可能的）： subjunctive mood 虛擬語氣   adjoin [ad-=to 於；join=to join 連接→「to join to 與……相連」→] v. be next to and often connected with 貼近；毗連：Our school adjoins the fields.我們的校園與農田相連。   rejoin [re-=again 再；join v.連接→] v. join again after being separated 重新連接：to rejoin the severed arm 斷臂再植   subjoin [sub-=under 在……之下；join=to join 連接→「to join under 連在下面，添加上去」→] v. add at the end or afterwards 增補；附加：to subjoin a postscript to a letter 在信末加上附言	
48. jur, just [L]=	law, right 法律，正義 在常用詞jury（陪審團）和just（公正的）中可以找到一對拉丁詞根，它們都來自拉丁名詞 jus（法律）。作為名詞性的詞根，jur 來自jus 的單數屬格juris，意思是law（法律）；作為動 詞性詞根jur 來自jurer，意為to swear，即在法庭上「發誓」。just 來自與jus 相應的形容 詞justus，意為right 或justice 即「公正」。因為，在古羅馬人看來法律即代表著公正。   jury [jur=to swear by law 發誓；-y n.→「group of people to swear at court 在法庭上發誓的一群 人」→] n. twelve people who are sworn to decidea case at court 陪審團：The jury found her not guilty.陪審團判她無罪。  ▽juryman [jury;man n.] n.陪審團一員，陪審員 juror [jur(y);-or n.] n.陪審員；（競賽時）評獎人   jurist [jur=law 法律；-ist n.=person engaged in 從事……者→「person engaged in law 從事法律 工作的人」→] n. an expert in law, esp. a judge 法學家，律師，法官：This case challenged a lot of jurists to find an answer.該案使許多法學家苦尋對策。  ▽juristic [jurist;-ic a.] a.法學家的；法律的   injury [in-=not 不；jur=right 公正；-y n.=the result 表行為結果→「the result of being not right 不公正的結果」→] n. harm or wrong done 損害，損傷：He never did injury to others.他從不做 損人的事。  ▽injure [in-;jur;-e] v.損害，損傷 injurious [inju(y);-i-;-ous a.] a.有害的，致傷的；中傷的   jurisdiction [juris=law 法律；dict=to say 說；-ion n.=-ing 表行為→「saying by law 依法說話」 → ] n. the right or authority to administer justice 司法， 司法權： A country's courts have jurisdiction over all citizens.一國法庭對全體公民有司法權。  ▽jurisdictional [jurisdiction;-al a.] a.司法的，司法權的   justice [just=right 正義；-ice n.=the quality 表性質→] n.１ righteousness, fairness 正義，公平： sense of justice 正義感２ judgement by judical process 司法，審判：The courts administer justice.法院負責司法。  ▽justiciary [justic(e);-i-;-ary a.] a.司法上的 justiciable [justic(e);-i-;-able a.] a.應受法院審判的 injustice [in-;justice] n.不公平；不公正   justify [just=right 正當；-ify v.=to cause 使→「to cause to be right 使正當」→] v.１ prove to be right or reasonable 證明……正當或有理：The best quality of the goods justifies its high cost.貨 物品質優良說明它價格高得有道理。２ defend as permitted 為……辯解：to justify one's actions 為自己的行為辯解  ▽justification [justif(y);-ication n.] n.證明為正當；辯護 justifiable [justif(y);-i-;-able a.] a.可證明為正當的；有理的   adjust [ad-=to 向；just=right 正確→「to the right condition 向正確的狀況」→] v. change so as to be better 調整，調節：to adjust the picture on the television 調好電視圖像  ▽adjustment [adjust;-ment n.] n.調整，調節；核准 adjustant [adjust;-ant n.] n.助手 adjustable [adjust;-able a.] a.可調整的；可核准的	
49. lat [L]=	to carry, to bring, to bear 持，帶，負 在常用詞translate, relate, superlative 和legislate 中，詞根lat 來自拉丁動名詞latum，本意是 to carry（持）；to bring（帶）或to bear（擔負，產生）。讀者也許還記得：詞根fer 與此同 義。其實，lat 正是不規則拉丁動詞ferre 的動名詞詞干。由於lat 的形態與fer 相去甚遠，又 有相當強的孳生能力，所以把它作為常用詞根，單獨處理。   translate [trans-=from……to……自……到……；lat=to carry 持，送；-e→「to carry an idea from a language to another 把意思從一種語言傳送到另一種語言」→] v. render 翻譯：to translate an English essay into Chinese 把英語論文譯成漢語  ▽translation [translat(e);-ion n.] n.翻譯；譯文 translator [translat(e)-or n.] n.翻譯者；譯員 translative [translat(e);-ive a.] a.翻譯的   relate [re-=back, again 回，再；lat=to bring 帶；-e→「to bring back in mind so as to say again 帶回腦中以便重提」→] v.１ recount;tell 敘述；講：He related his family history.他講了自己 的家史。２ bring back into connection 使聯繫：to relate the result with the cause 把結果與原 因聯繫起來  ▽relation [relat(e);-ion n.] n.聯繫；關係；敘述 relative [relat(e);-ive a./n.] a.相關的n.親戚；關係詞   superlative [super-=above 在……之上；lat=to carry 送；-ive a.=having the quality 有……性質 的→「being carried above the others 被送到他物之上的」→]Ⅰa. of the highest degree 最高級 的：superlative wisdom 極高的智慧→Ⅱn. adjective or adverb in the superlative degree（形容 詞或副詞的）最高級形式：「Coldest」is a superlative.「Coldest」是個最高級形容詞。   legislate [legis=law 法律；lat=to bring or bear 攜帶，產生；-e→「to bring forth or bear laws 產 生法律」→] v. make laws 立法：In the United States, the Congress legislates.美國國會立法。  ▽legislature [legislat(e);-ure n.] n.立法機關   ablation [ab-=away 離開；lat=to carry 拿；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「carrying away (some part of the body) 取走（身體某部分）」→] n. removal of any part of body in surgery 外科切除術：the ablation of a kidney 腎切除手術  ▽ablate [由ablation 逆生的動詞] v.切除   collate [col-(com-)=together 一起；lat=to bring 拿；-e→「to bring together for comparison 拿到 一起比較」→] v. examine and compare as booksand manuscripts 校對；核對：Please collate the document with its draft.請把文件與草稿核對一下。  ▽collation [collat(e);-ion n.] n.核對 collator [collat(e);-or n.] n.校對者   delate [de-=down 下來；lat=to bring 帶，送；-e→「to bring somebody down 使某人變得卑微」 →] v. charge with a crime 控告，告發：He delated a robbery.他告發了一件搶劫案。  ▽delation [delat(e);-ion n.] n.告發 delator [delat(e);-or n.] n.告發者   illation [il-(in-)=to 到；lat=to bring 帶，引；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「bringing to a conclusion 引到結論」→] n. inference 推論，演繹：a fair illation 公正的推論  ▽illative [il-;lat;-ive a.] a.推論的；演繹的	
51. loc [L]=	place 地方 在常用詞local，locate 和locomotive 中，詞根loc 來自拉丁名詞locus，意思為place（地方）。   local [loc=place 地方；-al a.=of……的→] a. of a place 地方的，當地的：local standard time 當 地標準時間  ▽locality [local;-ity n.] n.地點；所在地   locate [loc=place 地方；-ate v.=to make or put into 使……，置於……→「to put into a place 置 於某地」→] v. establish in a place;situate 使設置於；使定位於：The station is to be located in the western suburb.車站將建在西郊。  ▽location [locat(e);-ion n.] n.位置；定位 locator [locat(e);-or n.] n.定位器   locomotive [loc=place 地方;-o-;mot=to move 移動；-ive a.=capable of 能……的→「capable of moving from place to place 能移動到另一個地方的」→]Ⅰa. capable of moving in space 運動的， 移動的：locomotivecrane 移動式起重機→Ⅱn. locomotive engine;railway engine 機車；火車頭  ▽locomotion [loc-;-o-;mot;-ion n.] n.運動；移動 locomotor [loc-;-o-;mot;-or n. ] n. 有運動能力的人或物 locomotory [loc-;-o-;mot;-ory a.] a.運動的；運動器官的   allocate [al-(ad-)=to 到；loc=place 地方；-ate v.=to make or put 使……，放……→「to put something to a place 把某物放到某地」→] v.１ locate to a certain spot 定位：to allocate the central point of the future square 把要建的廣場的中心點位置定下來２ locate (duty, job, etc.) to, or give as a share 把……落實於；分配：They allocated the hardest tasks to themselves.他們 把最艱巨的任務分配給自己。  ▽allocation [allocat (e);-ion n.] n.分配；配給物   collocate [col-(com-)=together 一起；loc=a place 地方；-ate v.=to put 放置→「to put one thing together with another in a place 把一物與另一物放在一個地方」→] v. set side by side 並置， 搭配：It is not suitable to collocate the auditorium and the workshops in a line.把禮堂與車間並 排蓋不太合適。  ▽collocation [collocat (e);-ion n.] n.並置；配置；搭配   dislocate [dis-=to undo 做……相反之事；locate v.定位→「to undo that of locating 做與定位相 反的事」→] v.１ displace;put out of joint 使脫位；使脫臼：He fell from the tree and dislocated his left ankle.他從樹上摔下，左腳踝關節脫臼了。２ put out of order 使混亂：The traffic was dislocated by the storm.暴風雨打亂了交通秩序。  ▽dislocation [dislocat (e);-ion n.] n.脫臼；混亂   relocate [re-=again 再；locate v. 定位→] v. locate again;move to a new residence 重新定位；重 新安置：We relocated some villages before starting the project.工程動工前，我們把一些村莊 遷移了。  ▽relocation [relocat (e);-ion n.] n.重新安置	
52. log, logue [GK]=	speech, reason 說話，推理 在常用詞logic，dialogue，apologize 和eulogy 中，詞根log 來源於希臘名詞logos，原意相當 於speech 或reason,即「說話」或說話中的「推理」。異形詞根logue 是log 在詞尾時的拼寫 形式。   logic [log=reason 推理；-ic n.=the science or art of……學→] n. the science and art of reasoning correctly 邏輯學（正確推理的科學）：He argued with learning and logic.他的辯論既有學問又 合邏輯。  ▽logical [logic;-al a.] a.邏輯的；符合邏輯的 logician [logic;-ian n.] n.邏輯學家   dialogue [dia-=between 在……之間；logue=speech 談話→「speech between two persons 兩 人之間的談話」→] n. conversation between two or more persons 對話：a dialogue between two countries 兩國之間的對話  ▽dialogic [dialog (ue);-ic a.] a.對話的 dialogist [dialog (ue);-ist n.] n.對話者   apologize [apo-=away, off 離開；log=speech 話；-ize v.=to make 做→「to make a speech off (after an offence)（在犯了過失後）說些藉以解脫的話」→] v. express regret for a fault 道歉：to apologize for being late 因遲到道歉  ▽apology [apo-;log;-y n.] n.道歉；謝罪 apologetic [apo-;log;-etic a.] a.道歉的；辯護的 apologia [apo-;log;-ia n.] n.辯解；自辯書   eulogy [eu-=good 好；log=speech 話；-y n.=the act 表行為→「the act of making a good speech 說好聽的話」→] n. praise 頌揚，讚頌：to pronounce a eulogy on somebody 向某人致頌詞  ▽eulogize [eulog (y);-ize v.] v.頌揚；讚頌 eulogistic [eulog (y);-istic a.] a.頌揚的；歌功頌德的   prologue [pro-=before 前；logue=speech 言→] n. speech or words before a play or poem 戲劇的 開場白；序詩：the prologue to a long poem 一首長詩的序詩   epilogue [epi-=after 在……之後；logue=speech 言→「speech after a play 在全劇結束後說的話」 →] n. speech at the end of a play;concluding part of a book 戲劇的收場白；書的結尾部分：the epilogue of a novel 一本小說的尾聲   philology [phil=to love 愛；-o-;log=speech 言；-y n.=the art 藝術→「the art for people who love good speech 為講究語言藝術的人提供技巧」→] n. (old-fashioned) the science and art of language（舊稱）語言學  ▽philologic [philolog (y);-ic a.] a.（舊稱）語言學的   順便指出，log 與-y 結合，就成為術語後綴-logy,表示：（1）語言特色，如tautology；（2）研 究對象，如sociology, zoology；（3）論述過程，如trilogy 等。   tautology [tauto=the same 同樣； -logy n.=the character of speech 語言特點→ 「 speech characterized by repeating the same idea 重複同樣意思的語言特點」→] n. fault style of using words that say the same thing 同義反覆的語病；贅述：a speech full of tautologies 充滿無謂的 重複的演說  ▽tautological [tautolog (y);-ical a.] a.重複的；贅述的   sociology [socio=social 社會的；-logy n.=the study of……學→] n. the study of social structure and fuctioning 社會學：modern sociology 現代社會學  ▽sociological [sociolog(y);-ical a.] a.社會學的   trilogy [tri=three 三；-logy n.=speech 說話，敘述→「discourse in three sections 分成三個部分 的敘述」→] n. group of three related literary or operatic works（小說或戲劇的）三部曲：a trilogy by Theodore Dreiser 德萊塞寫的三部曲	
53. loqu, locut [L]=	to speak 講 古羅馬人是以能言善辯著名的。在拉丁語中有個很重要的動詞loqui，表示「講」這個概念。 現在要介紹的詞根loqu 就是這個動詞的不定式詞干，locut 是它的完成式詞干。   eloquent [e-(ex-)=out 出；loqu=to speak 說；-ent a.=having the quality 有……性質的→「having the ability of speaking out freely 能自如地發言的」 → ] a. able to make effective use of language;forceful and moving 有口才的；雄辯的：Facts are most eloquent.事實最雄辯。  ▽eloquence [e-;loqu;-ence n.] n.口才；雄辯術   elocution [e-(ex-)=out;locut=to speak 說；-ion n.=the act or manner of 表行為或方式→「the act or manner of speaking out 發言或發言的方式」→] n. act or art of public speaking 演說；演說術： Lawyers have to study elocution.當律師要研究演說術。  ▽elocutionist [elocution;-ist n.] n.演說家；演說術教師 elocutionary [elocution;-ary a.] a.演說術的   colloquial [col-(com-)=together 一起；loqu=to speak 說；-i-;-al a.=of……的→「of speaking together 一起說話的」→] a. １ belonging to conversational style 會話體的，口語的：Don't use colloquial words in formal writing.在正式的文體中不要使用口頭用語。２ informal 非正式的， 通俗的：a colloquial phrase 俗語  ▽colloquialism [colloquial;-ism n.] n.口語；口語詞；口語用法   interlocutor [inter-=among 在……中間；locut=to speak 說；-or n.=person 人→「person who speaks among a group 在群體中說話的人」→] n. person who takes part in a conversation 參加 談話者；對話者：He was my only interlocutor that night.當晚他是唯一與我交談的人。  ▽interlocution [inter-;locut;-ion n.] n.對話；交談 interlocutory [inter-;locut;-ory a.] a.對話的；對話體的   loquacious [loqu=to speak 說；-acious a.=inclined to 有……傾向的→「inclined to speak 喜歡說 話的」→] a. talkative;chattering 多嘴的；饒舌的：He is not eloquent but loquacious before girls. 他口才並不好，只是在女孩子面前變得多話起來。  ▽loquacity [loqu;-acity n.] n.多話；饒舌   locution [locut=to speak 說話；-ion n.=the act or mood 表行為或方式→] n. act or mood of speaking;style of speech 說話語氣；說話風格：The boy struck us not by his words but by his locution.那男孩語不驚人，但說話的語氣卻使我們吃驚。   circumlocution [circum-=around 環繞；locut=to speak 說；-ion n.=the act or manner 表行為或 方式→「speaking around 繞著圈子說話」→] n. roundabout expression;use of more words than necessary 迂迴說法；累贅的話：circumlocution office 辦事拖拉的官僚機關  ▽circumlocutory [circum-;locut;-ory a.] a.說話迂迴的   magniloquent [magni-=grand 大的；loqu=to speak 說；-ent a.=-ing……的→「speaking in a grand style 說話誇大的」→] a. boastful;bombastic 唱高調的；誇張的：a magniloquent statesman 唱 高調的政治家  ▽magniloquence [magni-;loqu;-ence n.] n.虛誇；華而不實	
54. lud, lus [L]=	to play or mock 玩，戲弄 在常用詞delude（欺騙）和illusion（錯覺）中可以看到一對異形根lud 和lus，它們分別來 自拉丁動詞ludere 及其過去分詞lusum，其基本意思是to play or mock，即「玩，戲弄」。   delude [de-=down 下；lud=to play 戲弄；-e→「to play down 在下面戲弄，貶低」→] v. mislead the mind of, or deceive 哄騙；欺騙：She deluded herself into thinking she had lost weight.她自 我欺騙，幻想減肥成功了。  ▽delusion [delus (e);-ion n.] n.欺騙；迷惑   illusion [il-(in-)=in 在……內；lus=to play 戲弄；-ion n.=the state 表狀態→「the state of playing in heart 在心中戲弄的狀態→」] n. the state of being fooled;false belief 錯覺；幻覺：I was under illusion you really cared for me.我錯以為你真的很在乎我。  ▽illusionism [illusion;-ism n.] n.引起錯覺的藝術手法 illusional [illusion;-al a.] a.錯覺的，幻覺的   prelude [pre-=beforehand 事先；lud=to play 演奏；-e→「to play before-hand 事先演奏」→] Ⅰv. play a short music to introduce another 奏序曲→Ⅱn.１ short music before a large one 序 曲：Chopin's preludes 肖邦的序曲集２ event before an more important one 預兆，先導：The bombing was just a prelude to the full-scale attack.轟炸只是全面進攻的前兆。  ▽preludial [prelud (e);-ial a.] a.序曲（式）的 preludize [prelud (e);-ize v.] v.作序曲；奏序曲   elude [e-(ex-)=out 在……外；lud=to play 玩耍；-e→「to play out of the rule 在規則之外玩」 →] v. avoid capture by, or escape from 逃避，躲避：The thief eluded the police.小偷躲過了警方 的搜捕。  ▽elusion [e-;lus;-ion n.] n.逃避，躲避   ludicrous [lud=to play or mode 戲弄；-icrous (-ous)=having the quality 表性質→「having the quality of playing or mocking 有戲弄性質的」→] a. causing laughters, or ridiculous 滑稽有趣的， 荒唐可笑的：His efforts resulted in a ludicrous failure.他的努力以可笑的失敗告終。   collude [col-(com-)=together 共；lud=to play 耍弄；-e→「to play together 共同玩弄」→] v. work together secretly for fraud or illegal act 共謀， 勾結： The union leaders colluded with the management.工會頭頭跟管理層串通一氣。  ▽collusion [col-;lus;-ion n.] n.共謀，勾結 collusive [col;lus;-ive a.] a.共謀的，欺詐的   postlude [post-=after 在……之後；lud=to play 演奏；-e→「music that plays after others 在其 他曲子之後演奏的曲子」→] n. concluding music, esp. in church（教堂禮拜後的）尾曲：They hurried away before the postlude.尾曲還沒有演奏，他們就匆匆離開教堂了。	
55. man, manu [L]=	hand 手 常用詞manual，manage，manuscript 和manner 的詞根man 的語源是拉丁名詞manus，它 等於英語的hand，漢語的「手」。man 在構詞中常帶有連接字母-u-，可以將manu 看成異形 根。   manual [manu=hand 手；-al a.=pertaining to……的→]Ⅰa.１ pertaining to the hand 手的：a sign manual 親筆簽名２ done or used by hand 手工做的；用手操作的：a manual fire engine 手壓 滅火機→Ⅱn. hand book 手冊：a driver manual 司機手冊  ▽manualism [manual n.;-ism n.] n.（對聾啞者的）手勢教法   manage [man=hand 手；-age v.=to do 做→「to do by hand 用手操作」→] v.１ handle or control 操縱：to manage a horse 馭馬２ take charge of 管理：to manage a factory 管理工廠  ▽manager [manag(e);-er n.] n.管理人；經理 management [manage;-ment n.] n.安排；管理 manageable [manage;-able a.] a.易操縱的；易管理的   manner [mann (man)=hand 手→doing 做；-er n.=the mood 表方式→「the mood of doing 做事 的方式」→] n.１ the way in which anything is done 方式：Do it after the manner of your sister. 照你姐姐的樣子做。２ personal style of acting 舉止；風度：good manners 優雅的風度  ▽mannerless [manner;-less a.] a.沒有禮貌的 mannerism [manner;-ism n.] n.言行的癖性，習氣   manuscript [manu=hand 手；script=to write 寫→「something written by hand 手寫的東西」→] n. book or document written by hand 手寫本；手稿：a novel in manuscript 未付印的小說稿   manufacture [manu=hand 手；facture (=fact)=to make 製造→] v.１make by hand 手制；加工２ make by machinery and on large scale（使用機器大規模）製造：The factory manufactures machine tools.該廠製造機床。  ▽manufacturer [manufactur (e);-er n.] n.製造者；製造廠   manipulate [man=hand 手；-i-;pulate (=ply)=to fill 裝填→「to fill by hand 手工裝填」→] v. handle with skill 熟練地操作：to manipulate the market 操縱市場  ▽manipulation [manipulat (e);-ion n.] n.（熟練）操作；控制   manacle [man=hand 手；-acle n.=small thing 小物→「small tool used to fetter the hand 束縛手 的小器具」→]Ⅰn. handcuff 手銬：The prisoner was in manacles.犯人帶著手銬。→Ⅱv. fetter with manacles;restrain 上手銬；束縛：Religion even manacles some great scientists.宗教思想甚 至束縛著一些大科學家。   quadrumana [quadru=four 四；mana (-a 表複數) n.=hands→「four hands 四隻手」→] n. the group of mamals with four hand-like limbs 靈長類動物（有像手一樣的四肢的哺乳動物）：Monkeys belong to quadrumana.猴子屬於靈長類動物。  ▽quadrumanous [quadruman (a);-ous a.] a.靈長類動物的   maintain [main (man 的異體)=hand 手；tain=to hold 握→「to hold by hand 用手握住」→] v. keep possession of 保持，維持：to maintain close ties with the masses 與群眾保持密切聯繫  ▽maintenance [main;ten (tain);-ance n.] n.保持；維持 maintainable [maintain;-able a.] a.可保持的；可維持的	
56. medi [L]=	middle 中間 在常用詞immediate，medium，mediate 和mediterranean 中，medi 是個孳生能力很強的詞 根。它的詞源是拉丁形容詞medius，意思為middle（中間）。   immediate [im-(in-)=not, without 不，無；medi=middle 中間；-ate a.=having 有……的→「having nothing in the middle, or without anything between 沒有間隔的；沒有阻隔的」→] a.１ without delay 即刻的：to give an immediate answer 立即回答２ direct 直接的：the immediate cause 直 接原因   medium [medi=middle 中間；-um n.=thing 物→「thing in the middle 中間物」→] n. substance in the middle through which any effect is transmitted 媒介物（在中間起傳播作用的物質）：Sound travels through the medium of air.聲音以空氣為媒介進行傳播。   mediate [medi=middle 中間；-ate v.=to act 做→「to act in the middle 在中間起作用」→] v. act as a peacemaker between two opposing sides 居間調停，調解：to mediate between the workers and the employers 在勞資雙方之間調解  ▽mediation [mediat (e);-ion n.] n.調解；調停 mediator [mediat (e);-or n.] n.調停者 mediative [mediat (e);-ive n.] a.調停的；調解的   mediterranean [medi=middle 中間；terr=land 陸地；-ane (-ana)=place 地方；-an a.=belonging to 屬於……的→「belonging to the middle place of land 屬於陸地中間地方的」→] a. situated in the middle of land 位於陸地中間的：Mediterranean (Sea)地中海（位於歐亞非大陸中間） medieval [medi=middle 中間；ev (來自aevum)=age 時代；-al a.=of……的→] a. of the Middle Ages 中世紀的：medieval history 中世紀史  ▽medievalism [medieval;-ism n.] n.中世紀精神 medievalist [medieval;-ist n.] n.中世紀文化藝術的愛好者   median [medi=middle 中間；-an a.=belonging to 屬於……的→「belonging to the middle 屬於 中間位置的」→] a. in the middle;running through themiddle 當中的；穿過當中的：a median line of a triangle 三角形的中線   intermediate [inter-=between 在……之間；medi=middle 中間；-ate a.=being……的→「being in the middle position between two limits, stages 在兩極限、兩階段之間處於中間位置的」→]Ⅰa. done or happening between two things 中間的；兩者之間的：intermediate course（初、中、 高三級的）中級課程２ half way 中途的：an intermediate port 中途口岸→Ⅱ v. act as a mediator 調停：He refused to intermediate in the case.他拒絕在該事件中進行調停。  ▽intermediation [intermediat (e) v.;-ion n.] n.仲裁；調停 intermediary [inter-;medi;-ary n.] n.中間形態；中間人   mediocre [medi=middle 中；ocr (來自ocris)=rugged mountain 崎嶇的山；-e→「of middle high mountain 中等高度的山」→] a. of middle quality;neither good nor bad 中等的；平庸的：a mediocre scholar 平庸的學者  ▽mediocrity [mediocr (e);-ity n.] n.平庸；平庸的人	
57. min [L]=	smaller, less 較小，較少 從表面上看，單詞minute，minus，minority 和minister 相差很遠，實際上卻是同根詞。它 們的詞根來自拉丁形容詞minor，意思為smaller（較小的）或less（較少的）。這個形容詞 還直接被引進英語，成為意義相同的英語單詞minor（較小的，少數的）。   minute1 [min=smaller 較小的；-ute n.=thing 事物→「smaller unit of time than the basic unit hour 比小時低一級的時間單位」→] n. sixtieth part of an hour 一分鐘：five minutes 五分鐘   minute2 [min=smaller 較小的；-ute a.=being ……的→「being smaller than anything concerned 比任何參照物都小的」→] a.１ very small 微小的：minute improvement 微小的改進２giving attention to the smallest points;very careful and exact 詳細的；細緻的：minute description 細緻 的描寫  ▽minutia [minut (e) a.;-ia n.] n.細節；小節   minus [直接來自minor 的中性形式minus=less 更少的→]Ⅰ a. less than zero, or negative 小於 零的，負的：a minus quantity 負數→Ⅱ prep. being less by 減去：Five minus two is three.五減 二等於三。   minority [minor=smaller 較小的；-ity n.=the quality 表示性質→「smaller quantity 較小的數量」 →] n.１ smaller number, or smaller part 少數；少數派：the minority in a vote 選舉中的少數派 ２ smaller racial group in a community 少數民族：The Indians become a minority in the United States now.現在印第安人變成美國的少數民族了。   minister [mini=less important or inferior 次要的，低下的；-ster n.=person 人→「person in an inferior position, or servant 身份卑下的人，僕人」→「person serving the country and inferior to the head of state 地位次於元首的公僕」→] n. person in charge of a department in a government 大臣；部長：prime minister 首相；總理→Ⅱv. act as servant 服務；伺候：It's our duty to minister to an old man's wants.照顧老人是我們的責任。  ▽ministry [minist (e) r n.;-y n.] n.政府的部；內閣 ministerial [minister n.;-ial a.] a.部長的；部的 ministrant [minist (e) r v.;-ant a./n.] a.服侍的n.服侍者   diminish [di-(dis-)=apart 離去；min=less 較少的；-ish v.=to make 使……→] v. make less by taking apart 使減少：The illness diminished his strength.這場病使他衰弱無力。  ▽diminishable [diminish;-able a.] a.可縮減的   adiminister [ad-=to 對；minister v.=to give service, or to perform duties 服務,執行→「to perform duties to 熱行……的職責」→] v. govern;manage 執行；管理：The courts administer the law. 法院執行法律。  ▽administration [administ(e)r;-ation n.] n.管理；行政 administrative [administ(e)r;-ative a.] a.行政的；管理的 administrator [administ(e)r;-ator n.] n.行政官員；管理人   ministration [minist(e)r v.=to give service 服務；-ation n.=the act 表行為→] n. giving service or help to those in need 服侍；幫助：The patient soon recovered under the tender ministrations of the nurses.在護士們的精心護理下，病人很快康復了。	
58. mit, miss [L]=	to send 發，送 詞根mit 和miss 是同源的。mit 來自拉丁動詞mittere 的不定式詞干mitt；miss 是動名詞詞 干，意思相當於to send（發，送）。其構詞特點是：mit 構成動詞，miss 一般構成名詞或形 容詞。   admit [ad-=to, into 去，進；mit=to send or let go 發送，放行→「to send into, or to let go into 送進去，放進去」→] v.１ let in;let enter 讓……進入：One ticket only admits one person to the theater.一張戲票只能進一個人。２ allow to join 接納：They are admitted to the trade unions. 他們被批准加入工會。  ▽admittance [ad-;mit(t);-ance n.] n.進入；允許進入 admission [ad-;miss;-ion n.] n.允許進入；入場費   commit [com-表示加強詞義；mit=to send 送→] v. １ send in custody 把……送押：The theif was committed to prison.小偷被押送到監獄去。２ send to the care of 把……提交給：We committed the case to the department concerned. 我們把案件提交有關部門處理。３ send or devote oneself to some duty;pledge 使負責；使承擔（義務）：He refused to commit himself to supporting the family.他拒絕贍養家庭。  ▽commitment [commit;-ment n.] n.關押；提交；承擔義務 committee [commit(t);-ee n.] n.負責審議提案的團體；委員會 commission [com-;miss;-ion n.] n.委託；委任；委員會   dismiss [dis-=away 離開；miss=to send 送，發→] v. send away from a place, a job, etc.打發走； 解雇等：The boss dismissed him without any reason.老闆毫無道理地把他解雇了。  ▽dismissal [dismiss;-al n.] n.打發；解雇，免職   missile [miss=to send 發送；-ile a.=capable of 可……的→]Ⅰa. capable of being sent or thrown 可發送的；可投擲的：A hand-grenade is a missile weapon.手榴彈是一種投擲武器。→Ⅱn. missile object 投擲物；發射物：guided missile 導彈  ▽missilery [missil(e);-ery n.] n.導彈技術；[總稱]導彈   emit [e-(ex-)=out 出；mit=to send 送，發→] v. send out or give off (sound, light, heat, etc.)散發； 發射出（聲、光、熱等）：The firecraker emitted sparks in all directions.爆竹一響，火花四射。  ▽emission [e-;miss;-ion n.] n.散發；發射 emissive [e-;miss;-ive a.] a.發出的；發射的   omit [o-(ob-)=in front of 在……面前；mit=to send 送→「to send something in front of someone else 把某物送到他人面前」→「to let something go away from oneself 讓某物離開自己」→] v. leave out;fail to use 刪去；省略：This paragraph can be omitted.這段文字可以刪去。  ▽omission [o-;miss;-ion n.] n.刪節；省略 omissive [o-;miss;-ive a.] a.刪節的；省略的   permit [per-=through 通過；mit=to send 送→「to send or let go through 送其過去，讓其通過」 →] v. allow 許可，允許：You are not permitted to smoke here.你不能在這裡吸煙。  ▽permission [per-;miss;-ion n.] n.允許；同意 permissive [per-;miss;-ive a.] a.容許的；隨意的   submit [sub-=under 在……之下；mit=to send 送→「to send under the control of somebody 送 到某人的控制之下」→] v.１ send or put forward for consideration or decision 送交；呈交：to submit a case to the court 向法院起訴２ cause to yield, or subject 使服從；屈從：Soldiers must submit themselves to army discipline.士兵必須遵守軍紀。  ▽submission [sub-;miss;-ion n.] n.提交；服從 submissive [sub-;miss;-ive a.] a.服從的；順從的；謙恭的   transmit [trans-=across 越，mit=to send 送→] v. send across, or pass on 傳送；傳達：The news was transmitted by email.這消息是用電子郵件發送的。  ▽transmitter [transmit(t);-er n.] n.傳送者；傳達者 transmission [trans-;miss;-ion n.] n.傳送；傳達 transmissive [trans-;miss;-ive a.] a.傳送的；能傳送的	
59. mort [L]=	death 死 有生就有死。拉丁語中表示死亡的單詞是mors，它的屬格mortis 為英語留下一個有不少同 根詞的名詞詞根mort。常見的同根詞有mortal，immortal，mortgage 和postmortem。   motral [mort=death 死；-al a.=having the nature 有……特性的→「having the nature of death 有死亡特性的」→] a.１ that will suffer death 終有一死的：Man is martal.人終有一死。２ causing death, or fatal 致死的，致命的：a mortal wound 致命傷  ▽mortality [mortal;-ity n.] n.必死性，致命性   immortal [im-(in-)=not 不；mortal a.必死的→] a.１ not mortal 不朽的：The heroes of people are immortal.人民英雄永垂不朽。２ everlasting 永世的，長久的：immortal wisdom 永生大智  ▽immortality [immortal;-ity n.] n.不朽；永存 immortalize [immortal;-ize v.] v.使不朽；使名垂千古   mortgage [mort=death 死；gage n.=pledge 抵押（品）→「a pledge given in case of one's death 為防死亡無法踐約而作的抵押」→] Ⅰn. １ an agreement to give up property if one is unable to pay 抵押協議：He signed a 80％mortgage for the new house.他簽了百分之八十的抵押貸款 協議購新房。２ money loaned to buy a house 購房抵押貸款：They bought the flat on a mortgage.他們靠抵押貸款買了單元房。→Ⅱv. place (property) under a mortgage 抵押：Faust mortgaged his soul to the devil.浮士德將靈魂抵押給魔鬼。  ▽mortgagor [mortgag(e);-or n.] n.抵押人，押出人 mortgagee [mortgag(e);-ee n.] n.受押人，押入者   postmortem [post-=after 在……之後；mortem=death 死→] a. after death 死後的：postmortem examination 驗屍→n. examination of body after death 驗屍，屍體解剖   mortify [mort=death 死；-i-;-fy v.=to make 使→「to make or put (someone) to death 使（某人） 想去死」→] v. humiliate (someone) by an injury to self-respect 羞辱，使丟臉：He was mortified by his poor marks.他因成績差感到丟臉。  ▽mortification [mortif(y);-ication n.] n.受辱感；羞愧感   mortician [most=death 死；-ician (-an) n.=person 人→「a person who handles business of one's death 料理死者事務的人」→] n. person who conducts burial and funeral services 殯葬業者： Morticians make money from the alive.殯葬業賺的是活人的錢。 mortuary [mort=death 死；-u-;-ary n.=place 地點→「place provided for the death 為亡者提供 的場地」→] n. building for the bodies of the dead 太平間  ▽premortuary [pre-;mortuary] a.葬禮前的   antemortem [ante-=before 在……之前；mortem=death 死亡→] a. before one's death;dying 死 前的；臨死的：antemortem confession 臨終懺悔	
60. mov, mot, mob [L]=	to move 運動 常用詞move（運動）的詞根是mov，它源於拉丁動詞movere。mov 有個同源異形根mot， 它來自movere 的動名詞詞干。mob 是movere 的形容詞性分詞的詞干，基本含義也是to move。   move [mov=to move 移動；-e→] v.１ change place or position 移動：Don't move or I'll shoot. 不許動，不然開槍了。２ make somebody feel strong feelings 感動：I was deeply moved by their story.我被他們的故事所深深感動。  ▽movable [mov(e);-able a.] a.可移動的   remove [re-=back, away 回，離；mov=to move 移動；-e→「to move back or away from a certain place 從某個地點移走」→] v.１ take away 移走，搬開：Please remove the extra chairs.請把多 余的椅子搬走。２ go to live in another place 搬家，遷移：My family has removed to the countryside.我家搬到鄉下去了。  ▽removal [remov(e);-al n.] n.移動；遷居；調動 removable [remov(e);-able a.] a.可移動的   remote [re-=back, away 回，離；mot=to move 移動；-e→「being moved back or away from a certain place 從某地移走的」→] a. located far away from a certain place;distant 遠離某地的； 遙遠的：The city is remote from the sea.城市離海邊很遠。   emotion [e-(ex-)=out 外；mot=to move 移動；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「moving out of one's feeling 感情的外移」→] n. strong surge of feelingthat is expressed outward 外露的激情；衝動： Hate is a powerful emotion.憎恨是一種強烈的感情。  ▽emotional [emotion;-al a.] a.感情上的；激動的   promote [pro-=forward 向前；mot=to move 移動；-e→「to move forward 使向前移動」→] v. １ help (something) in progress or growth 促進；助長：to promote popular education 促進平 民教育２ advance (some-body) in rank or positon 提升，提拔：He is promoted to the rank of first mate.他被提升為大副。  ▽promotion [promot(e);-ion n.] n.促進；發揚；提升 promotive [promot(e);-ive a.] a.促進性的；宣傳的   demote [de-=dwon 下；mot=to move 移動；-e→「to move down 向下移動」→] v. bring lower in rank 降級：The officers concerned were all demoted.有關的官員全都降了級。  ▽demotion [demot(e);-ion n.] n.降級   motive [mot=to move 運動；-ive a.=able to 能……的→「able to move 能使運動的」→]Ⅰa. causing movement 發動的，運動的：motive power 動力→Ⅱn. cause or reason for movement 動 機：the unity of motive and effect 動機和效果的統一  ▽motivity [motiv(e) a.;-ity n.] n.發動力；原動力 motivate [motiv(e) a.;-ate a.] v.促動；激發   commotion [com-=violently 激烈地（加強詞義）；mot=to move 運動；-ion n.=the act or state 表 行為或狀態→ 「the act or state of moving violently 激烈的運動」 →] n. violent and noisy movement; great and noisy excitement 混亂；騷動：The commotion in the classroom was heard in the office.教室裡一片混亂的聲音，在辦公室裡也聽得見。   以下介紹的是同源異形根mob 的常見派生詞。   mobile [mob=to move 運動；-ile a.=able to 可……的→] a.１ able to move, or able to be moved 可動的；運動的：mobile warfare 運動戰２ movable 流動的：a mobile medical team 巡迴醫 療隊３ not fixed 活動的：a mobile chair 折椅  ▽mobility [mobil(e);-ity n.] n.運動性；機動性；流動性   mobilize [mobil (e) a.可動的，活動的；-ize v.=to make 使……→] v.１make mobile or movable 使可動；使活動：The doctor mobilized my stiff elbow joint.醫生使我那僵硬的肘關節活動起來。 ２ call (troops) into active service 動員（軍隊）：The army and navy have been mobilized.陸軍 和海軍已經動員了。  ▽mobilization [mobiliz(e);-ation n.] n.活動；動員 mobilizable [mobiliz(e);-able n.] a.可動員的   demobilize [de-=to undo that of 做與……相反的行為；mobilize v.動員→「to undo that of mobilizing troops 做與動員軍隊相反之事」 → ] v. send (soldiers) back from the army to peacetime life 使（軍人）復員：He was demobilized after the war.戰後他復員了。  ▽demobilization [demobiliz(e);-ation n.] n.復員；遣散	
61. nasc, nat [L]=	to be born 出生 nation，native，nature 等常用詞的詞根是nat，它來自拉丁動詞nasci 的完成時詞干（這個 動詞沒有動名詞形式），其意思是to be born（出生）。nasc 是nasci 的不定式詞干，它在英 語中的派生詞數量較少，常用的只有nascent，renascence 等幾個。   nation [nat=to be born 出生；-ion n.=the state 表行為狀態→「the condition of people's being born 人們出生的環境」→「the origin of people 人們的出身種族」→] n. body of persons born in a common country or having a common origin 國民；民族：the Chinese nation 中華民族  ▽national [nation;-al a.] a.國家的；民族的   native [nat=to be born 出生；-ive a.=characterized by 有……特點的→「characterized by being born 帶有出生的特點的」→] a.１ by birth or origin 出生（地）的：native land 祖國２ inborn or nature 天生的：native ability 本能３ not foreign 本國的：native language 母語  ▽nativity [nativ(e);-ity n.] n.出生；出生地 nativism [nativ(e);-ism n.] n.本土主義；先天論 nativist [nativ(e);-ist n.] n.本土主義者；先天論者   nature [nat=to be born 出生；-ure n.=the state or result 表行為狀態或結果→「the state or result of the birth of all things in the world 世上萬物降生的狀況或結果」→] n. the established order of things in the world 自然（世上萬物的現有秩序）：Mother Nature 大自然  ▽natural [natur(e);-al a.] a.自然的；自然界的   cognate [co-(com-)=together 共同；gnat (nat)=to be born 出生；-e→「being born together 共 同出生的」→] a. of the same origin;related in origin 同種的；同族的：Italian and Spanish are cognate languages.意大利語與西班牙語是同族語。  ▽cognation [cognat(e);-ion n.] n.親族；同詞源；同語系   natal [nat=to be born 出生；-al a.=of……的→「of being born 出生的」→] a. of or connected with one's birth 出生的；誕生時的：natal day 生日  ▽natality [natal;-ity n.] n.出生率   innate [in-=within 在……之內；nat=to be born 出生；-e→「being born within a person 出生時 內在的」→] a. inborn;inherent 天生的；固有的：Man's knowledge is not innate in the mind.人 的知識不是頭腦裡固有的。   prenatal [pre-=before 在……之前；nat=to be born 出生；-al a.=of……的→「of the time before being born 出生前那段時間的」→] a. prior to birth 胎兒期的：prenatal education 胎教   pregnant [pre-=before 在……之前；gnant (nat)=to be born 出生→「before being born 在出生 前的」→] a.１ having an unborn child or young in the body 懷孕；懷胎：She is five months pregnant.她懷孕五個月。２ full of important but hidden meaning 含蓄的：His words were followed by a pregnant pause.說了那些話，他意味深長地停頓了一下。３ full, or rich 充滿的： All nature is pregnant with life.整個自然界充滿生機。  ▽pregnancy [pregnan(t);-cy n.] n.懷孕；富有意義；充滿   neonate [neo=new 新的；nat=to be born 出生；-e→] n. baby newly born 新生兒：neonate period 嬰兒期  ▽neonatal [neonat(e);-al a.] a.新生兒的   nascent [nasc=to be born 出生； -ent a.=-ing … … 的→ 「 being born 出生的」 → ] a. newly conceived;beginning to exist or develop 初生的；開始形成的：a nascent republic 新生的共和國  ▽nascence/nascency [nasc;-cence/-ency n.] n.發生；起源 renascence/renaissance [re-=again 再； nasc/naiss (nasc 的變體)=to be born 出生； -ence/-ance=the act 表行為→「being born again 再次誕生」→] n. new birth;revival 新生；復 活，復興：the Renaissance（歐洲14 到16 世紀的）文藝復興  ▽renascent [re-;nasc;-ent a.] a.新生的；復活的，復興的 renaissant [re-;naiss;-ant a.] a.新生的；復興的	
62. not [L]=	to get to know 知曉 常用詞note，notice，notion 和denote 等，都來自詞根not，它是拉丁動詞noscere 的動名 詞詞干，原意是to get to know（知曉）。在實際構詞中，它有to know（知道），to note（表 明）和to mark（標明）等含義。   note [not=to know 知曉；-e→「something written for one to know 讓人知曉的書面材料」→] Ⅰn.１short informal letter 便條：a note of information 通知書２ record in writing 筆記：notes of a journey 旅行筆記→Ⅱ v.１ take notes 做筆記：He noted down his impression.他把觀感記 下來。２ pay attention to 注意：Please note the spelling of this word.請注意這個單詞的拼法。   notice [not=to know 知曉；-ice n.=things 物→「thing written for the public to know 讓大眾知 曉的文字」→]Ⅰ n.１ announcement;information 通告；通知：meeting notice 開會通知２ attention 注意：Take notice of the road signs.注意路標。→Ⅱ v. pay attention with the senses 注意到：I noticed that he left very early that day.我注意到那天他很早就離開了。  ▽noticeable [notice v.;-able a.] a.值得注意的；顯而易見的   notion [not=to get to know 知曉；-ion n.=the state or result 表行為狀態或結果→「the state or result of getting to know something 對某事的知曉或理解」→] n.１ conception 概念：to stick to the old notion 死抱住過時的概念２ belief or opinion in the mind 看法；見解：to give up an unrealistic notion 放棄不切合實際的想法  ▽notional [notion;-al a.] a.概念的；名義上的   denote [de-=down 下；not=to mark, to make to know 做記號，使知道；-e→「to make known by marking down 做記號使人知曉」→] v.１indicate by mark or sign 表明；指示：A smile often denotes pleasure.微笑通常表示高興。２ be the mark or name of 意味著：The sign「=」denotes that two things are equal.符號「=」意味著兩邊相等。  ▽denotation [denot(e);-ation n.] n.表示；符號；意義 denotable [denot(e);-able a.] a.可表示的；可指示的 denotative [denot(e);-ative a.] a.表示的；指示的   notify [not=to know 知道；-ify v.=to make 做……→] v. make to know;give information of 宣佈； 通知：Please notify me of the time you may arrive.請把您到達的時間通知我。  ▽notifiable [notif(y);-iable a.] a.應通知的；應報告的 notification [notif(y);-ication n.] n.通知   notorious [not=to know 知道；-orious (-ory+-ous) a.=having a special quality of 有……特點的→ 「 being publicly known (now used in a bad sense) 眾所周知的（ 現用於貶義）」 → ] a. unfavourably known; infamous 臭名昭著的；聲名狼藉的：a notorious political swindler 臭名昭著的政治騙子  ▽notoriety [not;-oriety (-ory+-ety) n.] n.臭名昭著   annotation [an-(ad-)=at 在；not=to mark 標明；-ation n.=the act 表行為→「marking at the point 在要點處標明」→] n.１ writing of notes or explanation 做註解或註釋：The annotation of the book took ten months.註釋這本書花了十個月時間。２ note in a book 註釋，註解：an annotation on an archaic word 對一個古詞的註釋   connote [con-(com-)=together, in addition 一起，附加；not=to mark or note 標明，表明；-e→ 「to mark or note a meaning in a word in addition to its formal meaning 表明一個詞原義之外的 附加含義」→] v. suggest or imply (an added meaning in a word)意味著；含蓄著：The word 「tropics」connotes heat.「熱帶」這個詞內涵著「炎熱」的意思。  ▽connotation [connot(e);-ation n.] n.含蓄；內涵 connotative [connot(e);-ative a.] a.含蓄的；內涵的	
63. ord, ordin [L]=	order 順序 在常用詞order，ordinary 中有一對拉丁詞根ord 和ordin，它們分別來自拉丁名詞ordo 及其 屬格ordinis，其意思為regular series（順序），即英語單詞order 的基本義。   order [ord=regular series 順序；-er（法語-re）n.=the way 表方式→「the way of arranging things in regular series 按順序排列的方式」→]Ⅰn.１ succession, sequence 次序，順序：in alphabetical order 按字母順序排列２ good arrangement 整齊，有條理：Put your room in better order.把 你的房間整理清楚些。３ command or instruction 命令；指示：to obey orders 服從命令→Ⅱ v. １ give order to 下命令：He ordered them to leave at once.他命令他們馬上動身。２ direct some-thing to be made 定貨：Please order before the price goes up.請在漲價之前盡快定貨。  ▽orderless [order n.;-less a.] a.無條理的，不整齊的 orderly [order n.;-ly a.] a.整齊的；有秩序的   ordinary [ordin=order 順序；-ary a.=having the quality 表性質→「having the quality of keeping in order 按順序來的」→] a. of no special quality;unexceptional 尋常的；普通的：I'm not a hero, but an ordinary man.我不是英雄人物，而是普通人。  ▽extraordinary [extra-;ordinary] a.非常的；破例的；離奇的 superordinary [super-;ordinary] a.超常的   ordinal [ordin=order 順序；-al a.=of→] a. of order 順序的：Third is an ordinal number. Third 是 個序數詞。   subordinate [sub-=under 在……之下；ordin=series 順序；-ate a.=-being……的→「being under in order 按順序排在下面的」→]Ⅰa.１ being in a lower order or rank 下級的：subordinate unit 下屬單位２secondary 從屬的，次要的：The minority is subordinate to the majority.少數服從 多數。→Ⅱv. make subordinate or secondary 使從屬，使服從：to subordinate personal desires to the public interests 使個人需求服從公共利益→Ⅲ n. subordinate person 下屬：Trust your subordinates.要信任你的下屬。  ▽subordination [subordinat(e) v.;-ion n.] n.從屬性     ordain [ord=order 順序；-ain [F] v.=to do 做→「to do according to order 按順序辦事」→] v.１ make a priest 委任為牧師：He was ordained priest.他被授以牧師職。２ order by law 命令： The King ordained everyone should pay tax.國王有令，人人都得納稅。  ▽ordainer [ordain;-er n.] n.委任者；授命者 preordain [pre-;ordain v.] v.預先決定；注定     disorder [dis-=lack of 無；order n. 秩序，整齊→]Ⅰn. lack of order;confusion 無序；混亂：When the burglars left, the house was in complete disorder.竊賊光臨之後，房子一片狼藉。→Ⅱ v. destroy the order of 使混亂：The scene of fire was disordered.火災現場一片混亂。   coordinate [co-(com-)=together 共同；ordin=order 順序；-ate a.=-being……的→「being together in order 按順序排在一起的」→]Ⅰa. of the same degree;equal in importance 同等級的；同樣 重要的：He has power coordinate with me.他和我有同樣權力。→Ⅱn. man or thing equal in position 同等的人或物：Citizens are coordinates by law.公民在法律上是平等的。→Ⅲ v. manage the elements of 協調，整理：She coordinated the relief efforts.她負責協調救濟工作。  ▽coordinator [coordinat(e);-or n.] n.協調人；統籌者 coordination [coordinat(e);-ion n.] n.協調，整理	
64. part [L]=	part 部分 part（部分）作為英語常用詞為初學者所熟悉，其實它是個外來詞，來源於拉丁名詞pars， 意為「部分」，part 則是其屬格partis 的詞幹部分。part 構成大量英語常用詞。 part [partis 的詞干=part 部分→]Ⅰn. a separate portion of a whole 部分，局部：the rear part of the house 房子的後部→Ⅱv. be or become divided in parts（使）分開：The clouds parted and the sun shone.雲開日出。  ▽partible [part;-ible a.] a.可分開的 partage [part;-age n.] n.分割，分配；份額   apart [a-=in 在……之中；part=part 部分→「in parts 在部分之中」→] ad.１ into parts;to pieces 成零碎：to break apart 破碎２ at one side 在一邊，分離著：to hold oneself apart 與他人格 格不入３ separately 相間隔：5miles apart 相隔5 英里  ▽apartheid [apart;-heid(-hood) n.] n.隔離；種族隔離 apartment [apart;-ment n.] n.一套公寓房間   depart [de-=away 離；part=to part 分開→「to part away 分離」→] v.１ go away; leave 離開； 起程：to depart on a journey 出門旅行２ pass away, or die 去世，死：The author departed this life at an early age.作者英年早逝。  ▽departure [depart;-ure n.] n.離開，起程   department [de-=away 離；part=to part 分開；-ment n.=the product 表結果→「the product of being parted away 被分離的產物」→] n. part of a larger structure, or division 部分；部門：the sales department 營業部  ▽departmental [department;-al a.] a.部門的   participate [part=part 部分；-i-;cip=to take 佔取；-ate v.→] v. take part, or have a share 參加； 共享：to participate in a conversation 參加交談   particular [part=part 部分；-i-; -cular a.=charactered by 有……特點的→「charactered by a part rather as a whole 部分的而不是整體的」 → ] a. considered separately from others;specific;distinct 特殊的；特別的；獨特的：a particular item 特殊項目  ▽particularity [particular;-ity n.] n.特殊性；個性 particularize [particular;-ize v.] v.詳述，列舉；使特殊   partial [part=part 部分；-i-;-al a.=pertaining to 屬於……的→「pertaining to a part 屬於一部分 的」→] a.１ being in a part only;not complete 部分的；不完全的：partial payment 分批付款 ２ prejudiced in favor of one side 偏袒的：The judge was partial.法官偏袒一方。   partner [part=part 部分；-ner (-er) n.=person 人→「person who shares a part with other(s)與他 人分擔部分者」→] n.１ one who is associated with another 同夥，搭檔：business partners 業 務夥伴２ husband, wife;lover 配偶；伴侶：a life partner 終身伴侶  ▽partnership [partner;-ship n.] n.合夥關係；合夥人身份   impart [im-(in-)=in 在……之中；part=to part 分開→「to part something in...在……之中分東西」 →] v.１ give;bestow 分予；傳授：to impart basic skills to students 向學生傳授基本技巧２ make known 告知,透露：to impart the findings 透露結果  ▽impartment [impart;-ment n.] n.給予；告知，透露 impartable [impart;-able a.] a.可給予的；能告知的   counterpart [counter-=corresponding 對應的；part n. 部分→「a corre-sponding part in another place 在另一處的對應部分」→] n. person or thing closely resembling another 對手方；配對物： The new French President came to Washington to meet his counterpart.法國新任總統到華盛頓 拜會美國總統。	
65. pati, pass [L]=	to suffer or endure；feeling 承受，忍受；感受 大家可能想不到，patient 與passion 居然是同根生的。詞根pati 是個拉丁動詞，pass 是它的 過去分詞passus 的詞干。pati 的基本意思是to suffer 或endure，指精神上，感情上的「承 受」或「忍受」。因此，動名詞詞干pass 有feeling（感受）的意思。   patient [pati=to endure 忍受；-ent a.=-ing 的……→]Ⅰa. enduring calmly without complaining 忍耐的，容忍的：Be patient with the pupils.對小學生要耐心。→Ⅱn. one under medical care 病人：Do be patient since you are a patient here.作為病人住院，既來之則安之。  ▽patienthood [patient n.;-hood n.] n.患病（狀態） patientless [patient n.;-less a.] a.無病人的   patience [pati=to endure 忍受；-ence n.=the ability 表能力→「the ability of enduring 忍受的能 力」→] n. the ability of controlling one's feelings 忍耐，耐心：Mother has endless patience with us.媽媽對我們極有耐心。  ▽impatience [im-;patience] n.不耐煩；焦急，焦躁   compatible [com-=together 共同；pati=to endure 容忍；-(i) ble a.=able to 能……的→「able to suffer together 能共同忍受的→] a.１ capable of living together in peace 能和睦相處的：Cats and birds are seldom compatible.貓和鳥難得和睦相處。２ (a computer, etc) able to work with another system（計算機等）兼容的：compatible colour TV system 兼容制彩電系統  ▽compatibility [compat(ble);-ibility n.] n.兼容性；相容，適合   passion [pass=to suffer 承受；-ion n.=the result 表行為結果→「the result of suffering of one's mind 精神上承受壓抑的結果」→] n.１ strongfeeling 激情：Sometimes his passions get the better of him.有時他激情難抑。２ strong fondness 酷愛：passion for music 酷愛音樂  ▽passional [passion;-al a.] a.激情的，熱情的 passionate [passion;-ate a.] a.熱情的；熱戀的   passive [pass=to endure 忍受；-ive a.=tending to 傾向……的→「tending to suffer 傾向於忍受 住的」→] a. not acting much;inactive 被動的；消極的：passive resistance 消極抵抗  ▽passivism [passiv(e);-ism n.] n.被動（性）；消極主義 passivity [passiv(e);-ity n.] n.被動（性）；消極狀態   compassion [com-=together 共同；pass=to suffer 承受；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「the act of suffering together 共同承受」→] n. feeling of sympathy for others' misfortune 同情，憐憫：to show compassion on the unfor-tunate 憐憫不幸者  ▽compassionate [compassion;-ate a.] a.有同情心的，同情的   passible [pass=to suffer 承受；-ible a.=easy 易……的→「easy to suffer in mind 精神易受影響的」 →] a. easy to be moved 易感動的：She is too passible to be a lawyer.她心腸太軟，不能當律師。  ▽impassible [im-;passible] a.無動於衷的；不感苦痛的   dispassionate [dis-=not 無；passion n.激情；-ate a.=having 有……的→「not having passion 無 激情的」→] a. free from passion;without personal feeling 不動感情的；冷靜的：He described the accident in a dispas-sionate way.他不帶感情地描述事故的過程。	
66. patri, patern [GK]=	father, fatherland 父親，祖先，祖國 我們已經在單詞patriarch（家長）中見過詞根patri。它來自希臘名詞pater，其意思為father （父，祖先）或fatherland（祖國）。異形根patern，則直接來自這個名詞。   patriarch [patri=father 父；arch=ruler 統治者→「ruler who is a father 父權統治者」→] n. man who rules a family or tribe 家長；族長：an aged patriarch 年老的族長  ▽patriarchal [patriarch;-al a.] a.家長的；族長的 patriarchy [patriarch;-y n.] n.父權制；父權制社會   patriot [patri=fatherland 祖國；-ot n.=person or native 人，本地人→] n. person or native who loves his fatherland 愛國者：The hero was praised as a patriot.那位英雄被讚譽為愛國者。  ▽patriotic [patriot;-ic n.] a.愛國的 patriotics [patriot;-ics n.] n.愛國行為 patriotism [patriot;-ism n.] n.愛國主義；愛國精神   patrimony [patri=father 父；-mony n.=thing 物→「things from one's father 來自父輩的東西」 →] n. property inherited from one's father or ances-tors;heritage 祖傳財產；遺產：The patrimony of the poor is their own hands.窮人的祖傳財產就是自己的雙手。  ▽patrimonial [patrimon(y);-ial a.] a.世襲財產的；世襲的   patron [patr(i)=father 父；-on n.=person 人→「person who supports like a father 父親般的支持 者」→] n. protector;supportor 庇護人；資助人：a patron of school 學校的贊助人  ▽patronage [patron;-age n.] n.庇護人的身份；庇護；資助 patronize [patron;-ize v.] v.庇護；資助   compatriot [com-=together 共同；patri=fatherland 祖國；-ot n.=person 人→「person who has the same fatherland with the people of a certain country 與某民族同祖國的人」 → ] n. fellow-countryman 同國人；同胞：overseas compatriots 海外同胞  ▽compatriotic [compatriot;-ic a.] a.同國人的；同胞的   expatriate [ex-=out of 出；patri=fatherland 祖國；-ate v.=to cause to be 使……→「to cause to be out of his fatherland 使身處國外」→] v. sendout of one's country;expel 把……逐出國外；流放： The Russian writer was expatriated for some political reason.那個俄國作家因某種政治原因被 流放國外。  ▽expatriation [expatriat(e);-ion n.] n.逐出祖國；流放國外   patrilineal [patri=father 父；line=line 線；-al a.=of……的→「of the father's line 父親這條線的」 →] a. reckoned through the father and male line alone 父系的：patrilineal society 父系社會   paternal [patern=father 父；-al a.=of……的→] a.１ of or like a father 父親的；父親般的： paternal care 父親（般）的關懷２on the father's side 父方的：paternal grandfather 祖父  ▽paternalism [paternal;-ism n.] n.家長式統治；家長作風 paternalist [paternal;-ist n.] n.搞家長式統治的人   paternity [patern=father 父；-ity n.=the state or quality 表狀況或性質→「the state or qualilty of a father 為父的狀況或品質」→] n.１ fatherhood 父親的身份；父權：to perfrom one's paternity 盡為父之道２ origin on the father's side 父系：a child's paternity 小孩的父系親屬	
67. pel, puls [L]=	to drive, to push 逐使，推動 compel 和compulsion 或compulsive 雖然詞幹不一樣，單詞的基本含義卻是一致的。這是因 為它們的詞根pel 和puls 是一對同源異形根。pel 來自拉丁動詞pellere 的不定式詞干pell； puls 則是該動詞的動名詞詞干。詞根的意思相當於to drive（逐使）或to push（推動）。這 對異形根構詞很有規律：pel 加上前綴構成動詞；plus 則構成相應的名詞和形容詞。   compel [com-表加強詞義，pel=to drive 逐使→「to drive (somebody into doing something)驅使 （某人干某事）」→] v. urge forcefully;require by force 迫使；強求：His conscience compelled him to tell the truth.良心迫使他說出了實話。  ▽compellable [compel(l);-able a.] a.可強迫的 compulsion [compel 的對應名詞：compuls=to compel 迫使；-ion n.=the act or state 表行為或 狀態→] n. force 強制，強迫：under compulsion 被迫的  ▽compulsive [com-;puls;-ive a.] a.強迫的 compulsory [com-;puls;-ory a.] a.強制性的；義務的   repel [re-=back 回；pel=to drive or push 逐，推→] v.１ drive or push back 逐回；擊退：to repel the enemy's attack 擊退敵人的進攻２push or keep away 排斥；防，抗：This coat will repel water. 這外套不透水。  ▽repellent [repel(l);-ent a.] a.擊退的；排斥的 repellency/repellence [repel(l);-ency/-ence n.] n.抵抗性；排斥性   repulse [re-=back 回；puls=to drive or push 逐，推；-e→]Ⅰv.１ drive back 擊退：to repulse the enemy 擊退敵人２ push, away, or refuse coldly 排斥；嚴拒：to repulse an invitation 不接受邀 請→Ⅱn.１ driving back 擊退：The enemy met with a repulse.敵人被擊退。２ refusal 嚴拒： Her repulse was to be expected.她的拒絕乃意料中的事。  ▽repulsion [repuls(e) v.;-ion n.] n.排斥；嚴拒 repulsive [repuls(e) v.;-ive a.] a.排斥的；嚴拒的   expel [ex-=out 出；pel =to drive 逐→] v.１ drive out 驅出：A foreign secret agent was expelled from the country.一個外國間諜被驅逐出境。２ dismiss in disgrace 開除：The boy was expelled from school.那男生被學校開除了。  ▽expellant/expellent [expel(l);-ant/-ent a.] a.驅除的 expulsion [ex-;puls;-ion n.] n.驅逐；開除 expulsive [ex-;plus;-ive a.] a.逐出的；開除的   impel [im-(in-)=on 上，前；pel=to drive or push 逐，推→] v. drive or push on;urge on 推動；激 勵：His desire for knowledge impelled him to study hard.求知慾望推動他努力學習。  ▽impellent [impel(l);-ent a.] a.推動的；推進的 impulse [im-;puls;-e] n.衝動；刺激 impulsion [im-;puls;-ion n.] n.推動；推動力；刺激 impulsive [im-;puls;-ive a.] a.衝動的；由衝動所造成的   propel [pro-=forward 向前；pel=to drive or push 逐，推→] v. drive or push forward 推動；推進： The ship is propelled by steam.那條船是靠蒸汽推進的。  ▽propellant/propellent [propel(l);-ant/-ent a.] a.推進的 propulsion [pro-;puls;-ion n.] n.推進；推進力 propulsive [pro-;puls;-ive a.] a.推進的；有推進力的   dispel [dis-=away 離開；pel=to drive 驅逐→] v.１ drive away and scatter 驅散：The sun dispelled the thick fog. 太陽驅散了濃霧。２ send away, remove 消除；消釋：His words dispelled my doubts.他的話消除了我的疑慮。	
68. pend, pens [L]=	to hang, to weigh, to pay 懸掛，稱量，支付 pend 和pens 是同源異形根，它們來自拉丁動詞pendere 和它的動名詞pensum。這個動詞 有三個意思：to hang（懸掛）；to weigh（稱量）和to pay（支付）。三個意思都與古羅馬時 用天平「稱量」金銀「支付」費用一事相關聯，而稱量的東西是必須「懸掛」在天平上的。 三者之中，「懸掛」是基本義。   depend [de-=down 下；pend=to hang 懸掛→「to hang down form some-thing 掛在某物下」→ 「be supported by something 靠某物支持」→] v.１ rely (on)依靠；依賴：All living things depend on air.萬物生長都有賴於空氣。２ be determined 取決於：Whether we go for an outing depends on the weather.去不去郊遊要看天氣而定。  ▽dependence [depend;ence n.] n.依靠；從屬 dependant [depend;-ant n.] n.受贍養者；侍從 dependent [depend;-ent a.] a.依靠的；由……決定的；從屬的   independent [in-=not 不；dependent a.依賴的→] a.１ not relying on 獨立的：independent thinking 獨立思考２ self-governing 自治的：inde-pendent country 主權國家  ▽independence [in-;depend;-ence n.] n.獨立；自主 independency [in-;depend;-ency n.] n.獨立；獨立國   suspend [sus-(sub-)=under 在……之下；pend=to hang 懸掛→「to hang under 掛在……之下」 →] v.１ hang from a supporter above 吊；懸：The lamp is suspended from the ceiling.電燈從天 花板掛下。２ put off for a period of time 使懸而不決，暫停：to suspend talks 中止會談  ▽suspense [sus-;pens;-e] n.懸而不決；未定 suspensor [sus-;pens;-or n.] n.吊繃帶 suspension [sus-;pens;-ion n.] n.懸，吊；暫停，中止 suspensive [sus-;pens;-ive a.] a.暫停的；懸而未決的   append [ap-(ad-)=to 到；pend=to hang 掛→「to hang to a main body 掛到某主體上」→] v. add 附加：I want to append some words to the drawing.我要給圖樣附上文字說明。  ▽appendage [append;-age n.] n.附加物；附屬物 appendant/appendent [append;-ant/-ent a.] a.附加的；附屬的   pendulum [pend=to hang 掛；-ulum (-um) n.=thing 物→「thing that hangs 懸掛著的東西」→] n. thing hanging from a fixed point so as to swing freely, as in a clock 懸擺；鐘擺：simple pendulum 單擺  ▽pendular [pendul(um);-ar a.] a.鐘擺運動的；擺動的 pendulous [pendul(um);-ous a.] a.懸垂的；擺動的 以下分析幾個包含「稱量」或「支付」概念的同根詞。   expend [ex-=out 出；pend=to pay 支付→] v.１ pay out, or spend 付出；花費：He expended lots of time in writing this book.他花許多時間寫這本書。２ use up 用盡：Don't expend your energy on such a foolish business.別在這種蠢事上耗盡精力。  ▽expenditure [expend;-iture n.] n.支出；支出額 expense [ex-;pens;-e] n.花費；消耗 expensive [ex-;pens;-ive a.] a.花費多的；昂貴的   dispense [dis-=apart 分開；pend=to weigh 稱；-e→「to weigh apart from the amount 從總量中 稱出一部分」→] v.１ deal out;distribute 分發；分配：The machine dispenses coffee to anyone who puts in a coin.只要投入硬幣，這機器就會給你一份咖啡。２ mix and give out (medicines) 配（方）；發（藥）：Who dispensed the medicine to you?誰給你配的藥？  ▽dispensation [dispens(e);-ation n.] n.分配；分配物；配方 dispensary [dispens(e);-ary n.] n.配藥處；藥房 spend [expend 或dispense 的詞頭脫落形式→] v.１ expend (time)消耗（時間）：He spent three years writing this book.他花三年時間寫這本書。２ dispense or give out (money) in payment 花 費（金錢）：How much did you spend on the car?你買這部車花了多少錢？  ▽spendable [spend;-able a.] a.可花費的   compensate [com-=together 一起；pens=to weigh 稱；-ate v.=to make 使……→「to make one thing weighed together with another so as to make a balance 使某物與其他物一起稱，以達到 平衡」→] v. make a balancing payment for some loss;make up 賠償；補償：to compensate the workers injured at work 賠償負工傷的工人  ▽compensation [compensat(e);-ion n.] n.補償；賠償；賠償費 compensator [compensat(e);-or n.] n.賠償者；（機器）補償器	
69. pet, petit [L]=	to seek, to strive 尋求，追求 常用詞compete，competent，appetite 和petition 的詞根pet 來自拉丁動詞petere，意為to seek （尋求）或to strive（追求）。petit 是動名詞詞干，用以構成相應的名詞或形容詞。   compete [com-=together 共同；pet=to strive 追求；-e→「to strive together with others 與他人 共同追求」→] v. take part in a contest;be a rival 比賽；競爭：Two teams competed for the championship.兩隊爭奪冠軍。  ▽competition [compet(e);-ition n.] n.競爭；比賽 competitor [compet(e);-itor n.] n.競爭者；比賽者；敵手 competitive [compet(e);-itive a.] a.有競爭力的；比賽的 competent [compet (e) v.競爭；-ent a.=able to 能……的→「able to compete 能競爭到的」→] a. capable;qualified 有能力的；勝任的：He is com-petent for the job.他能勝任那項工作。  ▽competence [compet(e);-ence n.] n.能力；勝任 competency [compet(e);-ency n.] n.富裕收入；充裕   appetite [ap-(ad-)=to 向；petit=to strive 追求；-e→「striving to something 對某種事物的追求」 →] n.１ desire 慾望；愛好：She has an appetite for social activites.她愛好社交活動。２ desire for food 食慾：to have a good appitite 食慾很好  ▽appetitive [appetit(e);-ive a.] a.關於食慾的 appetizer [appetit(e);-iz(e) v.;-er n.] n.開胃品；刺激慾望的事物 appetizing [appetit(e);-iz(e) v.;-ing a.] a.開胃的；促進食慾的   appetent [ap-(ad-)=to 向；pet=to seek 追求；-ent a.=-ing……的→「seeking to a goal 向某個目 標追求的」→] a. eagerly desirous;longing 渴望的：The patient was appetent for early recovery. 病人渴望早日恢復健康。  ▽appetence [ap-;pet;-ence n.] n.強烈的慾望；嗜好   petition [petit=to seek 尋求；-ion n.=the act 表行為→「seeking or asking 尋求或請求」→]Ⅰn. request, or formal application 請求；請願書：to sign a petition for higher wages 在要求加薪的 請願書上簽名→Ⅱv. make a petition;appeal 請求；請願：to petition for lower taxes 請求降低 稅收  ▽petitioner [petition v.;-er n.] n.請求者；請願人 petitionary [petition v.;-ary which is repeated 重複的事物：He succeeded after many repeti-tions. 經過多次反覆，他終於成功了。  ▽repetitious [re-;petit;-ious a.] a.重複的；囉唆的 repetitive [re-;petit;-ive a.] a.重說的；反覆的   impetus [im-(in-)=into, on
