deci-sion 草率 的決定  ▽impetuosity [impetuo(u)s;-ity n.] n.猛進；魯莽	
70. ple(t), plen [L]=	to fill;full 裝滿（的） 常用詞complement，complete 和plenty 之間有同根關係。詞根ple 來自拉丁動詞plere 的不 定式詞干，plet 是它的過去分詞pletum 的詞干，意為to fill（充滿）；plen 是同源的拉丁形 容詞plenus 的詞幹部分，意為full（充滿的），因為同源近義，把它們放在一起介紹。 complement [com- = together 一起；ple = to fill 裝滿；-ment n. = the means 表手段→「the means of filling together 一起填滿的手段」→]Ⅰn. something that completes or makes perfect 補充，補充物：Travel is an excellent complement to education.旅行能彌補學識之不足。→Ⅱv. form a complement to 補足，補充：Reading and writing complement each other.讀與寫相輔相 成。  ▽complementary [complement;-ary n.] n.（互為）補充的   supplement [sup-(sub-）=from under 自下；ple=to fill 裝滿；-ment n.=the act or result 表行為 或結果→「the act or result of filling from under 自下而上裝滿的行為或結果」→]Ⅰn. something added to complete or reinforce 填補物，增補物：a supplement to an encyclopedia 百科全書的 補編→Ⅱv. complete or extend by a supplement 增補；補充：He supplements his income by sparetime work.他靠業餘打工補充收入。  ▽supplementary [supplement;-ary a.] a.增補的；追加   complete [com-=together 一起；plet =to fill 裝滿；-e→「to fill together 一起裝滿，不留餘地 的」→]Ⅰa.１ having all parts;lacking nothing 全部的；完整的：a complete set of Shakespeare's plays 整套莎士比亞戲劇集２ finished 完成的：My homework is complete.我的作業做完了。 →Ⅱv. finish 完成：to complete an assignment 完成任務  ▽completist [complet(e) a.;-ist n.] n.求全主義者 completive [complet(e) v.;-ive a.] a.起完全作用的；完成的   deplete [de-=to undo 取消；plet=to fill 裝滿；-e→「to undo that of filling 取消裝滿的東西」→] v. use up the supply of;decrease badly 耗盡；大大減少：The drought depleted our water supply. 乾旱耗盡了我們的水源。  ▽depletion [deplet(e);-ion n.] n.耗盡；枯竭   replete [re-=again 再；plet=to fill 裝滿；-e→「to fill again and again 不斷裝滿的」→] a. fully supplied 充滿的，充實的：a speech replete with humor 幽默十足的講演   plenty [plen=fill 充滿的；-ty n.=the state 表狀態→「the state of being full 充滿的狀態」→] n. full amount;abundance 充分；豐富：resources in plenty 豐富的資源  ▽plentiful [plent(y);-i-;-ful a.] a.豐富的；充足的   replenish [re-=again 再；plen=full 充滿的；-ish v.=to make 使……→] v. make full again;fill again 把……再裝滿，再備足：to replenish the refrigerator with food 把空冰箱再裝滿食物  ▽replenisher [replenish;-er n.] n.補充物；補償物	
71. plic, plicate, ply [L]=	to bend or fold 彎，折 常用詞apply，appliance，applicant，application 之間存在著詞義相連的派生關係。這組詞中 包含的ply（pli），plic，plicate 都是拉丁動詞plicare 的詞根。plic 是不定詞干，plicate 是動 名詞干；pli 是plic 在法語中的形式，ply 則是pli 經英語「正字」之後的標準形式，只能出 現在動詞的詞尾。這些異形根形式多樣,詞根的基本義卻較簡單，相當於to fold（折）或to bend （彎）。   apply [ap-(ad-)=to 向；ply=to fold 折→「to fold to something so as to attach it 折向某物以便與 之相連」→] v.１ put to use 運用，應用：to apply the brakes 扳閘剎車２ be suitable 適用： The theory doesn't apply in this case.這個理論在此行不通。３request（to attach to）申請（參 與）：She applied to several colleges.她向好幾個大學申請入學。  ▽appliance [appli (=apply);-ance n.] n.器具，器械；應用 applicable [ap-;plic;-able a.] a.可應用的；適用的 applicant [ap-;plic;-ant n.] n.申請者 application [ap-;plicat;-ion n.] n.申請；申請書   imply [im-(in-)=in 進；ply=to fold 折→「to fold in so as not to show out 折進去以免直露」→] v. １ indicate or suggest without words 暗指，暗示：His actions implied a lack of faith. 他的行為 暗示缺乏信任。２ involve as necessary 必然包含：A fair trial implies a jury that is not biased. 一場公平審判的前提是陪審團必須公正不倚。  ▽implicit [im-;plic;-it a.] a.含蓄的；內含的 implicate [im-;plic;-ate v.] v.涉及；意味著；暗指 implication [im-;plic;-ation n.] n.涉及；暗示，暗指   reply [re-=back 回；ply=to fold 折→「to fold back 折回」→] v.１ respond by action 反應，回 應：to reply to the enemy's fire 反擊敵火的炮火２ give an answer 回答，答覆：to reply to a question 回答問題  ▽replicate [re-;plic;-ate a.] a.折轉的，反折的 replication [re-;plic;-ation] n.反折；回答   multiply [multi=many 多；ply=to fold 折→「to fold many times 折疊多次」→] v. １ (cause) to grow in number（使）增加：Problems multi-plied under his leadership.由於他的領導，問題增 多了。２ find the product by multiplication 乘：to multiply 3 by 4 3 乘4  ▽multiplier [multipl(y);-ier n.] n.乘數 multiplication [multi;plic;-ation n.] n.增加；乘法   comply [com-=together 一起；ply=to bend 彎→「to bend together 一起彎下腰來」→] v. obey 依從，服從：to comply with rules 遵守規則  ▽compliance [compl(y);-iance n.] n.依從；服從 compliant [compl(y);-iant a.] a.依從的；服從的 compliment [compl(y);-iment n.] n.恭維（話）   complicate [com-=together 一起；plic=to fold 折；-ate v.=to make 使……→「to make (things) fold together 使事物折疊在一起」→]Ⅰv. make intricate or difficult 使複雜化：There is no need to complicate matters.沒有必要使事情複雜化。  ▽complication [complicat(e);-ion n.] n.糾紛，複雜；複雜化   explicate [ex-=out 出；plic=to fold 折；-ate v. =to make 使……→「to make something fold out to be seen 使某物折翻外露」→] v. explain in detail 解釋，說明：to explicate a theory 闡述理論  ▽explication [explicat(e);-ion n.] n.說明，闡述 explicative [explicat(e);-ive a.] a.解釋的，說明的 explicit [ex-;plic;-it a.] a.詳述的，明確的 explicable [ex-;plic;-able a.] a.可解釋的，可說明的 supplicate [sup- (sub-) =under 下；plic =to bend 彎；-ate v. =to make 使……→「to make to bend under somebody 使向某人彎下腰」→] v. beg humbly 懇求，哀求：to supplicate for pardon 求 饒  ▽supplication [supplicat(e);-ion n.] n.懇求，哀求；祈求 supplicatory [supplicat(e);-ory a.] a.懇求的，哀求的 supplicant 72. pon, pos(it) [L]=	to place, to put 放，置 pon 和pos (it)是一對結合力非常強的同源異形根。pon 來自拉丁動詞ponere 的不定式詞干， pos (it)是動名詞詞干，其意思為to place 或to put，即「放」或「置」。這族同根詞不下百個。 compose [com- = together 一起；pos = to place 放置；-e→「to place together 放置在一起」 →] v.１make up, or form as a whole 組成：Water is composed of hydrogen and oxygen. 水由氫 和氧組成。２ create (literal or musical work)創作：Beethoven composed nine symphonies.貝多 73. port [L]=	to carry 拿，運 portable，import，export，important 等都是詞根port 的常見派生詞。port 來自拉丁動詞 portare，意思為to carry（拿，運，持，傳）。 portable [prot = to carry 拿，帶；-able a. = capable of 可……的→] a. capable of being exports in value last year.去年輸入品的價值超過輸出品。  ▽importable [import;-able a.] a.可進口的 importation [import;-ation n.] n.進口；進口品   important [im-(in-)=in 入；port =to carry 帶；-ant a.=-ing……的→「carrying or 74. prehend, prehens, pris [L]=	to seize 抓住 常用詞comprehend 和prison, surprise 有同根關係，其中的拉丁詞根prehend 來自動詞 prehendere，意為to seize（抓住），prehens 是動名詞詞干，而pris 則是prehens 在法語中的 變體。   comprehend [com-=together 一起；prehend=to seize 抓住→「to seize all the points together 抓 住所有的要點」→] v. grasp with the mind 理解，領會：Man does not yet comprehend the universe. 人類尚未瞭解宇宙。  ▽comprehension [com-;prehens;-ion n.] n.理解（力） comprehensible [com-;prehens;-ible a.] a.可理解的   apprehend [ap-（ad-）=to 到；prehend=to seize 抓→「to seize to some place 抓到某處去」→] v.１ take into custody;arrest 拘押；逮捕：The police apprehended the burglars.警察拘捕了竊 賊。２grasp the meaning of 領會，理解：to apprehend the difference between two words 領會 兩詞的差別之處  ▽apprehension [ap-;prehens;-ion n.] n.憂慮；抵押；理解 apprehensible [ap-;prehens;-ible a.] a.可理解的，可領會的   reprehend [re-=back 回；prehend=to seize 抓→「to seize someone back 把某人抓回來」→] v. blame or rebuke 指摘，斥責：The boy was severely reprehended for his bad conduct.男孩因行 為不端被嚴加申斥。  ▽reprehension [re-;prehens;-ion n.] n.斥責；指摘 reprehensible [re-;prehens;-ible a.] a.應受斥責的   prehensile [prehens=to seize 抓；-ile a.=able 可……的→「able to seize 可抓住的」→] a. made for seizing 能抓的，能握的：The monkey has a prehensile tail.猴子有能纏住東西的尾巴。   prison [pris=to seize 抓住；-on（-ion）n.=the act or result 表行為結果→「the result of seizing someone 抓住某人的結果」→] n. place for keeping people accused of crime 監獄：Prison may not be a cure for crime.監獄未必能杜絕犯罪。  ▽prisoner [prison;-er n.] n.犯人，囚犯   surprise [sur-（super-）= over 越過；pris = to seize 抓；-e→「to seize somebody over some place 越過某地抓住某人」→] v. １ make an unexpected attack on figures surprise me.銷售數額使我大吃一驚。 comprise [com- = together 一起；pris = to seize 抓；-e→「to seize all together 全抓在一起」 →] v.１ include or contain 包含，包括：The former Soviet Union comprised several republics. 前蘇聯包括許多加盟共和國。２ consist of 構成，組成：The advisory board comprises six members.顧問小組由六個成員組成。  ▽comprisable [compris(e);-able a.] a.能被包含的 enterprise [enter（- inter-）=between在……之間；pris=to seize or take抓取；-e→「to take chances between risks 在風險中抓取機會」→] n.１ adventurous spirit or ingenuity 冒險精神，進取心： a man of great enterprise 進取心很強的人２ business firm;company 企事業：the leading foreign enterprises 重要的外國企業  ▽enterpriser [enterpris(e);-er n.] n.企業家；創業者	
75. press [L]=	to press 壓 press 是個非常顯現的拉丁詞根，因為它成為英語的單根詞press，廣為初學者所認識。press 來自拉丁動詞pressare，意為to press（壓），其動名詞pressum 的詞干也是press，所以不存 在異形根。   press [press=to press 壓→]Ⅰv.１ put steady force on 壓：to press the doorbell 按門鈴２squeeze 擠取，搾取：to press the grapes to produce wine 搾葡萄汁造酒３ emphasize with force 強調， 堅持：to press for a reform on the education 堅持要求教育改革Ⅱn.１ the act of pressing 壓， 按：three presses on the bell 按三下鈴２ printed publications or news organizations as a group 出版業，新聞機構：Oxford University Press 牛津大學出版社  ▽pressing [press v.;-ing n.] a.迫切的；堅持的 pressure [press v.;-ure n.] n.壓，按；壓力；緊迫   express [ex-=out 出；press=to press 壓→] v.１ press out 搾，擠壓出：to express juice from the oranges 搾橙汁２ show;reveal 表達，體現：to express one's anger 表露出惱怒３ put into words 用言詞表達，陳述：to express an idea 表述思想  ▽expression [express;-ion n.] n.表達（法）；表現；表情 expressive [express;-ive a.] a.表達的；富於表情的   impress [im-(in-)=in 進；press=to press 壓→] v.１ press in;imprint 壓印；印：to impress one's fingers on a card 在卡片上按指印２ affectdeeply; influence 給……深刻印象；使感動：He impressed us as sincere.他的誠懇給我們留下很深的印象。  ▽impression [impress;-ion n.] n.印記；影響；印象 impressive [impress;-ive a.] a.給人以深刻印象的；感人的   oppress [op-(ob-)=against 對抗；press=to press 壓→「to press against 對壓，壓服→」] v. weigh down 使沉重，使煩惱：She was oppressed with worry.她心事重重。２ use power over 壓迫， 壓制：The tyrant oppressed his countrymen.暴君壓迫百姓。  ▽oppression [oppress;-ion n.] n.壓迫（手段）；壓抑，沉悶 oppressive [oppress;-ive a.] a.壓迫的；暴虐的；壓抑的   compress [com-=together 一起；press=to press 壓→] v.１ press together;force into less space 壓緊；壓縮：to compress cotton into bales 將棉花打包２ condence; shorten 壓縮（言語）； 精練：She compressed one-hour lecture into a ten-minute talk.她將一小時的講座壓縮成十分鐘 的訪談。  ▽compression [compress;-ion n.] n.壓緊，壓縮；簡練的措詞 compressive [compress;-ive a.] a.有壓縮力的，起壓縮作用的   depress [de-=down 下；press=to press 壓→] v.１ press down 壓下，按下：Depress the brake pedal.按下剎車閘。２ lessen 減少：to depress the income 減少收入３ make sad or gloomy 使抑鬱，使消沉：The sad movie depressed her.看了那部悲傷的電影她心情抑鬱。  ▽depression [depress;-ion n.] n.按下；降低；抑鬱；蕭條 depressive [depress;-ive a.] a.令人沮喪的；壓抑的   repress [re-=back 回；press=to press 壓→「to press back 壓回去」→] v.１ hold back or keep down 抑制，約束：to repress one's anger 制怒２ hold down or control unfairly 鎮壓，壓制：to repress civil rights 壓制公民權利  ▽repression [repress;-ion n.] n.抑制；壓制；鎮壓 repressive [repress;-ive a.] a.抑制的，壓制的，強制性的   suppress [sup-(sub-)=under 在……之下；press=to press 壓→「to press down 壓在下面」→] v. １ keep back from public knowledge 禁示發表，查禁：to suppress information 封鎖消息２ hold back deliberately 抑制，忍住：to suppress a laugh 忍住不笑３put an end to the activities of 壓 制；禁止：to suppress democratic movement 壓制民主運動  ▽suppression [suppress;-ion n.] n.壓制；禁止；忍住；隱瞞 suppressive [suppress;-ive a.] a.壓制的；起抑製作用的	
76. prob, prov [L, F]=	to test 試驗，驗證 在常用詞probe，probable，prove 和approve 中有一對常用的詞根prob 和prov。prob 來自 拉丁動詞probare，prov 來自它在法語中的形式prover，基本意思都是to test（試驗，驗證）。   probe [prob=to test 試驗；-e→「to test or examine 試驗，檢驗」→]Ⅰv. examine thoroughly or search into 探索；探究：to probe the roots of social problems 探索社會問題的根源→II n. investigation of suspected activity 探查，調查：He ordered the probe into the scandal.他下令調 查該醜聞。  ▽probing [prob(e);-ing a.] a.（好）探索的；（好）探查的   probable [prob=to test 驗證；-able a.=able 可……的→「able to be tested 可受驗證的」→] a. likely occur or prove true 可能發生的，可能成為事實的：a probable outcome 可能的結果  ▽probability [probab(le);-ility n.] n.可能性，或然性 probabilize [probab(le);-ilize v.] v.使成為可能，使有希望 probably [probab(le);-ly ad.] ad.很可能；或許；大概   probate [prob=to test 驗證；-ate v.=to cause 使→「to cause to be tested 使……得以驗證」→] Ⅰv. prove（a will）to be valid 檢驗（遺囑）→Ⅱn. the process of probating a will 遺囑檢驗→III a. of probating a will 遺囑檢驗的   probation [prob=test 試驗；-ation n.=the process 表過程→「the process of testing 試驗的過程」 →] n.１ status or period of trial 試用（期）：a student on probation 試讀生２ status or period of a convicted offender to go free under supervision 緩刑（ 期）： The courts released him on probation.法庭判他緩刑予以開釋。  ▽probationary [probation;-ary a.] a.試用的；緩刑的   reprobate [re-=back 返回；prob=to test 驗證；-ate v. =to cause 使→「to cause someone to go back for testing 使某人返回受驗」→]Ⅰv. criticize sharply 譴責：to reprobate one's evil behaviour 譴責邪惡行為→Ⅱa. wicked;evil 墮落的，邪惡的：reprobate conduct 墮落的行為→III n. wicked person 墮落者，惡棍：a gambling reprobate 賭棍  ▽reprobation [reprobat(e) v.;-ion n.] n.譴責   prove [prov=to test 驗證；-e→] v. establish the truth by evidence or argu-ment 證實，證明：to prove one's innocence 證實自己無罪  ▽proven [prov(e);-en a.] a.被證實的   approve [ap-(ad-)=to 向；prov=to test 驗證；-e→「to test something to someone 向某人驗證 某事」→] v.１ provide evidence for 為……提供證據２ comfirm formally; pass 批准；核准： The Senate voted to approve the bill.參議院投票批准該法案。３ have a favorable view of 贊成， 同意：I can't approve his rude behavior.我不贊成他的粗暴無禮。  ▽approval [approv(e);-al n.] n.贊成，同意；批准，核准 approving [approv(e);-ing a.] a.贊成的，嘉許的   disprove [dis-=not 不；prov=to test 驗證；-e→「to test something to be not true 驗證某事不實」 →] v. prove to be false or wrong;refute 證明……虛偽或不正確；反駁：The latest evidence disproves the theory.最新的證據證明該理論不能成立。  ▽disproval [disprov(e);-al n.] n.反證，證偽；駁斥 disprovable [disprov(e);-able a.] a.可證偽的；可駁斥的	
77. reg, rect [L]=	to rule, to guide, to govern 劃直線，引導，治理 在常用詞region，regular，correct 和direct 中，有一對同源異形根reg 和rect。它們分別來 自拉丁動詞regere 的不定式詞干和動名詞詞干，其基本意思為to rule。在具體的派生詞中， 詞根的意思可能是to rule or lead straight（劃直線）；to rule or guide（引導，指正）；to rule or govern（治理，統治）。在這三種意思中，詞根都內涵著「be right or straight」即「正」，「直」 的概念。   region [reg=to rule or govern 治理；-ion n.=the state 表行為狀態→「the state of ruling 治理的 狀態」→「area under ruling 治理下的地區」→] n.１ administrative area or division 行政區： an autonomous region 自治區２ any area or division 地帶；地區：forest region 林區  ▽regional [region;-al a.] a.地區的；局部的   regular [reg=to rule or lead straight 劃直線；-ular (-ar) a. =like 像……的→「like leading straight 像劃直線似的」→] a.１ according to a rule, or proper 正規的，正式的：regular warfare 正規 戰爭２ happening or done according to a rule or habit, or not changing 有規律的；固定的： regular work 固定工作３ arranged or shaped by a rule 整齊的，勻稱的：a man of regular features 五官端正的人  ▽regularity [regular;-ity n.] n.正規；規律性；整齊；勻稱 regularize [regular;-ize v.] v.使有規律；使規則化；使整齊   correct [cor-(com-)=completely 完全地； rect=to rule or lead straight 劃直線→ 「 to draw a completely straight line 劃筆直的線」→]Ⅰv. make straight or right 改正；糾正：correct mistakes 糾正錯誤→Ⅱa. straight or right 正確的：correct policy 正確的方針  ▽correction [correct v.;-ion n.] n.改正；校正 corrective [correct v.;-ive a.] a.改正的；矯正的   direct [di-(dis-)=apart 離開；rect=to rule or lead straight 劃直線→「to draw a straight line apart form a point 從某點畫出一條直線」→]Ⅰa. straightforward;by the shortest way 直接的；徑直 的：a direct train 直達列車→Ⅱv. １ keep straight; point or aim 保持直線；對準：He directed his gun to the aim.他把槍對準目標。２ point out the proper course to, or guide 指引；指導： Would you direct me to the park?請問到公園怎麼走？  ▽direction [direct v.;-ion n.] n.方向；指導 directive [direct v.;-ive a./n.] a.指引的n.指示 下面再介紹幾個rect 的派生詞。為了簡要起見，把詞根rect 的含義歸納為（be）staight or right， 即「正」或「直」。   erect [e-(ex-)=upward 向上的；rect=be straight or right 正，直→]Ⅰa. being right upward;upright 正對上方的；垂直的：The soldiers held themselves erect.士兵們挺直站著。→Ⅱv.１ set upright;raise 使豎直；使樹立：to erect a flagstaff 豎旗桿２establish;build 建立；樹立：to erect a monument 立紀念碑  ▽erection [erect v.;-ion n.] n.豎立；建立 erective [erect v.;-ive a.] a.直立的；豎起的；建立的 erectile [erect v.;-ile a.] a.可豎直的；可建立的   rectify [rect=straight or right 正，直；-ify v.=to make 使……→「to make right 使正確」→] v. １ correct 糾正：to rectify one's error 糾正錯誤２ reform 改過：to rectify one's life 改過自新３ adjust 校正：to rectify an instrument 校正儀器  ▽rectifiable [rectif(y);-iable a.] a.可糾正的；可調整的 rectification [rectif(y);-ication n.] n.糾正；整頓；校正   rectangle [rect=right 直，垂直的；angle n.角→「figure having only right angles 只有直角的圖 形」→] n. four-sided figure with four right angles 矩形  ▽rectangular [rectang(le);-ular a.] a.矩形的；成直角的   rectilineal [rect=straight 直；-i-;line=line 線；-al a.=of ……的→] a. of a straight line 直線的： rectilineal motion 直線運動	
78. rupt [L]=	to break 破 常用詞corrupt，interrupt，disrupt 和erupt 都是rupt 的派生詞，詞根rupt 是拉丁動詞rumpere 的動名詞詞干，意思相當於to break（破）。   corrupt [cor-(com-)=thoroughly 完全地；rupt =to break 破→「to break thoroughly 完全破壞」 →]Ⅰv. destroy morally;spoil 使腐敗；腐蝕：to corrupt the minds of young people 腐蝕年輕人 的思想→Ⅱa. dishonest;immoral 貪污的；腐敗的：corrupt officials 貪官污吏  ▽corruption [corrupt;-ion n.] n.腐化；貪污 corruptible [corrupt;-ible a.] a.易腐化的；可收買的 interrupt [inter- = between 在……中間；rupt = to break 破→「to break between 在中間破入」 →] v. break into the continuity of;stop temporarily 打斷；中斷：to interrupt the speaker 打斷演 講者  ▽interruption [interrupt;-ion n.] n.打斷；中斷   disrupt [dis-=apart 分開；rupt=to break 破→「to break apart 破開」→] v.１ break up 分裂：to disrupt a nation 分裂一個民族２ upset 破壞：to disrupt a meeting 破壞集會  ▽disruption [disrupt;-ion n.] n.分裂；破壞   erupt [e-(ex-)=out 出；rupt=to break 破→] v. break out, or burst out 爆發；噴出：The volcano erupted at noon.火山在中午爆發。  ▽eruption [erupt;-ion n.] n.爆發；噴發 rupture [rupt = to break 破；-ure n. = the state 表狀態→「the state of breaking 破裂的狀態」 →] n. breaking off 破裂：The rupture between the two countries was healed.兩國間的破裂關係 修復了。   bankrupt [bank=bench 板凳；rupt=to break 破，斷→「the broken bench of a money-exchanger 錢商的斷板凳」→「broken business 破產的生意」→]Ⅰn. person who breaks his business 破 產者→Ⅱ a. broken in business 破產的：The company went bankrupt last year.該公司去年破產 了。  ▽bankruptcy [bankrupt;-cy n.] n.破產；無償付能力   abrupt [ab-=off 分離；rupt =to break 破，裂→「to break off 分裂；分離」→] a.１ very sudden or unexpected, as if broken off（像斷離似的）突然的；出其不意的：The road is full of abrupt turns.這條路有許多急轉彎。２ suddenly sloping 陡峭的：abrupt slope 陡峭的斜坡  ▽abruption [abrupt;-ion n.] n.突然分離；分裂；斷裂   irrupt [ir-(in-)=in 入；rupt=to break 破→] v. break in, or enter forcibly 侵入；闖進：to irrupt into a house 闖入民宅  ▽irruption [irrupt;-ion n.] n.侵入；闖進	
79. sci [L]=	to know 知，曉 常用詞science，scientist，conscience 和conscious，都以詞根sci 為基礎。sci 來自拉丁動詞 scire，意思相當於to know（知，曉）。   science [sci=to know 知；-ence n.=the result 表行為結果→「the result of knowing, or knowledge 知的結果，知識」→] n. systematic knowledge 系統知識；科學：Science means honest, solid knowledge.科學是老老實實的學問。   scientist [scient=science 科學；-ist n.=person 人→] n. person who does work in science 科學工作 者；科學家：a famous scientist 著名的科學家  ▽scientism [sci;-ent;-ism n.] n.科學態度；科學方法 scientific [sci;-ent;-ific a.] a.科學的；系統的；精確的   conscience [con-(com-)=wholly 完全地；sci=to know 知道；-ence n.=the state 表狀態→「the state of knowing wholly in mind 內心完全知道」→] n. inner sense that knows the difference between right and wrong 良知，良心：for conscience' sake 憑良心  ▽conscienceless [conscience;-less a.] a.沒良心的 conscientious [con-;sci;-ent;-ious a.] a.本著良心行事的   conscious [con-(com-)表加強詞義；sci=to know 知道；-ous a.=having the quality 有……性質的 →「having the ability of knowing well 有知覺能力的」→] a.１ having the knowledge or feeling of 有意識的；有感覺的/I was conscious that I had made a mistake.我意識到自己犯了錯誤。２ aware 神志清醒的：He is badly hurt but still conscious.他傷勢很重，但神志依然清醒。  ▽consciousness [conscious;-ness n.] n.意識；覺悟   subconscious [sub-=under, imperfectly 下，不完全地；conscious a. 有意識的→「imperfectly conscious 不完全有意識的」→] a. not fully known by the mind;present at a hidden level of the mind 下意識的；潛意識的：subconscious desire 下意識的慾望   omniscient [omni-=all 全；sci=to know 知；-ent a.=having the quality 有……性質的→「having the ability to know all 能知一切的」→] a. having infinite knowledge 無所不知的：Do you believe in an omniscient man?你相信存在著無所不知的人嗎？  ▽omniscience [omni-;sci;-ence n.] n.無所不知；（大寫）上帝   nescience [ne-=not 不；sci=to know 知；-ence n.=the state 表狀態→「the state of not knowing 不知」→] n. absence of knowledge 無知，缺乏知識：He admitted his nescience of the subject. 他承認對該學科一無所知。  ▽nescient [ne-;sci;-ent a.] a.無知的   prescient [pre-=beforehand 事先的；sci =to know 知；-ent a.=having the quality 有……性質的 →] a. having the ability to know beforehand;able to know what will happen 能預知的；有先見 的：I don't think that he was prescient of the incident.我認為他不可能預知那個事件的發生。  ▽prescience [pre-;sci;-ence n.] n.預知；先見	
80. scrib, script [L]=	to write 寫 scrib 和script 是一對同源異形根。scrib 是拉丁動詞scribere 的不定式詞干，script 是動名詞 詞干，意思是to write（寫）。在英語中，scrib 多出現在動詞中；script 則出現在相應的名詞 和形容詞中。   describe [de-=down 下；scrib=to write 寫；-e→「to write down 寫下」→] v. give an account of 寫；敘述：Can you describe his appearance?你能描述一下他的外貌嗎？  ▽description [de-;script;-ion n.] n.描寫；敘述 descriptive [de-;script;-ive] a.描寫的；敘述的   inscribe [in-=in 入；scrib =to write 寫；-e→「to write something in some place 把某物寫入某處」 →] v.１ write (one's name) in (a book, etc.)題寫；題名：The author inscribed a copy of his book to his best friend.作者題名贈書給好友。２ write by marking into a surface 刻寫；銘刻：The monument is inscribed with the names of martyrs.紀念碑上銘刻著烈士的英名。  ▽inscription [in-;script;-ion n.] n.銘刻；碑文；題詞 inscriptive [in-;script;-ive a.] a.銘文的；題詞的 prescribe [pre- = beforehand 事先；scrib = to write 寫；-e→「to write beforehand 事先寫好」 →] v. １ set down a rule to be followed 規定：The invitation prescribed formal dress. 請柬上寫 明要正式著裝。２ order the use of medicine or treatment 開（處方）：The doctor prescribed his patient a complete rest.醫生要求病人全休。  ▽prescription [pre-;script;-ion n.] n.規定；處方 prescriptive [pre-;script;-ive a.] a.規定的；約定俗成的   subscribe [sub-=underneath 在下方；scrib=to write 寫；-e→「to write one's name underneath as to show agreement 把名字寫在下方以示同意」→] v. １ sign 簽署：We all subscribed our names to the written statement.我們都在聲明書上簽了名。２ agree to pay money for the delivery (of a newspaper, magazine, etc. )訂閱（報刊、雜誌等）：to subscribe to China Daily 訂 閱《中國日報》  ▽subscriber [subscrib(e);-er n.] n.簽署者；訂閱者 subscription [sub-;script;-ion n.] n.簽署；同意；訂閱(費) subscript [sub-;script] a.寫在下方的   proscribe [pro-=before 在……面前；scrib=to write 寫；-e→「to write (an outlaw's name) before the public 在公眾面前寫出（罪犯的名字）」→] v.１ outlaw, or banish 剝奪公民權；放逐：He was proscribed from the realm.他被驅逐出境。２ prohibit 禁止：to proscribe germ warfare 禁 止細菌戰  ▽proscription [pro-;script;-ion n.] n.禁止；剝奪公民權 proscriptive [pro-;script;-ive a.] a.禁止的；剝奪公民權的   transcribe [tran-(trans-)=from...to...從……到……；scrib=to write 寫；-e→「to write from one place to another 從一個地方轉寫到另一個地方」→] v. copy from an original 轉抄；謄寫：to transcribe shorthand notes 謄寫速記稿  ▽transcript [tran(s)-;script] n.抄本；謄本；副本   ascribe [a-(ad-)=upon 在……之上；scrib=to write 寫；-e→「to write a result upon 把結果記 在……之上」→] v. attribute to 把……歸因於：to ascribe success to hard work 把成功歸因於 努力  ▽ascription [a-;script;-ion n.] n.（功過等的）歸於   postscript [post-=after 在……之後；script =to write 寫→「that which is written after 寫在後面 的東西」→] n. the part written in a letter after the signature 信後的附言   scripture [script=to write 寫； -ure n.=thing 物→ 「 written thing 書寫的東西」 → ] n. １ handwriting;document 手寫稿； 文件２ holy book of a religion 宗教經典： the Buddhist scriptures 佛經	
81. sect [L]=	to cut 切 在常用section，sector 和insect 中有個拉丁詞根sect。它來自拉丁動詞secare 的動名詞詞干， 意為to cut（切）。   section [sect=to cut 切；-ion n.=the result 表結果→「the result of cutting something 切割某物 的結果」→] n.１ part cut off 切下的部分，塊：to cut the cake into four sections 把蛋糕切成 四塊２ separate part of any-thing（事物的）部分：the richer sections of town 城鎮中富裕的 地區  ▽sectional [section;-al a.] a.部分的；局部的；地區的 subsection [sub-;section] n.分部，小類；分段，小節   sector [sect=to cut 切；-or n.=thing 物→「something that is cut off 被切下之物」→] n.１ part cut off from the whole 部分：a sector of a circle 扇形２distinct part of society（社會的）部門，行 業：the manufacturing sector 製造業  ▽sectorial [sector;-ial a.] a.扇形的   insect [in-=into 成為；sect=to cut 切→「an animal looking like being cut into several parts 看起 來好像身體被切成幾部分的動物」→] n. anthropad having a body divided into three parts 昆蟲： Beetles, ants and flies are all insects.甲蟲、螞蟻和蒼蠅都是昆蟲。  ▽insectual [insect;-u-;-al a.] a.昆蟲似的；小蟲子似的   bisect [bi-=two 二；sect=to cut 切分→] v. cut into two equal parts 把……平分：Use the compass to bisect an angle.用羅盤平分方位角。  ▽bisector [bisect;-or n.] n. [數]平分線   dissect [dis-=apart 分；sect =to cut 切→「to cut apart 切開」→] v.１ cut apart (an animal body, etc.) to examine its parts 解剖：to dissect a frog 解剖青蛙２ examine part by part 仔細分析：to dissect a problem 仔細分析問題  ▽dissection [dissect;-ion n.] n.解剖；分析 dissector [dissect;-or n.] n.解剖者，解剖學家；分析者   intersect [inter-=between 在……之間；sect=to cut 切→「to cut between 在……之間切過去」 →] v.１ cut across 橫切：The highway intersects the town.公路穿城而過。２ meet and cross 交叉：Two lines intersect at point A.兩線在A 點相交。  ▽intersection [intersect;-ion n.] n.橫斷；交叉（點）   transect [tran-(trans-)=arcoss 橫穿；sect=to cut 切→] v. cut arcoss 橫切，橫斷：The ridge transects north of this province.該山脈橫穿這個省的北部。  ▽transection [transect;-ion n.] n.橫切；橫斷面   vivisect [viv=alive 活的；-i-;sect=to cut 切→「to cut alive 切割活物」→] v. cut into or dissect (a living animal)解剖（動物活體）：The Japanese troops vivisected human bodies in World WarⅡ. 日本軍隊在二戰中用人體進行活體解剖。  ▽vivisection [vivisect;-ion n.] n.活體解剖	
82. sent, sens [L]=	to feel 感覺 在常用詞sentence，sentiment，sense，nonsense 中，有一對同源異形根sent 和sens。它們 分別來自拉丁動詞sentire 和它的動名詞sensum，意思相當於to feel（感覺）。 sentence [sent =to feel 感覺；-ence n. =thing 物→「expression of one's feeling or meaning 表達 感覺或想法的東西」→] n. number of words giving a complete sense or meaning 句子（意思完 整的一組詞）：a simple sentence 簡單句   sentiment [sent=to feel 感覺；-i-;-ment n.=the state or result 表狀態或結果→「the state or result of feeling 感覺或感覺的結果」→] n. tender of fine feeling;thought arising from feeling 情感；思 想感情：a man of sentiment 感情豐富的人  ▽sentimental [sentiment;-al a.] a.多愁善感的；感傷的 presentiment [pre-;sentiment] n.預感   sense [sens=to feel 感覺；-e→]Ⅰn. faculty of feeling;inward feeling 感官；感覺：the sense of smell 嗅覺→Ⅱv. have a feeling without being told 感覺，意識到：He sensed danger and stopped moving.他意識到危險，就站住不動。  ▽senseless [sense n.;-less a.] a.無知覺的；無感覺的 sensible [sens(e) v.;-ible a.] a.感覺得到的   nonsense [non-=no 無；sense n.感覺，意義→「no sense 沒有意義」→] n.１ speech or writing with no meaning 廢話：I want no more of your nonsense.我不許你再瞎說了。２anything meaningless or absure 胡鬧：It's all nonsense.這全是胡鬧。  ▽nonsensical [nonsens(e);-ical a.] a.無意義的；荒謬的   consent [con-(com-)=together 共同；sent=to feel 感覺→「to feel together with others 與他人共 同感覺到」→] v. be of the same feeling;agree 同感；同意：The committee consented to the plan. 委員會同意那項計劃。  ▽consentient [consent;-ient a.] a.同意的；贊成的 consensus [con-;sens;-us n.] n.（意見的）一致；輿論   dissent [dis-=apart 分離；sent=to feel 感覺→「to feel apart from others 與他人感覺相分離」 →] v. think differently;disagree in opinion 持異議；不同意：He and I dissent from each other.我 與他意見不一致。  ▽dissentient [dissent;-i-;-ent a.] a.（對多數人意見）不同意的 dissension [dis-;sens;-ion n.] n.意見分歧；不和   assent [as-(ad-)=to 對；sent=to feel 感覺→「to feel agreeable to something 對某事感覺良好」 →]Ⅰv. express agreement;consent 贊同；同意：I [re-=against 對抗；sent=to feel 感覺→「to feel against 覺得與……相對抗」→] v. feel angry or bitter at 對……怨恨：He resents being called a fool.他恨人家叫他傻瓜。  ▽resentment [resent;-ment n.] n.怨恨；不滿 resentful [resent;-ful a.] a.忿恨的；不滿的   sensitive [sens=to feel 感覺；-itive (-ive) a.=having a special quality 有……特點的→「having a special ability of feeling 有特別的感覺能力的」→] a. quick to feel the effect of 敏感的：His ears are highly sensitive to any unusual sound in the machine.他的耳朵對機器的異常聲音十分敏 感。  ▽sensitivity [sensitiv(e);-ity n.] n.敏感性；靈敏性 sensitize [sens;-itize(-ize) v.] v.使敏感；變敏感 sensuous [sens = to feel 感覺；-u-; -ous a. = belonging to ……的→「belonging to feeling or sense of feeling 屬於感覺或感官方面的」→] a.１of senses 感官方面的：sensuous delight 感 官上的樂趣２ giving pleasure of senses 給人以美感的：a sensuous painting 一幅引起美感的 畫	
83. sequ, secut [L]=	to follow 跟隨 常用詞consequent，subsequent，consecutive 和execute 是同根詞。其中詞根sequ 來自拉 丁動詞sequi；詞根secut 來自其過去分詞secutus，這對詞根的意思相當於to follow（跟隨）。   consequent [con-(com-)=completely 完全地； sequ=to follow 跟隨； -ent a.=-ing … … 的→ 「following completely or closely 緊緊跟隨的」→] a. following as an effect;resulting 隨之發生 的；作為結果的：The reces-sion has a consequent impact on jobs.經濟蕭條隨之影響了就業機 會。   subsequent [sub-=under 在……之下；sequ=to follow 跟隨；-ent a.=-ing……的→「following under 跟在下面的」→] a. occurring after;succeeding 繼……之後的，隨後的：In subsequent lessons the teacher made his points clearer.在隨後的講課中，老師把觀點說得更清楚。   sequence [sequ=to follow 跟隨；-ence n.=the quality or condition 表性質或狀態→「the quality or condition of following 表性質或狀態」→] n.１series of things 連貫，接續：a sequence of calamities 連二接三的災禍２the following of one thing after another 次序，順序：in alphabetical sequence 按字母順序  ▽sequential [sequ;-ent;-ial a.] a.連續的；順序的   sequel [sequ=to follow 跟隨；-el n.=thing 事物→「thing that follows 跟隨其後的事物」→] n. １ something that develops from something else 結果，結局：The sequel of war is often famine. 戰爭的結果經常是饑荒。２book, play, etc. that continues 續篇，續集：a sequel to the novel 小說的續集   consecutive [con-(com-）=together 一起；secut=to follow 跟隨；-ive a.=-ing……的→「following together 一起跟隨著的」→] a. following one after another 連續的，連貫的：five consecutive days 連續5 天  ▽consecution [con-;secut;-ion n.] n.連貫；邏輯順序   execute [ex-=out 出；(s)ecut=to follow 跟隨；-e→「to follow out of the procedure 跟著程序出 來」→] v. １ carry out 實行，執行：to execute a command 執行命令２ put to death according to law 對……執行死刑：The murderer was executed in the electric chair. 殺人犯被電刑處決。  ▽executive [execut(e);-ive a.] a.執行的；行政的；經理人員的 executor [execut(e);-or n.] n.執行者；指定的遺囑執行人   persecute [per-=throughout 始終；secut=to follow 跟隨；-e→「to follow throughout 始終跟隨 不放」→] v.１ annoy without stopping 跟……糾纏：I was persecuted by mosquitoes last night. 昨夜我飽受蚊子的騷擾。２ treat cruelly or unfairly 虐待，迫害：These sects were persecuted and suppressed.這些教派受到迫害和鎮壓。  ▽persecutee [persecut(e);-ee n.] n.受虐待者；受迫害者   prosecute [pro-=forward 向前；secut=to follow 跟隨；-e→「to follow forward 跟隨向前」→] v. １ follow up or carry forward to completion 徹底進行；執行：to prosecute an investigation 徹 底進行調查２begin legal proceedings against 對……起訴：to prosecute somebody for murder 以謀殺罪起訴某人  ▽prosecutor [prosecut(e);-or n.] n.檢察官；公訴人；起訴人 prosecutive [prosecut(e);-ive a.] a.起訴的；檢舉的	
84. sid, sess [L]=	to sit 坐 在常用詞president，reside，session 和possess 中，有一對同源異形根sid 和sess。sid 來自 拉丁動詞sidere 的不定式詞干，sess 來自動名詞詞干，其意思相當於to sit（坐）或to settle （安放）。   preside [pre-=before 前；sid=to sit 坐；-e→「to sit before others 坐在其他人前面」→] v. sit in authority;act as chairman 主持；作會議主席：to preside at a meeting 主持會議  ▽presider [presid(e);-er n.] n.（會議的）主席；主持者 presidium [presid(e);-ium n.] n.主席團；常務委員會 president [presid(e) v.主持，當權；-ent n.=person 人→] n. person chosen to preside over a nation, university or any other organization 總統；大學校長；會長；社長等  ▽presidency [pre-;sid;-ency n.] n.總統等的職位或任期 presidential [president;-ial a.] a.總統（或校長等）的   reside [re-=back, down 回，下；sid=to sit or settle 坐，安放；-e→「to sit backward, to settle down 靠背安坐，安頓下來」→] v. make one's home at a place 安家，居住：to reside in the city 在城 市居住  ▽resident [resid(e);-ent n.] n.居民 residence [resid(e);-ence n.] n.居住；住宅   subside [sub-=under, down 下；sid=to sit or settle 坐，停留；-e→「to settle down 停在下面， 停息」→] v.１ sink down 下沉；沉降：The building subsides gradually.這座房子逐漸下沉。２ fall into a state of quiet 平息：The wind has subsided.風停了。  ▽subsidence [subsid(e);-ence n.] n.下降；沉降；平息   dissident [dis-=apart 分開；sid=to sit 坐；-ent n.=person 人→「person who sits apart from others 與別人分開坐的人」→] n. person openly disagreeing with an opinion; 85. sign [L]=	mark 記號 常用詞sign，signal，signature 和signify 中含有一個常用的拉丁詞根sign，它來自拉丁名詞 signum 或拉丁動詞signare 的詞幹部分，意思為mark（記號）或to mark（加記號）。   sign [sign=mark, or to mark（加）記號→]Ⅰn.１ mark or symbol 86. sist [L]=	to stand 站立 常用詞assist，consist，insist 和resist 的詞根是sist，它來自拉丁動詞sistere，意思是to stand （站立）。   assist [as-(ad-)=to, at 在；sist=to stand 站→「to stand at one's side 站在某人身邊」→] v. help 幫助：He [re-=against 對抗；sist=to stand 站立→「to stand against 對立」→] v. fight against;oppose 抵抗；反對：to resist an aggression 反抗侵略  ▽resistance [resist;-ance n.] n.抵抗；反抗 resistible [resist;-ible a.] a.抵抗得住的   exist [ex-=out 出來；(s)ist=to stand 站→「to stand out or forth 站出來」→「to appear 出現」 →] v.１ have an actual being 實際存在：The Roman Empire existed for several centuries. 古羅 馬帝國歷時數百年之久。２ be real, or live 生存：We can't exist without air.沒有空氣我們就無 法生存。  ▽existence [exist;-ence n.] n.存在；存在物；生存   persist [per-=throughout 始終；sist=to stand 站→「to stand throughout 始終站著」→] v.１ continue firmly 堅持：He persisted in the experiment and succeeded in the end.他堅持實驗終獲 成功。２ continue to exist 繼續存在，持續：The bad weather will persist for several days.壞天 氣還會持續好幾天。  ▽persistence [persist;-ence n.] n.堅持；持續   desist [de-=away 離開；sist=to stand 站立→「to stand away from one's job 離開工作站在一旁」 →] v. leave off;cease 撇下；停止：As soon as the teacher went away, they desisted from reading. 老師一走開，他們就扔下書不念了。  ▽desistence [desist;-ence n.] n.停止   subsist [sub-=under 在……之下；sist =to stand 站立→「to stand under some pressure 在壓力 之下站立著」→] v. １ stand fast, or remain 堅持；維持：A school cannot subsist without students.沒有學生學校就無法維持。２ keep alive 維持生活，生存：to subsist on wages 靠工 資為生  ▽subsistence [subsist;-ence n.] n.生存；生活維持費	
87. speci, spect, spic [L]=	to look 看 標題中的三個異形根都來自拉丁動詞specere，意為to look（看）。其中，speci 是不定式詞 干；spic 是spec 的音變異體；spect 是specere 的強調形式動詞spectare 的詞干，它的孳生 力最強。   expect [ex-=out 外；(s)pect=to look 看→「to look out for something 向外看望著某物」→] v. １ look forward to 盼望；期待：I expect that he will come.我盼望他會來。２ require 要求；期望： You are expected to finish it in time.希望你及時完成這項工作。  ▽expectancy [expect;-ancy n.] n.期待；期望；期望的事物 expectant [expect;-ant a.] a.期待的；期望的 expectation [expect;-ation a.] n.期待；期望；[複數]前程   inspect [in-=into 入；spect=to look 看→] v. look into;examine carefully 檢查；審查：to inspect fingerprints 檢查指紋  ▽inspection [inspect;-ion n.] n.檢查；審查 inspector [inspect;-or n.] n.檢查員；監察員   respect [re-=again 再；spect=to look 看→「to look again 再看，重看」→]Ⅰv.１ treat with consideration 重視：to respect one's wishes 重視某人的意願２ have regard to 尊重，尊敬：to respect teachers 尊敬老師→Ⅱn. honour and esteem 尊敬：to show respect for the aged 尊敬老 人  ▽respectable [respect v.;-able a.] a.可敬的 respectful [respect n.;-ful a.] a.恭敬的；尊重他人的 disrespect [dis-;respect v./n.] v.不尊重，不尊敬n.無禮，失禮   prospect [pro-=forward 向前；spect=to look 看→「to look forward 向前看」→] n.１ something that one looks forward to 盼望的事物：A rich harvest is in prospect.豐收在望。２ distant or wide view;scene 遠景，視野；景象：The hill commands a fine prospect.從這座山可以眺望美景。  ▽prospective [prospect;-ive a.] a.預期的；未來的   suspect [sus-(sub-)=under 在……下面；(s)pect=to look 看→「to look at someone from under or askance 私下斜眼看某人」→] v. doubt;imagine to be guilty 不信任；懷疑有罪過：I suspect him to be a pickpocket.我懷疑他是扒手。  ▽suspectable [suspect;-able a.] a.可疑的 suspicion [sus-;(s)pic;-ion n.] n.懷疑；嫌疑 suspicious [sus-;(s)pic;-i-;-ous a.] a.可疑的；多疑的   spectator [spect=to look 看；-ator n.=person 人→] n. person who looks at or watches an event, sport, etc.旁觀者；觀眾：spectators at a football match 足球賽的觀眾   spectacle [spect=to look 看；-acle n.=thing 物→「things for people to look at 供人們觀看的東西」 →] n.１ something exhibited to public view 公開的場面：The opening ceremony was a fine spectacle.開幕式的場面很壯觀。２ grand public sight or scene 壯觀；奇景：Viewed from theseashore, the sunrise is indeed a spectacle.從海邊看去，日出真是個奇觀。  ▽spectacular [specta(cle);-cular a.] a.壯觀的；驚人的 以下介紹幾個由spec 或spic 構成的本族同根詞。 species [spec = to look 看；-ies n. = thing(s) 物→「thing(s) that can be looked at or seen 可以看 見的物體」→「visible form of thing(s)物體的形式或外觀」→] n.１ kind or sort 種類：a species of advertisement 一種廣告２ group of individuals having common characteritics, placed under a genus 種；物種：Wheat is a species of grass.小麥是禾本植物的一種。  ▽speciate [spec;-iate v.] v. [生物]物種形成 specific [spec;-ific a.] a.特有的；特定的；[生物]種的 speciology [spec;-i-;-ology n.] n. [生物]物種學 special [spec;-ial a.] a.特殊的；特別的 specious [spec = to look 看；-i-; -ous a. = full of 富於……的→「full of good looking 富於好看的， 外觀的」→] a. looking well at first sight;showy and deceptive 外表美觀的；華而不實的：a specious person 華而不實的人  ▽speciosity [spec;-i-;-osity n.] n.外表美觀；華而不實   conspicuous [con-(com-)=altogether 完全；spic=to look 看；-u-;-ous a.=tending to 易於……的 →「tending to be looked at altogether 容易一下子被看見的」→] a. easily seen, or noticeable 明顯的；惹人注目的：conspicuous errors 明顯的錯誤 auspice [au (avis) = bird 鳥；spic = to look or observe 觀看；-e→「to observe birds' flying in order to foretell fortune 觀察飛鳥以預示運氣」→] n.１ omen drawn by observing birds 根據飛鳥行 動所做的占卜２ forecast; augury 預言；預兆３ (pl.) patronage 保護，贊助：a school under civilian auspices 民辦學校  ▽auspicious [auspic(e);-i-;-ous a.] a.吉利的，吉祥的   despise [de-=down 向下；spis (spic 的異體)=to look 看；-e→] v. look down upon 看不起，鄙視： Don't cheat or you will be despised.不要作弊，不然會被瞧不起的。  ▽despicable [de-;spic;-able a.] a.可鄙的；卑鄙的	
88. spir [L]=	to breathe 呼吸 spirit（精神），inspire（鼓舞），conspire（共謀）和respire（呼吸）等表面意思互不相關的 詞卻有共同的詞根spir，它來自拉丁動詞spirare，意思等於to breathe（呼吸）。   spirit [spir=to breathe 呼吸；-it n.=the act 表行為→「breathing or breath 呼吸，氣息」→「vital principle 生存的要素」→「soul 靈魂」→] n. one's soul or mind;the principle of thought 靈魂； 精神：body and spirit 肉體和精神  ▽spiritual [spirit;-u-;-al a.] a.精神的；心靈的 spiritless [spirit;-less a.] a.沒精打采的；灰心的 spiritism [spirit;-ism n.] n.招魂論；招魂術 inspirit [in-v.;spirit] v.鼓舞；激勵   inspire [in-=into 入；spir=to breathe 呼吸；-e→「to breathe into body or mind 吸入空氣，注入 生氣」→] v. １ draw in (air)吸（氣）２ giveencouragement to 鼓舞，激勵：The teacher inspired us to greater efforts.老師鼓勵我們作更大的努力。  ▽inspirator [in-;spir;-ator n.] n.吸入器 inspiratory [in-;spir;-atory a.] a.吸入的；吸氣的 conspire [con-(com-) = together 共同；spir = to breathe 呼吸；-e→「to breathe together 呼吸 與共，同氣相求」→] v. plot or scheme together 共謀；陰謀：The criminals conspired to rob a bank. 罪犯們圖謀搶劫銀行。  ▽conspiracy [conspir(e);-acy n.] n.陰謀；共謀 conspirator [con-;spir;-ator n.] n.陰謀家；共謀者   respire [re-=again 再；spir=to breathe 呼吸；-e→] v. breathe again and again;take breath 呼吸（尤 指連續地）；歇口氣：The patient respired smoothly.患者呼吸通暢。  ▽respirable [respir(e);-able a.] a.能呼吸的 respirator [re-;spir;-ator n.] n.呼吸器；口罩 respiratory [re-;spir;-atory a.] a.呼吸（作用）的   aspire [a-(ad-)=towards 向；spir=to breathe 呼吸；-e→「to breathe hard towards a goal 向著目 標努力吸氣」→] v.１ aim at, or strive for 追求：to aspire after truth 追求真理２ desire eagerly 渴望：He aspires to be an artist.他渴望成為科學家。  ▽aspirer [aspir(e),-er n.] n.渴望者；追求者 aspirant [aspir(e);-ant n.] a.有上進心的；有野心的   expire [ex-=out 出；(s)pir=to breathe 呼吸；-e→] v.１ breathe out 呼出，吐氣：The whales expire air from the lungs.鯨魚從肺部呼氣。２ die 斷氣，死亡：He expired at midnight.他半夜斷了氣。 ３ come to an end 期滿，終止：The agreement expires on Monday.該協議於星期一期滿。  ▽expiratory [ex-;(s)pir;-atory a.] a.呼氣的；吐氣的 perspire [per- =through 通過；spir =to breathe 呼吸；-e→「to breathe through the pores 通過 毛孔呼吸」→] v. sweat 出汗，排汗：Man must perspire all the time.人必須不斷排汗。  ▽perspirable [perspir(e);-able a.] a.汗液可通過的 perspiratory [per-;spir;-atory a.] a.排汗的；引起排汗的   transpire [trans-=across 穿過；(s)pir=to breathe 呼吸；-e→「to breathe out across the surface 穿過表面呼出去」→] v.１ give off (water-vapour) through leaves 散發；蒸發２ leak out, or become known 洩露；為人所知：It later transpired that the king had been ill then.後來才透露 說，當時國王已經病了。  ▽transpiration [trans-;(s)pir;-ation n.] n.蒸發[植物]蒸騰作用	
89. st, stat [L]=	to stand 站立 st 和stat 是一對很重要的同源異形根。st 來自拉丁動詞stare；stat 是它的動名詞詞干，意思 都是to stand（站立）。（大家可能會想起，詞根sist 的意思也是to stand；其實，sist 的詞源 也是stare。）   state [st=to stand 站立；-ate n.=thing 物→「that which stands or is set up 立著的物體，建立的 東西」→] n.１ the general mode of things that stand around 總的模樣，狀態：the state of war 戰爭狀態２ the political organization which is set up in a country 政府；國家：capitalist states 資本主義國家  ▽statehood [state;-hood n.] n.國家地位 stateless [state;-less a.] a.無國家的；無國籍的 stately [state;-ly a.] a.尊嚴的，莊重的；雄偉的   station [stat=to stand 站立； -ion n.=the act or state 表行為或狀態→ ] n. １ standing; standing-place; position 停留；站立點；位置２ fixed standing-place for trains, buses, planes, etc. 車站；機場等：railway station 火車站  ▽stationary [station;-ary a.] a.固定的；靜止的 stay [stay (stat)=to stand 站立→] v. stand and remain rather than go on or leave 停留：Stay here until I return.呆這兒等我回來。   distance [di-(dis-)=apart 分離；st=to stand 站立；-ance n.=the state 表狀態→「the state of standing apart 分立的狀態」→] n.１ separation in space;remoteness 相距；遠隔：The picture looks better at a distance.這幅畫遠看更好。２ amount of separation in space or time（空間或 時間的）距離：a distance of 20 miles 20 英里距離  ▽distant [di-;st;-ant a.] a.在遠處的；久遠的   constant [con-(com-)=thoroughly 徹底地；st=to stand 站立；-ant a.=-ing……的→「standing thoroughly 始終站立的」→] a.１ fixed or firm 堅定的：a constant believer in science 堅信科學 的人２ continual 持續的：constant growth 持續增長３ unchanging 不變的：constant temperature room 恆溫室  ▽constancy [con-;st;-ancy n.] n.堅定；經久不變   circumstance [circum-=around 周圍；st=to stand 站立；-ance n.=thing 物→「thing standing around 在周圍站立的東西」→] n. fact, condition or event concerned 有關事實、情況等：I want to consider each circum-stance in turn.我要逐一考慮有關情況。  ▽circumstantial [circum-;st;-ant;-ial a.] a.按情況的；偶然的 contrast [contra- = in opposition 相對；st = to stand 站立→「to stand in opposition 相對而立」 →]Ⅰv. set in opposition in order to show differ-ence 使對比：to contrast good and evil 對比善 與惡→Ⅱn. difference in things contrasted 對比物之間的差別：the striking contrast between wealth and poverty 貧富之間的懸殊差別   ecstasy [ec-(ex-)=out of 外；st=to stand 站立；-asy (-acy) n.=the state 表狀態→「the state of standing out of one's own place because of joy 因為高興站到自己位置之外去」→] n. being put out of the normal mental state;excessive joy 出神，入迷；狂喜：He listened to the music with ecstasy.他聽音樂聽得出了神。  ▽ecstasize [ecstas(y);-ize v.] v.使入迷；使狂喜 ecstatic [ec-;stat;-ic a.] a.入迷的；欣喜若狂的   obstacle [ob-=in the way 攔阻；st=to stand 站立；-acle n.=thing 物→] n. anything that stands in the way and hinders advance 障礙物：to over-come obstales to progress 排除前進的障礙   rest [re-=back 後；st =to stand 站立→「to stand back or stay behind 站在後面，留在後頭」→] Ⅰv.１ stay, or remain 停留；餘下２ remain or still be 保持著，依然是：The affair rests a riddle. 這件事依然是個謎。→Ⅱ n. persons that still remain;what is left 其餘的人；剩餘部分：Ten of us will go, the rest are to stay here.我們去十個人，其餘的留在這兒。	
90. tang, tact [L]=	to touch 接觸 tang 和tact 是一對同源異形根，tang 來自拉丁動詞tangere 的不定式詞干，tact 是動名詞詞 干，意思相當於to touch（接觸）。   contact [con-(com-)=wholly 完全地；tact=to touch 接觸→]Ⅰn. touch;meeting 接觸；聯繫：to come into contact with new ideas 接觸新思想→Ⅱv. touch;get in touch with 接觸；與……聯 系：Please contact our office. 請與我們辦公室聯繫。→III a. having or keeping touch with 保持 接觸的：contact battle 遭遇戰  ▽contactual [contact n.;-u-;-al a.] a.接觸的 contactor [contact v.;-or n.] n.接觸器；開關   tact [tact=to touch 接觸→「skill in making touch with others 與他人接觸的技巧」→] n. skill in avoiding what would offend;quick sense of what is proper or right the sense of touch 觸 覺的：tactile organs 觸覺器官２ that can be felt by touching 能觸知的：This cloth gives a good tactile impression.這種布料手感很好。  ▽tactility [tactil(e);-ity n.] n.觸知性；觸覺能力   intact [in-=not 不；tact =to touch 觸→「not touched 未被觸動的」→] a. remaining whole because no part has been touched or spoiled 完整無缺的：The fire destroyed the house but left the garage intact.房子被燒了，車庫卻完好無損。 tangent [tang = to touch 觸；-ent n. = thing 物→] n. line that touches a curved line at a point 切 線：Line A is a tangent of the circle.直線A 是圓的切線。  ▽tangential [tangent;-i-;-al a.] a.切線的；正切的   tangible [tang=to touch 觸；-ible a.=capable of 可……的→「capable of being touched 可接觸 的，可觸知的」→] a.１having a touchable ordefinite shape 有形的：tangible assets 有形資產 ２ clear and certain;real 明確的；確實的：tangible proof 確鑿證據  ▽tangibility [tangib(le);-ility n.] n.有形性；確實性   contagious [con-(com-)=with 與；tag (tang 的變體)=to touch 接觸；-ious a.=characterized by 有……特點的→「characterized by touching with others 特別會與其他人或物接觸的」→] a. １communicable by contact 可傳染的；有感染力的：contagious laughter 有感染力的笑聲２ that can carry disease by contact 接觸傳染的：contagious disease 傳染病  ▽contagion [con-;tag;-ion n.] n.接觸傳染；傳染病；感染；傳播 contagiosity [con-;tag;-i-;-osity n.] n.接觸傳染率 contagium [con-;tag;-i-;-um n.] n.接觸傳染物	
91. ten, tin, tent, tain [L]=	to hold 握，持 這組異體詞根有四個：ten 是基本形式，它來自拉丁動詞tenere 的不定式詞干，意思相當於 to hold（握，持）；tent 來自動名詞詞干；tin 是ten 在某些前綴之後的音變形式；tain 是ten 的重讀形式，是從法語轉引進英語的，它在英語中的構詞能力很強。   contain [con-(com-)=together 一起；tain=to hold 保持→「to hold together 保持在一起」→] v. １ hold, or be able to hold 容納；裝得下：The hall can hold a hundred people.這大廳裝得下一 百人。２ include 包含：Sea water contains salt. 海水含鹽分。３ hold within bounds;restrain 控制；抑制：to contain oneself 自製  ▽container [contain;-er n.] n.容器；集裝箱 containment [contain;-ment n.] n.抑制；遏制；牽制 content [con-;tent] n.容量；內容a.滿足的   detain [de-=away 離；tain=to hold 保持→「to hold away from free action 約束使之無自由」→] v.１ stop or delay 阻留：I was detained by heavy traffic.交通擁擠把我給耽誤了。２ hold or confine in jail 拘留；扣押：to detain the suspect 拘留疑犯  ▽detainee [detain;-ee n.] n.被拘留者 detention [de-;tent;-ion n.] n.拘留；阻留   obtain [ob-=against 對抗；tain=to hold 握住→「to hold against difficulty 頂住困難把握住」→] v. １ get hold of by efforts 獲取；取得：to obtain freedom through stuggle 通過鬥爭獲得自由 ２ gain;get 得到；買到：Where did you obtain this book?你在哪裡買到這本書？  ▽obtainer [obtain;-er n.] n.獲得者 obtainment [obtain;-ment n.] n.獲得；取得；買到   retain [re-=back 回；tain=to hold 保持→「to hold back for oneself 保持為己所有」→] v. keep in one's possession, use, or mind 保有；保留；記住：My mind can't retain these figures.我的腦子 記不住這些數字。  ▽retention [re-;tent;-ion n.] n.保持；記憶（力） retentive [re-;tent;-ive a.] a.保持的；記憶力強的   sustain [sus-(sub-)=under 在……下面；tain=to hold 保持，支持→「to hold from under 在下面 支持著」→] v.１ hold up, or uphold 支撐；承擔：A few pillars sustain the roof. 幾根柱子撐住 屋頂。２ support, or provide for 支持；供養：He sustains the whole family.他一人養活全家。  ▽sustention [sus-;tent;-ion n.] n.支持；供養 sustenance [sus-;ten;-ance n.] n.食物；營養   abstain [abs-(ab-)=from 離；tain=to hold 保持，約束→「to hold oneself from 約束自己離開」 →] v. １ keep from 避開：to abstain from voting 不參加投票２ restrain 戒；節制：to abstain from wine 戒酒  ▽abstention [abs-;tent;-ion n.] n.戒；避開 以下介紹幾個ten 和tin 的同根派生詞。   tenant [ten=to hold 保持，佔有；-ant n.=person 人→] n. person who holds the possession of a room, land, etc. by paying rent 房客；佃戶；承租者：I am the owner of the house, he is a tenant. 我是房東，他是房客。  ▽tenantry [tenant;-ry n.] n. [總稱]承租人 tenantable [tenant;-able a.] a.可租賃的 tenancy [ten;-ancy n.] n.租用   tenacious [ten=to hold 持；-ac;-ious a.=tending to 有……傾向的→] a. tending to hold opinion, belief, etc. strong;stubborn 堅強的；固執的：He is tenacious of his purpose.他的目標始終如一。  ▽tenacity [ten;-ac;-ity n.] n.堅強；固執   continent [con-(com-)=together 一起；tin=to hold 保持；-ent n.=thing 物→「land that holds together 保持成一塊的土地」→] n. mass of land holding together;large land mass of the earth 大陸；大洲：the continent of Africa 非洲大陸  ▽continental [continent;-al a.] a.大陸的；大陸性的   continue [con-(com-)=together 一起；tinu (tenere 的完成時詞干)=to hold 保持；-e→「to hold one thing together with another 使一事物與另一事物保持相連」→] v. go on happening;go forward 連續；繼續：He left but the meeting continued.他走了，但會議繼續開。  ▽continual [continu(e);-al a.] a.不斷的；頻繁的（常用於壞事） continuous [continu(e);-ous a.] a.連續的；繼續的 continuity [continu(e);-ity n.] n.連續性；繼續性	
92. tend, tens, tent [L]=	to stretch 伸 在常用詞attend，attention，extend，pretend 和intense 中，可以看到tend，tens，tent 這 三個同源異形根。tend 來自拉丁動詞tendere，意思為to stretch（伸開，伸長，延伸）；tens 和tent 都是這個拉丁動詞的動名詞詞干（tendere 有兩個動名詞形式：tensum 和tentum）， 主要用來構成相應的名詞和形容詞。   attend [at-(ad-)=to 向；tend=to stretch 伸→「to stretch one's mind to 把心思伸向」→] v.１ pay notice or care to;fix the mind on 注意；專心：Please attend to what he is saying.注意聽他講。 ２ be present at 出席：to attend a meeting 出席會議  ▽attendance [attend;-ance n.] n.看護，照料；出席（人數） attendant [attend;-ant n./a.] n.僕役，侍從a.伴隨的 attention [at-;tent;-ion n.] n.注意；注意力 attentive [at-;tent;-ive a.] a.注意的；當心的   extend [ex-=out 出；tend=to stretch 伸→] v.１ stretch out 伸出：He extended his arms in front of him.他向前伸出雙臂。２ make longer orgreater 延長；擴大：We are to extend the railway to the city.我們計劃把鐵路延長到那座城市。  ▽extent [ex-;tent] n.長度；廣度；限度；程度 extension [ex-;tens;-ion n.] n.伸長；擴大 extensive [ex-;tens;-ive a.] a.廣大的；廣泛的 extensible [ex-;tens;-ible a.] a.可延伸的；可擴展的   intend [in-=upon 在……上面；tend=to stretch 伸→「to stretch one's eye upon something 把目 光伸到某事之上」→] v.１ plan or purpose 打算：What do you intend to do next?下一步你打 算怎麼辦？２ mean to be 意指：What did he intend by that remark?他說那話是什麼意思？  ▽intendance [intend;-ance n.] n.監督；管理 intendant [intend;-ant n.] n.監督人；管理人 intent [in-;tent] a.集中的；專心致志的n.意圖；含義 intention [in-;tent;-ion n.] n.意圖；目的；意義；意旨 pretend [pre- = before 在……之前；tend = to stretch 伸展→「to stretch one's mind before the public 在眾人面前展開或誇張自己的想法」→] v.１ profess, or claim 聲稱；自稱：He pretends to be a scholar.他自稱學者。２ profess falsely;give a false appearance 偽稱；假裝：Don't pretend to know what you do not know.不要不懂裝懂。  ▽pretender [pretend;-er n.] n.佯裝者；冒充者；妄求者 pretense [pre-;tense] n.假裝；自命；借口；托詞 pretension [pre-;tens;-ion n.] n.要求；權利；借口；自稱 pretentious [pre-;tent;-i-;-ous a.] a.自負的；矯飾的   intense [in-=to 到；tens=to stretch 伸；-e→「being stretched to a high degree 伸展到高度的」 →] a.１ strained 緊張的：intense but orderly work 緊張而有秩序的工作２ extreme 極度 的：intense heat 酷熱３ strong in quality or feeling 強烈的：intense sorrow 強烈的悲痛  ▽intension [intens(e);-ion n.] n.緊張；強度；加強 intensive [intens(e);-ive a.] a.加強的；集中的；深入細緻的 intensity [intens(e);-ty n.] n.（思想、感情的）強烈；強度 intensify [intens(e);-ify v.] v.加強；加劇   tense [tens=to stretch 伸展；-e→]Ⅰa. stretched tightly;strained 繃緊的；緊張的：tense situation 緊張的形勢→Ⅱv. cause to be stretched or strained 拉緊；使緊張：to tense the muscles 繃緊肌 肉  ▽tensity [tens(e) a.;-ity n.] n.緊張；緊張度 tension [tens(e) v.;-ion n.] n.繃緊；緊張 tensile [tens(e) v.;-ile a.] a.拉力的；能伸長的 tensor [tens(e) v.;-or n.] n.張肌；張量   tend [tend=to stretch 伸→] v.１ stretch or develop in some direction 伸向；趨向：The prices are tending upward.物價趨於上漲。２ incline 傾向：to tend to optimism 有樂觀主義傾向  ▽tendency [tend;-ency n.] n.趨向；傾向；傾向性 tendentious [tend;-ent;-i-;-ous] a.有傾向性的；有偏見的   contend [con-(com-)=together 共同；tend=to stretch 伸長→「to stretch for something together 共同伸取某物」→] v. １ strive; struggle in emulation 競爭；鬥爭：to contend for spheres of influence 爭奪勢力範圍２ debate or dispute 爭論：He often contends against me.他常常與我 爭論。  ▽contender [contend;-er n.] n.競爭者；鬥爭者；爭論者 contention [con-;tent;-ion n.] n.競爭；爭論；論點 contentious [con-;tent;-i-;-ous a.] a.好爭論的；引起爭論的   distend [dis-=away 開；tend=to stretch 伸展→] v.１ stretch away;stretch in three dimensions 擴 伸；膨脹：Iron distends by heat.鐵受熱膨脹。２ swell 腫脹：The injured wrist began to distend up.受傷的腕部開始腫起來。  ▽distension [dis-;tens;-ion n.] n.擴張；膨脹；腫脹 distensible [dis-;tens;-ible a.] a.可膨脹的 ostentation [os-(obs-) = in front of 在……之前；tent = to stretch 展開；-ation n.=the act 表行 為→「the act of stretching one's belongings in front of others 在他人面前展示財物」→] n.１ act of showing;display to draw attention or admiration 顯耀；賣弄：I hate ostentation in any form. 我憎惡任何形式的虛飾。２ boasting 出風頭：to be free from ostentation 杜絕風頭主義  ▽ostentatious [os-;tent;-atious a.] a.賣弄的；虛飾的 ostensive [os-;tens;-ive a.] a.明顯表示的；表面的；詭稱的	
93. tract [L]=	to draw 拉，抽 詞根tract 的意思與tend 正好相反，它來自拉丁動詞trahere 的動名詞詞干，意為to draw（拉， 抽）。在英語中，tract 直接作為名詞，意思為「一片土地」，「地帶」。 attratct [at-(ad-) = towards 向；tract = to draw 拉→] v. draw towards oneself 吸引：A magnet attracts iron.磁石吸鐵。  ▽attraction [attract;-ion n.] n.吸引；吸引力 attractive [attract;-ive a.] a.有吸引力的   contract [con-(com-)=together 一起；tract=to draw 拉→「to draw together 拉在一起」→]Ⅰv. １ draw together and become more compact 收縮：Cold contracts metals.金屬遇冷收縮。２ draw (two sides) together to make a legal agreement 締結（條約）；訂立（合同）：The two countries contracted an alliance.兩國締結了盟約。→Ⅱn. a legal agreement that draws together two sides 契約；合同：to sign a contract 簽訂契約  ▽contraction [contract v.;-ion n.] n.收縮；縮約詞 contracture [contract v.;-ure n.] n. [醫學]攣縮 contractive [contract v.;-ive a.] a.收縮的；有收縮性的 contractual [contract n.;-u-;-al a.] a.契約的   extract [ex-=out;tract=to draw 抽→]Ⅰv.１ draw out or pull out 抽出；拔出：to extract a bad tooth 拔掉壞牙２draw out or obtain by squeezing 抽取；搾取：to extract juice from sugarcanes 從甘蔗搾出糖汁３ draw out or copy imformation from a book, etc.摘錄；引用：to ex-tract a passage from the story 從故事中選出一段→Ⅱn.１ anything drawn out 抽出的東西：beef extract 牛肉汁２ passage copied out 摘錄：extracts from newspapers 報刊摘錄  ▽extraction [extract;-ion n.] n.抽出（物）；提出（物）；摘要 extractive [extract;-ive a.] a.抽出的；提取的   retract [re-=back 回；tract=to draw 抽→] v.１ draw back or draw in 抽回；縮進：The cat retracted its claws.貓把爪子縮了回去。２ draw back or take back (a remark, promise, etc.)收回；取消（意 見、諾言等）：He retracted the insult and apologized.他收回無禮之詞並賠禮道歉。  ▽retraction [retract;-ion n.] n.收回；撤消；縮回；縮進 retractive [retract;-ive a.] a.縮回的；易縮回的 retractile [retract;-ile a.] a.（爪等）能縮回的；收縮的   detract [de-=away 去；tract=to draw 抽→] v. draw away or take away a part of (value, reputation, etc.) 減損；貶低：The criticisms do not detract from his merit.批評並不貶低他的功績。  ▽detraction [detract;-ion n.] n.減損；貶低 detractive [detract;-ive a.] a.減損的；貶低的   distract [dis-=apart 分開；tract=to draw 抽，牽引→] v. draw apart (the mind), or divert (the attention)引開（心思）；分散（注意力）：The noise distracted me form reading.吵鬧聲使我無 法專心讀書。  ▽distraction [distract;-ion n.] n.精神渙散；精神錯亂 protract [pro- = forward 向前；tract = to draw 拉→「to draw the time forward 把時間向前拉」 →] v. prolong 拖延，延長：Can you protract your stay for two days?你能在這兒多呆兩天嗎？  ▽protraction [protract;-ion n.] n.延長；拖延 subtract [sub- = under, down 下；tract = to draw 拉→「to draw down a quantity 把數量拉下」 →] v. take away by deducting 去掉；減去：to subtract the expenditure 裁減開支  ▽subtraction [subtract;-ion n.] n.減去；減法運算 subtractive [subtract;-ive a.] a.減少性的；帶負號的 subtrahend [sub-;trah;-end n.] n.減數	
94. un [L]=	one 一 詞根un 來自拉丁數字形容詞unus，意思是one（一）。從形態上看，它與前綴un-完全一樣， 但兩者含義不同，發音也不一樣。詞根un 總是發[ju:n]，而前綴un-總是發[?n]。 unify [un =one 單一；-ify v. =to make 使……→] v. make into one, or consolidate 使成一體；使 統一：We will unify our country.我們一定要統一祖國。  ▽unifiable [unif(y);-iable a.] a.可統一的；能一致的 unifier [unif(y);-ier n.] n.統一者；使一致者 unification [unif(y);-ication n.] n.統一；聯合   unite [un=one 一；-ite v.=to make 使……→] v. make one;join into one;combine 統一；聯合；團 結：the United Nations 聯合國  ▽united [unit(e);-ed a.] a.團結的；聯合的；統一的 unitive [unit(e);-ive a.] a.統一的；團結的；（傾向）聯合的   union [un=one 一；-ion n.=the state or result 表行為狀態或結果→「the state or result of being one 成為一體的狀態或結果」→] n.１ uniting or the state of being united 聯合；團結：Union gives strength.團結就是力量。２ united group of countries or states 聯邦；聯盟：the former Soviet Union 前蘇聯３ association or league 聯合會；協會：labor union 工會  ▽unionism [union;-ism n.] n.工會主義；工聯主義 unionist [union;-ist n.] n.工會主義者；工聯主義者 unionize [union;-ize v.] v.使成為工會；使加入工會   unity [un=one 一；-ity=the quality 表性質→「the quality of being one 單一的性質」→] n.１ oneness;a single whole 單一性；整體：A nation has more unity than a group of tribes.一個國家 比一群部落有更多的單一性。２ the agreement of aims and interests 一致；統一：the unity between the army and the people 軍民一致３ the state of being united 團結：Unity is strength. 團結就是力量。   unit [un=one 單一；-it n.=thing 物→] n. thing regarded as a complete and single one 單一體；單 位：monetary unit 貨幣單位  ▽unitary [unit;-ary a.] a.單元的；一元的；單一的 unitize [unit;-ize v.] v.使成一個單位   unique [un=one 一；-ique (-ic) a.=of……的→] a. of one only;sole 唯一的；獨一的：This stamp is unique.這是獨張的郵票。  ▽uniqueness [unique;ness n.] n.唯一性；獨一性 請注意un 常帶有連接字母-i-，以uni 的形式參加構詞。   uniform [uni=one 一；form=form 式樣→]Ⅰa. of one form;alike all over 一樣的；相同的：The two boxes are of uniform size and shape.兩隻箱子的大小和形狀是一樣的。→Ⅱn. certain form of clothing for all members of a group 制服：The soliders are in full uniform.戰士們穿著全套軍禮 服。  ▽uniformity [uniform a.;-ity n.] n.一式；一律 uniformize [uniform a.;-ize v.] v.使一樣；使一致   unicorn [uni=one 一；corn=horn 獸角→] n. imaginary animal with one horn 獨角獸（古代西歐 傳說中的一種神獸）   unilateral [uni=one 一；later=side 邊，方面；-al a.=of……的→] a. of one side;one-sided 單邊的； 單方面的：unilateral contract 單方面承擔義務的契約   unison [uni=one 一；son=sound 聲音→「one sound or voice 一個聲音，一個調子」→] n.１ the singing in one note by everybody 齊唱：to sing in unison 齊聲歌唱２ perfect agreement 一致， 調和：to work in unison 協調一致地工作  ▽unisonant [unison;-ant a.] a.一致的；[音]同音的；同度的	
95. ven, vent [L]=	to come 來 在常用詞convene，convenient，invent 和prevent 中，有一對同源異形根ven 和vent，意思 相當於to come（來）或to happen（發生）。ven 來自拉丁動詞venire 的不定式詞干；vent 是動名詞詞干。   convene [con-(com-)=together 一起；ven=to come 來；-e→] v. come or call together;assemble 集 合；召集：The committee convened every Monday.委員會每星期一開會。  ▽convener [conven(e);-er n.] n.會議召集人 convention [con-;vent;-ion n.] n.會議；召集；常規 conventicle [con-;vent;-icle n.] n.集會；集會場所   convenient [con-(com-)=together 一起；ven=to come 來；-i-;-ent a.=having the quality 有……性 質的→ 「 easy for people to come together 便於人們來到一起的」 → ] v. １ within easy reach;handy 近便的；附近的：My house is in a convenient location for shopping.我住的地方上 街買東西很近便。２ suited to what one needs 便利的；方便的：convenient time 方便的時 間  ▽convenience [con-;ven;-ience n.] n.便利；方便；適當的機會   event [e-(ex-)=out 出；vent=to come 來→「something that comes out or happens 出來或出現 的事情」→] n.１ coming out, or result 結局；結果：Those who play with fire will get burned in the event. 玩火者終將自焚。２ happening;incident or occurrence 事件；事變；大事：historical events 歷史事件  ▽eventual [event;-u-;-al a.] a.最後的；結局的；可能發生的 eventuate [event;-u-;-ate v.] v.結果；歸結 eventful [event;-ful a.] a.多事的；多變故的   invent [in-=upon 到；vent=to come 來→「to come upon 來到，碰上」→] v. think up or make something new;originate or create for the first time 發明；創造：The first compass was invented in China. 指南針是中國首先發明的。  ▽invention [invent;-ion n.] n.發明；創造；發明物；創造力 inventive [invent;-ive a.] a.發明創造的；有創造力的   prevent [pre-=before 先；vent=to come 來→「to come before so act earlier 先來所以早行動」 →] v.１ keep from happening by taking measures beforehand 預防：to prevent diseases 預防疾 病２hinder effectually 妨礙：A poor vocabulary prevents me from getting ahead.詞彙量太少妨 礙我進步。  ▽prevention [prevent;-ion n.] n.預防；妨礙 preventive [prevent;-ive a./n.] a.預防的n.預防措施 preventable [prevent;-able a.] a.可預防的   avenue [a-(ad-)=to 到；ven=to come 來；-ue n.=thing 物→「way for people to come to some place 讓人們來到某地的路」→] n.１ way to a result; the means of getting something 途徑；手段： an avenue toprosperity 通向繁榮的途徑２ road;wide street 道路；大街：the Fifth Avenue in New York 紐約的第五大街   intervene [inter-=between 在……之間；ven=to come 來；-e→] v. come between; be between 干 涉；介入：I won't intervene your private affairs.我不想干涉你的私事。  ▽intervenient [interven(e);-i-;-ent a.] a.干涉的；介入的 intervention [inter-;vent;-ion n.] n.干涉；介入   revenue [re-=back 回；ven=to come 來；-ue n.=thing 物→「thing that comes back from a certain source 從某種來源收回來的東西」→] n.１ income 收入：one's revenue 一個人的總收入２ the income of a state 國家歲入；稅收：the Public Revenue 國庫收入  ▽revenuer [revenu(e);-er n.] n.稅務官   adventure [ad-=to 到；vent=to come 來；-ure n.=the result 表結果→「the result of a coming to somebody 來到某人身上的事情」→]Ⅰn.１ chance 機會；運氣２ chance one takes;risk 冒險： military adven-ture 軍事冒險→Ⅱv.１ chance or risk 拿……進行冒險：He adven-tured his life to save you.他冒生命危險去救你。２ risk oneself 冒險：He adventured on commercial speculation. 他冒險作商業投機。  ▽adventurism [adventur(e) n.;-ism n.] n.冒險主義 adventurous [adventur(e) v.;-ous a.] a.愛冒險的；有危險性的   circumvent [circum-=around 環繞；vent =to come 來→] v.１ come or move around 圍繞；繞行 ２ surround so as to capture by wit 圍困：to circumvent enemy troops 圍困敵軍３sidestep;keep away from 迴避：to circumvent the law 鑽法律的空子  ▽circumvention [circumvent;-ion n.] n.圍繞；包圍；迴避	
96. vert, vers [L]=	to turn 轉 詞根vert 來自拉丁動詞vertere，意為to turn（轉，旋轉，轉變）。vers 是這個動詞的反覆形 式versare 的詞幹部分，也是動名詞versum 的詞幹部分，可以用來構成動詞、名詞或形容詞。 convert [con-(com-)表加強詞義；vert = to turn 轉變→] v. １ turn or change 改變；改成：to convert an old temple into a night school 把舊廟改成夜校２ transform 轉變，變換：to convert dollars into pounds 把美元換成英鎊  ▽convertible [convert;-ible a.] a.可改變的；可轉換的 conversion [con-;vers;-ion n.] n.變換；轉化；更換   converse [con-(com-)表加強詞義；vers=to keep turning 不斷轉變；-e→「to keep turning one's ideas into another's, or exchange ideas 不斷把自己的想法變成對方的想法，交換看法」→] v. talk familiarly 交談；談話/Whom did you converse with just now?剛才你和誰交談了？  ▽conversation [convers(e);-ation n.] n.談話；會話 conversable [convers(e);-able a.] a.容易談得來的；健談的   reverse [re-=back, against 回，反；vers=to turn 轉；-e→] v.１ turn back;return 97. vid, vis [L]=	to see 看見 在常用詞evident，provide，divide，television 和visit 中，vid 和vis 是一對同源根。vid 來自 拉丁動詞videre，其意思是to see（看見），vis 是它的動名詞詞干。   evident [e-(ex-)=out 出；vid=to see 看；-ent a.=-ing……的→「seeing out 看得出的」→] a. easily seen or recognized;clear 顯而易見的；明白的：It is evident that you have made much progress. 顯然你已經取得很大的進步。  ▽evidence [e-;vid;-ence n.] n.明顯；明白；證據 evidential [evident;-i-;-al a.] a.證據的；證明的 self-evident [self-;evident a.] a.不證自明的   provide [pro-=beforehand 事先；vid=to see 看；-e→「to see beforehand 事先預見到」→] v. １ prepare or supply beforehand 預備；供給：to provide the food 供應食物２ supply with necessary things for life;support 提供生計；贍養：to provide for five children 贍養五個孩子  ▽provider [provid(e);-er n.] n.供應者；家庭的供養人 provision [pro-;vis;-ion n.] n.供應；供應品；預備   divide [di-(dis-)=apart 分開；vid=to n.] n.除數 division [di-;vis;-ion n.] n.分開；劃分；分配 divisible [di-;vis;-ible a.] a.可分的；可除盡的   provident [pro-=beforehand 事先；vid=to see 看見；-ent a.=-ing……的→] a. seeing beforehand and providing for the future;prudent 有遠見的；遠慮的：provident statesmen 有遠見的政治家  ▽providence [pro-;vid;-ence n.] n.遠見；[大寫]天意；上帝 providential [provident;-i-;-al a.] a.上帝的；天意的   television [tele-=far 遠；vis=to see 看；-ion n.=the 參觀學校→Ⅱ n. visiting 參觀；訪問：to pay a visit to an exhibition 參觀展覽會  ▽visitor [visit v.;-or n.] n.參觀者；遊客；訪問者；來賓 visitation [visit v.;-ation n.] n.訪問；探望；視察；巡視   advise [ad-=to 到；vis=to see 看；-e→「to see to, 98. viv, vit [L]=	to live;life 活；生命 viv 和vit 是同源異形根。viv 來自拉丁動詞vivere，意為to live（活，生活）；vit 來自同根拉 丁名詞vita，意為life（生活，生命）。   vivid [viv=to live 活；-id a.=characterized by 有……特點的→「charac-terized by living 特別活的」 →] a.１ lively;active 有生氣的；活潑的：The boy has a vivid imagination.那男孩的想像力很活 躍。２lifelike 生動的：His novels are full of vivid characterizations.他的小說充滿栩栩如生的人 物描寫。  ▽vividness [vivid;-ness n.] n.活潑；活躍；生動；逼真   revive [re-=again 再；viv=to live 生活；-e→] v.１ live again;make to live again 再生；使復活： The doctor revived him by artificial respira-tion.醫生施行人工呼吸救活了他。２ bring back to health, strength, or consciousness 使恢復精力；使甦醒：The rain revived the withered plants. 雨水使枯萎的作物復甦了。  ▽revival [reviv(e);-al n.] n.復活；甦醒；復興 revivable [reviv(e);-abl a.] a.可復活的；可甦醒的；可恢復的 survive [sur- (super-) = beyond 超；viv = to live 活；-e→] v. １ live beyond or outlive 比…… 活得長：She survived her husband for two years.她比丈夫多活兩年。２ live after coming close to death;remainalive 倖存；活下來：Others died in the accident, but he survived.其他人死於那 次事故，他倖免了。  ▽survival [surviv(e);-al n.] n.倖存；殘存；殘存物 survivor [surviv(e);-or n.] n.倖存者；逃生者   vital [vit=life 生命；-al a.=pertaining to……的→] a.１ pertaining to life or necessary for life 生 命的；生命攸關的：Oxygen is vital for all animals.氧氣是一切動物生存所必需的。２ full of life 充滿活力的：a vital youth 朝氣蓬勃的青年  ▽vitality [vital;-ity n.] n.生命力；活力 vitalize [vital;-ize v.] v.給予……生命力；使有生氣   revivify [re-=again 再，復；viv=to live 活；-ify v.=to make 使……→] v. make to live again; 99. voc, vok [L]=	to call；voice 叫喊；聲音 詞根voc 來自拉丁動詞vocare（意為to call「叫喊」）或者同根拉丁名詞vox 的屬格形式vocis （意為voice「聲音」）。vok 是voc 的同音異體。其實，voice 就是voc 的派生詞，它是從法 語引進英語的。   advocate [ad-=to 對；voc=to call 叫喊；-ate n.=person 人→「person who calls to another's aid 對他人呼喊助威者」→]Ⅰn. person whopleads in favor of another;defender 辯護者；擁護者： a warm advocate of a new theory 一種新理論的熱烈擁護者→Ⅱv. speak in favor of;recommend 擁護；提倡：to advocate free speech 提倡言論自由  ▽advocator [advocat(e);-or n.] n.提倡者；擁護者 advocacy [ad-;voc;-acy n.] n.辯護；擁護；提倡   provoke [pro-=forth 向前；vok=to call 呼喊；-e→] v.１ call forth, or arouse 喚起；引起：His slip of tongue provoked shouts of laughter.他一時失言引起哄堂大笑。２ call out, or challenge, or stimulate 對……挑釁；煽動；刺激：The waiter's insult provoked me to anger.侍者的侮辱激怒 了我。  ▽provocation [pro-;voc;-ation n.] n.惹起；激怒；挑釁 provocative [pro-;voc;-ative a.] a.激怒的；挑釁的   vocal [voc=voice 聲音；-al a.=pertaining to……的→] a.１ pertaining to voice, speaking, etc. 聲 音的；發音的：vocal organs 發音器官２ expressing oneself freely in words 暢所欲言的：vocal critic 暢言無忌的批判家  ▽vocalic [vocal;-ic a.] a. [語音學]元音的；與元音有關的 vocalist [vocal;-ist n.] n.歌唱家；聲樂家 vocalize [vocal;-ize v.] v.發音；說；唱   vocation [voc=to call 喊；-ation n.=the state or result 表狀態或結果→「the state or result of being called by God, one's interest, etc.為上帝、個人興趣等所呼喚或感召的狀態或結果」→] n.１ job which one feels he is chosen to do certainly 天職；使命：I feel no vocation for teaching.我覺得 我天生就不是教書的。２ one's main job;regular occupation 職業；行業：She chose music as her vocation.她選擇音樂為職業。  ▽vocational [vocation;-al a.] a.職業的；業務的   avocation [a-(ab-)=away 離開；voc=to call 召喚；-ation n. 表行為結果→「calling one away from his regular employment 使人離開其主業的召喚」→] n. hobby or diversion;secondary job 業餘 愛好；副業：My uncle's vocation is medicine, his avocation is music.我叔叔的職業是醫生，業 余愛好是音樂。   evoke [e-(ex-)=out 出；vok=to call 呼喚；-e→] v.１ call out, or summon forth 呼喚出；召出： The photo evoked his memories of the past.那張照片喚起他對過去的回憶。２ call out, or produce (a reaction)引起（反應）：His words evoked great indignation.他的話引起強烈的憤慨。  ▽evocation [e-;voc;-ation n.] n.引起；喚起 evocative [e-;voc;-ative a.] a.喚起……的；引起……的   invoke [in-=upon 於……之上；vok=to call 呼喚；-e→] v.１ call upon (as for aid, protection, etc.) 要求（幫助）；祈求（保佑）：to invoke God's blessing 祈求上帝賜福２ appeal to (a law or help) 訴諸；援引（法規）：The lawyer invoked an amendment.律師援引了一項修正案條文。  ▽invocation [in-;voc;-ation n.] n.祈禱；援引 invocatory [in-;voc;-atory a.] a.祈禱的；求神的   revoke [re-=back 回；vok =to call 召喚；-e→「to call back a messenger 把信使召喚回來」→] v. concel;withdraw (a decree, permission, etc.)撤回；廢除；取消（法律、允諾等）：The committee revoked a decision.委員會取消了一項決議案。  ▽revocation [re-;voc;-ation n.] n.撤回；取消；廢除 revocatory [re-;voc;-atory a.] a.廢除的；撤銷的   vocable [voc=voice 聲音； -a-;-ble n.=thing 物→ 「 that which stands for voice or sound in a language 在一種語言中表示聲音的東西」→] n. word in form and sound than in meaning（作為 音與形單位不作為意義單位的）詞；語 vocabulary [vocabul (= vocable) = word 詞，語；-ary n. = thing 物→「whole body of words 詞 語的整體」→] n. words used in a language or by a person, etc.一種語言的詞彙；（一個人等的） 詞彙量：You should improve your vocabulary.你要擴大詞彙量。	
100. volv, volut [L]=	to roll 滾，轉 這是我們在第二部分中介紹的最後一個詞根。volv 來自拉丁動詞volvere，意為to roll（滾動） 或to turn（轉動）。volut 是這個動詞的動名詞詞干。此外，這個詞根還有vol 和volt 兩個異 體。   involve [in-=into 進入；volv=to roll 滾，卷；-e→「to roll into 滾進去，捲入」→] v.１ bring into （trouble, difficulty, etc.）使捲入；使陷入：to get involved in an argument 捲入糾紛２ include as a necessary part 必須包含：Building a good vocabulary involves much effort.擴大詞彙量的過 程包含著許多的努力。  ▽involvement [involve;-ment n.] n.捲入；牽連；包含 involution [in-;volut;-ion n.] n.捲入；糾纏   revolve [re-=back 回；volv=to roll 滾，轉；-e→「to roll back;to roll around 轉回去，轉圈圈」 →] v.１ move in a circle around a center;rotate 旋轉；周轉：The earth revolves around the sun. 地球繞太陽周轉。２ occur regularly again and again 週期性發生：Seasons revolve every year. 季節年年循環。  ▽revolver [revolv(e);-er n.] n.旋轉者；左輪手槍；轉爐   revolution [revolut=to revolve 旋轉，循環；-ion n.=the act or result 表行為或結果→] n.１ revolving 旋轉， 循環：the revolution of the earth around the sun 地球繞日運轉一周２ complete turning or changing in society, outlook, etc. 變革；革命：Sometimes revolutions are the locomotives of history.有時革命是歷史前進的火車頭。  ▽revolutionary [revolution;-ary a.] a.革命的n.革命者 revolutionize [revolution;-ize v.] v.使革命化；使徹底改革 volume [vol (volv)=to roll 卷；-ume n.=thing 物→「thing that rolls up 捲起來的東西」→] n. roll or scroll which is the form of an ancient book;book 一卷（古書卷成一卷）；一冊：The novel is in three volumes.這部小說有三卷。  ▽voluminous [volum(e);-in;-ous a.] a.多卷的；著作多的   evolve [e-(ex-)=out 外；volv=to roll 捲動；-e→「to roll out, or to unroll 向外捲動，展開」→] v. １ unfold; develop 展開；發展：His idea evolved into a plan for increasing production.他的想 法發展為一項增產的計劃。２ develop from a lower to a higher stage 演變，進化：Man has evolved from the ape.人是從類人猿進化來的。  ▽evolution [e-;volut;-ion n.] n.發展；展開；進化 evolutive [e-;volut;-ive a.] a.（促進）發展的；（促進）進化的   devolve [de-=down 下；volv=to roll 滾，轉；-e→] v. １ roll down or flow down 滾下；流下２ hand down;pass over in succession 轉移；移交：He has devolved his duties upon me.他已經把 工作移交給我了。  ▽devolution [de-;volut;-ion n.] n.（責任等的）轉移；移交   revolt [re-=back, against 回，抗；volt (volut)=to roll or turn 轉→「to roll back or to turn against 轉回頭，轉而相抗」→]Ⅰv. rise in rebellion 造反，反叛：The peasants revolted against the landlords.農民起來造地主的反。→Ⅱn. uprising; rebellion against authority 起義；反叛：armed revolts 武裝起義 voluble [volu (volut)=to roll 滾；轉；-ble (-able) a.=easy to 易……的→] a. １ easy to roll 易滾 動的；易旋轉的：the voluble and restless earth 旋轉不息的地球２ flowing smoothly in speech 說話流利的：voluble speaker 言語流暢的演說家  ▽volubly [volub(le);-ly ad.] ad.流利地；滔滔不絕地
